001DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S286

cd19/cd22双特异性car-t细胞治疗复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤及其机制研究：一项前瞻性、单臂、单中心、2期临床试验

cd19/cd22 bispecific car-t cell therapy for relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma and mechanistic investigation: a prospective, single-arm, single-center, phase 2 clinical trial

P 患者群体

B细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤；大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=73；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CD19/CD22靶向CAR-T(同仁医院)；靶点：CD19，CD22；类别：CAR-T，自体细胞，经基因修饰；分组：试验组：CAR2219

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

最佳客观缓解率(ORR): 95.9% 最佳完全缓解率(CRR): 56.2% 中位无进展生存期(PFS): 未达到 中位总生存期(OS): 未达到 估计24个月PFS率: 68.5% [95%CI: 57.2-79.8%] 估计24个月OS率: 82.3% [95%CI: 73.5-91.1%] 不良事件: 中性粒细胞减少93.2%, 血小板减少76.7%, 贫血76.7%; CRS 83.6% (3级2例); ICANS 5.5% (3级2例, 4级1例)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Chimeric antigen receptor T-cells (CAR-T) targeting CD19 have shown promising benefits to patients of relapsed or refractory large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL), but only one-third patients got durable remission and the resistance mechanisms were complicated. CAR-T cells targeting CD22 were found to be effective in patients who failed previous anti-CD19 CAR-T cell therapy. Aims: In this prospective study, we aimed to evaluate the efficacy and safety of CD19/CD22 bispecific CAR-T cell therapy (CAR2219) in patients with R/R LBCL, and to explore the underlying mechanisms associated with therapeutic response using single-cell sequencing and in vitro experiments. Methods: Till February 10, 2026, this ongoing phase 2 clinical trial have enrolled 73 patients with R/R LBCL, and all were evaluable for efficacy and safety profiles. Bridging therapy was allowed. A 3-day lymphodepletion (cyclophosphamide: 250 mg/m2/d; fludarabine: 25 mg/m2/d) was followed by an intravenous dose of CAR2219 (2×10e6/kg). For patients who responded to CAR2219 therapy, maintenance therapy using PD-1 inhibitors, XPO1 inhibitors, BTK inhibitors, or HDAC inhibitors were also allowed. The primary endpoint was best overall response rate (ORR) as of 3 months post-CAR-T cells infusion. The secondary endpoints included best complete response rate (CRR), progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS), and adverse events (AE). Meanwhile, single-cell RNA sequencing was performed on CAR-T cell products collected from 14 patients; clustering and functional analyses were conducted after stratification by PFS with a cutoff of 6 months, and double-stranded RNA (dsRNA) levels in CAR-T cell products were detected by immunofluorescence.

结论（EHA原文）

CD19/CD22 bispecific CAR-T cell therapy demonstrated encouraging efficacy and a favorable safety profile in patients with R/R LBCL. Enrichment of specific CD4⁺ T cell subsets, activation of the interferon pathway, and activation of viral mimicry may be closely associated with the efficacy of this therapy. (ClinicalTrials.gov Identifier: NCT06081478)

002DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S284

cd19car t细胞扩增过程中支链氨基酸的生物利用度与lbcl中有利的t细胞状态和临床反应有关

branched-chain amino acid bioavailability during cd19 car t-cell expansion associates with favorable t-cell states and clinical response in lbcl

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=66

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Tisagenlecleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

支链氨基酸（缬氨酸和异亮氨酸）升高与完全缓解率及生存期延长显著相关 Profile A患者（氨基酸、葡萄糖、胰岛素、乳酸普遍升高）表现出更高的CD4和CD8 CAR-T细胞水平，以及平衡的CAR+和CAR- CD4中央记忆细胞和CD8效应记忆细胞比例，活化CD4 T细胞占优势 Profile B（饱和脂肪酸升高、氨基酸下降）和Profile C（普遍营养物质下降）患者CD4中央记忆细胞频率降低，Treg细胞富集，活化CD4 T细胞减少；Profile C还表现出活化CD8 T细胞增加

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The metabolic environment critically regulates T-cell activation, differentiation, and effector function. Distinct T-cell subsets exhibit specific metabolic programs: effector T cells are predominantly glycolytic or even lipogenic, whereas regulatory T-cells (T REG ) rely more heavily on oxidative and lipid metabolic pathways. Nutrient deprivation impairs effector function and promotes dysfunctional states. The host metabolic milieu may therefore represent an underappreciated determinant of CAR T-cell expansion and anti-tumor efficacy. Aims: We sought to determine whether dynamic changes in plasma nutrient availability following CD19 CAR T-cell infusion associate with T-cell subsets and clinical outcomes in patients with large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL). Methods: Plasma and cryopreserved peripheral blood mononuclear cells were collected at baseline (D0) and day 7 (D7) following infusion of axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel) or tisagenlecleucel in LBCL patients from the CeVi_Collection. Glucose, lactate, and insulin were quantified on the Roche Cobas 8000 platform. Amino acid concentrations were measured by ultra-performance liquid chromatography-tandem mass spectrometry (Waters Xevo-TQD), and plasma fatty acid composition was assessed by gas liquid chromatography with flame-ionization detection. Unsupervised hierarchical clustering of D0-D7 variations was used to define metabolic profiles. Single cell RNA-Seq was performed on sorted D7 CAR+ and CAR- T-cells (10x Genomics) to characterize T cell subsets and cellular states.

结论（EHA原文）

Dynamic changes in plasma nutrient availability following CD19 CAR T-cell therapy define distinct metabolic trajectories that associate with T-cell differentiation states and clinical outcome in LBCL. In particular, increased branched-chain amino acid bioavailability correlates with favorable CAR T-cell phenotypes and therapeutic response. These findings support the development of metabolic or nutritional interventions to optimize CAR T-cell expansion and anti-tumor efficacy.

003DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S236

vispa-cel，一种pd-1敲除的异基因抗cd19car-t细胞疗法，用于复发/难治性b细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤患者（鹿角1期临床试验）

vispa-cel, an allogeneic anti-cd19 car-t cell therapy with a pd-1 knockout, in patients with relapsed/refractory b cell non-hodgkin lymphoma (antler phase 1 clinical trial)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Vispacabtagene regedleucel (vispa-cel, formerly CB-010) is an allogeneic anti-CD19 CAR-T cell therapy manufactured from healthy donor T cells. The Cas9 chRDNA genome-editing technology is used for three genome edits: (1) KO of TRAC to reduce risk of GvHD, (2) insertion of a CD19-specific CAR (FMC63 scFv, 4-1BB), and (3) KO of PD-1 to prevent premature CAR-T cell exhaustion and potentially enhance antitumor activity. Aims: ANTLER is a Phase 1 trial (NCT04637763) with 3+3 dose escalation and expansion to evaluate the safety and efficacy of vispa-cel in patients (pts) with r/r B-NHL and determine the RP2D. Methods: All pts received lymphodepletion of sequential cyclophosphamide (60 mg/kg/day x 2 days) then fludarabine (25 mg/m 2 /day x 5 days) followed by a single infusion of vispa-cel. Three vispa-cel doses (40 million [M], 80M, and 120M cells) were evaluated in dose escalation and dose expansion. 80M cells was selected as the RP2D. Subsequently, a 2L LBCL confirmatory cohort prospectively evaluated donor-recipient matching ≥4 HLA alleles. A retrospective analysis was performed and identified LBCL pts treated with vispa-cel manufactured from a young donor (

结论（EHA原文）

Vispa-cel is an allogeneic CAR-T cell therapy that results in deep and durable responses on par with approved autologous CAR-T cell therapies in 2L LBCL pts with a generally well-tolerated safety profile supporting outpatient administration. Improved PFS was observed in pts treated with vispa-cel manufactured from young donors (

004DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S235

epcore dlbcl-1的结果：epcoritamab（epcor）与研究者选择的化学免疫疗法（cit）在复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤（r/r lbcl）患者中的随机3期研究

results from epcore dlbcl-1: randomized phase 3 study of epcoritamab (epcor) vs investigator’s choice chemoimmunotherapy (cit) in patients with relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma (r/r lbcl)

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=483；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：艾可瑞妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：试验组：Epcoritamab单药治疗；对照组：研究者选择的化学免疫治疗（包括R-GemOx和BR）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组：Epcoritamab单药治疗|||对照组：研究者选择的化学免疫治疗（包括R-GemOx和BR）

O 结局指标

主要终点PFS：HR 0.74 (95% CI 0.60-0.92; P=0.0059)，24个月PFS率：30% vs 13%|||关键次要终点OS：HR 0.83 (95% CI 0.67-1.04; P=0.1003)（未达到统计学显著性）|||完全缓解率(CRR)：38% vs 26% (名义P=0.0032)|||缓解持续时间(DOR)中位数：37个月 vs 6个月|||完全缓解持续时间(DOCR)中位数：未达到 vs 11个月|||至下次治疗时间(TTNT)中位数：7个月 vs 4个月 (名义P<0.0001)|||安全性：Epcor组3-4级感染30% vs 12%；5级TEAE 17% vs 6%；CRS 53%（3级3%）；ICANS 4%（3-4级1%）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Epcor is a CD3×CD20 bispecific antibody (bsAb) approved as monotherapy for R/R DLBCL after ≥ 2 prior lines of systemic treatment (pLOT). The phase 3 EPCORE DLBCL-1 trial (EudraCT No. 2020-003016-27) evaluated epcor monotherapy vs investigator’s choice CIT (rituximab + gemcitabine/oxaliplatin [R-GemOx] or bendamustine + rituximab [BR]) in R/R LBCL. Aims: To report primary results from EPCORE DLBCL-1. Methods: Eligible patients (pts) had CD20+ R/R LBCL, were ASCT-ineligible or relapsed after ASCT, and had ≥ 1 systemic pLOT (1 pLOT capped at 25%). Pts were randomized 1:1 to epcor monotherapy or CIT. Epcor was given in 28-d cycles (2 step-up doses then 48-mg full doses QW in C1–3, Q2W in C4–9, Q4W in C10+ until disease progression or unacceptable toxicity). R-GemOx was given as standard Q2W for four 28-d cycles and BR Q3W for six 21-d cycles. Dual primary endpoints were PFS (Lugano criteria; IRC) and OS.

结论（EHA原文）

EPCORE DLBCL-1 is the largest randomized phase 3 trial in R/R LBCL and the first to demonstrate a statistically significant improvement in PFS with a CD3×CD20 bsAb monotherapy vs combination CIT. Furthermore, compared with CIT, epcor resulted in clinically meaningful improvements in CRR, DOR, DOCR, and less frequent use of subsequent tx, demonstrating deep and durable responses. OS was not significantly different, being confounded by COVID-19 mortality and use of novel subsequent tx. Observed AEs were consistent with the established epcor safety profile and the expected profile for a CD3×CD20 bsAb.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: 483 pts (epcor 241; CIT 242 [R-GemOx 174; BR 68]) were randomized; 67% were randomized in 2022 or later, coinciding with the COVID-19 Omicron period. Median follow-up was 43.2 mo (epcor) and 42.3 mo (CIT). Median age was 71 y (range, 28–89); 53% of pts were from North America/Western Europe; 73% had ≥ 2 pLOT, and 34% had ≥ 3 pLOT; 69% were refractory to last line of treatment (tx); 15% had prior SCT, and 11% had prior CAR-T. \n A statistically significant improvement in PFS was demonstrated with epcor vs CIT (HR, 0.74 [95% CI, 0.60–0.92]; P =0.0059; 24-mo PFS: 30% vs 13%). Furthermore, clinically meaningful higher complete response rate (CRR: 38% vs 26%; nominal P value 0.0032), longer durability of response (median DOR 37 vs 6 mo; DOCR NR vs 11 mo) and longer TTNT (7 vs 4 mo; nominal P value \n Mean tx duration was longer for epcor vs CIT (11 vs 2 mo); 31% of pts received ≥ 12 cycles of epcor. Higher rates of grade 3–4 infections (30% vs 12%) and any-grade COVID-19 (36% vs 11%) were reported in the epcor arm; exposure-adjusted event rates were 4.3 vs 4.9 (grade 3–4 infections) and 4.4 vs 3.4 (any-grade COVID-19) per 100 pt-mo. Grade 5 TEAEs occurred in 17% vs 6% (exposure-adjusted, 1.5 vs 1.8 per 100 pt-mo) and were largely attributable to grade 5 COVID-19 (9% vs 2%). CRS was reported in 53% (grade 3, 3%) in the epcor arm and ICANS in 4% (grade 3–4, 1%). Conclusion: EPCORE DLBCL-1 is the largest randomized phase 3 trial in R/R LBCL and the first to demonstrate a statistically significant improvement in PFS with a CD3×CD20 bsAb monotherapy vs combination CIT. Furthermore, compared with CIT, epcor resulted in clinically meaningful improvements in CRR, DOR, DOCR, and less frequent use of subsequent tx, demonstrating deep and durable responses. OS was not significantly different, being confounded by COVID-19 mortality and use of novel subsequent tx. Observed AEs were consistent with the established epcor safety profile and the expected profile for a CD3×CD20 bsAb.

005DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2342

cd19/cd22双特异性car-t细胞治疗复发/难治性弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤后pd-1抑制剂和selinexor的维持治疗：回顾性分析

maintenance therapy with pd-1 inhibitor and selinexor following cd19/cd22 bispecific car-t cell therapy in relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: a retrospective analysis

P 患者群体

B细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤；大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=32；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

分组：维持治疗组：PD-1抑制剂（tislelizumab或serplulimab）+ selinexor

O 结局指标

中位随访时间：260天（范围59-529）|||维持治疗前完全缓解率：38%|||第1个月总缓解率：56%（完全缓解率38%）|||第3个月总缓解率：83%（完全缓解率57%）|||第6个月总缓解率：81%（完全缓解率71%）|||中位无进展生存期：407天|||估计1年无进展生存率：56.8%（95%CI: 0.40-0.80）|||估计1年总生存率：71.2%（95%CI: 0.53-0.95）|||中位总生存期：未达到|||CD3+PD-1+ T细胞显著减少（15例评估患者）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy targeting CD19 has revolutionized the treatment landscape for relapsed/refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (R/R DLBCL). Despite impressive initial response rates, disease relapse remains a significant challenge, often attributed to CAR-T cell exhaustion and immune evasion mechanisms. In our prospective phase 2 trial, CD19/CD22 bispecific CAR-T (CAR2219) demonstrated a remarkable 100% best overall response rate; however, strategies to prolong remission duration and prevent relapse are urgently needed. Maintenance therapy represents a promising approach to enhance response persistence by targeting underlying mechanisms of treatment failure. Programmed cell death protein 1 (PD-1) inhibitors have shown potential to reverse CAR-T cell exhaustion and restore anti-tumor immunity, while the exportin 1 (XPO1) inhibitor selinexor exhibits direct anti-lymphoma activity and synergistic effects when combined with immunomodulatory agents. Aims: To evaluate the efficacy, safety, and immunomodulatory effects of maintenance therapy combining PD-1 inhibitor with selinexor following CAR2219 therapy in patients with R/R DLBCL. Methods: This retrospective analysis included 32 patients enrolled in our prospective phase 2 clinical trial (NCT06081478) who achieved disease control following CAR2219 infusion and subsequently received planned maintenance therapy. The maintenance regimen consisted of PD-1 inhibitor (tislelizumab 200 mg or serplulimab 240 mg intravenously every 3 weeks) plus selinexor (40-60 mg orally once weekly) for 1-2 years duration. The primary endpoint was progression-free survival (PFS). Secondary endpoints included duration of response (DOR), overall survival (OS), safety profiles, and correlative biomarker analyses. Treatment responses were assessed according to Lugano 2014 criteria, and adverse events were graded per CTCAE version 5.0. Longitudinal monitoring of circulating T-cell subsets, including CD3+PD-1+ T-cells, was performed by flow cytometry in a subset of patients.

结论（EHA原文）

Maintenance therapy combining PD-1 inhibitor and selinexor following CD19/CD22 bispecific CAR-T cell therapy demonstrates promising clinical activity in R/R DLBCL, characterized by deepening responses over time and durable disease control. The observed reduction in PD-1+ T-cells supports an immunomodulatory mechanism of action. These findings warrant further investigation in prospective randomized trials to establish the optimal maintenance strategy post-CAR-T therapy.

Strategies to overcome these limitations, including combination with PD-1 blockade, often face issues with systemic toxicity and variable efficacy. Secondary endpoints included efficacy, CAR-T persistence, progression-free survival (PFS), and overall survival (OS). \n

PD-1Ab21-CD19 CAR-T therapy demonstrated a manageable safety profile and promising antitumor activity in patients with heavily pretreated R/R DLBCL. 007DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2323

循环car t细胞中cd4/cd8平衡对大b细胞淋巴瘤总生存率的双相预后影响

cd4/cd8 balance in circulating car t-cells shows biphasic prognostic impact on overall survival in large b-cell lymphomas

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=139

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

总CAR-T细胞水平与达到完全代谢反应(CMR)的关系：HR 1.12 per doubling (95%CI 1.04-1.21, Holm-adjusted p=0.022) DiffNorm与总生存期(OS)的早期关系：HR 1.31 per +0.1 DiffNorm increase (95%CI 1.10-1.56, Holm-adjusted p=0.006) DiffNorm与总生存期(OS)的晚期关系：HR 0.91 (0.85-0.97, p=0.006) CMR率：74.1% (103/139) ORR：86.3% 中位PFS：42.5个月 中位OS：58.1个月 CAR-T细胞持续可检测比例：M1 98.5%, M6 97.6%, M12 93.0%, M24 94.7%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Anti-CD19 CAR-T expansion/persistence and the balance of CD4+ vs CD8+ CAR T-cells may influence outcomes in large B-cell lymphomas (LBCL), but their temporal dynamics and phase-dependent prognostic value remain unclear. Aims: To assess (i) CAR T-cell persistence over 24 months and (ii) the association of CAR-T levels and DiffNorm with response kinetics and survival. Methods: In a single-center cohort of 139 consecutive patients treated with anti-CD19 CAR T-cells for R/R LBCL, CAR T-cell levels (total, CAR-CD4, CAR-CD8) were quantified by flow cytometry in peripheral blood from M1 to M24 (LOD 0.1% of lymphocytes). Time-to-complete metabolic response (CMR), PFS and OS were analyzed using a time-varying Cox model. DiffNorm ((CAR-CD4 - CAR-CD8)/(CAR-CD4 + CAR-CD8)) were analyzed using a piecewise time-varying Cox approach (day 21 cutpoint) to account for the sign inversion observed between peak and M3 in timepoint analyses, reflecting early expansion vs post-expansion phases. For time-to-CMR and PFS analyses, CAR T-cell measurements obtained after disease progression were excluded. Holm correction was applied for multiple comparisons.

结论（EHA原文）

CAR T-cells remain detectable in over 90% of patients throughout 2 years of follow-up. The CAR-CD4/CD8 balance undergoes a biologically meaningful inversion, from early CD8-dominant expansion to progressive CD4 predominance. Absolute CAR T-cell levels accelerate CMR achievement, while DiffNorm shows opposite phase-dependent associations with OS - early CAR-CD8 dominance favoring cytotoxic expansion, late CAR-CD4 predominance favoring immune memory - independent of baseline immune status. Pre-lymphodepletion CD4 lymphocyte count emerges as an independent prognostic factor. These findings warrant external validation and may inform risk stratification and product optimization.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Relapsed or refractory large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) treated with CAR-T therapy shows heterogeneous outcomes, and early identification of patients at risk of progression remains challenging. Tumor-informed circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) assays enable highly sensitive minimal residual disease (MRD) detection and offer a noninvasive strategy for dynamic monitoring. Aims: We aim to evaluate the prognostic impact of early and longitudinal patient-specific ctDNA assessment in LBCL patients receiving CAR-T therapy and its complementary role alongside PET/CT. Methods: Seventy-nine LBCL patients treated with CD19 CAR-T therapy and available liquid biopsy at day +7, +14, or +30 were included. Six lacked suitable molecular markers for MRD analysis, and 10 of the remaining 73 were excluded due to insufficient cfDNA input (

结论（EHA原文）

Tumor-informed ctDNA monitoring enables very early risk stratification after CAR-T therapy in LBCL, identifying high-risk patients within the first two weeks post-infusion, before radiologic assessment. At day +30, ctDNA MRD positivity shows strong prognostic value, and integration of molecular and metabolic response improves outcome discrimination. ctDNA analysis is particularly useful when PET findings generate uncertainty, clarifying disease status. These results support incorporating longitudinal ctDNA monitoring into prospective CAR-T trials to enable earlier, biology-driven, risk-adapted strategies.

009DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2352

晚些时候输注car‑t会增加细胞因子释放综合征（crs）：免疫治疗相关毒性昼夜节律调节的证据

later car‑t infusions increase cytokine release syndrome (crs): evidence for circadian modulation of immunotherapy-related toxicity

P 患者群体

多发性骨髓瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=96

I 干预措施

分组：上午输注组：CAR-T细胞；下午输注组：CAR-T细胞

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：上午输注组：CAR-T细胞；下午输注组：CAR-T细胞

O 结局指标

任何级别CRS发生率：AM组55%，PM组88%（p=0.013） 调整后OR (PM vs AM)：aOR 8.15 (95%CI 1.45-45.78, p=0.017) 托珠单抗和/或类固醇使用率：AM组59%，PM组88%（aOR 5.11, 95%CI 1.09-23.97, p=0.027） 每小时晚输注的CRS风险：aOR 1.82 (95%CI 1.14-2.90, p=0.012) 30或60天完全缓解率：AM组60%，PM组31%（OR 0.30, 95%CI 0.083-1.09, p=0.072） 无进展生存期：PM组有恶化趋势（HR ~1.25） 总生存期：无显著差异 严重CRS/ICANS：与输注时间无关 探索性分析：DLBCL亚组毒性更大，男性可能更明显

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Circadian rhythms regulate adaptive and innate immune responses through cell-intrinsic molecular clocks in T cells and macrophages, with core clock genes modulating T-cell activation, cytokine production, and inflammatory transcriptional programs. Proinflammatory mediators central to CRS exhibit diurnal oscillation, and macrophage cytokine transcription is under circadian control. Emerging clinical evidence indicates that chimeric antigen receptor (CAR)-T cell infusion timing may influence outcomes: later infusion times have been associated with inferior progression-free survival (PFS) and higher inflammatory markers (Luan, Blood 2025), and increased risks of mortality and neurotoxicity (Lyons, JCI Insight 2025). Mechanistic studies further demonstrate circadian regulation of CD8⁺ T-cell trafficking and function that can alter immunotherapy efficacy (Wang, Cell 2024). Whether infusion timing directly modulates CRS or immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) remains unclear. We hypothesized that circadian timing of CAR-T administration influences treatment-related inflammatory toxicity. Aims: To evaluate whether CAR‑T infusion time-of-day (and apheresis time) is associated with CRS/ICANS in adults receiving commercial CAR‑T. Methods: We conducted an IRB-approved retrospective study of 96 adults receiving commercially available CAR-T at a tertiary center (Jan 2018–Dec 2025). Infusion time was analyzed dichotomously (AM 00:00-11:59 vs PM 12:00-23:59) and continuously by clock-hour. The primary endpoint was CRS (any grade). Secondary endpoints included CRS ≥3, ICANS (any grade), tocilizumab and/or steroid use, complete remission (CR), PFS, and overall survival (OS). Multivariable logistic regression adjusted for age, sex, performance status, CAR-T dose, and product type; interaction and Bayesian subgroup analyses were exploratory.

结论（EHA原文）

Later CAR-T infusion time was independently associated with increased CRS incidence with an hour-dependent gradient consistent with circadian modulation. Because infusion timing is a modifiable exposure, prospective chronotherapy trials should test whether earlier scheduling reduces inflammatory toxicity without compromising clinical benefit.

starglo合格患者二线car-t治疗的疗效比较分析

outcomes of second-line car-t therapy in starglo-eligible patients: a comparative analysis

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=38；治疗线数/场景：二线

I 干预措施

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：二线CAR-T治疗（CAR-T） 对照组：STARGLO二线亚组（glofitamab, gemcitabine, oxaliplatin）

O 结局指标

2L CAR-T队列完全缓解率：65.8%；STARGLO 2L完全缓解率：63.5% 2L CAR-T队列24个月无进展生存率：38.9%（95% CI: 24.9-60.6）；STARGLO 2L：49.9%（95% CI: 38.8-61.0） 2L CAR-T队列24个月总生存率：50.1%（95% CI: 34.2-73.4）；STARGLO 2L：57.4%（95% CI: 47.9-66.9） 早期复发亚组：2L CAR-T队列24个月无进展生存率：45.0%（95% CI: 28.4-71.3）；STARGLO：40.2%（95% CI: 27.2-53.2） 早期复发亚组：2L CAR-T队列24个月总生存率：60.9%（95% CI: 42.1-88.2）；STARGLO：46.5%（95% CI: 35.2-57.8）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CAR-T therapy has redefined the treatment paradigm for relapsed or refractory (R/R) DLBCL and is the established second-line (2L) standard of care. However, this is based on pivotal trials comparing CAR-T to chemoimmunotherapy rather than bispecific antibodies (bsAbs). The Phase III STARGLO trial demonstrated the efficacy of glofitamab plus gemcitabine and oxaliplatin (Glofit-GemOx) in the 2L setting for autologous stem cell transplant (ASCT) ineligible patients. Aims: In the absence of direct comparative data, we aimed to evaluate whether 2L CAR-T patients meeting STARGLO inclusion criteria achieved comparable outcomes to the Glofit-GemOx arm benchmarks. Methods: We analyzed a real-world cohort of patients receiving 2L CAR-T therapy between 12/2022 and 09/2025. Patients were selected based on the specific inclusion and exclusion criteria of the Phase III STARGLO trial. To facilitate a rigorous comparison, individual patient data (IPD) were reconstructed from the published STARGLO 2L sub-analysis Kaplan-Meier curves using the Guyot iterative algorithm. Curves were digitized via WebPlotDigitizer using an automated extraction process with high-density coordinate sampling (ΔX and ΔY of 1 pixel) to capture all granular step changes in survival trajectories. Survival estimates were further refined using the published Number at Risk (NAR) for both progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) to account for censoring.

结论（EHA原文）

In this \"STARGLO-eligible\" real-world cohort, 2L CAR-T achieved high initial response rates. At 24 months, numerical differences in PFS and OS favored STARGLO in the general population, whereas in the high-risk early-relapse sub-population, 24-month PFS and OS were higher in the CAR-T cohort. The overlapping confidence intervals suggest comparable survival outcomes between these regimens in this sample. These signals warrant exploration in larger prospective cohorts to better define the 2L treatment landscape and refine patient selection.

O 结局指标

3个月ORR（研究者评估）：58.33% 3个月CRR（研究者评估）：41.67% 最佳ORR（研究者评估）：66.67% 最佳CRR（研究者评估）：41.67% 3个月ORR（IRC评估）：58.33% 3个月CRR（IRC评估）：58.33% 最佳ORR（IRC评估）：75.00% 最佳CRR（IRC评估）：58.33% 中位DOR、PFS、OS：未达到 细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：83.3%（均为1-2级） 神经毒性：未发生

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Relma-cel, a CD19-directed CAR-T therapy, is an approved treatment for relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-Cell lymphoma (LBCL). To reduce manufacturing costs and enhance supply-chain stability, an in-house lentiviral vector manufacturing process was established. This study was a post-approval bridging study to evaluate the relma-cel manufactured using the domestically produced lentiviral vector (JWLV011). Aims: To assess the efficacy, safety and pharmacokinetic (PK)/ pharmcodynamic (PD) profiles of relma-cel manufactured with JWLV011 in adult patients with R/R LBCL. Methods: This phase II study enrolled adults (≥18 years) with histologically confirmed R/R LBCL who had relapsed or progressed after ≥2 prior systemic therapies, including an anthracycline-containing regimen and anti-CD20 monoclonal antibody, or following autologous stem cell transplantation. Following by lymphodepleting chemotherapy with cyclophosphamide (250 mg/m 2 /day × 3 days) and fludarabine (25 mg/m 2 /day × 3 days), and then received a single infusion of relma-cel at a dose of 100 × 10 6 CAR + T cells. The primary endpoint was investigator-assessed objective response rate (ORR) at 3 months post-infusion.

结论（EHA原文）

Relma-cel manufactured using the domestically produced lentiviral vector demonstrated favorable efficacy and a manageable safety profile in adult patients with R/R LBCL. These findings support the feasibility of in-house lentiviral vector manufacturing without compromising clinical performance.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of July 15, 2025, 14 patients underwent leukapheresis and 12 received relma-cel. The median age was 61.5 years (range, 46–76; 41.7% ≥65 years), and 58.3% were male. High-risk disease features were common: 50.0% had an International Prognostic Index ≥3, 83.3% had Ann Arbor stage III/IV disease, 41.7% had elevated baseline lactate dehydrogenase, and 83.3% had the non-germinal center B-cell-like subtype. Prior therapies included ≥3 lines in 41.7% of patients; 25.0% had received polatuzumab vedotin and 25.0% had received CD3/CD20 bispecific antibodies (one patient was primary refractoriness, two patients were relapsed within 12 months of first-line therapy, and three patients were subsequently treated with bispecific antibodies, and all were refractory to bispecific antibody). Overall, 33.3% had relapsed disease, 66.7% were refractory to their most recent therapy. 41.7% of patients received bridging therapy. With a median follow-up was 4.6 months (range, 2.79–5.85), in the modified intent to treatment (mITT) population (n=12), the investigator-assessed ORR at 3 months was 58.33%, with a CRR of 41.67%, meeting the primary endpoint. The best investigator-assessed ORR was 66.67%, with a best CRR of 41.67%. Independent review committee (IRC)-assessed ORR at 3 months was 58.33%, with a CRR of 58.33%. The best ORR was 75.00%, with a best CRR of 58.33% ( Figure 1 ). Three patients refractory to bispecific antibodies achieved PR, PD and CR, respectively, at 1 month; excluding the patient with PD, the other two patients had PD and CR respectively at 3 months. Median DOR, PFS, and OS have not been reached. Relma-cel manufactured with JWLV011 demonstrated a manageable safety profile with no treatment-related deaths, or study discontinuations due to adverse events. All patients experienced treatment-related adverse events, 8.3% developed serious treatment-emergent adverse events. Cytokine release syndrome occurred in 83.3% of patients, all grade 1-2. No patient developed neurological toxicities. Conclusion: Relma-cel manufactured using the domestically produced lentiviral vector demonstrated favorable efficacy and a manageable safety profile in adult patients with R/R LBCL. These findings support the feasibility of in-house lentiviral vector manufacturing without compromising clinical performance.

012DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2111

复发/难治性弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤单靶（cd19）与双靶（cd19/cd22或cd19/cd20）car t细胞治疗的系统评价和荟萃分析

single-target (cd19) versus dual-target (cd19/cd22 or cd19/cd20) car t-cell therapy in relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: a systematic review and meta-analysis

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=1425；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：单靶点(CD19) CAR-T细胞治疗；试验组2：双靶点(CD19/CD22或CD19/CD20) CAR-T细胞治疗

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：单靶点(CD19) CAR-T细胞治疗；试验组2：双靶点(CD19/CD22或CD19/CD20) CAR-T细胞治疗

O 结局指标

总缓解率(ORR): 双靶点86% vs 单靶点75% (P=0.06) 完全缓解率(CR): 62% vs 53% (P=0.22) 1年无进展生存率(PFS): 67% vs 48% (P=0.23) ≥3级血液学毒性: 81% vs 55% (P=0.02) ≥3级感染: 4% vs 13%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) T-cell therapy has become a pivotal treatment option for patients with relapsed/refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (R/R DLBCL). While single-target CD19 CAR T-cell therapy is widely used in clinical practice, dual-target strategies (e.g., CD19/CD22 or CD19/CD20) have been developed to reduce antigen escape and potentially improve treatment durability. However, direct comparisons between these approaches remain limited. Aims: This meta-analysis aimed to systematically compare the efficacy and safety of single-target (CD19) versus dual-target (CD19/CD22 or CD19/CD20) CAR T-cell therapy in patients with R/R DLBCL. Methods: A systematic review and meta-analysis were conducted following predefined inclusion criteria. PubMed, Embase, Cochrane Library, Web of Science, and major conference proceedings (ASH, EHA, ASCO, ICML) were searched from database inception to December 31, 2025. Clinical studies evaluating single-target (CD19) or dual-target (CD19/CD22 or CD19/CD20) CAR T-cell therapies in R/R DLBCL were included. Primary efficacy outcomes included overall response rate (ORR), complete response (CR) rate, and 1-year progression-free survival (PFS). Safety outcomes included grade ≥3 cytokine release syndrome (CRS), immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS), infections, and hematologic toxicities. Literature screening, data extraction, and risk-of-bias assessment were independently performed by two investigators. Meta-analysis was conducted using R (version 4.3.1) with the meta and metafor packages under a random-effects model.

结论（EHA原文）

This meta-analysis suggests that dual-target (CD19/CD22 or CD19/CD20) CAR T-cell therapy may provide numerically improved response rates compared with single-target CD19 therapy in R/R DLBCL, although differences in CR and 1-year PFS were not statistically significant. Dual-target therapy was associated with higher rates of grade ≥3 hematologic toxicity but a lower incidence of severe infections, while other major adverse events were comparable between groups. Given the indirect nature of comparisons and potential heterogeneity across studies, these findings should be interpreted cautiously. Prospective randomized trials are warranted to determine the optimal CAR T-cell strategy in R/R DLBCL.

013DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2102

cd3xcd20双特异性抗体（bsab）单药治疗与bsab联合治疗复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤的现实世界比较：美国双特异性联盟（cubic）的一项合作研究

a real-world comparison of cd3xcd20 bispecific antibody (bsab) monotherapy vs bsab combinations in relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma: a collaborative us bispecific consortium (cubic) study

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=352；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：艾可瑞妥单抗；格菲妥单抗；莫妥珠单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：BsAb单药（glofitamab, epcoritamab, mosunetuzumab）；试验组2：BsAb联合治疗（包括BsAb-化疗、BsAb-ADC、BsAb-其他组合）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：BsAb单药（glofitamab, epcoritamab, mosunetuzumab）；试验组2：BsAb联合治疗（包括BsAb-化疗、BsAb-ADC、BsAb-其他组合）

O 结局指标

总体缓解率（ORR）：BsAb单药组54.0%，BsAb联合组63.9%（p=0.12） 完全缓解率（CR）：BsAb单药组35.0%，BsAb联合组44.6%（p=0.12）；多因素分析中BsAb-ADC组较单药组CR优势显著（OR 3.21, p=0.026） 无进展生存期（PFS）：未报告具体数值，多因素分析显示治疗策略与PFS无独立关联 总生存期（OS）：未报告具体数值，多因素分析显示治疗策略与OS无独立关联 细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）：BsAb单药组38.8%，BsAb联合组31.5%（p>0.05） 免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）：BsAb单药组13.1%，BsAb联合组12.6%（p>0.05） 治疗后感染：BsAb单药组33.6%，BsAb联合组30.0%（p>0.05） ICU入住率：BsAb单药组15.2%，BsAb联合组12.5%（p>0.05）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies (BsAb) demonstrate substantial activity in relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) and are being combined with chemotherapy, antibody-drug conjugates (ADCs), and targeted agents; however, without prospective comparisons, real-world data are required to inform comparative efficacy, safety, and regimen selection. Aims: To compare real-world efficacy and safety outcomes of BsAb monotherapy versus BsAb-based combination regimens in patients (pts) with R/R LBCL. Methods: This CUBIC multicenter retrospective consortium study included adult pts with R/R LBCL treated with BsAb alone or in combination across 9 centers. Endpoints included overall response rate (ORR), complete response (CR), progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS), and safety outcomes of cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS). Multivariable logistic regression and Cox proportional hazards models adjusted for age, sex, ECOG status, stage, extranodal involvement, lactate dehydrogenase (LDH), line of therapy, prior chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T), and treatment regimen.

结论（EHA原文）

In this large real-world multicenter consortium analysis, BsAb-combination approaches demonstrated numerically higher response rates, with significantly higher CR observed with BsAb-ADC combinations vs monotherapy after adjustment for baseline factors. Safety profiles and early survival were comparable across treatment strategies. Limitations include short follow-up and small sample sizes in the BsAb-combination subgroups.

tafasitamab（tafa）治疗复发/难治性弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤（r/r dlbcl）后嵌合抗原受体t细胞（car-t）治疗的有效性和安全性：一项现实研究

effectiveness and safety of chimeric antigen receptor t-cell (car-t) therapy after tafasitamab (tafa) in relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma (r/r dlbcl): a real-world study

O 结局指标

客观缓解率（ORR）：81.1%（338例中274例） 完全缓解率（CR）：58.6% 部分缓解率（PR）：22.5% ≥3级细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：7.4% ≥3级免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）发生率：3.8% 二线CAR-T客观缓解率：91.9% 三线CAR-T客观缓解率：80.2% 四线CAR-T客观缓解率：77.6%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The expanding landscape of CD19-directed therapies for DLBCL, including tafa and CAR-T, holds promise for patients (pts). However, there exist theoretical concerns that prior exposure to anti-CD19 therapy may compromise the efficacy of subsequent treatment with CAR-T. Several studies have demonstrated retention of CD19 expression following the use of tafa, with limited evidence on the effectiveness and safety of sequential use of CAR-T post tafa. Aims: Assess effectiveness and safety of CAR-T post tafa among adult pts with R/R DLBCL. Methods: A retrospective, US and EU panel-based chart review collected data for adults with R/R DLBCL who received tafa (± lenalidomide) and also subsequent CAR-T (index date) in second line (2L)/3L/4L. Pts had to have at least 6 months of follow-up post CAR-T except in the event of death; pts were followed until the earlier of either start of new anticancer therapy after CAR-T, end of data availability, or death. Outcomes were overall response rate to CAR-T (ORR, proportion of pts with physician-assessed complete/partial response [CR/PR]), proportion of pts with cytokine release syndrome (CRS) within 6 weeks, and immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome ( ICANS) within 3 months after CAR-T. Outcomes were reported overall, by CAR-T line, and by tafa/CAR-T treatment sequence.

结论（EHA原文）

This large, global, real-world study shows that prior exposure to tafa does not appear to adversely affect the effectiveness nor safety of subsequent CAR-T therapy in patients with R/R DLBCL. These results are particularly relevant with recent phase 3 data for tafa in the front‑line setting of DLBCL. While these real-world study findings should be interpreted in the context of an observational cohort, they support tafa followed by CAR-T therapy as a feasible and potentially favorable sequencing strategy.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

a phase 1 study of kite-753 in patients (pts) with relapsed/refractory (r/r) b-cell lymphoma: updated safety and efficacy results

总体反应率（ORR）在CAR-naive患者最高剂量组（DL3，n=17）为88%；完全缓解率（CR）在数据截止时71%，数据截止后76%（1例从PR转为CR）；在既往接受过CAR-T治疗的患者（所有剂量水平，n=10）中，3例（30%）达CR，2例（20%）达PR；任何级别CRS：24%为1级，24%为2级，3%为3级，无4/5级；任何级别ICANS：2例1级，4例2级，无≥3级；中位CRS发生时间6.0天，中位持续时间6.0天；中位ICANS发生时间10.5天，中位持续时间3.5天；5例死亡（2例与KITE-753无关的感染，3例疾病进展）；与axi-cel相比，KITE-753的神经毒性相关细胞因子IL-15水平更低，CAR-T细胞扩增峰值延迟

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: KITE-753 is an autologous CD19/CD20 chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) T-cell therapy under investigation for pts with R/R B-cell lymphoma (BCL). KITE-753 uses a unique bicistronic design to optimally engage CD19 and CD20, synergistic CD28/4-1BB co-stimulation to enhance T-cell function, and a rapid manufacturing process that preserves naive and stem cell memory T cells. In a multicenter, Phase 1 study in pts with R/R BCL (4.0 months median follow-up), KITE-753 demonstrated an overall response rate (ORR) of 86% and a complete response (CR) rate of 79% in CAR-naive pts at the highest dose level (DL; n=14), with a safety profile of low-grade cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and 2 cases of low-grade immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) at the highest DL (n=19; Dahiya et al. ASH 2025). Aims: To report updated safety and efficacy results from the Phase 1 study of KITE-753. Methods: Adults with BCL R/R after ≥2 lines of therapy or with second-line primary refractory large BCL (LBCL) were eligible. The trial included dose escalation (1A) and dose expansion (1B; LBCL only) cohorts. After lymphodepletion, pts received KITE-753 at 1 of 3 DLs (0.3×10 5 , 1×10 5 , or 2×10 5 CAR T cells/kg in DL 1, 2, or 3, respectively). The primary endpoints were incidence of dose-limiting toxicities (DLTs; 1A) and investigator-assessed ORR (per Lugano; 1B).

结论（EHA原文）

KITE-753, with a unique CAR design and rapid manufacturing process preserving a naive T-cell phenotype, at the highest DL showed high CR rates in CAR-naive pts and a favorable safety profile with only low-grade CRS and ICANS.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of 12/03/25, 33 pts received KITE-753 (3 in DL 1, 8 in DL 2, 22 in DL 3). Median follow-up was 7.4 months (range, 5.8-12.7). Median age at analysis was 59.0 years (range, 25-84); 88% of pts had LBCL and 12% had indolent non-Hodgkin lymphoma, and 76% had Stage III/IV disease. Nine pts (27% of all; 31% of LBCL) were primary refractory and 10 (30%) had received prior CAR T-cell therapy. No DLTs occurred in dose escalation. Grade ≥3 adverse events occurred in 85% of pts (91% in DL 3), primarily cytopenias. Eight pts (24%) had max Grade 1 CRS, 8 (24%) had max Grade 2 CRS, 1 had max Grade 3 CRS (LBCL, DL 2), and none had Grade 4/5 CRS. Median time to CRS onset was 6.0 days; median duration was 6.0 days. Two pts had Grade 1 ICANS (1 each in DL 2 and DL 3), 4 had Grade 2 ICANS (1 in DL 2, 3 in DL 3), and none had Grade ≥3 ICANS. Median time to ICANS onset was 10.5 days; median duration was 3.5 days. Five pts died: 2 due to infections unrelated to KITE-753 per investigator assessment and 3 due to progression. ORR in CAR-naive pts at DL 3 (n=17) was 88%; CR rate was 71% (12/17) at the data cutoff and 76% (13/17) post-data cutoff, with 1 pt converting from a partial response (PR) to a CR. In pts with prior CAR exposure (all DLs; n=10), 3 (30%) had a CR and 2 (20%) had a PR. In a comparative analysis of KITE-753 vs axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel; ZUMA-1), levels of the neurotoxicity-associated cytokine, IL-15, were lower with KITE-753, coinciding with an improved toxicity profile. Peak CAR T-cell expansion was delayed with KITE-753 vs axi-cel; IL-2, INF-γ, and granzyme B kinetics correlated with delayed time to peak. These favorable pharmacokinetic and pharmacodynamic profiles may reflect KITE-753’s optimized CAR T-cell dose that mitigates toxicity and its rapid manufacturing process that preserves CAR T-cell fitness. Conclusion: KITE-753, with a unique CAR design and rapid manufacturing process preserving a naive T-cell phenotype, at the highest DL showed high CR rates in CAR-naive pts and a favorable safety profile with only low-grade CRS and ICANS.

016DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF996

快速增加glofitamab治疗复发难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤的可行性和安全性

feasibility and safety of rapid glofitamab ramp-up for the treatment of relapsed and refractory large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=83；疾病阶段：复发，难治

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：BiCAR样组（obinutuzumab预处理，glofitamab在8-14天内加速给药）；试验组2：快速glofitamab组（obinutuzumab预处理，glofitamab在4-7天内加速给药）

O 结局指标

细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：47%（39/83），其中多数为1级（36%[30/39]），3级以上CRS未发生|||免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）发生率：持续较低，3级以上未发生|||总缓解率（ORR）：53%（44/83），其中完全缓解/代谢完全缓解（CR/CMR）12%，部分缓解（PR）41%|||中位无进展生存期（PFS）：6.3个月|||中位总生存期（OS）：21.5个月

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Large B-cell lymphomas (LBCL) are biologically and clinically heterogeneous. Immunochemotherapy cures 75% of patients, but high proliferation rates and clinical need for fast-acting treatments often characterize chemotherapy-refractory or relapsed disease (r/rLBCL). Prognosis in r/rLBCL is substantially diminished despite the use of CD19-directed chimeric antigen receptor T-cells (CAR-T), and approximately 50% of patients relapse after or are refractory to CAR-T, highlighting the medical need for further treatment optimization following CAR-T. \n Glofitamab is a CD20xCD3 bispecific, T-cell-engaging monoclonal antibody that is approved for the treatment of r/rLBCL. Standard dosing protocol for glofitamab requires an obinutuzumab-pretreatment to mitigate CRS and a step-up dosing of glofitamab (2.5mg, 10mg) before reaching the full therapeutic dose three-weeks after treatment start.The delayed disease control during the ramp-up phase of glofitamab is contrasted by high proliferation and often high tumor burden at diagnosis of r/rLBCL, limiting the use of single-agent glofitamab and resulting in the development of the BiCAR trial and other off-label accelerated step-up protocols in clinical practice. Aims: To assess whether the full dose of glofitamab can be administered more rapidly without compromising patient safety and thereby accelerating disease control in patients with r/rLBCL. Methods: In this retrospective multicenter study, we analyzed 83 patients from 11 centers across Germany, Austria and Switzerland who had received glofitamab between December 2020 and November 2025 in an accelerated step-up dosing schedule. These patients (Accelerated Glo group) were further divided into the BiCAR-like group if glofitamab was administered within 1-2 weeks, and the rapid glofitamab group in which glofitamab was administered within less than 1 week. Efficacy including response rates and survival as well as adverse events were analyzed.

结论（EHA原文）

Accelerated administration of glofitamab for patients with r/rLBCL is feasible without compromising patients’ safety or response, supporting its use in clinical practice for patients with r/rLBCL.

introduction of car-t cell therapy dramatically improved outcomes of patients with relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma receiving second-line treatment at a population level

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=524；疾病阶段：复发/难治；治疗线数/场景：二线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CAR-T(达博生物)；类别：CAR-T，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

O 结局指标

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The introduction of CAR-T and other innovative therapies has changed the treatment landscape for patients with relapsed/refractory (r/r) large B-cell lymphomas (LBCL). We have previously demonstrated that these novel treatments improved outcomes for r/r LBCL patients in the third-line setting in recent years (EHA 2025, PF939). Subsequently, CAR-T was approved in the second line (L2) in 2022 in our region, creating the potential for similar survival improvements. Aims: We aimed to evaluate evolving treatment patterns in the L2 for r/r LBCL and to assess the impact of novel therapies on overall survival (OS) within a real-world patient population on a national-based level. Methods: We analyzed data from 524 consecutive patients with r/r LBCL from the prospective NiHiL registry (NCT03199066) who received L2 therapy between 2020–2024. Patients were stratified into two eras based on CAR-T access: Era 1 (2020–2021; n=239) and Era 2 (2023–2024; n=285), with 2022 excluded (transitional year). Patients were included regardless of whether they ultimately received CAR-T. The primary endpoint was OS; secondary endpoints included cumulative incidence (CIF) of lymphoma-related mortality (LRM) and shifts in treatment patterns. Subgroup analysis was conducted for \"early-r/r\" patients, defined as progressive (PD), refractory disease (stable [SD], partial remission [PR]), or relapse ≤12 months after the end of L1 (n=393). We used Cox regression for time-to-event analysis (OS) and Fine-Gray models for CIF of LRM (non-lymphoma death as a competing risk).

结论（EHA原文）

\n The adoption of CAR-T and innovative therapeutic strategies has significantly improved the OS of L2-treated r/r LBCL patients in recent years, by reducing the risk of death by 29% in the overall population and by 24% in the early-r/r subgroup. These real-world data confirm that shifting novel therapies to earlier lines of treatment translates into substantial clinical benefits and a reduction in LRM. \n Support: NU23-03-00127, CU Hem-Onc Cooper, BBMRI_CZ LM2023033. \n

018DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF975

zamtocabtagene autoleucel，一种串联cd20-cd19导向的car-t细胞治疗复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤：来自随机关键daly2-eu试验的交叉分析（第三线）

zamtocabtagene autoleucel, a tandem cd20-cd19 directed car-t cell therapy in relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma: crossover analysis (third-line) from the randomized, pivotal daly 2-eu trial

P 患者群体

I 干预措施

最佳总体缓解率（BOR）：79.3% 完全缓解率（CR）：65.5% 6个月无事件生存率：79%（95% CI 53%-92%） 6个月无进展生存率：79%（95% CI 53%-92%） ≥3级细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）：6.9% ≥3级免疫细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）：3.4%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Zamtocabtagene autoleucel (zamto-cel) is an autologous, non-cryopreserved tandem CD20-CD19 directed CAR-T cell therapy. In the primary analysis of the DALY 2-EU trial (NCT04844866) in transplant ineligible (TI) adults with relapsed/refractory (r/r) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), zamto-cel demonstrated superior event-free survival (EFS; median 6.2 vs 2.5 months), improved best overall response (BOR; 72.0 vs 44.9%) and complete response (CR; 53.7 vs 14.1%) vs R-GemOx (standard of care [SoC]) as assessed by an independent review committee. Zamto-cel had a manageable safety profile, with low rates of grade ≥3 immune cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS; 1.3%) and cytokine release syndrome (CRS; 5.3%). Aims: To evaluate the efficacy and safety of zamto-cel for crossover patients (pts) from SoC in DALY 2-EU. Methods: DALY 2-EU is a randomized, European, open-label trial. Informed consent was obtained from adult (≥18 years [y]) pts with r/r (≤24 months after start of first-line therapy) LBCL with Eastern Cooperative Oncology Group performance status ≤2 who met one TI criterion (age ≥65y with impaired organ function or age ≥70y). \n Between Oct 2021 and Jul 2024, 168 pts were randomized to zamto-cel or SoC (R-GemOx or Pola-BR). Zamto-cel pts started lymphodepletion (fludarabine and cyclophosphamide) during manufacturing and received zamto-cel (target dose of 2.5×10 6 CAR-T cells/kg body weight). A protocol amendment (Feb 2023) allowed one-sided crossover from SoC to zamto-cel as third-line (3L) therapy, no crossover occurred before the amendment. Eligible pts had relapsed or progressed ≤1y after randomization, or failed to achieve partial response (PR) or CR in ≥8 weeks. Leukapheresis product was collected after randomization, cryopreserved and used after manufacturing following crossover approval. Bridging therapy was allowed prior to zamto-cel administration. Exploratory efficacy endpoints in the crossover population were investigator assessed and included EFS, progression-free survival (PFS), and BOR. Safety was also evaluated; treatment-emergent adverse events (TEAEs) were defined as any AE occurring from zamto-cel infusion to 90 days post-infusion, and before new anti-lymphoma therapy.

结论（EHA原文）

In this 3L setting, most intended pts received zamto-cel. Analysis of this mainly refractory 3L pt population revealed clinically meaningful efficacy of zamto-cel with low rates of severe CRS and ICANS, consistent with second-line treatment with zamto-cel.

019DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF969

il-7/ccl19装甲car-t细胞早期car-t收缩期间时间限定的pd-1阻断与高危复发/难治性lbcl标志的反应加深有关

time-defined pd-1 blockade during early car-t contraction of il-7/ccl19–armored car-t cells is associated with response deepening in high-risk relapsed/refractory lbcl logo

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=20；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：替雷利珠单抗；靶点：PD-1；类别：单特异性抗体；分组：试验组：IL-7/CCL19–armored CD19 CAR-T cells，tislelizumab

O 结局指标

1. 3个月客观缓解率(ORR): 85% 2. 累积完全缓解率(CR): 70% 3. 2年无进展生存期(PFS): 60.0% 4. 2年总生存期(OS): 71.1% 5. 中位随访时间: 21.8个月 6. 安全性: 未出现新的CRS或ICANS

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD19-directed CAR-T therapy induces high response rates in relapsed/refractory large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL), yet durable remission remains suboptimal in patients with bulky disease or PD-L1–enriched tumor microenvironments. CAR-T functional states evolve dynamically after peak expansion, but whether the early contraction phase represents a clinically actionable window for checkpoint modulation remains uncertain. Aims: To assess the safety and preliminary efficacy of PD-1 blockade administered during early CAR-T contraction and to explore its association with response deepening in biologically high-risk R/R LBCL. Methods: In this investigator-initiated phase I study (NCT04381741), 20 patients with R/R LBCL received lymphodepletion followed by IL-7/CCL19–armored CD19 CAR-T cells (2×10⁶/kg). Based on longitudinal CAR-T kinetics, PD-1 blockade (tislelizumab 200 mg) was initiated on day +30 (±2), corresponding to early contraction.Primary endpoints were safety and 3-month objective response rate (ORR). Secondary endpoints included complete response (CR), progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS), and duration of response. Immune profiling included CAR transgene monitoring, multiparameter flow cytometry, single-cell RNA sequencing, and TCR clonotype analysis.

结论（EHA原文）

CAR-T cells undergo an early contraction phase marked by checkpoint-sensitive functional restraint rather than terminal exhaustion. PD-1 blockade timed to this window reprogrammed dysfunctional CAR-T cells, deepened responses, and overcame the negative prognostic impact of PD-L1^high expression and bulky disease—without increasing immune-related toxicity. These results highlight timing as a key therapeutic variable in CAR-T therapy and support a dual-axis strategy combining intrinsic IL-7/CCL19 armoring with phase-specific checkpoint inhibition to enhance durability in immune-resistant LBCL. Given the single-arm design and small sample size, findings are hypothesis-generating and warrant validation in prospective controlled trials.

impact of prior lines of therapy on progression risk and post-failure overall survival following axicabtagene ciloleucel or lisocabtagene maraleucel car t-cells therapy.

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=627

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Lisocabtagene maraleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰；分组：总人群：Axicabtagene ciloleucel 或 Lisocabtagene maraleucel（按治疗线数分为2L组、3L组、4L+组）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CAR T-cells have improved outcomes for relapsed/refractory aggressive large B-cell lymphomas. Over the last decade, Axicabtagene ciloleucel (Axicel) and Lisocabtagene maraleucel (Lisocel) were approved for patients who had failed two or more therapies, with 5-year OS of 38%- 42%. Recently, based on the Zuma-7 and Transform trials, their use expanded to 2 nd (2L), with a 3-year OS of 50%. \n Aims: Our study evaluates how prior therapies influence the risk of progression and post-failure OS (OS2) in real-world settings. Methods: CART-SIE is a prospective observational study of patients (pts) treated with anti-CD19 CAR T-cells at 22 Italian centers. A total of 627 pts were treated: 604 received Axicel, and 23 Lisocel. Time to progression was calculated from infusion to first documented progression and analyzed using a competing-risks framework, with death as the competing event. Cumulative incidence functions were estimated, and between-group comparisons were performed using univariable and multivariable Fine and Gray models. Six-month progression estimates were derived from the final multivariable model across covariate combinations to identify factors associated with early relapse/progression. Post-failure overall survival (OS2) was measured from relapse/progression to death and estimated using the Kaplan–Meier method

结论（EHA原文）

Despite limitations inherent to our population and the high number of primary refractory pts treated in 2L, this study showed that the probability of PD within 6 months following CAR T-cells was 20% lower in 2L+ than in 4L+. Despite a significant increase in bispecific therapy after 2L CAR T-cells failure, 1-year OS2 remained poor, underscoring a critical unmet clinical need.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Of 627 pts, 221 (35%) received CAR T-cells in the 2L, 282 (45%) in 3 rd (3L), and 124 (20%) in 4 th or later line (4L+). Patient characteristics differed significantly across groups for the following factors: 1) High-grade B-cell lymphomas were more common in 4L+ and 3L than in 2L (20% vs 17% vs 9%, p Conclusion: Despite limitations inherent to our population and the high number of primary refractory pts treated in 2L, this study showed that the probability of PD within 6 months following CAR T-cells was 20% lower in 2L+ than in 4L+. Despite a significant increase in bispecific therapy after 2L CAR T-cells failure, 1-year OS2 remained poor, underscoring a critical unmet clinical need.

中位完全缓解持续时间（DOCR）：60.0个月（95% CI: 24.9–NE） 中位无进展生存期（PFS）：61.4个月（95% CI: 26.3–NE） 5年PFS率：51.5%（95% CI: 41.2–61.8） 中位总生存期（OS）：未达到（95% CI: NE） 5年OS率：67.5%（95% CI: 57.8–77.1） 5年疾病特异性生存率：86.0%（95% CI: 78.6–93.4） ≥3级不良事件发生率：63.6%（最常见为中性粒细胞减少37.4%） 5级不良事件发生率：3.7%（急性髓系白血病2例，复发性胰腺癌1例，COVID-19 1例；均判断与研究药物无关）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Long-term follow-up data demonstrate that chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) T-cell therapy is a curative option for patients with relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), particularly those who achieve a complete response (CR). CD20xCD3 bispecific antibodies, such as glofitamab, have demonstrated durable responses with a favorable safety profile in R/R LBCL. However, to date the curative potential of CD20xCD3 bispecific antibodies has not been well defined. Aims: To evaluate the long-term outcomes, with ~5 years of follow-up, of glofitamab monotherapy in patients with R/R LBCL who achieved a CR in the Phase 1/2 NP30179 (NCT03075696) trial. Methods: Patients with ≥1 prior line of therapy for LBCL received obinutuzumab pre-treatment (1000mg) 7 days prior to the first glofitamab dose. Glofitamab was given intravenously at a fixed dose (0.6–25mg) or with step-up dosing (2.5/10/16 or 30mg) for up to 12 cycles. This exploratory analysis evaluated investigator-assessed duration of CR (DOCR), progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) in patients with a CR, as well as the safety and tolerability of glofitamab monotherapy. All patients provided written informed consent.

结论（EHA原文）

After a ~5-year follow-up, fixed-duration glofitamab monotherapy demonstrated continued benefit with durable long-term remissions and manageable safety in patients with R/R LBCL who achieved a CR. Overall, the durable remissions observed with glofitamab treatment in patients who achieved a CR suggest a curative potential in a proportion of patients.

022DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF1410

复发/难治性dlbcl中epcoritamab家庭护理途径与常规epcoritamad和glofitamab医院护理方案的比较：成本最小化和预算影响分析

epcoritamab home-based care pathways in relapsed/refractory dlbcl versus conventional epcoritamab and glofitamab hospital-based care patwhay : a cost-minimization and budget impact analysis

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

分组：护理路径1：Epcoritamab在医院护理中心给药；护理路径2：Epcoritamab从第2周期开始家庭住院给药；护理路径3：Epcoritamab从第1周期开始家庭住院给药；护理路径4：Glofitamab在医院护理中心给药

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：护理路径1：Epcoritamab在医院护理中心给药；护理路径2：Epcoritamab从第2周期开始家庭住院给药；护理路径3：Epcoritamab从第1周期开始家庭住院给药；护理路径4：Glofitamab在医院护理中心给药

O 结局指标

Epcoritamab医院护理路径总成本：12,922€ Epcoritamab从第2周期家庭住院路径总成本：10,145€（节省21.5%） Epcoritamab从第1周期家庭住院路径总成本：7,858€（节省39.1%） Glofitamab医院护理路径总成本：7,268€ 对于管理50名患者的医院，逐步转为第1周期家庭住院五年累计节省约673,000€

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: In France, epcoritamab and glofitamab in monotherapy have received a favorable reimbursement opinion from the French National Authority for Health (HAS) and are currently available through an early access program for the treatment of adults with relapsed or refractory (R/R) diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) after at least two prior systemic therapies, who are ineligible for all available treatments or who have failed CAR-T cell therapies. These CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies primarily differ by their mode and duration of administration: epcoritamab is administered subcutaneously until disease progression and/or unacceptable toxicity while glofitamab is administered intravenously for a fixed duration of 12 cycles. Both treatments are delivered in a Health Care Center (HCC); however, only epcoritamab is eligible for a Hospitalization at Home (HaH) administration pathway, due to its shorter administration time. In a context of capacity and budget constraints and an expected increasing use of bispecific antibodies, HCCs need to develop alternate care pathways. Moreover, allowing patients to remain in their home environment throughout their care pathway is likely to improve quality of life. Aims: To assess the economic impact of epcoritamab HaH care pathway versus epcoritamab and glofitamab usual HCC care pathways for the treatment of patients with R/R DLBCL. Methods: Four care pathways were compared: (1) epcoritamab administered exclusively in HCC (reference), (2) epcoritamab with HaH starting from cycle 2, (3) epcoritamab with HaH from cycle 1, and (4) glofitamab administered exclusively in HCC. Pathway definitions were informed in 2025 by a French clinician advisory panel (n=7) to ensure alignment with routine clinical practice in France. A cost-minimization model was developed from the perspective of the National Health Insurance, including administration, follow‑up, and transportation costs over a two‑year horizon. A budget impact model was developed using a multi‑cohort incident approach over five years. Treatment duration was extrapolated using a Weibull model from time-to-discontinuation (TTD) data from EPCORE NHL-1, a phase I/II trial of epcoritamab monotherapy in R/R large B-cell lymphoma. To focus on care pathway costs, efficacy was assumed equivalent across pathways as between epcoritamab and glofitamab.

结论（EHA原文）

HaH for the administration of epcoritamab in patients with R/R DLBCL reduces costs by 21–39% compared with HCC‑based care, leading to total pathway costs in the same range as in-hospital glofitamab (7,858€ vs 7,268€), despite glofitamab involving fewer administrations. These findings support the organizational and economic relevance of HaH, whenever feasible, for patients with R/R DLBCL receiving epcoritamab, highlighting potential gains in patient quality of life and healthcare system efficiency

023DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF1240

hyper-fractionated radiotherapy as a bridging strategy attenuates t-cell exhaustion to enhance cd19 car-t efficacy in relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=25；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CD19靶向CAR-T(北京大学人民医院)；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，经基因修饰；分组：试验组1：超分割放疗，CD19 CAR-T

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

1个月CR率：64%（16/25）|||6个月CR率：76%（19/25）|||2年PFS率：63.3%|||2年OS率：75%|||CRS：44% 1级，24% 2级，16% 3级|||ICANS：20%发生率（8% 1级，8% 3级，4% 4级）|||3-4级粒细胞减少：88%，中位持续时间5.5天

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Recent clinical studies have confirmed the safety and efficacy of radiotherapy as a bridging strategy prior to CAR-T therapy in R/R DLBCL. Conventional fractionation regimens remain the most commonly adopted, with a daily dose of 3–5 Gy per fraction. Hyper-fractionated radiotherapy, characterized by lower fractional doses and higher treatment frequency, allows effective target-dose delivery within a shorter timeframe while minimizing radiation-related toxicity. Beyond reducing tumor burden, this approach may also remodel the tumor microenvironment and potentiate the efficacy of immunotherapy. \n Aims: We aim to investigate the efficacy and safety of bridging hyper-fractionated radiotherapy in combination with CD19 CAR-T therapy for R/R DLBCL. The potential mechanisms would also be explored. Methods: This was a single-center, prospective clinical study (NCT05514327) enrolling patients with R/R DLBCL with measurable lesions. Hyper-fractionated radiotherapy was administered following T-cell apheresis. A total dose of 30 Gy was prescribed to all patients using a hyper-fractionated regimen of 1.5 Gy twice daily over approximately 10 treatment days (weekends excluded). CAR-T cell infusion started within 1-2 weeks after the completion of radiotherapy. The efficacy and adverse reactions at different time points after radiotherapy and CAR-T cell infusion were monitored and analyzed.

结论（EHA原文）

Hyper-fractionated radiotherapy as a bridging therapy can not only reduce tumor burden, but also reduce exhausted T cells (CD8+PD1+T). The lower exhausted T cells are significantly related to better PFS and OS. These findings suggest that hyper-fractionated radiotherapy acts synergistically with CAR ‑ T therapy by modulating the host immune status, thereby facilitating durable long ‑ term remission in patients with R/R DLBCL.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Loncastuximab tesirine (LT), an anti-CD19 pyrrolobenzodiazepine-conjugated monoclonal antibody, is now approved for the treatment of large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) patients from their third line onwards. According to the results of the phase 2 registration trial, responses occurred quickly and lasted for over a year in patients receiving at least 2 previous treatments, including chimeric antigen receptor T (CART) cells. Aims: An observational study reporting the Italian real-life experience with LT as compassionate use, with the purpose of assessing its effectiveness, in terms of response rate and time to response. Secondary endpoints were progression-free, overall survival, response duration and safety in a cohort of patients with LBCL relapsing after or refractory to at least 2 previous lines. Methods: LT was administered in accordance with its prescribing indications until disease progression or unacceptable toxicity, whichever came first. Patients in the study were not subjected to any procedures outside normal practice and the variables collected were retrieved from patients’ medical records.

结论（EHA原文）

LT displays rapid disease control in a population of highly pretreated LBCL patients with severe presentation. More disappointing survival results have been documented in our population compared to registration study due to much more unfavorable disease characteristics. Extra-hematologic toxicity remains a concern.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CAR-T cell therapy has demonstrated clear efficacy in relapsed/refractory B-cell malignancies, including B-cell acute lymphoblastic leukemia (B-ALL), diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), and multiple myeloma (MM). CAR-T cells can penetrate the blood-brain barrier and are effective in patients with central nervous system (CNS) involvement. Recently, the mainly infusion of CAR-T was through intravenous. The evaluation of the safety and efficacy of combined intrathecal and intravenous CAR-T infusion remain scarce. Aims: To evaluate the safety and clinical efficacy of intrathecal combined with intravenous CAR-T therapy in patients with relapsed/refractory B-cell malignancies accompanied by CNS involvement. Methods: This study analyzed patients with B-cell malignancies and CNS involvement treated at our center from January 2025 to February 2026 using intrathecal combined with intravenous CAR-T therapy. Flow cytometry was used to detect the CAR-T cell expansion and cytokine levels in cerebrospinal fluid (CSF) and peripheral blood (PB). Efficacy was assessed via CSF minimal residual disease detection and MRI imaging. Patient demographics and adverse events were collected, with follow-up until February 28, 2025.

结论（EHA原文）

Intrathecal combined with intravenous CAR-T cell therapy enables rapid CNS tumor clearance in B-cell malignancies with CNS involvement, with favorable safety. These findings establish intrathecal CAR-T as a promising strategy for CNS-limited B-cell tumors.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Glofitamab, a CD20xCD3 bispecific antibody, plus GemOx (Glofit-GemOx) has shown significant improvements versus rituximab-GemOx in overall survival and progression-free survival in the randomized Phase 3 STARGLO trial (NCT04408638) in autologous stem-cell transplant (ASCT)-ineligible R/R DLBCL. The observed cytokine release syndrome (CRS) profile with Glofit-GemOx in STARGLO allows for treatment without mandatory hospitalization. Implementing outpatient strategies can further improve patient convenience and optimize healthcare resource utilization. Aims: Present preliminary safety results from an ongoing Phase 2 trial (GO45434; NCT06806033), evaluating CRS profile optimization for outpatient Glofit-GemOx treatment via an enhanced steroid premedication, and a revised monitoring regimen for treated patients (pts) with R/R DLBCL. Methods: Pts had R/R DLBCL; those with 1 prior line of therapy (LOT) had to be ASCT-ineligible. After 1000mg obinutuzumab pretreatment, pts received Glofit-GemOx (8 cycles plus 4 cycles glofitamab monotherapy), with glofitamab given in step-up doses (SUD; 2.5/10mg) in Cycle (C)1, then 30mg target dose every 21 days from C2. Pts received oral dexamethasone (Dex) 20mg one day prior to and after glofitamab SUD in C1, in addition to the premedication used in STARGLO. Pts were monitored in the outpatient setting for 4 hours during SUD and 90 minutes after the first target dose, in both academic and community centers. Primary endpoint was CRS incidence. Other safety parameters and efficacy were secondary endpoints. All pts provided informed consent. In this ongoing study, 100 pts in 7 countries will be recruited.

结论（EHA原文）

In this preliminary analysis, pts with R/R DLBCL receiving Glofit-GemOx were monitored in the outpatient setting after receiving additional oral Dex one day prior to and after glofitamab infusion in C1. The rate and severity of CRS events were similar to those reported in STARGLO. Data are encouraging and support further optimization of outpatient Glofit-GemOx treatment. Updated data will be presented.

tumour microenvironment archetypes that support anti-tumour t-cell immunity and cd4⁺ t-cell cytotoxic differentiation underpin response to glofitamab in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：格菲妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体

C 对照措施

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Glofitamab, CD20×CD3 T-cell engager (TCE), redirects T cells to kill tumour cells. We showed that combining glofitamab with standard first-line (1L) chemotherapy (RCHOP/Pola-R-CHP) in DLBCL produced a historically high rate of complete remissions, which were durable in an ultra-high-burden population [COALITION-study (NCT04914741/Minson et al., JCO-2025)]. Despite overall treatment success, some patients relapsed or were refractory (10%). Understanding the mechanisms underlying resistance will inform ongoing 1L TCE development and may stem from tumour intrinsic, microenvironmental (TME) factors, or T-cell-intrinsic dysfunction. Aims: To elucidate the TME and T-cell-intrinsic mechanisms that limit therapeutic response to glofitamab in first-line DLBCL. Methods: Baseline and progression tumour biopsies from COALITION trial patients were analysed using bulk RNA seq and mIHC. In parallel, we performed scRNA-seq and spectral flow cytometry on longitudinal COALITION blood samples collected pre- and post-TCE treatment. To further interrogate observations from patient samples, we established in vitro co-cultures comprising DLBCL tumour cells, donor- or COALITION patient-derived T cells, and glofitamab. Co-cultured cells were subsequently profiled using scRNA-seq, flow cytometry, spatial proteomics (Pixelgen), and live-cell imaging

结论（EHA原文）

Overall, our results indicate that a pre-treatment TME that supports productive T-cell engagement with tumour cells, and differentiation of CD4-CTLs, underpins successful responses to glofitamab. We also identify downregulation of CD20, alongside adhesion molecules, and co-stimulatory pathways as potential immune-escape mechanisms. \n

028DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL双抗PS2504

longitudinal patient-reported outcomes highlight improved quality of life for r-chop-ineligible patients with aggressive b-cell lymphomas treated within the frontline phase ii r-pola-glo trial

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=80；疾病阶段：侵袭性；治疗线数/场景：一线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；格菲妥单抗；利妥昔单抗；靶点：CD79B；CD20，CD3；CD20；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；双特异性抗体；单特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：利妥昔单抗，泊洛妥珠单抗，格洛菲他单抗

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

全球健康状况（QLQ-C30 GHS）：治疗期间改善+10.7分，具有临床意义；44%患者在C4时改善≥10分；至EOT和随访时仍高于基线 身体功能：维持治疗前水平 疲劳：未增加负担 情绪功能：持续改善 FACT-Lym总分：C4时增加+10分，具有临床意义；至EOT和随访仍高于基线 试验结果指标（TOI）：类似模式

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) predominantly affects older adults, many of whom are frail and ineligible for standard R-CHOP. While R-CHOP achieves high cure rates in fit patients, older, frail, and medically unfit patients often require attenuated regimens with inferior efficacy. This unmet need prompted development of the R-Pola-Glo trial integrating rituximab (R), polatuzumab vedotin (Pola), and the CD20×CD3 bispecific antibody glofitamab (Glo). The R-Pola-Glo phase II trial achieved high overall and complete metabolic remission rates (90% and 81% at end of treatment [EOT]) and 1-year progression-free and overall survival of 85% and 90%, respectively. Beyond efficacy, preservation of health-related quality of life (HRQoL) is critical, and patient-reported outcomes (PROs) provide complementary insights. Aims: To evaluate longitudinal HRQoL during frontline R-Pola-Glo therapy in R-CHOP–ineligible DLBCL patients enrolled in the initial phase II cohort (n=80). Methods: PROs were assessed longitudinally (baseline; day 1 of cycles (C) 2, 4, 6, 8, 10, 12, EOT, and 3-monthly follow-up). HRQoL was measured using the European Organization for Research and Treatment of Cancer Quality of Life Questionnaire-Core 30 (EORTC QLQ-C30; scale 0–100; higher scores indicate better functioning/global QoL and greater symptom burden on symptom scales) and lymphoma-specific HRQoL using the Functional Assessment of Cancer Therapy–Lymphoma ( v4; higher scores indicate better ). Analyses were descriptive (observed cases; no imputation). Mean change from baseline with 95% confidence intervals was calculated per visit. Clinically meaningful change was defined as ≥ 10 points for QLQ-C30 scales and ≥3 points for FACT-Lym. Questionnaire completion was reported per visit. Timepoints with at least 20% evaluable patients were included.

结论（EHA原文）

In this frail, high-risk population, R-Pola-Glo demonstrated preserved or clinically meaningful improvements in HRQoL alongside high disease control. Global and emotional functioning improved, physical functioning was maintained, and lymphoma-related symptoms improved early and durably. These findings support the patient-reported tolerability of R-Pola-Glo as a chemotherapy-light, immune-based frontline strategy in patients with limited options.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Glofitamab, a CD20×CD3 bispecific antibody, has demonstrated encouraging efficacy in relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL). We conducted a prospective single-center analysis to evaluate clinical outcomes and exploratory biomarkers in routine practice. Aims: To evaluate clinical outcomes of glofitamab in a high-risk R/R LBCL cohort and to explore early circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) dynamics and immune microenvironment characteristics associated with treatment response. Methods: Tumor-informed ctDNA profiling using a 152-gene DLBCL panel was performed at baseline and cycle 2 day 1 (C2D1) in 48 patients. Log-fold change (LFC) between baseline and C2D1 was calculated. Bulk RNA sequencing of tumor biopsies obtained at relapse or progression (n=57) was analyzed using TIMER, CIBERSORT, and xCell to evaluate immune infiltration patterns.

结论（EHA原文）

In this high-risk R/R LBCL cohort, including patients commonly underrepresented in clinical trials, glofitamab achieved meaningful response rates with manageable toxicity. Early ctDNA reduction after one treatment cycle was associated with improved progression-free survival. Immune profiling further indicates that an inflamed tumor microenvironment may underlie sensitivity to bispecific antibody therapy. Together, these findings expand the clinical applicability of glofitamab and support the integration of early molecular monitoring and biological stratification in future treatment strategies.

030DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL双抗PS2107

glofitamab、polatuzumab vedotin和zanubrutinib在未经治疗的老年dlbcl患者中的2期试验：安全性磨合结果

phase 2 trial of glofitamab, polatuzumab vedotin and zanubrutinib in untreated elderly dlbcl patients: safety run-in results

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=10；治疗线数/场景：一线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；格菲妥单抗；泽布替尼；靶点：CD79B；CD20，CD3；BTK；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；双特异性抗体；化药；分组：试验组1：glofitamab，polatuzumab vedotin，zanubrutinib（第1周期加用obinutuzumab进行set-up）

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

安全性：10例患者均完成28天安全导入期观察；90%发生1-2级CRS；1例（10%）基线有小肠受累的患者出现3级下消化道出血和4级肿瘤溶解综合征，该患者停药；20%发生2级肺部感染，10%发生3级肺部感染；无肿瘤耀斑发生。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: R-miniCHOP is the current standard of care for elderly diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), however, treatment-related toxicities remained challenging. There is an unmet need for effective and safe first-line regimens for elderly patients. Glofitamab is now being actively investigated in combination with standard immunochemotherapy for first-line adult DLBCL and exhibited high response rates. Therefore, we designed and initiated a prospective phase 2 clinical trial (NCT07012980) to investigate the efficacy and safety of glofitamab, polatuzumab vedotin and zanubrutinib in untreated elderly DLBCL patients. Aims: In this trial, we aim to investigate safety and efficacy of glofitamab, polatuzumab vedotin and zanubrutinib in untreated elderly DLBCL patients. Here, we present the results of safety run-in. Methods: Untreated DLBCL patients aged over 70 years old will be enrolled in this study. Central nervous system involvement is excluded. All patients will receive zanubrutinib lead-in 7 days prior to the first cycle. Twenty-one days is a cycle. The regimen consists of 12 cycles, divided into three phases. Zanubrutinib is given 160 mg twice a day orally from day 1 to day 21 throughout all 12 cycles. For cycle 1, the set-up phase, obinutuzumab is administered 1,000 mg intravenously on day 1, polatuzumab vedotin 1.8 mg/KG intravenously on day 2, and glofitamab 2.5mg intravenously on day 8 and 10 mg on day 15. For cycle 2 to 6, target dose phase, polatuzumab vedotin is administered 1.8 mg/KG intravenously on day 1, and glofitamab 30 mg intravenously on day 1. For cycle 7 to 12, consolidation phase, only zanubrutinib remains as maintenance. Whole body 18F-FDG PET/CT scan or contrast-enhanced CT scan is scheduled every 3 cycles. Adverse events are graded by NCI-CTCAE v5.0. The primary end point is 1-year progression-free survival rate. The secondary end points are safety, complete response rate and overall survival. The first 10 patients enrolled in this study will be assigned in the safety run-in phase and reviewed after 28 days of initial treatment.

结论（EHA原文）

In general, the combination of glofitamab, polatuzumab vedotin and zanubrutinib were considered tolerable in untreated elderly DLBCL patients. The trial is still ongoing, and the follow-up will be further updated.
