031DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL双抗PS2087

大b细胞淋巴瘤双特异性抗体治疗前最佳绝对淋巴细胞计数的确定：美国双特异性联盟（cubic）的一项合作研究

identification of an optimal absolute lymphocyte count before bispecific antibody therapy for large b-cell lymphomas: a collaborative u.s. bispecific consortium (cubic) study

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=317

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：艾可瑞妥单抗；格菲妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：组别1：低ALC组（ALC < 0.25×10³/µL）；组别2：高ALC组（ALC ≥ 0.25×10³/µL）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：组别1：低ALC组（ALC < 0.25×10³/µL）；组别2：高ALC组（ALC ≥ 0.25×10³/µL）

O 结局指标

总人群（317例）中：ORR 51%，CR 34%，中位PFS 3.9个月。低ALC组（57例）vs 高ALC组（260例）：ORR 37% vs 52%（p=0.05）；CR 18% vs 37%（p=0.008）；中位PFS 2.7个月 vs 4.3个月（p=0.004）。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies (BsAb), approved in the third-line or later setting for relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphomas (LBCL), harness CD3+ T cells to target CD20-expressing tumor cells. Thus, quantitative and functional endogenous T-cell impairments may influence their anti-lymphoma efficacy. Aims: We hypothesize that pre-treatment absolute lymphocyte counts (ALC) are associated with clinical outcomes in patients receiving BsAb for R/R LBCL, and aimed to identify an ALC threshold associated with superior progression-free survival (PFS). Methods: We conducted a multicenter retrospective study of adult patients with R/R LBCL who received commercial glofitamab (glofit) or epcoritamab (epco) between January 2023 and July 2025 at 10 U.S. cancer centers in the Collaborative US Bispecific Consortium (CUBIC). Baseline characteristics, including ALC, were collected prior to BsAb initiation. Cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) were graded per ASTCT consensus grading. Treatment response and survival were assessed per Lugano 2014 criteria. The dataset was randomly divided into training (60%) and validation (40%) datasets. An optimal ALC cutoff value for PFS was identified in the training dataset using maximally selected rank statistics and validated using univariate Cox regression with bootstrap resampling. Patients were then stratified by this threshold, and baseline characteristics, response rates (ORR, CR), and toxicities (CRS, ICANS) were compared between ALC groups. Fisher’s exact test or Wilcoxon rank-sum test were used for univariate associations of variables, and logistic regression for multivariate analysis.

结论（EHA原文）

An optimal ALC threshold of 0.25×10³/µL could identify patients with R/R LBCL who may experience deeper responses and longer PFS with BsAb. Biological analysis, aimed at investigating clinically relevant T-cell subgroups, and prospective validation of these findings are warranted.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 317 patients were included in the analysis: 165 (52%) received glofit and 152 (48%) epco. At BsAb initiation, median age was 70 years (range, 22-93), 13% had double-hit LBCL, 69% had an international prognostic index score of ≥3, median prior lines of therapy (LOT) was 3 (range, 1-9), and median ALC was 0.6×10³/µL (IQR, 0.3-1.0; range, 0-39.1×10³/µL). Any-grade CRS and ICANS occurred in 112 (36%) and 37 (12%) of patients, respectively, with grade ≥3 occurring in 13 (4%) and 6 (2%). Overall response rates (ORR) and complete response rates (CR) were 51% and 34%, respectively. After a median follow-up of 12.1 months, median PFS was 3.9 months. The optimal ALC threshold in the training dataset was 0.25×10³/µL. In the overall cohort, 260 patients (82%) had high ALC. Compared to the low pre-treatment ALC ( Conclusion: An optimal ALC threshold of 0.25×10³/µL could identify patients with R/R LBCL who may experience deeper responses and longer PFS with BsAb. Biological analysis, aimed at investigating clinically relevant T-cell subgroups, and prospective validation of these findings are warranted.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: A subset of newly diagnosed (1L) patients with LBCL are ineligible for curative chemotherapy due to age or comorbidities. EPCORE ® DLBCL-3 (NCT05660967) is a phase 2 trial evaluating the efficacy and safety of fixed-duration epcoritamab (epcor), a CD3×CD20 bispecific antibody, in elderly patients with 1L LBCL and comorbidities. Aims: To report efficacy and safety of fixed-duration epcor monotherapy after 22 months of follow-up in EPCORE DLBCL-3. Methods: Patients with 1L CD20+ LBCL ineligible for anthracycline-based chemotherapy due to age ≥ 80 years or ≥ 75 years with comorbidities received SC epcor monotherapy: step-up dosing (0.16 mg on cycle 1 day 1 [C1D1]; 0.8 mg on C1D8) followed by 48 mg QW in C1–3 and Q4W in C4–12, for up to 1 year. Primary endpoint was CR rate per investigator assessment (Lugano criteria). MRD negativity (MRD-neg) was assessed in responders by circulating tumor DNA (cutoff,

结论（EHA原文）

Fixed-duration epcor monotherapy showed robust efficacy, with early, deep, and durable responses in elderly patients with 1L LBCL and comorbidities. Safety outcomes, including the occurrence of CRS and ICANS, were consistent with expected rates in this elderly population. These findings suggest that epcor offers a single-agent, chemotherapy-free option for pts with 1L DLBCL who would be excluded from standard chemoimmunotherapy regimens due to age or comorbidities.

Background: Despite recent advances, R/R LBCL remains clinically challenging with poor outcomes, particularly in elderly patients, necessitating durable therapeutic options. In an open-label, multicenter, Phase 1b/2 study (NCT03533283), glofitamab plus polatuzumab vedotin (Glofit-Pola; an investigational regimen) demonstrated high response rates with durable clinical benefit, and manageable safety in patients with R/R LBCL after ≥1 prior line of therapy (LOT). Methods: Eligible patients were aged ≥18 years (y) with R/R LBCL after ≥1 prior LOT. Methods have been previously described (Hutchings, et al. JCO 2025). All patients provided informed consent. Efficacy endpoints were independent review committee-assessed overall response, durability of response, and survival outcomes.

结论（EHA原文）

Fixed-duration Glofit-Pola in patients with R/R LBCL demonstrated high and durable response rates in the elderly population, including those with HGBCL. Results are comparable with the overall population. These findings support the potential of this drug combination as an effective treatment option in elderly patients with limited therapeutic alternatives.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CRS is a common adverse event associated with bispecific antibody (bsAb) therapy. The step-up regimen for odronextamab (Odro; CD20×CD3 bsAb), was modified during the ELM‑2 study (NCT03888105) to include steroid pre-treatment (Tx) and an intermediate dose (0.7/4/20 mg), helping to mitigate risk of Grade (Gr)≥2 CRS (Kim et al. Blood 2022). Aims: To explore serum analytes in pts with relapsed/refractory DLBCL or FL treated with Odro in ELM-2, to better characterize pathways/proteomic signatures associated with CRS, and to elucidate the biological mechanisms driving CRS. Methods: A high-throughput proteomics approach (Olink Explore HT assay) was used to analyze serum proteins at baseline (BL) and on Tx. CRS severity (Gr≥2 vs Gr1/no CRS) was analyzed by disease type, step-up regimen, and CAR‑HEMATOTOX score (CAR-HT low [0–1] vs CAR‑HT high [≥2]; DLBCL only). Proteins associated with CRS were investigated using differential expression analyses. Cytokine data from a standard multiplex assay were used for comparison. Proteins were considered differentially abundant if they met minimal fold change ( 1.5) and false discovery rate (FDR)-adjusted p value criteria (p

结论（EHA原文）

Our analysis suggests that steroid pre-Tx attenuates the allograft rejection pathway and other inflammatory markers, potentially contributing to a reduced rate of Gr≥2 CRS in FL and DLBCL. FL pts with an inflamed systemic BL proteome may have a higher risk of Gr≥2 CRS. Further studies are needed to determine if proteomic profiling can identify pts at higher risk of severe CRS.

基线CD20高表达（>80%阳性肿瘤细胞）比例：89%（319/357）|||在进展性疾病（PD）患者中，69%（18/26）在C2D15或EOT出现CD20表达下降（相对基线减少≥50%）|||MS4A1突变频率：3%（8/287）|||转录下调频率：17%（2/12）|||一名病情稳定（SD）且维持CD20表达的患者携带可能干扰Epcoritamab结合的预存错义突变（细胞外环2）|||在18例PD患者中，7例维持CD20表达，其中4例在治疗中和EOT出现瘤内CD3+ T细胞减少

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Epcoritamab (epcor), a subcutaneous CD3×CD20 bispecific antibody, has demonstrated significant clinical benefit in DLBCL and FL as a monotherapy and in combinations. Modulation in CD20 expression has been reported with other CD3×CD20 bispecific antibodies, most often at disease progression, although the exact timing of these changes remains unclear. Aims: To describe modulation in CD20 expression in patients pre- and post- treatment (tx) with epcor, evaluate the impact of mutations and transcriptional downregulation on CD20 expression, and assess the association between intratumoral CD3+ T cells and progressive disease in the EPCORE NHL-1 trial (NCT03625037). Methods: Tumor biopsies from patients with R/R DLBCL or FL treated with 48-mg epcor in NHL-1 were collected. CD20 protein expression with and without PAX5 and T cells (CD3+) was quantified by immunohistochemistry at baseline, on tx (cycle 2 day 15 [C2D15]), or at the end of tx (EOT). Whole exome sequencing and EdgeSeq were performed on available patient samples to investigate mechanisms underlying reduced CD20 expression. Clinical responses at week 6 and EOT were assessed by investigator per Lugano criteria.

结论（EHA原文）

Whilst most patients with DLBCL and FL have high baseline CD20 expression and high response rates to epcor, clinical responses were also observed in some patients with baseline CD20 expression MS4A1 mutations and transcriptional downregulation in a subset of patients. Decreased intratumoral T-cell numbers were also identified as a potential mechanism of resistance. Similar changes in CD20 expression at progression have been reported with other CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies, suggesting antigen modulation may contribute to resistance in some patients. These findings support further exploration of strategies to overcome antigen escape and restore therapeutic sensitivity.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: High baseline CD20 expression (> 80% positive tumor cells) was observed in 89% (319/357) of biomarker-evaluable biopsies from patients with DLBCL and FL; CD20 expression 10% (PR, n = 3; SD, n = 2; PD, n = 18); patients with CR were excluded due to no detectable tumor at C2D15, limiting generalizability. CD20 expression was maintained on tx in 4 of 5 patients with PR/SD. CD20 expression MS4A1 mutations in the extracellular and transmembrane domains; transcriptional downregulation was observed in 2 (17%) patients. Notably, 1 patient with SD who maintained CD20 expression at C2D15 harbored a pre-existing missense mutation in extracellular loop 2 that may have interfered with epcor binding. Of the 18 pts with PD, 7 maintained CD20 expression, of whom 4 showed on-tx and EOT reductions in intratumoral CD3 T cells. Conclusion: Whilst most patients with DLBCL and FL have high baseline CD20 expression and high response rates to epcor, clinical responses were also observed in some patients with baseline CD20 expression MS4A1 mutations and transcriptional downregulation in a subset of patients. Decreased intratumoral T-cell numbers were also identified as a potential mechanism of resistance. Similar changes in CD20 expression at progression have been reported with other CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies, suggesting antigen modulation may contribute to resistance in some patients. These findings support further exploration of strategies to overcome antigen escape and restore therapeutic sensitivity.

total metabolic tumor volume and circulating tumor dna as early prognostic factors in relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: results from the phase 3 starglo trial

对照/比较：试验组1：glofitamab, gemcitabine, oxaliplatin（Glofit-GemOx） 对照组：rituximab, gemcitabine, oxaliplatin（R-GemOx）

O 结局指标

1. 基线高TMTV（≥125 cm³）与较差PFS相关：HR=1.49, p=0.004 2. 摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The Phase 3 STARGLO trial (NCT04408638) demonstrated significant 3-year overall survival and progression-free survival (PFS) benefits with fixed-duration glofitamab in combination with gemcitabine and oxaliplatin (GemOx; Glofit-GemOx), supporting its curative potential in autologous stem cell transplant (ASCT)-ineligible relapsed/refractory (R/R) diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). Nevertheless, identifying robust baseline and on-treatment biomarkers for the prediction of long-term outcomes remains a critical need. Aims: To evaluate the prognostic value of baseline total metabolic tumor volume (TMTV) alongside baseline and longitudinal circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) for the prediction of long-term outcomes in the STARGLO trial. Methods: Patients (pts) with ASCT-ineligible R/R DLBCL were randomized 2:1 to Glofit-GemOx or rituximab-GemOx (R-GemOx). ctDNA was analyzed using the AVENIO Oncology Assay NHL test and a customized linked somatic variants method, where co-occurring somatic variants 175 base pairs apart on single DNA fragments were identified. TMTV was assessed by fluorine-18 fluorodeoxyglucose positron emission tomography-computed tomography (PET-CT). Efficacy was assessed by PET-CT using Lugano criteria. Multivariate Kaplan–Meier and Cox-regression analyses were inverse probability weighting-adjusted to account for potential sampling bias in the biomarker-evaluable population. All pts provided written informed consent.

结论（EHA原文）

These results demonstrate the potential for TMTV and ctDNA as powerful prognostic tools in R/R DLBCL. Glofit-GemOx demonstrated superior efficacy over R-GemOx regardless of tumor burden (TMTV or ctDNA). In addition, longitudinal ctDNA monitoring supports early response assessment, with undetected ctDNA status by Cycle 3 emerging as a strong predictor of long-term PFS. Higher rates of undetectable ctDNA were observed with Glofit-GemOx vs R-GemOx, validating its clinical benefit and supporting the superior efficacy observed in the primary analysis of STARGLO.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Dose-attenuated rituximab plus cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, vincristine, and prednisone (R-mini-CHOP) is a standard of care (SOC) for patients (pts) with newly diagnosed (1L) DLBCL unable to receive full-dose R-CHOP due to age or comorbidities. Outcomes with R-mini-CHOP remain suboptimal, with 2-y PFS and OS rates of 47% and 59%, respectively. Aims: To report > 2-y follow-up results of epcoritamab, a CD3×CD20 bispecific antibody, plus R-mini-CHOP in elderly pts with 1L DLBCL ineligible for full-dose R-CHOP from the phase 1b/2 EPCORE ® NHL-2 trial (NCT04663347). Methods: Adults with 1L CD20+ DLBCL, ineligible for full dose R-CHOP due to age ≥ 75 y or ≥ 65 y with comorbidities, received fixed-duration SC epcoritamab 48 mg (QW, cycle(s) [C] 1–2 [21 d each]; Q3W, C3–6 [21 d each]; Q4W, C7–8 [28 d each]; with step-up dosing in C1 [0.16 mg on C1 day 1 (D1) and 0.8 mg on C1D8]) + R-mini-CHOP (Q3W, C1–6). The primary endpoint was ORR per Lugano criteria. MRD negativity, defined as

结论（EHA原文）

Fixed-duration epcoritamab + R-mini-CHOP led to high ORR and CR rates, rapid and sustained MRD negativity, and durable remissions in elderly pts with 1L DLBCL ineligible for full-dose R-CHOP. These outcomes compare favorably with historical outcomes of R-mini-CHOP alone. Safety was consistent with prior reports and the known safety profiles of epcoritamab and R-mini-CHOP. These results, along with those from other arms of the trial, support combinations of epcoritamab with SOC across a range of disease settings and pt populations. © American Society of Hematology (2025). Reused with permission.

038DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLADCS238

北欧淋巴瘤组3期北极熊试验在老年或体弱弥漫性大细胞淋巴瘤患者中的安全性数据和初步合并疗效数据-r-polamini-chp与r-mini-chop

safety data and initial pooled efficacy data from the nordic lymphoma group phase 3 polar bear trial in elderly or frail patients with diffuse large cell lymphoma - r-pola-mini-chp vs. r-mini-chop

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=300；疾病阶段：Ⅳ 期，Ⅲ 期，Ⅱ 期

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；靶点：CD79B；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；分组：试验组1：R-miniCHOP（标准治疗组）；试验组2：Pola-R-miniCHP（实验组，polatuzumab vedotin替代长春新碱）

O 结局指标

不良事件（AE）：任何等级AE发生率未明确给出，但报告了≥3级AE在Arm A为30%，Arm B为36%；感染≥3级：Arm A 7.3%，Arm B 12.7%；胃肠道毒性>2级：Arm A 3.3%，Arm B 6%；周围神经病变1-2级：Arm A 10.7%，Arm B 17.3%，≥3级仅Arm B 2例；5级AE：Arm A 2例，Arm B 8例；血液学毒性两组无差异。 疗效：合并的2年无进展生存期（PFS）为67%（95%CI 60-73）；合并的2年总生存期（OS）为76%；总事件85例，其中35例死亡为首发事件。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: For patients with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), overall survival (OS) has substantially improved during the last decade. An exception is the group of patients above 80 years of age, a group that also constitutes an increasing proportion of DLBCL patients due to a demographic shift, with a progressively aging population. Effective and safe treatment for this population is an obvious unmet medical need. Aims: In this randomized phase 3 trial (NCT04332822), we evaluated tolerability and efficacy of Pola-R-mini-CHP as first line treatment for elderly/frail patients with DLBCL, compared to the current treatment standard, R-mini-CHOP. Here, we present data on safety from the 300 patients in this trial, as well as efficacy pooled across treatment arms, including subgroups. Methods: Patients with newly diagnosed DLBCL, >80 years, or 75-80 years and frail, according to a simplified Comprehensive Geriatric Assessment, were randomized 1:1 to either the standard treatment for this population, R-miniCHOP (Arm A), or an experimental regimen, Pola-R-miniCHP (Arm B), where vincristine is substituted by polatuzumab vedotin, 1.8 mg/kg, day 1, both for 6 cycles. The sample size is based on a target HR for PFS of 0.64, and the total number of events necessary to achieve at least 80% power with type I error α=0.05, is 158. In this report, the highest grade of adverse event for each category, according to CTCAE v 5, was reported. The data cut-off was 31-AUG-2025.

结论（EHA原文）

Rituximab/anthracycline-based chemotherapy remains the standard of care for elderly and frail patients with DLBCL, demonstrating excellent outcomes with acceptable tolerability. Compared to historical data with R-mini-CHOP (Peyrade 2011), showing 2 year PFS of 47% and OS of 59%—our observed pooled 2-year PFS of 67% and OS of 76% are highly encouraging. Infectious complications, gastrointestinal toxicity, and peripheral neuropathy were generally manageable, and substitution of vincristine with polatuzumab vedotin in the R-mini-CHOP did not result in a significant increase in either the incidence or severity of toxicity .

克隆性造血与接受dlbcl治疗的老年患者持续贫血有关：北极熊3期试验分析

clonal hematopoiesis is associated with persisting anemia in elderly patients treated for dlbcl: analysis of the phase 3 polar bear trial

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=228；疾病阶段：Ⅳ 期，Ⅲ 期，Ⅱ 期

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；靶点：CD79B；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；分组：试验组1：R-miniCHOP；试验组2：R-miniCHP-polatuzumab vedotin

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：R-miniCHOP；试验组2：R-miniCHP-polatuzumab vedotin

O 结局指标

基线CHIP检出率：40% (92/228)；常见突变基因：DNMT3A (n=55), TET2 (n=45), SF3B1 (n=15)；大CHIP克隆(VAF≥10%, n=33)患者存在持续性贫血，治疗后未恢复；治疗后出现/增长与治疗相关白血病相关的突变 (TP53和PPM1D, n=7)；SF3B1突变克隆在免疫化疗后迅速缩小(VAF下降≥40%, n=9)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Cytopenias are common during immunochemotherapy, particularly among elderly patients (pts), and often result in dose reductions, diminishing treatment efficacy. The factors predicting these toxicities remain to be identified. Clonal hematopoiesis of indeterminate potential (CHIP), defined as somatic mutations in myeloid cells, in pts with lymphoma et al . Leukemia 2020). In particular, mutations in DNA repair pathway genes have been associated with poor survival. To our knowledge, the impact of CHIP on elderly pts with lymphoma has not been extensively studied. Aims: To investigate the impact of clonal hematopoiesis on toxicity in elderly patients with aggressive lymphoma undergoing curative-intent chemotherapy. Methods: A total of 393 blood samples - peripheral granulocyte pellets – from 228 pts in the phase 3 POLAR BEAR trial (NCT04332822; elderly pts with DLBCL, 1st line, randomized 1:1 to R-miniCHOP or R-miniCHP-polatuzumab vedotin) were collected prospectively and analyzed for CHIP by targeted next-generation sequencing of 31 genes associated with clonal hematopoiesis (min. depth of 1000X). The cut-off for mutation detection was variant allele frequency (VAF) 2.0%. Paired baseline and post-treatment samples were available for 161 pts. The study arm of patients has not yet been unblinded.

结论（EHA原文）

CHIP is very common in elderly pts with DLBCL treated with immunochemotherapy and large clones are associated with persistent anemia. In sequential samples we identify clonal evolutionary patterns with growth/gain of mutations associated with therapy-related leukemia. We also find that SF3B1 -mutated CHIP clones shrink during immunochemotherapy, which to our knowledge has not been described previously.

O 结局指标

最佳总缓解率(ORR): 90.2% 完全缓解(CR): 84.3% 部分缓解(PR): 5.9% 疾病进展(PD): 9.8% 12个月无进展生存期(PFS): 88.6% 中位随访: 13.2个月 3-4级血液学毒性: 51.0% 肺部感染: 9.8% 周围神经病变(1-2级): 19.6%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Optimizing first-line treatment for diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) remains clinically challenging, particularly in older and frail patients who are frequently underrepresented in prospective clinical trials. While the POLARIX trial established polatuzumab vedotin (Pola) plus R-CHP as a new standard for selected patients, real-world evidence regarding its efficacy across diverse patient populations and the predictive value of molecular subtyping remains limited. Integration of next-generation sequencing (NGS) may refine risk stratification and identify genetic determinants of treatment resistance. Aims: To evaluate the real-world efficacy, safety, and progression-free survival (PFS) of Pola-based first-line regimens in an unselected DLBCL cohort, and to explore associations between genetic subtypes, somatic variants, and treatment outcomes. Methods: We conducted a single-center retrospective analysis of 51 DLBCL patients treated with Pola-based first-line therapy between April 2023 and August 2025. Treatment allocation was stratified by age and geriatric assessment: Pola-R-CHP was administered to patients ≤60 years and fit patients >60 years, while unfit/frail elderly patients received Pola-R-miniCHP or Pola-ZR. Response assessment utilized whole-body 18F-FDG PET/CT after cycles 4 and 6, classified per Lugano 2014 criteria. Adverse events were graded using CTCAE v5.0. Tumor DNA underwent targeted capture NGS using a 169-gene panel to identify coding SNVs/indels and enable LymphGen molecular subtyping. An exploratory case-control analysis compared genomic profiles between progressors (PD) and responders (CR/PR). PFS was estimated using the Kaplan-Meier method.

结论（EHA原文）

In this real-world cohort, Pola-based first-line therapy achieved high response rates with durable disease control and manageable toxicity, extending benefit to patients traditionally excluded from clinical trials. The A53 molecular subtype may predict inferior outcomes, while CCND3 mutations emerge as a potential biomarker of primary resistance. These findings support the integration of genomic profiling into treatment algorithms and warrant prospective validation in larger cohorts to personalize Pola-based therapy in DLBCL.

polatuzumab vedotin combined with orelabrutinib and rituximab (pro regimen) as frontline therapy in very elderly and frail patients with dlbcl: updated results from a phase ii study

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=39

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：奥布替尼；维泊妥珠单抗；利妥昔单抗；靶点：BTK；CD79B；CD20；类别：化药；缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；单特异性抗体；分组：试验组：Polatuzumab vedotin, Orelabrutinib, Rituximab

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

完全缓解率（CR）: 58.6% (17/29) 客观缓解率（ORR）: 96.5% MCD亚型客观缓解率: 100% (12/12) MCD亚型完全缓解率: 66.7% (8/12) 治疗结束后完全缓解率（C6-response）: 91.7% (22/24) 中位无进展生存期（PFS）: 未达到 中位总生存期（OS）: 未达到 9个月无进展生存率: 92.8% 3-4级肺部感染发生率: 17.9% 3-4级中性粒细胞减少发生率: 10.3%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The management of very elderly patients (aged ≥75-80 years) with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) remains a significant clinical challenge due to comorbidities, frailty, and poor tolerance to standard immunochemotherapy. There is a critical need for effective, reduced-intensity, or chemotherapy-free regimens. Aims: The PRO regimen (Polatuzumab vedotin, Orelabrutinib, and Rituximab) was designed to address this unmet need. We present updated results from an ongoing Phase II study focusing on this vulnerable population. Methods: This open-label, multicenter Phase II study enrolled previously untreated elderly and frail patients with DLBCL. Patients received Polatuzumab vedotin (1.8 mg/kg), Orelabrutinib (150 mg daily), and Rituximab (375 mg/m²) every 3 weeks for up to six cycles, followed by two additional Rituximab cycles in responders. Tumor response was evaluated every three cycles by PET/CT or contrast-enhanced CT according to Lugano 2014 criteria. The primary endpoint was end-of-treatment CR rate; secondary endpoints included ORR, PFS, DoR, OS, and safety.

结论（EHA原文）

In summary, despite a high comorbidity burden (74.3%), updated data from 39 patients indicate that the chemotherapy-free PRO regimen is an effective and tolerable frontline option for elderly and frail DLBCL patients. It achieved a 91.7% CR rate at treatment completion and an estimated 9-month PFS of 92.8%, with 100% ORR in the MCD subtype. These results support PRO as a feasible strategy for vulnerable patients, including those ≥80 years who are unfit for intensive immunochemotherapy.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: By February 2026, 39 patients with a median age of 78.0 years (IQR: 75.0–84.0) were evaluable, including 43.6% (n=17) aged ≥80. High-risk features were prevalent: 69.2% each presented with an IPI score of 3–5, stage III–IV disease, or elevated LDH. Histologically, 97.4% had DLBCL, and one (2.6%) had primary cutaneous DLBCL, leg type (PCDLBCL, LT); 77.0% were of the non-GCB/ABC subtype. Comorbidities affected 74.3% (29/39) of this ultra-elderly cohort, most commonly cardiovascular diseases (41.0%), hypertension (35.9%), diabetes (15.4%), cerebrovascular diseases (15.4%), and prostatic hypertrophy (5.1%). \n At the data cutoff, of the 39 enrolled patients, 29 have completed the interim efficacy assessment, the CR rate was 58.6% (17/29), with an ORR of 96.5%. Among these, 37.9% (11/29) achieved a partial response, while 3.4% (1/29) experienced disease progression. Notably, in the 12 patients identified with the MCD subtype, the ORR rate was 100% (12/12), the CR rate was 66.7% (8/12). At the completion of combination therapy (C6-response), the CR rate was 91.7% (22/24), the ORR rate was 95.8 % (23/24). With a median follow-up of 7.0 months (range, 0.4–21.5), neither the median progression-free survival (PFS) nor the median overall survival (OS) has been reached. The estimated 9-month PFS rate was 92.8%. Subgroup analysis of patients aged ≥80 years (n=17) demonstrated survival outcomes comparable to the overall cohort, suggesting the sustained benefit of the chemo-free PRO regimen in the oldest-old. \n The PRO regimen demonstrated a manageable safety profile in this ultra-elderly and frail population. Grade 3-4 adverse events (AEs) were primarily pulmonary infections (17.9%) and neutropenia (10.3%). Most other hematological and non-hematological toxicities were confined to Grade 1-2 and were clinically manageable with supportive care. Conclusion: In summary, despite a high comorbidity burden (74.3%), updated data from 39 patients indicate that the chemotherapy-free PRO regimen is an effective and tolerable frontline option for elderly and frail DLBCL patients. It achieved a 91.7% CR rate at treatment completion and an estimated 9-month PFS of 92.8%, with 100% ORR in the MCD subtype. These results support PRO as a feasible strategy for vulnerable patients, including those ≥80 years who are unfit for intensive immunochemotherapy.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Detection of circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA)-based measurable/molecular residual disease (MRD) with phased variant (PV) enrichment and detection sequencing (PhasED-seq) is a minimally invasive, clinically validated method of response assessment in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). Patients (pts) with undetected ctDNA-MRD by PhasED-seq after 2 cycles of frontline therapy experienced a 2-year progression-free survival rate of 96% (Roschewski JCO 2025). Real-time ctDNA-MRD testing with the PhasED-seq-based Foresight CLARITY assay to guide de-escalation of frontline DLBCL therapy has not previously been performed. Aims: The co-primary aims were to 1) evaluate the feasibility of real-time ctDNA-MRD testing during frontline DLBCL treatment and 2) determine the outcomes of pts who became undetectable for ctDNA-MRD mid-treatment and discontinued chemotherapy early. Methods: We performed a single-center investigator-initiated feasibility study (NCT06693830) for pts with newly diagnosed stage II-IV DLBCL. Pts received 4 cycles of standard rituximab, cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, prednisone, and vincristine (R-CHOP) or polatuzumab vedotin (R-pola-CHP). Whole blood samples were drawn on cycle 4 day 1 (C4D1) for real-time ctDNA-MRD testing. These samples, alongside biopsy tissue to identify patient-specific PVs, were shipped to and analyzed at Foresight Diagnostics, Inc. (Boulder, CO). PET scans were performed on C4D15 (iPET4). Pts with undetected ctDNA-MRD on C4D1 and complete metabolic response (CMR) on iPET4 received rituximab alone for C5-6. All other pts continued standard therapy. Equivocal iPET4 response could be confirmed with biopsy. An end-of-treatment (EOT) PET was performed 10-14 weeks after C6D1. ctDNA-MRD was also evaluated in a batched manner from other timepoints.

结论（EHA原文）

Preliminary results from SHORTEN-ctDNA suggest that real-time ctDNA-MRD assessment with Foresight CLARITY to de-escalate frontline therapy in DLBCL is feasible. Short-term clinical outcomes and molecular remissions for pts with undetected mid-treatment ctDNA-MRD who stop chemotherapy early are excellent.

pola-rchp治疗结外受累的dlbcl患者：代表性不足人群的真实证据

pola-rchp for dlbcl patients with extranodal involvement: real-world evidence in an underrepresented population

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=103

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；靶点：CD79B；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；分组：试验组1：polatuzumab vedotin，利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松（pola-R-CHP）

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

客观缓解率（ORR）：86%|完全缓解率（CR）：81%|6个月无进展生存率：85.9%|12个月无进展生存率：77.3%|6个月总生存率：100%|12个月总生存率：97.4%|任何级别不良事件：中性粒细胞减少32%，恶心25%，周围神经病变20%|≥3级不良事件：中性粒细胞减少24%，感染10%，贫血9%|无治疗相关死亡

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The POLARIX trial established polatuzumab vedotin in combination with rituximab, cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, and prednisone (pola-R-CHP) as a new standard for first-line treatment of diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). However, patients with extranodal involvement—a well-recognized adverse prognostic factor—were underrepresented in that study, and data on the efficacy and safety of this regimen in the real-world population remain scarce. To address this gap, we conducted a single-center retrospective analysis of DLBCL patients with extranodal involvement treated with pola-R-CHP. Aims: The primary objectives were to assess overall response rate (ORR), complete response (CR) rate, and short-term survival outcomes; secondary objectives included safety evaluation and exploration of whether the pattern of extranodal involvement (single-site versus multi-site) influenced treatment outcomes. Methods: Eligible patients had pathologically confirmed DLBCL with at least one extranodal site, completed ≥2 cycles of pola-R-CHP followed by response assessment, and had no prior anti-lymphoma therapy. All patients were scheduled to receive six cycles of pola-R-CHP and two additional cycles of rituximab monotherapy. Efficacy and safety were assessed per Lugano 2014 criteria and CTCAE version 5.0, respectively. Survival was estimated using the Kaplan-Meier method, with data censored as of January 31, 2026.

结论（EHA原文）

To our knowledge, this represents the first real-world evidence demonstrating that pola-R-CHP is both highly active and well tolerated in DLBCL patients with extranodal involvement. Despite the uniformly high-risk features of this cohort, the observed CRR of 81% compares favorably with the 78% CRR reported in the overall POLARIX population. These findings support the use of pola-R-CHP in this challenging subgroup and underscore the need for larger prospective studies to further delineate outcomes according to specific extranodal sites.

bruton tyrosine kinase inhibitor maintenance therapy in first-line diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: a multicenter real-world study challenging conventional paradigms

O 结局指标

2年PFS率：90% 2年OS率：98% 高危（IPI≥3）2年PFS：87.0% 高危（CNS-IPI≥4）2年PFS：86.5% 多因素分析维持治疗为PFS独立预后因素（HR 0.42, 95% CI 0.20-0.88; P=0.019） BTKi治疗组（n=78）2年PFS：87.6%，2年OS：97.2% 无CNS复发（高危患者中） 维持时间≥12个月与更好PFS相关（P=0.042） 仅PR患者接受维持后PFS与CR患者相当 MCD亚型PFS优于A53亚型（P=0.078） ≥3级血小板减少发生率2.6%，无≥3级非血液学毒性

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) remains the most common aggressive non-Hodgkin lymphoma, with approximately 30% of patients experiencing relapse following standard R-CHOP induction therapy.The role of maintenance strategies in DLBCL has been controversial, with rituximab and lenalidomide maintenance failing to demonstrate consistent overall survival (OS) benefits. The emergence of novel targeted agents, particularly Bruton tyrosine kinase inhibitors (BTKi), has potentially reshaped first-line treatment paradigms, yet their efficacy as maintenance therapy remains inadequately characterized. Aims: This multicenter retrospective study aims to evaluate the prognostic impact of BTKi-based maintenance therapy in the context of modern DLBCL treatment. Methods: We conducted a retrospective analysis of 106 DLBCL patients who received first-line maintenance therapy. Eligible patients achieved complete (CR) or partial response (PR) following induction therapy. BTKi maintenance (zanubrutinib or orelabrutinib) was administered to 73.6% of patients. Using propensity score matching (PSM), we selected 44 patients from the publicly available REMoDL-B trial database as a control group. Next-generation sequencing was performed for molecular subtyping according to Wright's \"seven-gene\" model. Survival outcomes were analyzed using Kaplan-Meier methods and Cox proportional hazards regression.

结论（EHA原文）

This real-world study challenges established dogma by demonstrating that BTKi-based maintenance therapy significantly improves PFS and OS in DLBCL, particularly for high-risk patients and those achieving suboptimal responses to induction therapy. The absence of CNS relapses in high-risk patients and potential enhanced efficacy in MCD molecular subtype support BTKi maintenance as a promising strategy. These findings warrant prospective validation in randomized trials and suggest reconsideration of maintenance therapy's role in modern DLBCL management.

clinical characteristics and efficacy of myc/bcl-2 double-expressing diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: real-world data from the believe study

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：R-CHOP-like方案；试验组2：R-CHOP加靶向药物（包括BTK抑制剂等）；试验组3：R-CHOP+BTK抑制剂（奥布替尼常用）

O 结局指标

客观缓解率（ORR）：在可评估的1051例DEL-DLBCL患者中为75.9%；完全缓解率（CRR）：57.5%；R-CHOP加靶向药物组的ORR为84.2%；R-CHOP+BTKi组（n=69）的ORR为88.4%，CRR为75.4%；奥布替尼组（n=43）的ORR为88.3%，CRR为76.7%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) displays marked molecular heterogeneity. The phase Ⅱ GUIDANCE-01 trial showed that subtype-guided immunochemotherapy (R-CHOP-X) improves anti-tumor efficacy with manageable safety (Cancer Cell 2023:41:1705-1716) . The phase Ⅲ DEB trial confirmed that R-CHOP plus chidamide significantly prolongs survival in MYC/BCL-2 double-expressing DLBCL (DEL-DLBCL) (ASH 2025 oral 475) . Aims: We present the large‑scale Chinese real‑world BELIEVE study (NCT06026488) to assess the effectiveness of different therapeutic strategies in DEL‑DLBCL and generate real‑world evidence to support clinical decision‑making. Methods: This retrospective study enrolled DLBCL patients who underwent next‑generation sequencing (NGS). Baseline characteristics, treatments, efficacy, and survival data were collected. The primary endpoint was progression‑free survival (PFS); key secondary endpoints included objective response rate (ORR), complete response rate (CRR), and overall survival (OS).

结论（EHA原文）

In this large Chinese real‑world cohort, DEL‑DLBCL accounts for ~30% of DLBCL and is characterized by aggressive clinicopathological features and inferior outcomes compared with non‑DEL DLBCL, confirming its high‑risk nature. R‑CHOP‑like therapy shows limited efficacy in DEL‑DLBCL, whereas R‑CHOP plus BTKi show promising efficacy, supporting individualized, evidence‑based treatment options for DEL‑DLBCL. This study provides real‑world evidence to optimize DEL‑DLBCL management. Long‑term survival analyses including PFS are ongoing.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) patients with co-expression of MYC (≥40%) and BCL2 (≥50%), defined as double-expressor DLBCL (DE-DLBCL), typically have poor outcomes with the traditional first-line R-CHOP regimen. Given that the optimal first-line treatment strategy for DE-DLBCL patients remains unclear, there is an urgent need to explore more effective and therapeutic approaches. Orelabrutinib (O), a novel, potent, and highly selective Bruton’s tyrosine kinase (BTK) inhibitor, has demonstrated encouraging therapeutic potential in patients with DLBCL when combined with the R-CHOP regimen. Aims: We conducted a multicenter, single-arm, phase II study to evaluate the efficacy and safety of the O plus R-CHOP (O-RCHOP) regimen in newly diagnosed patients with non-germinal center B-cell-like (non-GCB) DE-DLBCL. Methods: All eligible patients received 6-8 cycles of 21-day treatment, including O 150 mg once daily on days 1-14 combined with R-CHOP (rituximab 375 mg/m 2 on day 0; cyclophosphamide 750 mg/m 2 on day 1; doxorubicin 50 mg/m 2 on day 1; vindesine 4 mg on day 1; prednisone 100 mg on days 1-5). The primary endpoint was event-free survival (EFS). The secondary endpoints included progression-free survival (PFS), complete response rate (CRR), objective response rate (ORR), 3-year overall survival (OS) rate, and safety.

结论（EHA原文）

In previously untreated non-GCB DE-DLBCL patients, O-RCHOP achieved promising efficacy with a manageable safety profile, supporting its promise as a feasible first-line regimen.

re‑evaluating the role of autologous stem cell transplantation in primary cns diffuse large b‑cell lymphoma in the targeted‑therapy era: a propensity score–matched multicenter real‑world study

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=291；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

分组：ASCT组/非ASCT组

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

主要终点：无进展生存期（PFS），ASCT组优于非ASCT组（p=0.023）；次要终点：总生存期（OS），ASCT组有获益趋势但未达统计学意义（p=0.085）。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The role of autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) in primary central nervous system diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (PCNS-DLBCL) is being re-evaluated, particularly in newly diagnosed patients, as BTK inhibitors (BTKi) and lenalidomide are increasingly used in induction, salvage, and maintenance therapy. In real-world clinical practice, ASCT allocation is influenced by baseline fitness and disease characteristics, highlighting the need for confounding control to assess outcomes and clarify whether post-induction consolidation strategies are key to long-term results in the Targeted Therapy era. Aims: This study aimed to evaluate the association between ASCT and progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) in patients with PCNS-DLBCL treated in the BTKi/lenalidomide era, using propensity score matching (PSM) to adjust for confounding factors. We also examined whether post-induction consolidation strategies (ASCT and/or maintenance) and BTKi/lenalidomide treatment pathways stratify outcomes, including among treatment responders. Methods: We conducted a retrospective, three-centre cohort study of PCNS-DLBCL patients treated in routine practice. The primary exposure was ASCT (yes vs no). PSM was performed using nearest-neighbour matching with a target ratio of 1:2 and caliper width of 0.1, adjusting for covariates listed in Table 1. Balance was assessed using standardized mean differences. Endpoints were PFS and OS, analyzed by Kaplan–Meier methods with log-rank comparisons. Prespecified exploratory analyses evaluated six subgroups based on regimen category (BTKi, lenalidomide, or neither) and ASCT status; four subgroups based on ASCT and maintenance therapy; and responder subsets (CR/PR and CR). All analyses were hypothesis-generating.

结论（EHA原文）

In patients with PCNS-DLBCL treated in the BTKi/lenalidomide era, ASCT was associated with improved PFS after PSM, while OS showed a favorable trend. Post-induction consolidation strategies most strongly differentiated long-term outcomes, with maintenance therapy being particularly beneficial for patients not receiving ASCT. Outcomes also varied by regimen type (BTKi-based, lenalidomide-based, or neither) and ASCT status. These findings support a risk-adapted approach for selecting ASCT and/or maintenance therapy, highlighting the need for prospective validation. Key survival curves are presented in the submitted figure.

总客观缓解率（ORR）在50mg和75mg剂量组中为47.6%（20/42） 完全缓解率（CRR）为31.0%（13/42） GCB亚型ORR 58.3%（7/12），CRR 41.7%（5/12） 非GCB亚型ORR 44.8%（13/29），CRR 27.6%（8/29） 完全缓解患者中位缓解持续时间（DoR）未达到，最长CR超过9.3个月 MCD-like亚型ORR 50.0%（6/12），CRR 33.3%（4/12） TP53-mut亚型ORR 50.0%（5/10），CRR 30.0%（3/10） NOS亚型ORR 50.0%（7/14），CRR 35.7%（5/14） 常见3/4级药物相关不良事件：血小板减少（20.7%）、中性粒细胞减少（12.1%）、肺炎（5.2%）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: A major hurdle in treating DLBCL is its high molecular heterogeneity. BTK inhibitors show efficacy primarily in the non-GCB (ABC) subtype and certain genomic clusters. T-cell-directed therapies expand the treatment landscape but are constrained by a challenging toxicity profile, including severe adverse events like CRS and ICANS. Therefore, there is a critical need for next-generation targeted agents that provide broad-spectrum activity across molecular subtypes and coupled with a favorable safety profile. LYN and BTK are critical mediators of B-cell receptor (BCR) signalling, driving lymphomagenesis across diverse molecular profiles. Birelentinib (DZD8586), a novel LYN/BTK dual inhibitor with excellent blood-brain barrier (BBB) penetration, is designed to overcome these barriers by targeting multiple components of the BCR signalling pathway. Here, we report updated results from the ongoing Phase 2 TAI-SHAN9 study (NCT06539195) for birelentinib in r/r DLBCL, including an analysis of activity across genetic subtypes. \n Methods: Adult patients aged ≥18 years with histologically confirmed DLBCL and prior standard chemoimmunotherapy were enrolled. Birelentinib was administered orally as monotherapy until disease progression, unacceptable toxicity, or patient withdrawal. Investigators assessed antitumor efficacy per Lugano 2014 criteria using PET and contrast-enhanced CT scans. Adverse events (AEs) were graded using CTCAE v5.0. Based on targeted sequencing, LymphPlex algorithm was applied to assign genetic subtypes, and clinical efficacy was analyzed across genetic subtypes.

结论（EHA原文）

Birelentinib demonstrated universal and potentially durable activity across molecular subtypes, with a manageable safety profile. These findings suggest broad therapeutic potential for birelentinib in DLBCL.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The prognosis of relapsed or refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (R/R DLBCL) is poor, and outcomes are particularly dismal for R/R CNS lymphomas (primary [PCNSL] or secondary [SCNSL]). R-ICE (rituximab, ifosfamide, carboplatin, and etoposide) chemotherapy has shown efficacy in these patients (pts) but the durability of response is limited. Recently, BTK inhibitors have demonstrated encouraging efficacy outcomes in systemic R/R non-GCB DLBCL and R/R CNS lymphomas. Aims: This phase I/II study aims to evaluate the efficacy, safety, and feasibility of combining zanubrutinib, a second-generation BTK inhibitor, with R-ICE (ZR-ICE) in pts with R/R systemic non-GCB DLBCL or R/R CNS lymphomas. Here we report the interim efficacy and safety results from the phase II part. Methods: In the phase I part, zanubrutinib 160 mg daily was established as the recommended phase 2 dose based on a standard 3+3 dose escalation design. In the phase II part, pts with R/R systemic non-GCB DLBCL (cohort A) or R/R CNS lymphomas (PCNSL or SCNSL) (cohort B) received zanubrutinib 160 mg daily in combination with R-ICE. The R-ICE regimen consisted of rituximab 375 mg/m² IV (D1), ifosfamide 1670 mg/m² IV (D1–3), etoposide 100 mg/m²/day IV (D1–3), and carboplatin AUC 5 IV (D2). Pts who were candidates for upfront autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) and achieved CR or PR after 3 cycles proceeded to ASCT. Pts who were not candidates for upfront ASCT received up to 6 cycles of ZR-ICE. Cohort B pts achieving CR or PR after 6 cycles of ZR-ICE or 3 cycles of ZR-ICE followed by ASCT received zanubrutinib 320 mg daily as maintenance for up to 24 months.

结论（EHA原文）

ZR-ICE demonstrated promising efficacy with a manageable safety profile in R/R systemic non-GCB DLBCL and R/R CNS lymphomas. These interim results support continued enrollment of this ongoing phase II study.

050DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLBTKiPF964

zanubrutinib联合r-chop作为myd88（l265p）/cd79b突变（mcd）弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤的一线治疗：一项ii期研究。

zanubrutinib plus r-chop as frontline therapy for myd88（l265p）/cd79b-mutated (mcd) diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: a phase ii study.

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=40

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：泽布替尼；靶点：BTK；类别：化药；分组：试验组：Zanubrutinib + R-CHOP

O 结局指标

总缓解率(ORR): 95% 完全缓解率(CR): 87.5% (35/40) 3年无进展生存率(PFS): 88.5% (95% CI, 71.4–95.7) 3年总生存率(OS): 97.5% (95% CI, 83.5–99.6) 中枢神经系统复发: 0 3级及以上不良事件发生率: 62.5% 最常见不良事件(所有级别): 中性粒细胞减少95%, 肺部感染20%, 贫血10%, 血小板减少8% 最常见的3-4级不良事件: 中性粒细胞减少

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: MCD-subtype DLBCL characterized by concurrent MYD88(L265P) and CD79B mutations is driven by chronic active B-cell receptor/NF- κ B signaling and is associated with suboptimal outcomes with standard R-CHOP. BTK inhibition represents a rational, biomarker-enriched strategy for this population. Aims: The present study aimed to investigate the efficacy and safety of Zanubrutinib in combination with R-CHOP in previously untreated DLBCL patients harboring both MYD88(L265P) and CD79B mutations. Methods: Eligible patients with previously untreated DLBCL harboring concurrent MYD88L265P and CD79B mutations (MCD subtype), identified by next-generation sequencing (NGS), and an ECOG performance status of 0 – 3 received Zanubrutinib 160 mg orally twice daily plus R-CHOP every 21 days. Treatment was response-adapted after four cycles based on interim response: patients achieving complete remission (CR) received two additional cycles of ZR-CHOP followed by rituximab consolidation, whereas patients with non-CR could receive up to four additional cycles of ZR-CHOP. The primary endpoint was progression-free survival (PFS). Secondary endpoints included overall response rate (ORR), overall survival (OS), and safety. Responses were investigator-assessed based on best overall response. Time-to-event endpoints were estimated using the Kaplan – Meier method.

结论（EHA原文）

Frontline ZR-CHOP demonstrated high CR rates and encouraging long-term PFS/OS with few progression events and no CNS relapse in previously untreated MYD88(L265P)/CD79B-mutated (MCD) DLBCL, including durable disease control in IPI 3 – 5 high-risk patients, with a manageable safety profile. These findings support a biomarker-driven BTK inhibitor – based frontline approach for this molecularly high-risk DLBCL subtype and warrant validation in a larger prospective study.

扎努布替尼联合r-chop（zr-chop）治疗非生发中心b细胞样（非gcb）弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤患者，这些患者在两个周期的r-chop治疗后正电子发射断层扫描呈阳性

zanubrutinib plus r-chop (zr-chop) in non-germinal center b-cell-like (non-gcb) diffuse large b-cell lymphoma patients who were positron emission tomography-positive after two cycles of r-chop

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=28

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：泽布替尼；靶点：BTK；类别：化药；分组：试验组1：泽布替尼，利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，长春新碱，泼尼松（ZR-CHOP诱导6周期，随后泽布替尼维持至多6个月）

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

中位随访28.3个月；2年无事件生存（EFS）率38.2%（95%CI 18.4-57.9）；中位EFS 17.6个月（8.3-NE）；最佳总缓解率（ORR）89.3%（CR 42.9%，PR 46.4%）；反应改善率54.2%（13/24，95%CI 32.8-74.5）；任意级别治疗期间不良事件（TEAE）发生率96.4%；≥3级TEAE发生率77.8%；严重不良事件（SAE）发生率18.5%。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: R-CHOP is a standard treatment for previously untreated diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), however, more than one-third of patients are not cured by R-CHOP. There is a clear need to improve the prognosis of patients, especially for those with factors associated with poor prognosis, such as non-GCB subtype and positive interim positron emission tomography (PET). Bruton's tyrosine kinase inhibitors (BTKi) have established therapeutic activity in B-cell malignancies, with modest activity in DLBCL. Zanubrutinib, a potent and selective BTKi, was evaluated in patients with relapsed or refractory (R/R) non-GCB DLBCL. Zanubrutinib showed minimized off-target activities against interleukin-2-inducible T cell kinase (ITK) and reduced interference of ITK-mediated, rituximab-induced, antibody-dependent cellular cytotoxicity. Therefore, ZR-CHOP is a potentially effective regimen. Aims: We designed a treatment escalation regimen with ZR-CHOP, followed by zanubrutinib maintenance, for non-GCB DLBCL patients who were PET positive after two cycles of R-CHOP. Methods: This was a single arm, multicenter, phase II study. Patients with non-GCB DLBCL who were PET positive (Deauville scores 4 or 5) after two cycles of R-CHOP were enrolled. Patients with PET negative or PD were excluded. Patients received ZR-CHOP in a 21-day cycle for 6 cycles (induction), followed by zanubrutinib monotherapy as maintenance up to 6 months for patients who achieved PR or CR. Zanubrutinib was administered orally twice daily at 160 mg. The primary endpoint was 2-year event-free survival (EFS) from start of RCHOP treatment, defined as disease progression, relapse from CR, initiation of subsequent systemic antilymphoma therapy for either PET-positive or biopsy-proven residual disease upon completion of at least 6 cycles of ZR-CHOP therapy, or death, whichever occurred first. Secondary endpoints included overall remission rate (ORR), complete remission rate, response improvement rate (defined as the proportion of patients whose response was improved from PR to CR or from SD to CR or PR during ZR-CHOP induction), and safety.

结论（EHA原文）

Our results showed that ZR-CHOP was a safe and effective scheme for non-GCB DLBCL patients who were PET positive after two-cycle R-CHOP. It indicates that adding zanubrutinib to escalate the treatment under the guidance of dynamic PET-CT can improve the remission and median EFS of these patients without significantly increasing toxicity.

052DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL化疗/免疫化疗S259

利用循环肿瘤dna双链体对侵袭性大b细胞淋巴瘤进行分子监测

molecular surveillance of aggressive large b-cell lymphoma using circulating tumor dna duplexes

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=123；疾病阶段：侵袭性

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：molecular surveillance of aggressive large b-cell lymphoma using circulating tumor dna duplexes

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

5年无进展生存率：82% 5年总生存率：90% 两个周期化疗后分子缓解率：67% 两个周期后MRD阳性患者5年OS：97% vs 75% 四个周期后MRD阳性患者中52%转为阴性 治疗结束时MRD阴性患者5年OS：96% vs 30% 随访中92%的患者在临床进展前ctDNA转为阳性（中位提前6个月）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Treatment failure occurs in one-third of patients with aggressive large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), and current tools are insufficient for determining remission. Liquid biopsies using plasma circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) complement diagnostics, predict treatment response and survival, and are expected to transform treatment decision-making. Aims: We aimed to assess the added clinical benefit of longitudinal ctDNA monitoring by duplex sequencing in plasma samples from patients with primary high-risk LBCL. Methods: We used a targeted duplex sequencing-based ctDNA assay on 447 longitudinal plasma cfDNA samples to analyze measurable residual disease (MRD) from 123 patients with primary LBCL at various time points during treatment and follow-up as part of the Nordic LBC-06 phase II trial (Leppä et al., 2025). The patients were young (aged 18-64 years), had clinically high-risk LBCL, and were treated with dose-intensified immunochemotherapy. The lowest ctDNA fractions detected were in the parts-per-million (ppm) range, and the median limit of detection was 1.69*10 -5, with 26% of the samples having a limit of detection in the ppm range.

结论（EHA原文）

Longitudinal plasma ctDNA detection during treatment and follow-up with duplex sequencing identifies refractory disease, predicts survival, determines therapy responses, and provides lead time before clinical progression. Overall, the results support incorporating molecular remission into LBCL response criteria to complement imaging and provide a dynamic molecular tool to guide clinical decision-making.

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is the most common aggressive non-Hodgkin lymphoma with marked clinical heterogeneity. Despite R-CHOP-improved survival, 30%-40% of patients have primary resistance or early relapse. TME imbalance drives progression; refined T/B subset correlations with DLBCL clinical features remain unclear, and IPI lacks immune parameters, making exploring immune subsets and developing tools for screening immune-related prognostic markers critical. Aims: This study aimed to characterize circulating T/B subsets in treatment-naive DLBCL, clarify their correlations with clinical features, and establish a \"clinical-immune\" prognostic model. Methods: One hundred and eleven treatment-naive DLBCL patients were enrolled and stratified by IPI risk, post-chemotherapy infection, and treatment response (CR/PD). Over 30 T/B lymphocyte subsets in peripheral blood were detected by multicolor flow cytometry. Group comparisons, univariate Logistic and multivariate COX analyses were performed to screen prognostic immune indicators. A prognostic nomogram integrating core immune markers and IPI score was established and validated by ROC, calibration curves and K-M analysis. P

结论（EHA原文）

This study examined the relationship between immune subsets and clinical outcomes in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma. High IPI risk was associated with higher DNB I but lower CD4+/CD8+ ratio, helper-inducer T cells, naive CD8+ T cells, DNB II and transitional B cells, accompanied by a higher relapse rate. These immune markers were negatively correlated with high IPI risk. Patients with post-chemotherapy infection showed increased effector memory CD4+/CD8+ T cells and decreased naive and central memory CD4+ T cells; infection was an independent poor prognostic factor. CR patients had higher naive CD8+ and cytotoxic T cells, while PD patients had higher DNB and Tph levels. We established a prognostic nomogram combining five immune indicators and IPI score, which showed satisfactory predictive efficacy with good calibration, well-stratified PFS and a C-index of 0.805.

弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤中cd20阳性细胞外囊泡充当抗原诱饵并降低利妥昔单抗活性

cd20-positive extracellular vesicles act as antigen decoys and reduce rituximab activity in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=116

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：利妥昔单抗；靶点：CD20；类别：单特异性抗体

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

在训练队列（n=26）中，高CD20阳性大EV组患者疾病特异性生存（DSS）和总生存（OS）显著更差；在验证队列（n=90）中，高CD20阳性大EV水平与更多疾病进展、更差的DSS和OS显著相关；多因素调整后CD20阳性大EV仍是独立预后因素。功能实验显示患者来源的CD20阳性大EV增强肿瘤细胞增殖、减弱利妥昔单抗介导的生长抑制和细胞毒性。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Loss or downregulation of CD20 has been considered a major mechanism of resistance to rituximab, an anti-CD20 monoclonal antibody in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). However, tumor-derived extracellular vesicles (EVs) may also contribute to antibody resistance. EVs are operationally categorized by size into small EVs ( 200 nm). Because large EVs are shed directly from the plasma membrane, tumor-derived large EVs circulating in the bloodstream may reflect tumor burden and contribute to treatment resistance. Given that CD20 is abundantly expressed on DLBCL cells, tumor-derived CD20-positive large EVs may act as antigen sinks for rituximab and thereby reduce effective antibody exposure to malignant B cells. We therefore hypothesized that circulating CD20-positive large EVs attenuate rituximab activity and predict treatment outcomes. Accordingly, we investigated the association between circulating CD20-positive large EVs and clinical outcomes in newly diagnosed DLBCL patients treated with R-CHOP. Aims: The aim of this study was to evaluate the prognostic impact of circulating CD20-positive large EVs in newly diagnosed DLBCL patients treated with standard R-CHOP therapy in routine clinical practice. Methods: CD20-positive large and small EVs were isolated from archived serum samples of patients with DLBCL and from supernatants of cultured primary tumor cells. The training cohort consisted of 26 patients selected from our second prospective cohort study (2012–2017). Patients were dichotomized into high and low groups according to the median levels of CD20-positive large EVs and small EVs. The prognostic value of circulating EVs was evaluated in an independent validation cohort with long-term clinical follow-up from our first prospective cohort study (n = 90, 2008–2011).

结论（EHA原文）

CD20-positive large EVs act as decoys that neutralize rituximab and suppress immune cytotoxicity, promoting resistance and immune evasion in DLBCL. Their serum levels may serve as a novel biomarker for predicting treatment response and prognosis.

中文结果摘录（原表）

055DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL化疗/免疫化疗PS2125

连续扩散，而非血行扩散：原发性经鼻dlbcl-94例患者中枢神经系统风险和治疗强度的再思考

contiguous spread, not hematogenous dissemination: rethinking cns risk and treatment intensity in primary sinonasal dlbcl—a 94-patient real-world evidence study

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=94；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：R-CHOP方案；试验组2：da-R-EPOCH方案；试验组3：Pola-R-CHP方案

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：R-CHOP方案；试验组2：da-R-EPOCH方案；试验组3：Pola-R-CHP方案

O 结局指标

5年无进展生存率（PFS）: 67.0% 5年总生存率（OS）: 73.1% 基线CNS受累: 9.6% CNS进展率: 3.2% ≥3级中性粒细胞减少: 83.0%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary sinonasal diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (PSN-DLBCL) is an exceptionally rare extranodal lymphoma (incidence ~1 per million) with undefined optimal management. Critical uncertainties persist regarding treatment intensity and central nervous system (CNS) prophylaxis necessity. Notably, CNS involvement at diagnosis appears more frequent than in nodal DLBCL, yet the mechanism—hematogenous versus direct extension—and appropriate prophylactic strategy remain uncharacterized. Aims: We conducted this large single-center retrospective study to delineate clinical features, CNS risk patterns, and real-world treatment outcomes. Methods: We enrolled 94 treatment-naïve PSN-DLBCL patients diagnosed at Beijing Tongren Hospital (2009–2024). CNS involvement required positive CSF flow cytometry or parenchymal brain lesions. Extensive local invasion (ELI) was defined as tumor extension beyond sinonasal bony confines into ≥2 adjacent structures. Treatment regimens included R-CHOP (60.6%), da-R-EPOCH (25.5%), and Pola-R-CHP (6.4%). CNS-directed strategies comprised intrathecal chemotherapy (52.1%), high-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX, 21.3%), or both.

结论（EHA原文）

This study provides substantive real-world evidence that PSN-DLBCL achieves excellent outcomes with standard R-CHOP immunochemotherapy, without incremental benefit from intensified regimens. The dissociation between relatively common baseline CNS involvement (9.6%) and rare CNS relapse (3.2%) suggests contiguous anatomical extension—via skull base erosion and cranial foramina—rather than hematogenous dissemination as the predominant mechanism. This pathophysiological insight carries direct therapeutic implications: intrathecal chemotherapy, which achieves limited parenchymal penetration, should not substitute for systemic HD-MTX when CNS-directed therapy is indicated. The favorable prognosis of ELI challenges conventional assumptions about local aggression. These findings support de-escalation strategies for most patients while highlighting the need for prospective studies to refine risk-adapted CNS prophylaxis in this rare extranodal subtype.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) is a biologically and clinically heterogeneous disease, with many patients relapsing despite standard immunochemotherapy such as R-CHOP. Prognosis relies on the IPI and biological markers (e.g., GCB/ABC subtype and MYC/BCL2 expression), but new non-invasive biomarkers are needed. MicroRNAs (miRNAs) are small (~22-nucleotide) regulatory molecules that modulate gene expression at the post-transcriptional level and circulating miRNAs have been proposed as potential diagnostic and prognostic biomarkers in LBCL. Aims: The aim of this study was to evaluate serum expression levels of miR-155-3p, miR-142-3p, and miR-22-3p at diagnosis and to investigate their associations with clinicopathological parameters, progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS). Methods: Serum samples were prospectively collected and analyzed from 45 newly diagnosed LBCL patients (age range 34–84 years; 26 males) treated at our center over a 4.5-year period, along with 26 healthy controls. All patients received immunochemotherapy. RNA isolation was performed using the miRNeasy Serum/Plasma Kit, and cDNA synthesis using the TaqMan Advanced miRNA cDNA Synthesis Kit (Applied Biosystems). Quantitative RT-PCR was conducted on a LightCycler 480 platform using TaqMan™ Advanced miRNA assays for miR-155-3p, miR-142-3p, and miR-22-3p. Exogenous spike-in Ath-miR-159 from Arabidopsis thaliana was used for normalization, and all samples were analyzed in duplicate. The 25th and 75th percentiles of controls were used as cutoffs for low and high expression. ROC curve analysis assessed the diagnostic accuracy of miRNAs. Statistical analyses included Mann–Whitney U and χ² tests, Kaplan–Meier survival analysis with log-rank testing, and multivariable Cox proportional hazards modeling for variables with p

结论（EHA原文）

Elevated serum miR-22-3p is characteristic of LBCL but not linked to OS, while high miR-155-3p and low miR-142-3p are independent adverse prognostic factors, supporting their potential as circulating risk-stratification biomarkers. These preliminary findings require validation in larger multicenter studies and further exploration of their integration into existing prognostic models.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is genetically and clinically heterogeneous. Epstein–Barr virus (EBV)–positive DLBCL accounts for ~8% of cases and is associated with inferior outcomes. Selinexor, an oral selective inhibitor of nuclear export (XPO1), has demonstrated activity in non-Hodgkin lymphoma and showed encouraging efficacy when combined with R-CHOP in early-phase clinical studies. This multicenter, single-arm phase Ib/II study (NCT05577364) aimed to assess the efficacy and safety of selinexor plus R-CHOP as frontline therapy in patients with EBV-positive DLBCL. Aims: To evaluate the safety and effectiveness of selinexor in combination with R-CHOP as first-line treatment in patients with EBV-positive DLBCL. Methods: Eligible patients were aged 18–80 years with pathologically confirmed DLBCL and EBV positivity defined by EBER in situ hybridization. Previously untreated patients with EBV-positive DLBCL received standard-dose R-CHOP every 21 days for up to six cycles, with selinexor initiated from cycle 2. The phase Ib portion followed a standard 3+3 dose-escalation design: selinexor was administered at an initial dose of 40 mg once weekly during cycle 2 and increased to 60 mg once weekly from cycle 3 onward in the absence of dose-limiting toxicities (DLTs). Following induction, patients received two consolidation cycles of rituximab plus selinexor. Patients achieving complete response (CR) after induction therapy proceeded to selinexor maintenance, with the overall treatment duration up to 2 years. Primary endpoints were the maximum tolerated dose (MTD) and recommended phase II dose (RP2D) for phase Ib, and the CR rate for phase II.

结论（EHA原文）

Frontline selinexor plus R-CHOP showed promising antitumor activity with a manageable safety profile in patients with EBV-positive DLBCL. Continued monitoring and optimized management of selinexor-related toxicities are warranted, and patient enrollment is ongoing to further validate these findings.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The germinal center B-cell-like (GCB) subtype is the most common molecular classification of diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). Approximately 30% of patients with GCB-DLBCL show resistance to R-CHOP therapy. An International Prognostic Index (IPI) score of 3-5 is recognized as one of the high-risk factors in patients with DLBCL. Current therapeutic strategies for high-risk GCB-DLBCL remain insufficiently defined , underscoring a critical unmet need in first-line treatment approaches. Selinexor, an oral selective inhibitor of nuclear export (SINE), targets exportin 1 (XPO1), leading to nuclear retention and reactivation of tumor suppressor proteins. In a real-world study involving 17 patients, Selinexor in combination with R-CHOP has shown promising results in treating high-risk GCB DLBCL. Aims: This phase II trial (NCT05422066) aims to evaluate the efficacy and safety of selinexor in combination with the R-CHOP regimen as a first-line treatment for patients with high-risk (IPI 3-5) GCB-DLBCL. Methods: P atients n ewly diagnosed with untreated GCB-DLBCL (IPI 3-5) were enrolled in this study. P atients will be treated with six cyclesof R-CHOP and selinexor (60 mg qw), with each cycle lasting three weeks . Treatment continue d for six cycles, or until intolerability, inadequate response, disease progression, consent withdrawal or death . Efficacy was evaluated according to the Lugano 2014 criteria. The primary endpoint was the complete response (CR) rate, and the secondary endpoints included the objective response rate (ORR), progression-free survival (PFS), disease-free survival (DFS), overall survival (OS), as well as safety and tolerability.

结论（EHA原文）

The combination of selinexor with the R-CHOP as a first-line treatment for high-risk (IPI 3-5) GCB-DLBCL demonstrates encouraging efficacy and and a manageable safety profile.

Background: Central nervous system involvement (CNSi) is a rare but often fatal event in systemic diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) patients. Circulating tumor DNA from cerebrospinal fluid (CSF-ctDNA) has played an important part in the application of liquid biopsy in CNS cancers. Nevertheless, larger-scale studies are needed to further characterize the mutational landscape of CSF-ctDNA and validate its clinical relevance in newly diagnosed (ND) DLBCL (ND-DLBCL). Aims: To thoroughly profile the mutational landscape of CSF-ctDNA and to explore its clinical significance in a large ND-DLBCL cohort. Methods: Between December, 2021 and January, 2026, 410 ND-DLBCL patients treated in our center were enrolled in the cohort. Baseline CSF, tissue and plasma samples were sequenced using a 475-gene lymphoma-specific panel. All patients were treated with R-CHOP or Pola-R-CHP regimen. Patients were identiﬁed as CSF-ctDNA positive (CSF(+)) based on two criteria: (1) at least one mutant variant detected in CSF-ctDNA was shared with tissue; (2) at least one mutant variant detected in CSF-ctDNA was canonical driver mutation in DLBCL ( Figure 1A ).

结论（EHA原文）

To conclude, in this large-scale cohort, we comprehensively depicted the mutational landscape of CSF-ctDNA, explored the biological characteristics of CSF(+) patients, and highlighted the importance of CSF-ctDNA in predicting clinical outcome and CNS relapse in ND-DLBCL patients.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Of the 410 ND-DLBCL patients, 98 (23.9%) were identified as CSF(+), among which 63 (64.3%) fulfilled both criteria, while 17 (17.3%) only met criterion 1 and 18 (18.4%) only met criterion 2 ( Figure 1B ). Among the 80 CSF(+) patients with matched tissue, plasma and CSF samples, the top 10 frequently mutated genes were MYD88 (35.8%), PIM1 (34.6%), CD79B (28.8%), KMT2D (24.2%), BTG2 (23.3%), TP53 (23.3%), H1-4 (23.3%), BTG1 (22.1%), BCL6 (20.8%) and ETV6 (19.6%) ( Figure 1C ). The mean variant allele frequency was significantly lower in CSF than in tissue and plasma samples ( Figure 1D ). As to genetic subtypes, CSF(+) patients were mostly distributed in MCD (N=37), Other (N=29), ST2 (N=10), BN2 (N=8) and TP53-disrupted subtypes (N=7), while TP53-disrupted (36.8%) and MCD (34.3%) subtypes showed highest CSF(+) ratio ( Figure 1E ). However, no difference in CSF-ctDNA burden was observed across genetic subtypes ( Figure 1F ). Furthermore, CSF(+) patients exhibited higher plasma ctDNA burden ( Figure 1G ). Patients with MCD subtype, non-GCB orign, specific extranodal sites involvement (reproductive system, kidney/adrenal gland, bone marrow) and higher IPI score were correlated with higher CSF(+) rate, while gastrointestinal tract involvement seemed negatively associated with CSF(+) ( Figure 1H ). In plasma samples, MYD88, CD79B, ETV6, IGLL5, CDKN2A, CARD11, CD274 mutations were associated with higher CSF(+) rate ( Figure 1I ), while in tissue samples, CARD11, PRDM1, MCL1 mutations seemed correlated with higher CSF(+) rate ( Figure 1J ). In RNA level, the dysregulated genes of CSF(+) patients were enriched in cytokine-cytokine receptor interaction, focal adhesion, cytoskeleton, and PI3K-AKT signaling pathways, potentially promoting CNSi in ND-DLBCL ( Figure 1K ). Moreover, CSF(+) significantly correlated with inferior response to initial treatment and worse survival in ND-DLBCL patients ( Figure 1L-1N ). Besides, CSF-ctDNA(+) demonstrated superior prediction capability for CNS relapse compared with high-risk CNS-IPI in ND-DLBCL ( Figure 1O ). Conclusion: To conclude, in this large-scale cohort, we comprehensively depicted the mutational landscape of CSF-ctDNA, explored the biological characteristics of CSF(+) patients, and highlighted the importance of CSF-ctDNA in predicting clinical outcome and CNS relapse in ND-DLBCL patients.

060DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL化疗/免疫化疗PF993

r-gemox+nivolumab vs r-gemox as 2nd-line therapy for large b-cell lymphoma in transplant-ineligible patients: final analysis of the niveau trial, a phase 3 study of the agmt, gla, hovon, lysa and plrg

P 患者群体

B细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤；弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=267；治疗线数/场景：二线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：纳武利尤单抗；靶点：PD-1；类别：单特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：R-GEMOX（利妥昔单抗、吉西他滨、奥沙利铂）；试验组2：R-GEMOX + 纳武利尤单抗，随后纳武利尤单抗维持治疗（最多1年）

1年无进展生存期（PFS）：试验组A 27% vs 试验组B 23%，p=0.686 1年无事件生存期（EFS）：试验组A 22% vs 试验组B 22%，p=0.897 1年总生存期（OS）：试验组A 51% vs 试验组B 58%，p=0.884 2年PFS：19% vs 18% 2年EFS：17% vs 17% 2年OS：39% vs 42% 客观缓解率（OR）：37% vs 34% 完全缓解率（CR）：22% vs 22% 疾病进展率（PD）：53% vs 45% 3-5级不良事件：胃肠道4% vs 8%；肝胆系统19% vs 23% 治疗相关死亡：6例(4%) vs 12例(9%)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Patients (pts) with relapsed or refractory ( R / R ) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) after first-line treatment, who are ineligible for high-dose chemotherapy (HDCT) and hematopoietic stem cell transplantation (HSCT) have poor outcomes. Rituximab, gemcitabine and oxaliplatin (R-GemOx) is a common regimen used in this setting. Aims: The objective of the open-label, randomized, phase 3 NIVEAU study (NCT03366272) was to evaluate efficacy and safety of Nivolumab added to R-GemOx. Methods: Adult pts with R/R LBCL after 1st-line therapy and not eligible for HDCT/HSCT based on of one of the following criteria: age ≥65 years; age ≥18 years and Hematopoietic Cell Transplantation-specific Comorbidity Index (HCT-CI) score ≥3; or age ≥18 years and prior ASCT (as 1st-line consolidation). Therapy consisted 8 cycles R-GemOx (arm A) or 8 cycles of R-GemOx + nivolumab followed by nivolumab as maintenance for a maximum of 1 year or until progression or unacceptable toxicity (arm B). Primary endpoint was progression-free survival (PFS) after 1 year. Major secondary endpoints were response rates, event-free-survival (EFS) (defined as progression, relapse, death or unplanned lymphoma treatment), overall survival (OS) and toxicity. \n Recruitment was stopped in March 2023, because a planned interim analysis revealed futility to demonstrate superiority for the primary endpoint. However, a trend for a better OS was observed in arm B ( Blood (2023)142(Suppl. 1):435). In total, 270 of 310 initially intended pts have been recruited. Here, we present the final analysis of the NIVEAU trial after a median follow-up of 42 months.

结论（EHA原文）

In pts with R/R LBCL, the addition of nivolumab to R-GemOx followed by nivolumab maintenance is feasible without relevant additive toxicity. The addition of Nivolumab did not improve PFS, EFS nor OS. The trend towards improved survival observed in the interim analysis was not confirmed in the final analysis. These results demonstrate that addition of checkpoint inhibition to immunochemotherapy does not improve the outcome in these patients.

large-scale real-world clinical characteristics and efficacy of diffuse large b-cell lymphoma across distinct molecular subtypes: interim data from the believe study

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=3773

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：large-scale real-world clinical characteristics and efficacy of diffuse large b-cell lymphoma across distinct molecular subtypes: interim data from the believe study

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

总体客观缓解率（ORR）为81.3%；完全缓解率（CRR）为64.1%；R-CHOP联合靶向药物亚组ORR为88.4%，CRR为74.6%；BN2-like和N1-like亚型疗效较好，TP53Mut亚型疗效最差

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) shows extensive molecular heterogeneity. Molecular subtypes can be identified by LymphGen (MCD, BN2, N1, EZB, A53, ST2) and the simplified 38‑gene LymphPlex ( TP53 Mut , MCD‑like, BN2‑like, N1‑like, EZB‑like, ST2‑like). LymphPlex showed high concordance with LymphGen (Sig Transduct Target Ther 2023:8:145) . These subtypes differ greatly in clinical features, treatment response and prognosis, but large‑sample real‑world evidence to guide subtype‑tailored management is still limited. The BELIEVE study (NCT 06026488) is a large Chinese real‑world registry. Aims: To clarify clinical characteristics, treatment patterns and efficacy differences across DLBCL molecular subtypes, and to generate high‑quality real‑world evidence for personalized therapy. Methods: A total of 3773 DLBCL patients from 35 centers were enrolled. All patients were classified into seven molecular subtypes (BN2-like, EZB-like, MCD-like, N1-like, ST2-like, TP53 Mut and Others) by NGS. Baseline characteristics, treatment regimens and efficacy were collected. Endpoints included progression-free survival (PFS), complete response rate (CRR), objective response rate (ORR), and overall survival (OS). Herein, efficacy was analyzed across molecular subtypes and first-line regimens.

结论（EHA原文）

In Chinese DLBCL patients, the most prevalent LymphPlex subtypes are Others, MCD‑like and TP53 Mut subtypes, with marked efficacy heterogeneity. R‑CHOP plus target agents significantly improves CRR across multiple subtypes. These data support molecular subtype‑tailored personalized treatment for DLBCL. Updated survival and safety data will be presented.

062DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCNS穿透/放疗/MTX策略S249

大剂量甲氨蝶呤不能降低超高危大b细胞淋巴瘤中枢神经系统复发的风险：1923例患者的国际回顾性分析

high-dose methotrexate does not reduce risk of cns relapse in ultra high-risk large b-cell lymphoma: an international retrospective analysis of 1,923 patients

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=1923；疾病阶段：高危

I 干预措施

分组：未接受HDMTX组（no HDMTX）；接受HDMTX组（HDMTX）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：未接受HDMTX组（no HDMTX）；接受HDMTX组（HDMTX）

O 结局指标

所有超高危患者3年CNS复发率：未接受HDMTX组 vs 接受HDMTX组 = 9.3% vs 8.1%，调整后HR 1.10 (95%CI 0.80-1.53) 孤立性CNS复发率：5.9% vs 5.7%，调整后HR 1.01 (95% CI 0.68-1.50) 6个月地标分析（n=1529）：3年OS：79.7% vs 83.8%；3年CNS复发率：6.7% vs 6.6%，调整后HR 0.89 (95%CI 0.58-1.35) 睾丸受累亚组：任何CNS复发率9.4% vs 6.8%，HR 1.54 (95%CI 0.78-3.03)；孤立性CNS复发6.1% vs 6.3%，HR 1.08 (95%CI 0.51-2.31)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The role of high-dose methotrexate (HDMTX) as CNS prophylaxis in high-risk large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) remains controversial. There are no large prospective RCTs supporting its use. Two recent retrospective studies suggested minimal impact on CNS relapse (CNSr). However, guidelines continue to recommend consideration of HDMTX in pts with ‘ultra high-risk’ (UHR) features due to a lack of robust data in these subgroups, where CNSr risk is 10-25%. Aims: To analyse the impact of HDMTX on LBCL pts considered UHR for CNSr. Methods: This multicentre, retrospective analysis combined data from 56 sites who contributed to the aforementioned studies ( Wilson et al, Blood 2022; Lewis et al, JCO 2023 ). All pts received curative intent chemo-immunotherapy. Wilson et al recruited LBCL pts who had received HDMTX, regardless of risk. Lewis et al recruited pts with ≥1 of these high-risk criteria: CNS-IPI 4-6; high grade B-cell lymphoma with MYC+BCL2+/-BCL6 rearrangements; testicular/breast/renal/adrenal extranodal (EN) involvement. \n For this analysis, pts were deemed UHR if they met ≥1 of the following: CNS-IPI 5-6; testicular, renal/adrenal or breast involvement; ≥3 EN sites. Time to CNSr was measured from diagnosis (or landmark) until first event (CNSr) or competing event (systemic relapse, stable disease at EOT or death); pts not experiencing an event were censored at last follow up. Groups were compared using competing risks survival analysis (Fine and Grey). Time to isolated CNSr was also analysed with synchronous events included as competing risks. A landmark analysis (LMA) was performed for all pts who had no event at 6 months.

结论（EHA原文）

This is the largest international comparative dataset of UHR LBCL pts treated with or without HDMTX prophylaxis, showing no significant reduction in CNSr with HDMTX in all UHR pts or in any individual high-risk subgroup. Despite inherent limitations, the data suggest HDMTX prophylaxis has no benefit and future studies should focus on alternative approaches to reduce risk in UHR pts.

综合血浆ctdna基因组分析对侵袭性dlbcl的诊断潜力评估

evaluating the diagnostic potential of comprehensive plasma ctdna genomic profiling in aggressive dlbcl

O 结局指标

1. 在56例DLBCL患者中，40例（71.4%）检测到体细胞变异，被定义为ctDNA阳性。 2. ctDNA阳性病例中共鉴定出972个体细胞变异，中位数为每个患者12个变异（IQR: 6-20），中位变异等位基因频率（VAF）为3%。 3.
