摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Genetic profiling for patient risk stratification is routinely performed on tumor tissue biopsies that are invasive, carry procedural risks and are limited in capturing spatial tumor heterogeneity. Analyzing circulating cell-free tumor DNA (ctDNA) from liquid biopsies such as plasma offers a promising, non-invasive approach for detecting somatic aberrations, potentially also from spatially distal lesions. Aims: This ongoing study aims to assess the diagnostic performance of plasma-based comprehensive genomic profiling in aggressive diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) and evaluate the concordance with paired paraffin-embedded tumor tissue biopsies. Methods: A total of 56 patients with DLBCL diagnosed at Karolinska University Hospital and enrolled in the ongoing prospective BioLymph study (ISRCTN12948913) (PMID: 37415362) were included, of whom 25 (44.6%) presented with advanced stage disease (IIE-IV). Routine genetic profiling of diagnostic tissue biopsies was conducted by targeted sequencing using Genomic Medicine Sweden Lymphoid Gene Panel (GMS-LGP) (Twist Bioscience, CA, US) according to the BioLymph protocol. Pre-treatment plasma ctDNA samples and matched germline DNA from peripheral blood, along with plasma samples from healthy individuals (n=6) were sequenced using GMS-LGP, incorporating unique molecular indices. Libraries were sequenced at a depth of 100 million read pairs on NovaSeq X (Illumina, CA, US) and unique duplex consensus reads were employed for somatic variant calling using BALSAMIC pipeline.

结论（EHA原文）

Our results so far demonstrate expected biological and technical contrasts between tissue and plasma sequencing for diagnostic profiling despite which the detection of overlapping variants across both biopsy types supports the utility of ctDNA as a complementary and minimally invasive tool for genomic profiling in DLBCL.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The median target coverage of unique duplex reads across patient ctDNA samples was 717X (interquartile range (IQR): 623-798X), with >88% of targets achieving ≥250X coverage. Somatic variants were detected in 40/56 patients (71.4%), classifying them as ctDNA positive (ctDNA+). Across ctDNA+ cases, 972 somatic variants were identified with a median of 12 variants per patient (IQR: 6-20) and a median variant allele fraction (VAF) of 3%. Stage I cases were significantly associated with ctDNA negativity (8/16 vs. 8/32 in stages II–IV; Fisher’s exact P= 0.047). \n In matching tissue biopsies, somatic variants were detected in 54/56 patients (96.4%) with median 15.5 variants per patient (IQR: 10-27) and median VAF of 23.6% (IQR: 12.7-36.4%). Concordance analysis in 38 ctDNA+ patients with variants detected in paired tissue biopsies a median Jaccard Index of 0.62 (IQR: 0.24-0.76). Shared variants exhibited significantly higher median VAFs in paraffin-embedded tissue compared with plasma (18.6% vs. 3.2%; Wilcoxon signed-rank test, P Conclusion: Our results so far demonstrate expected biological and technical contrasts between tissue and plasma sequencing for diagnostic profiling despite which the detection of overlapping variants across both biopsy types supports the utility of ctDNA as a complementary and minimally invasive tool for genomic profiling in DLBCL.

ctdna sequencing reveals mutational signatures with prognostic relevance in lbcl patients

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：ctdna sequencing reveals mutational signatures with prognostic relevance in lbcl patients

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Despite recent advances in treatment strategies, patients with relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) are at high risk of further relapses and death. Accordingly, the development of novel biomarkers and the identification of patients who might benefit from alternative treatment strategies remain important unmet medical needs. Circulating tumor (ct)DNA sequencing has emerged as a reliable tool for genotyping and response assessment in patients with LBCL. Its prognostic value could be further enhanced by integrating mutational signatures that reveal the underlying biological processes. Aims: The aim of this study is to extract and characterize single base substitution (SBS) mutational signatures from ctDNA in patients with LBCL, to identify distinct patterns and to assess their impact on progression free survival (PFS). Methods: We applied our previously published ctDNA sequencing approach (Sobesky et al., 2021; Heger et al., 2024) to 124 blood samples obtained from 88 patients with R/R LBCL across multiple treatment lines. All samples were obtained prior to treatment initiation and constituted the discovery cohort. Mutational signature analysis was performed with a customized pipeline developed around SigProfiler (Díaz-Gay et al., 2023). The prognostic impact of identified mutational signature subgroups was validated in two independent cohorts of patients with previously untreated LBCL from the Nordic phase II LBC-06 (n = 123; Leppä et al., 2025) and LBC-05 (n = 99; Leppä et al., 2020) trials.

结论（EHA原文）

ctDNA sequencing enables robust and reproducible identification of distinct mutational signature patterns, independent of technical workflows and targeted gene panel designs. Classification based on these signatures delineates two distinct subgroups that are reproducible and independently associated with PFS. Overall, incorporating the biological context of mutations could further enhance the prognostic power of ctDNA profiling, enabling earlier and more precise identification of patients at high risk for progressive disease.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: We identified four distinct mutational signatures: SBS1 and SBS5 both indicative of age, SBS39 of unknown etiology, and SBS84 induced by cytidine deaminase (AID) activity. Unsupervised k-means clustering of mutational signature profiles revealed two distinct molecular subgroups. Classification based on these signatures delineates two distinct subgroups that are reproducible and independently associated with PFS. Overall, incorporating the biological context of mutations could further enhance the prognostic power of ctDNA profiling, enabling earlier and more precise identification of patients at high risk for progressive disease.

065DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL其他/未明确药物PS2122

血浆铜作为弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤的预后标志物

plasma copper as prognostic biomarker in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=600

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：plasma copper as prognostic biomarker in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

中位无进展生存期：高铜组467天，低铜组3295天，P<0.001|||中位总生存期：高铜组1156天，低铜组4323天，P<0.001|||3年无进展生存率：高铜组47.4%，低铜组72.2%|||3年总生存率：高铜组65.8%，低铜组86.4%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) exhibits significant clinical heterogeneity, necessitating improved prognostic biomarkers beyond conventional risk stratification systems.Recent research highlights cuproptosis, a novel form of regulated cell death triggered by abnormal intracellular copper accumulation affecting mitochondrial function, as a promising target in cancer therapy. Its susceptibility depends on tumor metabolism and microenvironmental factors, including inflammatory signals. In DLBCL, cuproptosis-related genes and copper transporters influence prognosis and treatment response, but the role of systemic plasma copper levels remains unclear. This research aims to establish plasma copper as a prognostic biomarker and inform therapeutic strategies targeting cuproptosis and copper homeostasis to improve patient outcomes. Aims: This study aims to evaluate plasma copper levels as a prognostic biomarker in DLBCL. By integrating published genetic datasets and our patiients' cytokine profiling, it seeks to enhance understanding of copper’s role in lymphoma progression and guide novel therapeutic strategies. Methods: We analyzed 600 newly diagnosed DLBCL patients divided into training (n=360) and validation (n=240) cohorts. plasma copper levels were evaluated alongside comprehensive clinical, molecular, and inflammatory parameters. Copper chelator-related genes were systematically identified through bioinformatic analysis, with meta-analysis performed across six independent cohorts.

结论（EHA原文）

Plasma copper represents a novel, independent prognostic biomarker in DLBCL that captures unique disease biology through its association with inflammatory signaling. Integration of copper assessment into clinical practice could guide personalized treatment strategies in DLBCL.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Elevated plasma copper levels independently predicted inferior survival outcomes in both cohorts. High copper patients demonstrated dramatically shorter median PFS (467 vs 3,295 days, P Conclusion: Plasma copper represents a novel, independent prognostic biomarker in DLBCL that captures unique disease biology through its association with inflammatory signaling. Integration of copper assessment into clinical practice could guide personalized treatment strategies in DLBCL.

age-independent outcomes and competing risk dynamics in relapsed/refractory lbcl: a real-world analysis

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=401；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：age-independent outcomes and competing risk dynamics in relapsed/refractory lbcl: a real-world analysis

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

中位OS：≥70岁组24个月 vs <70岁组91个月，p=0.008 中位PFS：7个月 vs 8个月，p=0.068 2年淋巴瘤相关死亡率：37% vs 31%，p=0.4 2年非淋巴瘤死亡率：13% vs 7.3%，p=0.1 多变量分析中年龄与淋巴瘤相关死亡无关（HR 0.67, 95%CI 0.31-1.43, p=0.3） 接受ASCT患者2年OS：53% vs 73%，p=0.15

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: In relapsed/refractory large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL), age is a standard surrogate for “fitness for curative therapy”. However, the degree to which age-related survival differences reflect competing risk dynamics—specifically disease relapse/progression (R/PD), lymphoma-related and non-lymphoma related death —versus treatment selection remains unclear. Aims: We aimed to characterize this relationship by investigating if age independently influences the trajectory of R/R LBCL outcomes through an analysis of causes of mortality in a large real-world cohort. Methods: We performed a retrospective analysis of patients (pts) with R/R LBCL treated at Princess Margaret between 2017-2024. Pts were stratified by age ( progression-free survival (PFS), competing risk estimates of lymphoma-related vs. non-lymphoma-related death, and non-relapse mortality (NRM) defined as time from first R/PD to death without secondary R/PD, and overall survival (OS) post-autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT).

结论（EHA原文）

Factors influencing competing risk dynamics for R/R LBCL pts include disease, treatment toxicity, and comorbidities. In our cohort, lymphoma remains the primary cause of death regardless of age. Results were similar in lymphoma-related or non-lymphoma mortality between age groups; however, results may be influenced by sample size. While non-lymphoma related mortality and NRM appear numerically higher in Older, these results do not appear prohibitive - PFS outcomes also look inferior. Prospective controlled data are needed to better define the benefit of 2L curative approaches in older LBCL.

单核细胞cfdna谱的动态变化可识别大b细胞淋巴瘤的高危患者

dynamic changes in mononucleosomal cfdna profiles identify high-risk patients with large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=123；疾病阶段：高危

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：dynamic changes in mononucleosomal cfdna profiles identify high-risk patients with large b-cell lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

FSR分类与无进展生存期显著相关（p=0.00023）|||FSR分类与总生存期显著相关（p<0.0001）|||SFF从基线到治疗结束时下降>16%或增加>12.3%与较差生存相关

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) represents a heterogeneous group of aggressive lymphoid malignancies with diverse molecular features and clinical outcomes. Approximately 30% of patients develop relapsed or refractory disease. Current diagnostic approaches rely on invasive tissue biopsy, which captures only a single tumor site and time point, and thus fail to capture the full heterogeneity of the disease. Liquid biopsy approaches based on circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) allow non-invasive disease monitoring but require ultra-sensitive sequencing to detect tumor-derived fragments among abundant cell-free DNA (cfDNA). Length distribution of cfDNA, reflecting the underlying chromatin architecture and fragmentation biology, is non-random, typically peaking at ~166 base pairs (bp). Tumor-derived DNA fragment distributions tend to be enriched with shorter fragments, suggesting that cfDNA fragment length profiles may provide additional biologically and clinically relevant information for cancer care. Aims: The aim of the study was to investigate whether cfDNA fragment length profiles and their temporal changes during therapy are associated with clinical outcomes in high-risk LBCL patients. Methods: Plasma samples from 123 high-risk LBCL patients enrolled in the Nordic Lymphoma Group LBC-06 trial were collected before treatment (BL), during therapy, at end-of-treatment (EOT), and during follow-up. cfDNA was sequenced using a targeted ~750 kb panel. Analyses of fragment length distributions were performed in R environment. Fragment counts were Z-standardized to enable profile shape comparisons across timepoints. The short fragment fraction (SFF) was defined as the proportion of fragments +12.3%) in SFF.

结论（EHA原文）

The proposed fragmentome shift risk (FSR) metric may represent a novel non-invasive biomarker for outcome prediction. Integration of cfDNA fragmentomics with ctDNA mutation profiling and minimal residual disease assessment could improve disease monitoring and risk stratification in LBCL. Independent validation in additional cohorts is needed. Further insight into differences in fragmentation could be provided by studying the end-motif enrichment across distinct fragment lengths.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Fragment length profiles showed marked inter-patient heterogeneity and dynamic changes during treatment. Both large decreases and increases in SFF between baseline and EOT were associated with inferior survival. Patients classified as FSR had significantly worse progression-free survival (PFS) (p=0.00023) and overall survival (OS) (p Conclusion: The proposed fragmentome shift risk (FSR) metric may represent a novel non-invasive biomarker for outcome prediction. Integration of cfDNA fragmentomics with ctDNA mutation profiling and minimal residual disease assessment could improve disease monitoring and risk stratification in LBCL. Independent validation in additional cohorts is needed. Further insight into differences in fragmentation could be provided by studying the end-motif enrichment across distinct fragment lengths.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse Large B Cell Lymphoma (DLBCL) is the most common lymphoma in the elderly, with variable response to immunochemotherapy. Several prognostic systems have been developed to guide treatment. In this setting, comprehensive geriatric assessment (CGA) enables risk stratification and correlates with outcomes, with nutritional status representing a key evaluated component.Albumin, Body Mass index (BMI) and Geriatric Nutritional Risk Index (GNRI) are indices that reflect nutritional status and have been variably employed across different disease settings to explore their prognostic significance.To date, few studies have investigated the prognostic potential of these parameters in the elderly population undergoing treatment for DLBCL. Aims: To evaluate the predictive value of albumin, BMI and GNRI on outcomes of patients aged > 65 years undergoing first-line therapy for DLBCL. Methods: This is an ancillary analysis of Elderly Project of the Fondazione Italiana Linfomi, a prospective multicenter observational study aimed at validating a simplified geriatric assessment tool and a new prognostic score, the EPI. In this study, we selected patients whose complete anthropometric and laboratory parameters were available at baseline.The primary endpoint was the correlation between serum albumin levels, BMI and GNRI and overall survival

结论（EHA原文）

In the current therapeutic landscape, treatment personalization requires accurate risk stratification. In elderly patients with DLBCL undergoing antineoplastic treatment, albumin, BMI and GNRI represent independent prognostic parameters for survival, which are simple and easily applicable

069DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL其他/未明确药物PF1113

早期出现增殖性cd8+t细胞与接受自体造血干细胞移植加脐带血输注治疗的r/r dlbcl患者预后改善有关

earlier emergence of proliferative cd8+ t cells is associated with improved prognosis in r/r dlbcl patients treated with auto-hsct plus umbilical cord blood infusion

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=24；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：自体造血干细胞移植+脐带血输注；对照组：单纯自体造血干细胞移植

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：自体造血干细胞移植+脐带血输注||对照组：单纯自体造血干细胞移植

O 结局指标

联合组中性粒细胞植入中位时间11天（范围10-21天），血小板植入中位时间14天（范围12-31天） 对照组中性粒细胞植入中位时间11天（范围10-19天），血小板植入中位时间12天（范围10-20天） 联合组增殖性CD8+ T细胞出现中位时间比对照组早4天（2-5天） 联合组干细胞样记忆CD8+ T细胞出现中位时间比对照组早9天（8-10天） 联合组总队列2年总生存率90.9%，2年无进展生存率86.3%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Autologous hematopoietic stem cell transplantation (Auto-HSCT) remains a potentially curative treatment for patients with relapsed/refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (R/R DLBCL); however, disease relapse still occurs in a subset of patients following transplantation. A critical vulnerability period exists after Auto-HSCT between the decline of chemotherapy-induced cytotoxic effects and the reconstitution of host antitumor immunity, creating a window for tumor recurrence. Human umbilical cord blood stem cells (hUCBSCs) represent a potential cellular source capable of mediating a graft-versus-tumor (GVT) effect. Based on this rationale, we conducted a clinical study evaluating a novel strategy combining Auto-HSCT with unrelated hUCBSC infusion in patients with R/R DLBCL. In our cohort of 44 patients, the 2-year overall survival (OS) and progression-free survival (PFS) rates were 90.9% and 86.3%, respectively. Although these outcomes compare favorably with historical data, the biological mechanisms by which Auto-HSCT combined with hUCBSC infusion may prevent relapse remain unclear. Aims: To investigate the immune mechanisms associated with improved survival in R/R DLBCL patients undergoing auto-HSCT plus unrelated hUCBSC infusion (the combined strategy). Methods: We enrolled 24 R/R DLBCL patients (14 relapsed and 10 refractory; median age 35 years). Among them, 12 patients underwent the combined strategy, and 12 patients received auto-HSCT strategy alone. Both strategy utilized the BEAM conditioning. The combined strategy protocol was conducted as follows: after conditioning, patients received Auto-HSCT followed by a single infusion of unrelated hUCBSCs on day +2. The unrelated hUCBSCs units must satisfy the requirement of HLA matching ≥ 5/10 loci and blood type-compatible units will be prioritized for selection. Unrelated hUCBSCs was infused as a single dose, with the total nucleated cell (TNC) count ranging from 5 - 15 × 10⁸ and CD34⁺ cell count from 1.5 - 3.5 × 10⁶. Peripheral blood samples were collected from patients on transplantation Day 0, Day 7, Day 21, and Day 28 for flow cytometric analysis and single-cell transcriptomic sequencing.

结论（EHA原文）

Infusion of unrelated hUCBSCs may compensate for the lack of a graft-versus-tumor (GVT) effect in Auto-HSCT. The GVT observed in the combined strategy appears to be associated with the earlier emergence of CD8⁺ Tprolif cells, CD8⁺ Tscm cells, and the accelerated activation of CD8⁺ T cells following unrelated hUCBSC infusion.

070DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL其他/未明确药物PF1106

阶段性变体揭示dlbcl原癌基因启动子高突变和cfdna断裂模式

phased variants reveal proto-oncogene promoter hypermutation and cfdna fragmentation patterns in dlbcl

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=116

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：phased variants reveal proto-oncogene promoter hypermutation and cfdna fragmentation patterns in dlbcl

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

LymphGen分类成功率：50.8%（FFPE），加入cfDNA后提升至62.9%；未分类病例中7/57重新分类为MCD，4/57重新分类为EZB；肿瘤组织样本中位PVs数111.5（范围17-286）；86/116例cfDNA中可召回PVs，中位召回率58.4%；PVs常见于IGK、IGHM、BCL6、BCL2、PIM1、MYC、BCL7A、CXCR4、TMSB4X基因，除MYC外多数影响5'UTR或启动子区；ctDNA片段化程度显著高于野生型DNA和总cfDNA；BCL2和MYC的PV召回率低与血液中低表达、淋巴细胞中高表达相关。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is a clinically and molecularly heterogeneous disease for which robust, widely applicable patient-stratification tools are still lacking. Analysis of circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) has emerged as a promising approach for disease monitoring, yet its utility for molecular characterization and stratification remains incompletely understood. Phased variants (PVs) – closely spaced somatic mutations occurring in cis – represent stable, region-specific genomic features that may provide additional insight into DLBCL biology and improve ctDNA-based stratification. Aims: Our goal was to characterise a nationwide real-world DLBCL cohort to improve our understanding of the disease’s molecular landscape and investigate the applicability of cfDNA for molecular profiling and patient stratification. Methods: In Hungarian oncohematological centres 138 newly diagnosed DLBCL patients were prospectively enrolled in liquid biopsy collection between 2021-2023, of which 116 had corresponding diagnostic FFPE samples available. We performed targeted next generation DNA sequencing using a hybrid-capture Agilent XT HS2 panel spanning 251 genes, 4 translocation breakpoints and genome-wide CNA calling using off-target reads on FFPE samples and a smaller, 98 gene panel for ctDNA profiling involving highly-mutated regions in >5% of lymphoma genomes (Kurtz et al., 2021) for phased variant identification. Variant calling and analysis were performed using a custom pipeline.

结论（EHA原文）

CfDNA has been shown to be a viable and robust tool to help patient care in several cancers. CtDNA carries potentially relevant information on the disease; in our case, LymphGen classification improved with the use of ctDNA variants and parallel analysis of ctDNA and tumor tissue DNA allocated cases to therapeutically relevant LymphGen subtypes. Aberrant hypermutation in proto-oncogene promoter sites have been described in DLBCL and utilised as PVs for disease monitoring. We demonstrated that regions with lower cfDNA fragmentation and higher cfDNA amounts have worse PV recall, highlighting caveats to improve further in the non-invasive genotyping of DLBCL.

中文结果摘录（原表）

LymphGen分类成功率：50.8%（FFPE），加入cfDNA后提升至62.9%；未分类病例中7/57重新分类为MCD，4/57重新分类为EZB；肿瘤组织样本中位PVs数111.5（范围17-286）；86/116例cfDNA中可召回PVs，中位召回率58.4%；PVs常见于IGK、IGHM、BCL6、BCL2、PIM1、MYC、BCL7A、CXCR4、TMSB4X基因，除MYC外多数影响5'UTR或启动子区；ctDNA片段化程度显著高于野生型DNA和总cfDNA；BCL2和MYC的PV召回率低与血液中低表达、淋巴细胞中高表达相关。

071DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBL其他/未明确药物PF1089

基于预处理ctdna的dlbcl风险预测：非面板独立拷贝数分析克服了批间阈值变异

pretreatment ctdna-based risk prediction in dlbcl: panel-independent copy-number analysis overcomes inter-assay threshold variability

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=184

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：pretreatment ctdna-based risk prediction in dlbcl: panel-independent copy-number analysis overcomes inter-assay threshold variability

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

基于CNA的肿瘤分数>0.1定义高风险，对TTP的HR为4.97 (95% CI 2.52-9.83, p<0.001)；对PFS的HR为3.02 (95% CI 1.56-5.85, p=0.001)。SNV-based方法预测风险但定量差异大。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), is the commonest aggressive non-Hodgkin lymphoma. A plethora of emerging novel therapeutic modalities creates exciting opportunities to intensify first-line therapy. Such escalation would ideally be reserved for patients at highest risk to avoid unnecessary additional toxicity to standard risk patients who already achieve excellent outcomes with conventional immunochemotherapy. Circulating tumour DNA (ctDNA) is a promising pre-treatment risk stratification tool; however, implementation is limited by poor standardisation and substantial inter-assay variability in ctDNA thresholds. Methods: We benchmarked pretreatment ctDNA-based risk prediction in 184 prospectively recruited patients receiving first-line therapy for LBCL. We compared the predictive performance of pretreatment ctDNA burden estimated using single-nucleotide variants (SNVs) identified by multiple variant-calling workflows, or genome-wide copy-number aberrations (CNAs) inferred using ichorCNA. Clinical outcomes were evaluated for time to tumour progression (TTP) and progression-free survival (PFS).

结论（EHA原文）

In conclusion, CNA-based estimation of ctDNA tumour fraction provides a technically robust, panel-independent approach to pretreatment risk stratification in LBCL. Application of this computationally simple approach facilitates harmonisation of risk prediction without the requirement for individual centres to standardise sequencing panels and variant calling pipelines.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: All SNV-based approaches predicted clinical risk, but absolute ctDNA quantification varied markedly. Even within the same cohort, thresholds defining high-risk disease required separate optimisation for each SNV calling strategy and differed by >10-fold. This variation arose partly from different detection limits for low-allele-fraction variants leading to substantial differences in average mutant allele fraction across different variant calling approaches (matched-germline, unmatched-germline and tumour-only strategies employing different variant calling tools). This variability presents a practical barrier to deploying SNV-based risk stratification across centres, sequencing pipelines and panel designs. \n As an alternative, we derived tumour fraction from genome-wide CNAs. Panel-based sequencing profiles including off-target reads were normalised to cfDNA from 51 healthy individuals. A tumour fraction >0.1 was identified as optimal to define high risk. In univariate analyses, CNA-based stratification strongly predicted TTP (HR 4.97, 95% CI 2.52–9.83, p \n We then assessed technical robustness to variables that typically differ across ctDNA platforms, including genomic regions analysed and reference panel size. Tumour fraction from panel-based sequencing showed strong concordance with low-pass whole-genome sequencing (Pearson’s r >0.9). Tumour fraction remained stable when chromosome arms were iteratively excluded to simulate alternative panel design, suggesting that risk prediction was driven by global tumour-burden signal rather than individual copy number aberrations. Quantification was also stable when at least 20 healthy cfDNA samples were used as reference. Conclusion: In conclusion, CNA-based estimation of ctDNA tumour fraction provides a technically robust, panel-independent approach to pretreatment risk stratification in LBCL. Application of this computationally simple approach facilitates harmonisation of risk prediction without the requirement for individual centres to standardise sequencing panels and variant calling pipelines.

肠道微生物多样性：新诊断患者显著降低（更少的独有基因，受损的稳定性）|||核心菌群失调：新诊断患者拟杆菌门相对丰度升高（46.3%），厚壁菌门及其衍生分类群减少（Clostridia, Clostridiales, Lachnospiraceae, Eubacteriaceae）|||有益产短链脂肪酸菌属（Blautia, Roseburia, Ruminococcus）减少，厚壁菌门/拟杆菌门比值降低——这些在完全缓解后恢复|||代谢通路：新诊断患者中功能K06147（细菌ATP结合盒B亚家族）降低，功能K03088（RNA聚合酶sigma-70因子ECF亚家族）和K21572（淀粉结合外膜蛋白SusD/RagB家族）升高

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is the most common type of non-Hodgkin lymphoma. Despite numerous studies focusing on its genomic characteristics and molecular pathogenesis, systematic elucidation of the dynamic changes of gut microbiota during the course of DLBCL remains scarce. Aims: This study aims to investigate the dynamic changes of gut microbiome-metabolome in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma. Methods: This study compared fecal gut microbiota samples from 9 patients with DLBCL at initial diagnosis, samples from these patients after achieving complete remission (CR) through standard first-line chemotherapy, and samples from their healthy cohabitants living in the same environment as the patients. Differences in microbial composition and metabolic pathways among the 3 groups were investigated through metagenomic and metabolomic analysis.

结论（EHA原文）

This study demonstrates the dynamic remodeling of gut microbiota mediated by disease and treatment in DLBCL patients, supporting the characteristic dysbiosis and metabolic disorders of gut microbiota in untreated newly diagnosed DLBCL patients. After achieving complete remission through standard first-line chemotherapy, the gut microbiota structure of patients approximates the state of their healthy cohabitants. These findings characterize the changes in gut microbiota during the course of DLBCL, suggesting potential insights for the study of the pathogenesis of DLBCL and the development of new therapies.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Venous thromboembolism (VTE) represents a major cause of morbidity and mortality in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). Several predictive models, Khorana, ThroLy, and Model IX were developed to stratify thrombotic risk, yet their comparative performance in a DLBCL-exclusive population remains unclear. Aims: To comparatively assess the discriminative performance of Khorana, ThroLy, Model IX, and R-IPI for VTE occurrence and overall survival (OS) in a large, real-world, international DLBCL cohort. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed 1,504 consecutive DLBCL patients diagnosed between 2004 and 2024 at two European, two Asian and one United States center (ClinicalTrials ID NCT06694779) . VTE was defined as any objectively confirmed deep vein thrombosis or pulmonary embolism occurring after diagnosis. Model performance was evaluated using Cox regression and Harrell’s concordance index (c-index) with bootstrap-based estimation of 95% confidence intervals.

结论（EHA原文）

VTE is a frequent early complication in DLBCL and is associated with inferior survival. Model IX showed the best discrimination for VTE and outperformed the other models for OS, supporting its role as the most informative risk stratification tool in this setting. * PC, CGP and IC contributed equally

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: VTE occurred in 219/1504 patients (14.6%), with a 1-year cumulative incidence of 3.3% (95% CI 2.4–4.2). Median time to VTE was 72 days, confirming the early clustering of thrombotic events. VTE independently predicts inferior OS (38.5 vs 172.3 months). In univariate analysis, hemoglobin (hb) level, leukocytosis, hypoalbuminemia, body mass index (BMI) > 30, bulky disease, and deep vein compression, were significantly associated with increased VTE risk (p 30 (96.6%), hb level (92.8%), neutrophil count (77.9%), and R-IPI (65.8%), while higher albumin levels showed a consistent protective association (96.1% negative selection). These findings suggest residual multidimensional risk information in our cohort, not fully captured by the composite Model IX weighting. Regarding OS prediction, Model IX again showed superior performance (c-index 0.67, 95% CI 0.65–0.69), outperforming ThroLy, R-IPI, and Khorana. While R-IPI retained strong prognostic value for survival, its discriminatory ability for VTE was limited (see Tab. 1). Conversely, VTE-oriented models, particularly Model IX, captured prognostic information relevant to both thrombotic risk and survival, highlighting a partial biological overlap between disease aggressiveness and thrombotic propensity. Conclusion: VTE is a frequent early complication in DLBCL and is associated with inferior survival. Model IX showed the best discrimination for VTE and outperformed the other models for OS, supporting its role as the most informative risk stratification tool in this setting. * PC, CGP and IC contributed equally

polatuzumab vedotin plus rituximab, ifosfamide, carboplatin, etoposide (pola-r-ice) vs r-ice as second line treatment in large b cell lymphoma (lbcl). final analysis of a randomized phase 3 study

2年EFS: 26% vs 30%, HR=1.0, p=0.901 2年PFS: 47% vs 41% 2年OS: 75% vs 64% DLBCL亚组2年PFS: 52% vs 42%, p=0.040 DLBCL亚组2年OS: 77% vs 61%, p=0.033 复发疾病亚组2年PFS: 66% vs 46%, p=0.004 复发疾病亚组2年OS: 87% vs 71%, p=0.015 巨大肿块亚组2年PFS: 45% vs 23%, p=0.006 巨大肿块亚组2年OS: 76% vs 39%, p=0.011 高LDH亚组2年PFS: 44% vs 31%, p=0.034 高LDH亚组2年OS: 67% vs 49%, p=0.036 non-GCB亚组2年PFS: 54% vs 34%, p=0.040

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: R-ICE is one of the standard induction regimens prior to autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) in the treatment of patients (pts) with relapsed and refractory (r/r) LBCL after first line therapy and is also used as bridging therapy prior to CAR T-cell therapy (CART) in this situation. However, further improvement of induction and bridging regimens is needed. Polatuzumab vedotin is a CD-79b directed antibody-drug conjugate with proven efficacy in r/r LBCL. Aims: This open label, multinational, randomized phase III clinical study compared safety and efficacy of polatuzumab vedotin plus R-ICE (Pola-R-ICE; arm E) with R-ICE (arm S). Methods: Key inclusion criteria were diagnosis of first relapse or progression of LBCL, ECOG PS ≤ 2 and adequate organ function. Pts in arm E received polatuzumab vedotin 1.8 mg/kg at d1, in addition to SOC R-ICE. Pts went to consolidation therapy by ASCT or CART by decision of the investigator outside the clinical study. The primary endpoint was event-free survival (EFS). Key secondary endpoints included progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS). The threshold to reject the null hypothesis was a hazard ratio (HR) of 0.663 with a power of 80% and alpha 5% (two-sided).

结论（EHA原文）

This study could not detect a benefit of applying Pola-R-ICE over R-ICE as second line treatment for pts with LBCL. However, pts with DLBCL, relapsed disease (in contrast to those with primary refractory disease) and those with high tumour burden (bulky disease, high LDH) may clinically benefit from Pola-R-ICE instead of R-ICE when given prior to consolidative therapy with ASCT or CART.

sustained remissions beyond 4 years with epcoritamab monotherapy: long-term follow-up results from the pivotal epcore nhl-1 trial in patients with relapsed or refractory large b-cell lymphoma

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: R/R LBCL is challenging to treat; there remains a need for more effective treatment (tx) options for patients (pts) with LBCL in third-line or later (3L+). Epcoritamab (epcor) is a subcutaneous (SC) CD3×CD20 bispecific antibody approved for the tx of adults with R/R LBCL or R/R FL after ≥ 2 lines of systemic therapy, based on outcomes from the pivotal phase 2 EPCORE ® NHL-1 trial (NCT03625037), in which epcor monotherapy led to high CR rates and deep, durable responses with manageable safety in pts with R/R LBCL. Pivotal results have been reported previously (Vose JM, et al. Blood 2024;144[Suppl 1]:4480). Aims: Here, we report updated data with an extended follow-up of over 4 years. Methods: Adults with R/R CD20 + LBCL (including diffuse LBCL, high-grade B-cell lymphoma, primary mediastinal LBCL, and FL grade 3B) and ≥ 2 prior lines of systemic therapy were treated with SC epcor (0.16-mg and 0.8-mg step-up doses followed by 48-mg full doses) in 28-day cycles according to the approved dosing schedule: QW, cycles 1–3; Q2W, cycles 4–9; Q4W, cycles ≥ 10, until progressive disease or unacceptable toxicity. The primary endpoint was ORR per Lugano criteria. Efficacy results presented here are based on investigators’ assessment. The data cutoff date was May 2, 2025.

结论（EHA原文）

With more than 4 years of follow-up, epcor monotherapy continues to demonstrate deep and durable remissions. Nearly half (42%) of all complete responders remained in remission after more than 4 years of median follow-up and 57% remained alive, demonstrating the potential for long-term disease-free survival with epcor in this population with difficult-to-treat LBCL. The consistent safety profile and prolonged survival benefit highlight epcor as a favorable chemotherapy-free, readily available tx option in the 3L+ LBCL tx setting. © American Society of Hematology (2025). Reused with permission.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Single-antigen CD19-targeted chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) T-cell therapies are part of routine care for patients with relapsed or refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), yet opportunity remains to improve outcomes. Emerging dual-targeting CD19/CD20 CAR T-cell product candidates represent a next-generation approach to address antigen escape and improve durability of response. Rondecabtagene autoleucel (ronde-cel) is an autologous, dual-targeting CD19/CD20 CAR T-cell product candidate manufactured from CD62L-enriched T cells, which are associated with lower adverse cytokine production, such as IL-6 (Arcangeli 2022). Recent results from a Phase 1/2 trial (NCT05826535) evaluating ronde-cel in LBCL showed durable efficacy and an encouraging safety profile (Larson 2025). Aims: Here we report updated safety data from an expanded cohort with extended follow-up. We characterize the incidence, severity, time to onset, and resolution of cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS), as well as infections and cytopenias. Methods: Patients with R/R LBCL (N = 87) received ronde-cel following lymphodepletion with fludarabine and cyclophosphamide. Eligible patients had received at least one prior line of therapy (second-line [2L] or third- or later-line [3L+]). There was no upper age limit. Safety assessments included CRS and ICANS grading per ASTCT consensus criteria, infection monitoring, and hematologic laboratory evaluations. Low-dose dexamethasone (10 mg/day on Days 0, 1, and 2) was introduced for ICANS prophylaxis (N = 37) and is now standard for all patients in the ongoing clinical trial.

结论（EHA原文）

Ronde-cel continues to show a consistent and manageable safety profile with low rates of CAR T-cell associated toxicities. No Grade ≥ 3 CRS was observed, and

077DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验PMBCL/特殊亚型CAR-T/细胞治疗PF1248

a prospective, single-arm clinical study of ctdna-guided early second infusion of axi-cel in relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，原发纵隔大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=7；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；分组：单组：Axicabtagene Ciloleucel

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

疗效：在第二次输注前CR但ctDNA阳性的4例患者中，2例在输注后1个月达到ctDNA阴性CR并保持缓解（396天和257天），2例维持CR但ctDNA仍阳性（3个月评估待定）。在第二次输注前PR的3例患者中，1例ctDNA阴性PR维持1个月（3个月评估待定），2例ctDNA阳性PR早期疾病进展。中位随访93天，中位OS和中位PFS未达到。安全性：CRS发生3例（42.8%），均为1级；无ICANS；常见血液学不良事件为4级中性粒细胞减少（6/7, 85.7%）和3-4级血小板减少（3/7, 42.9%）；无治疗相关死亡或SAE。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD19 chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy has remarkably improved outcomes for relapsed or refractory large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL). However, patients failing to achieve deep remission early after the first infusion face a persistently high risk of relapse. Historical data indicates that a second CAR-T infusion administered after relapse or progression generally yields poor salvage outcomes. Therefore, exploring preemptive consolidation interventions represents a critical unmet clinical need. Aims: To evaluate the efficacy, safety, and cellular kinetics of an early second CD19 CAR-T cell infusion as a consolidation therapy for R/R LBCL patients who show initial response but fail to achieve deep remission early after the first infusion. Methods: In this prospective, single-center, single-arm clinical trial, adult patients with R/R LBCL who achieved PR by PET-CT, or CR with ctDNA positivity within 60 days after the first Axicabtagene Ciloleucel(Axi-cel , 2 × 10⁶ cells/kg) infusion were eligible for an early second axi-cel infusion. The second axi-cel infusion was administered at a dose of 2 × 10⁶ cells/kg between 30 to 90 days after the first infusion. FC conditioning regimen was also administered prior to the second infusion. The study has been registered on clinicaltrial.gov (NCT06902012).

结论（EHA原文）

Early second infusion of CD19 CAR-T cells is feasible and demonstrates a highly favorable safety profile with no high-grade CRS or ICANS, while also demonstrating reliable in vivo CAR-T cell expansion. ctDNA-guided early intervention at minimal tumor burden is critical for successful second CAR-T infusions. Ongoing enrollment will validate these results.

durable responses with rondecabtagene autoleucel (dual-targeting cd19/cd20 car t-cells) are associated with higher proportion of cytotoxic t cells with memory potential in infusion products

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，原发纵隔大B细胞淋巴瘤，大B细胞淋巴瘤；原发纵隔大B细胞淋巴瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=42；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：朗迪卡基奥仑赛；靶点：CD19，CD20；类别：CAR-T，自体细胞，经基因修饰；分组：试验组：rondecabtagene autoleucel

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

1. 在CD8+CAR+细胞中，ronde-cel产品与已批准的CD19 CAR-T细胞疗法相比，记忆相关基因（CD62L, IL7R, LEF1）表达更高。 2. 在细胞毒性T细胞（Tcmp）中，ronde-cel产品中记忆标志物（LEF1, IL7R, BACH2）表达更高。 3. 记忆表型细胞在输注后第28天（中位数83%，N=10）和第56天（中位数73%，N=4）仍存在，并可增殖、分泌细胞因子和杀死肿瘤细胞。 4. 持续完全缓解≥12个月的患者（N=8）在CD8+CAR+细胞中Tcmp比例中位数为23（IQR 10-28），而3个月内进展的患者（N=6）中位数为7（IQR 6-9），p=0.029。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Achieving durable complete responses (CR) remains a key goal of CAR T - cell therapy for large B - cell lymphoma (LBCL). Higher proportion of cells with memory phenotype in CAR T-cell products has been associated with higher expansion and favorable outcomes (Deng 2020), and CD62L is a n established marker of memory T cells ( Gattinoni 2017) . Rondecabtagene autoleucel (ronde-cel) is an autologous, dual-targeting CD19/CD20 CAR T-cell product candidate manufactured from CD62L - enriched cells , a process designed to preserve higher proportion of cells with memory phenotype and improve durable responses without extending manufacturing time . H igh rate s (76%) of CR with 18 - month median progression-free survival were reported from the Phase 1/2 clinical trial of ronde-cel in third- or later-line ( 3L+ ) patients ( Larson 2025). Aims: Evaluate the association between ronde-cel's durability of response in patients treated in the Phase 1/2 trial and ronde-cel product characteristics conf erred by CD62L enrichment. Methods: R onde-cel drug product phenotype was assessed by single-cell RNAseq ( scRNAseq ) . Peripheral blood (PB) was collected post - infusion at multiple time-points, and phenotype ( scRNAseq ) and ex vivo functionality (co-culture) were assesse d . Publicly available scRNAseq data from FDA - approved CAR T -cell therapie s ( Deng 2020, Haradhvala 2022, Li 2023 , Y u 2025 ) were used for comparison .

结论（EHA原文）

Ronde-cel manufactured with CD62L enrichment produced infusion products with higher expression of memory-related genes compared with FDA-approved CD19 CAR T-cell therapies for LBCL. This memory potential also existed in the cytotoxic cells of ronde-cel products, persisted post-infusion, and allowed for functionality two-months post-infusion. Patients with a higher proportion of Tcmp cells were more likely to achieve durable responses (≥12 months CR). These findings support the hypothesis of an association between ronde-cel's durability of response and CD62L enrichment during manufacturing.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary mediastinal B-cell lymphoma (PMBL) is a rare and aggressive subtype of lymphoma that typically affects young patients (pts). Excellent outcomes following first-line immunochemotherapy have been reported in clinical trials; however, prospective real-world data in this setting remain limited. Methods: REal world dAta in LYmphoma and Survival in Adults (REALYSA) is a prospective, multicenter, non-interventional cohort study that included pts newly diagnosed with lymphoma in France. We analyzed the PMBL population enrolled between November 2018 and August 2023. The primary endpoint was progression-free survival (PFS).

结论（EHA原文）

In this prospective real-world cohort, PMBL patients achieved excellent survival outcomes. R-CHOP21 was associated with inferior PFS compared with R-CHOP14 and R-ACVBP, which showed similar efficacy, confirming the relevance of dose-dense regimens in routine practice. (REALYSA, NCT03869619)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CNS involvement in PMLBCL is rare and associated with poor outcomes. The clinical features, prognosis and efficacy of modern CNS-directed therapies, including autologous transplantation (ASCT), and anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy (CAR-T), remain poorly defined. Aims: To provide management recommendations for CNS involvement in PMLBCL in routine practice. Methods: Data on pts with PMLBCL and CNS involvement at diagnosis or relapse treated between 2001 and 2024 in 27 centers across 7 countries were analyzed (NCT06024694).

结论（EHA原文）

In the largest series reported to date, durable remissions were achieved in PMLBCL pts with early CNS relapse treated with HD-MTX–based chemo followed by ASCT and/or brain irradiation. CAR-T, preceded by brain irradiation or ITC as bridging, provides long-term disease control even in HD-MTX-refractory pts. In contrast, late CNS involvement in multiply relapsed PMLBCL has a dismal prognosis.

pharmacokinetics, efficacy, and safety of subcutaneous pembrolizumab in relapsed or refractory classic hodgkin lymphoma (chl) or primary mediastinal large b-cell lymphoma (pmbcl): a phase 2 study

P 患者群体

O 结局指标

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Pembrolizumab is a well-established intravenous PD-1 inhibitor for relapsed or refractory (R/R) cHL and PMBCL, administered Q3W or Q6W. MK-3475A is pembrolizumab with berahyaluronidase alfa (MK-5180) for subcutaneous administration (subcutaneous pembrolizumab). Berahyaluronidase alfa, a human hyaluronidase variant developed and manufactured by Alteogen Inc., is a permeation enhancer that enables subcutaneous administration of pembrolizumab. Subcutaneous pembrolizumab is approved globally (outside of the US) for the treatment of cHL and PMBCL. Aims: To present pharmacokinetics (PK), efficacy, and safety from a single-arm, open-label, phase 2 study (NCT06504394) evaluating subcutaneous pembrolizumab in participants with R/R cHL or R/R PMBCL. Methods: Eligible participants were ≥18 years with histologically confirmed, FDG-avid cHL or PMBCL per WHO criteria, radiographically measurable disease, and an ECOG PS of 0 or 1. Participants with cHL or PMBCL were anti–PD-1 naive and had disease that was refractory to, did not achieve CR with, or had relapsed after prior therapy. Participants with cHL had received ≥1 multiagent regimen, and participants with PMBCL had received ≥2 prior therapies (including ≥1 rituximab-based regimen). All participants were ineligible for or had relapsed after autologous stem cell transplant. Participants received subcutaneous pembrolizumab 790 mg Q6W for ≤18 cycles (~2 years) or until disease progression or other discontinuation criteria were met. Primary end points were PK exposure measures during cycle 1 (C1) and ORR per Lugano criteria by investigator. Intensive PK samples were collected during C1, and noncompartmental analysis methods were used to determine PK end points based on observed data. Secondary end points included safety. Data cutoff date was June 10, 2025.

结论（EHA原文）

The PK profile of subcutaneous pembrolizumab in participants with hematologic tumors was similar to that in solid tumors and was consistent with the typical PK profile for subcutaneous monoclonal antibodies (Figure). Subcutaneous pembrolizumab at a dose of 790 mg Q6W showed a manageable safety profile and efficacy consistent with intravenous pembrolizumab.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary mediastinal B-cell lymphoma (PMBCL) is a distinct subtype of aggressive B-cell lymphoma, predominantly affecting young adults. While overall outcomes are favorable, a clinically relevant subset of patients experience early progression or death. To date, no widely accepted, disease-specific prognostic index exists for PMBCL, and risk stratification largely relies on tools developed for diffuse large B-cell lymphoma. Accurate prognostic stratification in PMBCL is clinically relevant for identifying patients at higher risk, informing treatment selection strategies, and optimizing patient selection and stratification in prospective clinical trials. Aims: To develop and externally validate a simple, point-based prognostic index for overall survival (OS) and progression-free survival (PFS) in patients with PMBCL, using routinely available baseline clinical variables. Methods: A retrospective multicenter cohort of 155 patients with PMBCL diagnosed between 2006–2024 in Turkey was used for model development. The prognostic index incorporated age >45 years, ECOG performance status ≥2, Ann Arbor stage ≥III, and hemoglobin \n External validation used data from the Danish Lymphoma Registry, including 228 patients diagnosed during 2000–2025. Model performance was evaluated using Kaplan–Meier survival analysis with log-rank tests, Cox proportional hazards regression, and discrimination assessed by Harrell’s concordance index (C-index).

结论（EHA原文）

The PMBCL-PI is a simple, disease-specific, point-based prognostic index that reliably stratifies patients with PMBCL according to relative risk using routinely available clinical variables. The model demonstrates robust discrimination in both development and external validation cohorts. To enhance clinical applicability, the PMBCL-PI has been implemented as an online decision-support tool, available at https://lymphomapredictor.rn.dk/.

083DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PF984

前瞻性实时ctdna监测在弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤患者常规临床护理中的可行性

feasibility of prospective real-time ctdna monitoring in routine clinical care of diffuse large b-cell lymphoma patients

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=75

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：feasibility of prospective real-time ctdna monitoring in routine clinical care of diffuse large b-cell lymphoma patients

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

主要终点：从采血到ctDNA报告的平均周转时间为18天；远处站点（>200 km）为21天 vs 本地站点16天（p<0.0001）||C2D1可检测到ctDNA的患者中，进展率显著高于不可检测者（p=0.025）||CART治疗障碍：体能状态差和高肿瘤负荷（n=6）、年龄/虚弱（n=4）||进展患者死亡率70%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Over 25% of patients with diffuse large B cell lymphoma (DLBCL) do not respond to frontline chemotherapy or relapse within 12 months of completing therapy. Half of these patients are eligible for second-line chimeric antigen receptor T cell (CART) therapy, but high tumor burden and low performance status decrease efficacy and increase toxicity. Circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) is a promising biomarker for monitoring treatment response in DLBCL, but its feasibility in routine clinical practice has not been established. Understanding logistical factors affecting turnaround time and data quality is critical for clinical implementation. We developed a 195-gene panel to detect treatment failure as early as cycle 2, day 1 (C2D1) of first-line therapy in a retrospective cohort of 245 patients. Aims: We evaluated the feasibility and clinical utility of our panel to detect early relapsed DLBCL in a prospective cohort of 75 patients. We hypothesized the assay could be performed in real time within 3 weeks of collection. The primary endpoint was the turnaround time from blood collection to ctDNA reporting at C2D1. The secondary objective was to determine the optimal timing for ctDNA testing at C2D1, C3D1, and end of treatment (EOT). Methods: Patients with de novo or transformed DLBCL undergoing curative-intent chemotherapy were enrolled from five Canadian hospitals. Plasma samples were collected in Streck tubes at diagnosis (DX), C2D1, C3D1, EOT, and follow-up. ctDNA was extracted from 5mL plasma and hybrid-capture libraries were prepared using a dual-UMI approach, then sequenced on a NextSeq 2000 (1500× coverage). Finally, somatic variants were called using germline-filtered and error-suppressed data. Results did not change clinical management.

结论（EHA原文）

Real-time ctDNA profiling is feasible, but logistical challenges for clinical implementation remain. There is significant attrition among refractory DLBCL patients eligible for CART in real-world settings. Our panel can identify high-risk patients as early as C2D1, supporting early intervention trials.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Between March 2024 and December 2025, 75 patients enrolled, provided 425 samples; 68 completed treatment (study ongoing). The mean age was 63; 44 patients had IPI>3, 10 had prior indolent lymphoma, and 13 experienced disease progression (PD). The mean turnaround time was 18 days, with distant sites (>200 km) requiring 21 days versus 16 days for local sites (p 3 (p Barriers to CART included poor performance status and high disease burden (n=6) and age/frailty (n=4). Mortality was 70% among PD patients. Conclusion: Real-time ctDNA profiling is feasible, but logistical challenges for clinical implementation remain. There is significant attrition among refractory DLBCL patients eligible for CART in real-world settings. Our panel can identify high-risk patients as early as C2D1, supporting early intervention trials.

axicabtagene ciloleucel作为晚期复发大b细胞淋巴瘤患者的二线治疗：西班牙淋巴瘤组geltamo晚期r临床试验的中期分析

axicabtagene ciloleucel as second-line treatment in patients with late-relapsed large b-cell lymphoma: interim analysis of the late-r clinical trial from the spanish lymphoma group geltamo

P 患者群体

O 结局指标

3个月完全缓解率（CR rate）：90%（基于21例可评估患者） 3个月总缓解率（ORR）：95%（基于21例可评估患者） 中位无进展生存期（PFS）：未达到 中位总生存期（OS）：未达到 估计6个月PFS：87.0%（95% CI 68.0-100） 估计6个月OS：95.7%（95% CI 86.7-100） 安全性：细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率74%，主要为1-2级；免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）发生率45.7%，主要为低中度；3-4级血液学毒性：血小板减少20%，中性粒细胞减少17.1%；严重感染5例（14%），其中1例死于感染性休克

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CAR T-cell therapy is the standard of care for patients with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) experiencing early relapse or primary refractory disease. In contrast, patients who relapse 12 months after first-line chemoimmunotherapy (CIT) represent a clinically heterogeneous population for whom prospective clinical trials specifically evaluating the role of CAR T-cell therapy are lacking. Aims: The LATE-R trial was designed to evaluate the efficacy and safety of axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel) in patients with late-relapsing aggressive B-cell lymphomas. Methods: This is an open-label, multicenter, single-arm, phase II study sponsored by GELTAMO in collaboration with Kite, a Gilead Company, Inc. Eligible patients were ≥18 years with either DLBCL, transformed follicular lymphoma (tFL), or high-grade B-cell lymphoma (HGBCL), relapsing 12–60 months after completion of first-line CIT. Bridging therapy was allowed at investigator discretion. The primary endpoint was complete response (CR) rate at 3 months after axi-cel infusion, assessed locally by PET-CT according to standard criteria. Secondary endpoints included overall response rate (ORR), progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS) and safety. Herein we present an interim analysis pre-specified in the protocol.

结论（EHA原文）

In this interim analysis of the LATE-R trial, axi-cel demonstrated remarkably high CR rates in patients with late-relapsing aggressive B-cell lymphomas treated in the second-line setting, with a manageable toxicity profile consistent with the known risks of axi-cel. These findings suggest that patients with late CIT relapses could benefit from axi-cel and support its use in this clinical setting.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of December 31 st 2025 (cut-off), 35 patients underwent leukapheresis and 31 had received axi-cel and were included in the present analysis. Median age was 63 years (range 28–79) and 19 (54%) patients were male. At study entry, 49% had relapsed within 12–24 months and 51% within 24–60 months from first-line CIT; 26% of patients had HBCL double hit, 83% showed Ann Arbor stage III–IV and 74% had an IPI ≥2. \n The CR rate and ORR at 3 months among the 21 patients who had reached this time point at the time of data cutoff were 90% and 95%, respectively. With a median follow-up of 5.9 months (Q1-Q3: 2,4-8.7), the median progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) had not been reached. The estimated 6-month PFS and OS were 87.0% (95% CI 68.0-100) and 95.7% (95% CI 86.7-100), respectively (Figure). \n Regarding safety, a total of 81 adverse events classified as serious adverse events (SAEs) or adverse events of special interest (AESIs) and occurring on or before the cut-off time, were reported. Cytokine release syndrome (CRS) occurred in 74% of patients, predominantly grade 1 (37%) and 2 (28.6%); grade ≥3 CRS was infrequent (8.6%), with no grade 4–5 events. Immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) was reported in 45.7% of patients. Most events were low to moderate in severity, with grade 3 and 4 events occurring in 14.6% and 8.3% of patients, respectively; no grade 5 neurotoxicity was observed. Hematologic toxicities were common, with thrombocytopenia (20%) and neutropenia (17.1%) being the most frequently reported grade ≥3 cytopenias. Severe infections were reported in 5 cases (14%), including one patient who died due to a septic shock at 34 days from axi-cel infusion. Conclusion: In this interim analysis of the LATE-R trial, axi-cel demonstrated remarkably high CR rates in patients with late-relapsing aggressive B-cell lymphomas treated in the second-line setting, with a manageable toxicity profile consistent with the known risks of axi-cel. These findings suggest that patients with late CIT relapses could benefit from axi-cel and support its use in this clinical setting.

baseline t-cell repertoire skewing and effector cd8 t-cell dynamics in prolonged cytopenias following anti-cd19 car t-cell therapy

P 患者群体

B细胞急性淋巴细胞白血病，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=10

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：baseline t-cell repertoire skewing and effector cd8 t-cell dynamics in prolonged cytopenias following anti-cd19 car t-cell therapy

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

扩增T细胞克隆比例：长期血细胞减少组56%，无血细胞减少组22%，p=0.05||T细胞受体库多样性（Shannon指数）：长期血细胞减少组中位数4.5，无血细胞减少组中位数5.5，p=0.0005||CD8:CD4比值：基线时长期血细胞减少组数值更高||CD8 TEMRA:CD4 Treg比值：长期血细胞减少组更高且持续30天||CD8 TEMRA表型：CD57+CD28-，符合细胞毒性效应状态

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy has transformed outcomes in B-cell malignancies, but prolonged cytopenias occur in up to 50% of patients and pathophysiology remains poorly understood. In particular, the role of immune repertoire architecture and T-cell phenotypic states in prolonged cytopenias is unexplored. Aims: To investigate whether pre-treatment T-cell immune repertoire architecture and phenotype are associated with the development of prolonged cytopenias following CD19-directed CAR T-cell therapy . Methods: This single-centre prospective observational study utilised anonymised clinical data and peripheral blood mononuclear cells (PBMCs) from patients receiving autologous anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy. Prolonged cytopenia was defined as persistent grade ≥3 cytopenia lasting >30 days post-infusion (neutrophils ) sequencing and flow cytometry. Longitudinal flow cytometry was performed at serial time points post-CAR T-cell infusion. Group comparisons were performed using non-parametric statistical tests.

结论（EHA原文）

In this prospective study, prolonged cytopenias following anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy were associated with baseline immune repertoire skewing and altered T-cell dynamics. Patients who developed prolonged cytopenias exhibited greater clonal expansion and reduced T-cell repertoire diversity before CAR T-cell therapy. Skewing towards highly differentiated CD8+ TEMRA populations was a feature of patients with prolonged cytopenias, whereas those without prolonged cytopenias demonstrated more stable T-cell profiles. These findings suggest that pre-existing immune repertoire characteristics and effector T-cell dynamics may influence the likelihood of developing prolonged cytopenias after CAR T-cell therapy. Further investigation in larger cohorts is warranted to identify immune biomarkers that can define patients at risk of developing prolonged cytopenias.

the phs w-index: a novel prognostic framework integrating nutritional and hematological markers to predict outcomes in dlbcl patients treated with glofitamab

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=101

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：格菲妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

12个月无进展生存率（PFS）: 41.0% (95% CI 29.3–52.3) 12个月总生存率（OS）: 52.9% (95% CI 40.3–64.0) 客观缓解率（ORR）: 48.1% (n=39) 完全缓解率（CR）: 35.8% (n=29) PHS w-Index区分能力（乐观校正C-index）: PFS 0.659, OS 0.681

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) management has been transformed by T-cell–engaging bispecific antibodies such as glofitamab, yet heterogeneity in response persists. Although the secondary International Prognostic Index (IPI), revised IPI (R-IPI), and NCCN-IPI are standards for outcome prediction in relapsed/refractory (R/R) disease, they do not fully capture host-related factors—such as nutritional status, anemia, and lymphopenia—that are highly relevant to T-cell–engager therapy. These host factors can be assessed through validated tools like the Prognostic Nutritional Index (PNI = (10 × serum albumin [g/L] ÷ 10) + (0.005 × total lymphocyte count [×10⁹/L] × 10⁶)). Aims: To develop and validate a weighted prognostic score for predicting progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) in DLBCL patients treated with glofitamab, and to compare its performance with established indices. Methods: Consecutive de novo LBCL patients from the Czech NiHiL registry (NCT03199066) were screened. 101 R/R DLBCL patients receiving glofitamab (Apr 2019–Sep 2025) were analyzed: 3 (3.0%) in 2nd, 44 (43.6%) in 3rd, and 54 (53.5%) in ≥4th line. 89 (88.1%) had monotherapy, 12 (11.9%) systemic combinations, mostly R-GemOx (n=7), then Loncastuximab (n=2), Pola-BR, R-ICE, and Gemcitabine (all n=1). Fourteen baseline variables at glofitamab initiation (stage, IPI, Hb, lymphocytes, LDH, age, B-symptoms, ECOG, extranodal sites, WBC/platelets, albumin, sex, and bulk >7.5 cm) were assessed for impact on PFS. Weighted points were assigned based on ROC-defined cut-offs (Hb ≤120 g/L, PNI ≤71.1). The resulting PHS w-Index assigns 2 points for low PNI, 2 for stage III–IV, and 1 for low Hb, stratifying patients into low- (0–1), intermediate- (2–3), and high-risk (4–5) groups. Validation was performed using 1,000 bootstrap iterations for optimism-corrected C-indices.

结论（EHA原文）

The PHS w-Index is a simple and promising tool that outperforms standard prognostic indices in glofitamab-treated DLBCL. By integrating host fitness (nutrition, anemia, lymphopenia) with tumor burden, it enables improved risk stratification and early identification of high-risk patients for tailored management. \n Acknowledgement: Supported by the Ministry of Health of the Czech Republic (NU21-03-00411) DRO (FNOL, 00098892). \n

总缓解率（ORR）：93.1% 完全缓解率（CRR）：79.1% 亚组分析（COO：GCB 92.9% vs non-GCB 92.5%，p>0.99；转化疾病：96.9% vs 初治92.4%，p=0.63；CCI<5 vs ≥5：CRR 79.6% vs 78.0%，p=0.72；年龄<70 vs ≥70：CRR 80.6% vs 77.4%，p=0.43） ≥3级感染：35.8%（≥70岁42.4% vs <70岁31.9%，p=0.035） 发热性中性粒细胞减少：29.6% 腹泻：48.0%（3-4级7.7%） 周围神经病变：32.1%（3级3.0%） 机会性感染：10.8%（PCP 8例，带状疱疹5例） 83.3%完成6个周期，未完成原因：不良事件35.7%，死亡25.0%，疾病进展23.2%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The Phase III POLARIX trial established Polatuzumab Vedotin plus R-CHP (Pola-R-CHP) as a new standard for frontline diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) with IPI 2-5.[1] However, real-world data (RWD) are essential to confirm these findings in broader patient demographics, including those with significant comorbidities and high-risk features often excluded from clinical trials. Aims: To assess the real-world efficacy (ORR, CRR) and safety profile of Pola-R-CHP in a large, multicentre UK cohort, including specific sub-group analyses with regards to age, Charlson Comorbidity Index (CCI), cell of origin (COO), transformed disease and HIV status. Methods: This retrospective study included 437 adults with previously untreated DLBCL receiving Pola-R-CHP across multiple UK centres (2023–2025). Data were collected on baseline characteristics, treatment compliance, best response (PET-CT), and key toxicities. Survival analysis, including progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS), is ongoing.\n

结论（EHA原文）

In this large real-world UK cohort, Pola-R-CHP demonstrated efficacy and deliverability. The CR rate in this series appears comparable to the trial despite being used in a cohort of patients with high-risk features and a broader range of indications than were included in the POLARIX trial. These data support Pola-R-CHP as a first line standard of care in the real-world setting, however the higher rates of grade ≥3 infections and reduced treatment intensity in patients with advanced age and comorbidities demonstrates a need for vigilant supportive care in this demographic. Survival outcomes will be presented. \n References: \n \n Tilly H, et al. Polatuzumab Vedotin in Previously Untreated Diffuse Large B-Cell Lymphoma. N Engl J Med 2022; 386:351-363. DOI: 10.1056/NEJMoa2115304 \n \n

primary analysis of the polatuzumab vedotin plus r-chp (pola-r-chp) cohort of fil-mab, a prospective, multicenter italian multicohort real-life study

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=177；疾病阶段：原发性

O 结局指标

完成治疗率：89%（155/174）||CR率：74%||PR率：11%||SD/PD率：4%||12个月PFS率：78.2%（95% CI 68.5–85.3）||12个月OS率：91.2%（95% CI 83.1–95.5）||de novo DLBCL亚组12个月PFS率为75.1%（95% CI 62.5–83.9）||de novo DLBCL亚组12个月OS率为90.6%（95% CI 79.5–95.8）||加权分析后估计12个月PFS率为87.8%（bootstrap 95% CI 78.3–94.4）||治疗相关死亡：1%（2例）||G3-4中性粒细胞减少：15%||G3-4感染：9%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Pola-R-CHP is a new standard of care for previously untreated DLBCL(Tilly, NEJM 2022)and is reimbursed in Italy for IPI 3–5. However, real-world (RW) data are still limited. FIL-MAB (NCT06008691) is an independent,academic,multicenter,prospective RW observational study evaluating effectiveness and safety of novel mAb-based therapies across 65 Italian centers and 8 cohorts. Aims: The Pola-R-CHP cohort has met the prespecified sample size for primary analysis,enabling assessment of its clinical value in routine practice in a large European country. Methods: Patients (pts) deemed candidates for Pola-R-CHP at participating centers, were prospectively enrolled and treated per routine practice. Baseline characteristics, feasibility, discontinuation rates, G3–5 AEs, ORR/CRR (PET-CT per Lugano 2014), PFS and OS were estimated by Kaplan–Meier. Outcomes were analyzed overall and benchmarked against the R-CHOP arm of the POLARIX trial using a matching-adjusted indirect comparison (MAIC) approach. Individual patient data were reweighted to match aggregate baseline characteristics(age,sex,stage,ECOG PS,LDH,IPI) of the POLARIX control arm.

结论（EHA原文）

To our knowledge, the primary analysis of the prospective FIL-MAB Pola-R-CHP cohort is the first European RW experience assessing this combination. With the limitation of a short follow-up, our data, including reweighted analyses aligned to the baseline characteristics demonstrate the good applicability and effectiveness of Pola-R-CHP in a broad RW multi-institutional setting.

089DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验转化/Richter其他/未明确药物PS1649

难治性血液系统恶性肿瘤患者使用卡莫地布与体外精密筛查药物敏感性筛查的i/ii期研究中期结果

interim results of the phase i/ii study investigating karonudib in patients with refractory haematological malignancies paired with ex-vivo precision screen drug sensitivity screening

P 患者群体

多发性骨髓瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，急性淋巴细胞白血病，急性髓系白血病，骨髓增生异常综合征；N=27；疾病阶段：难治

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：Karonudib；靶点：NUDT1；类别：化药；分组：试验组1：Karonudib单药（剂量递增）；试验组2：Karonudib联合Idarubicin

C 对照措施

O 结局指标

安全性：最常见治疗相关不良事件（≥25%）包括贫血（50%）、中性粒细胞减少（43%）、腹泻（43%）、恶心（36%）、血小板减少（29%）； 剂量限制性毒性（DLT）：1例5级颅内出血（可能相关）发生于队列2； 疗效-AML（2例可评估）：1例部分缓解（133天），1例疾病稳定（141天）； 疗效-MDS（4例可评估）：最佳反应为疾病稳定（65天）； 疗效-DLBCL（2例可评估）：最佳反应为疾病稳定（167天）； 联合队列（13例）：1例疾病稳定超过4个周期，骨髓原始细胞从40%降至17%；另一例在第1周期疾病稳定，原始细胞从17.5%降至12.4%，第2周期进展。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: MutT homologue 1 (MTH1) detoxifies cells from ROS-induced DNA damage and is essential for cancer cell survival. MTH1 depletion in RAS-transformed tumour cells causes proliferative abnormalities and numerous malignancies, including haematological tumours, which overexpress MTH1. Karonudib (TH1579, OXC-101) is a mitotic MTH1 inhibitor that arrests mitosis by disrupting microtubule dynamics and chromosome alignment, and increases incorporation of oxidised nucleosides into DNA, with improved survival demonstrated across several haematological preclinical models. Aims: To report Part 1 and Part 2 dose-escalation interim data from the phase I/II MAATEO trial (NCT04077307) of Karonudib in adults with advanced relapsed/refractory (R/R) AML, ALL, DLBCL, MM, and high-risk MDS. Methods: This single-arm, dose-escalation trial enrolled patients aged 18–75 years with adequate organ function receiving escalating oral doses of Karonudib using a 3+3 design. The primary objectives were safety and tolerability, assessed by the DLT rate over the first 4 weeks. Secondary objectives included clinical benefit, pharmacokinetics, and biomarker analyses. Disease assessment was performed on Cycle 1 Day 22 and at cycle end. Part 2 evaluates Karonudib at the RP2D in combination with idarubicin in R/R AML and high-risk MDS.

结论（EHA原文）

Karonudib was generally well tolerated with acceptable safety and preliminary clinical activity in R/R AML and MDS. The RP2D is now being evaluated in combination with idarubicin, with the aim of optimising delivery of this combination. The drug sensitivity screening shows strong correlation with prior and current clinical outcomes.

090CNSL前瞻性临床试验PCNSLBTKiPF992

在靶向治疗时代重新评估自体干细胞移植在原发性中枢神经系统弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤中的作用：一项倾向评分匹配的多中心现实研究

re‑evaluating the role of autologous stem cell transplantation in primary cns diffuse large b‑cell lymphoma in the targeted‑therapy era: a propensity score–matched multicenter real‑world study

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=291；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

分组：ASCT组/非ASCT组

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

主要终点：无进展生存期（PFS），ASCT组优于非ASCT组（p=0.023）；次要终点：总生存期（OS），ASCT组有获益趋势但未达统计学意义（p=0.085）。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The role of autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) in primary central nervous system diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (PCNS-DLBCL) is being re-evaluated, particularly in newly diagnosed patients, as BTK inhibitors (BTKi) and lenalidomide are increasingly used in induction, salvage, and maintenance therapy. In real-world clinical practice, ASCT allocation is influenced by baseline fitness and disease characteristics, highlighting the need for confounding control to assess outcomes and clarify whether post-induction consolidation strategies are key to long-term results in the Targeted Therapy era. Aims: This study aimed to evaluate the association between ASCT and progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) in patients with PCNS-DLBCL treated in the BTKi/lenalidomide era, using propensity score matching (PSM) to adjust for confounding factors. We also examined whether post-induction consolidation strategies (ASCT and/or maintenance) and BTKi/lenalidomide treatment pathways stratify outcomes, including among treatment responders. Methods: We conducted a retrospective, three-centre cohort study of PCNS-DLBCL patients treated in routine practice. The primary exposure was ASCT (yes vs no). PSM was performed using nearest-neighbour matching with a target ratio of 1:2 and caliper width of 0.1, adjusting for covariates listed in Table 1. Balance was assessed using standardized mean differences. Endpoints were PFS and OS, analyzed by Kaplan–Meier methods with log-rank comparisons. Prespecified exploratory analyses evaluated six subgroups based on regimen category (BTKi, lenalidomide, or neither) and ASCT status; four subgroups based on ASCT and maintenance therapy; and responder subsets (CR/PR and CR). All analyses were hypothesis-generating.

结论（EHA原文）

In patients with PCNS-DLBCL treated in the BTKi/lenalidomide era, ASCT was associated with improved PFS after PSM, while OS showed a favorable trend. Post-induction consolidation strategies most strongly differentiated long-term outcomes, with maintenance therapy being particularly beneficial for patients not receiving ASCT. Outcomes also varied by regimen type (BTKi-based, lenalidomide-based, or neither) and ASCT status. These findings support a risk-adapted approach for selecting ASCT and/or maintenance therapy, highlighting the need for prospective validation. Key survival curves are presented in the submitted figure.

中文结果摘录（原表）

主要终点：无进展生存期（PFS），ASCT组优于非ASCT组（p=0.023）；次要终点：总生存期（OS），ASCT组有获益趋势但未达统计学意义（p=0.085）。

091CNSL前瞻性临床试验PCNSL其他/未明确药物S257

通过脑脊液中的分子和免疫生物标志物诊断原发性中枢神经系统淋巴瘤：一项多中心前瞻性队列研究（pricelus）

diagnosing primary central nervous system lymphoma through molecular and immune biomarkers in cerebrospinal fluid: a multicentre prospective cohort study (pricelus)

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=255；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：diagnosing primary central nervous system lymphoma through molecular and immune biomarkers in cerebrospinal fluid: a multicentre prospective cohort study (pricelus)

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

单变量分析：6种细胞因子诊断AUC范围0.67-0.96|||MYD88-CSF检出率：56%的CNSL病例阳性，特异性99%|||多变量模型：MYD88-CSF、IL10、CXCL13独立与CNSL诊断相关|||三者组合：特异性100%，敏感性54%|||阴性预测值：三项标志物均阴性时阴性预测值为99.4%|||不确定患者：56例，其中36%为CNSL|||潜在避免活检比例：45%（13/29）的CNSL活检可能因阳性CSF标志物而避免

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is typically diagnosed by brain biopsy, a procedure with risks and diagnostic delay. Emerging cerebrospinal fluid (CSF) biomarkers, including the MYD88 L265P mutation in CSF (MYD88-CSF) and several cytokines, may improve diagnostic accuracy, but evidence is mostly derived from retrospective, non-consecutive cohorts. We conducted a nationwide, multicentre, prospective cohort study to validate the diagnostic utility of multiple CSF biomarkers in patients with suspected PCNSL. Aims: To prospectively validate the diagnostic performance of CSF biomarkers in suspected PCNSL and to construct a high-specificity diagnostic algorithm, with additional exploratory analyses of prognostic value, repeated lumbar puncture, and radiological features. Methods: Patients with suspected PCNSL who underwent CSF analysis were prospectively enrolled across five hospitals in the Netherlands between 2021 and 2025. Analyses focused on MYD88-CSF and cytokines with reported diagnostic value. Multivariable and LASSO regression were used to construct a diagnostic panel, followed by decision tree analysis to evaluate diagnostic performance. Exploratory analyses assessed associations between novel biomarkers and clinical outcomes. We also evaluated the diagnostic yield of repeated lumbar puncture and examined the relationship between radiological characteristics and CSF biomarker levels.

结论（EHA原文）

In this prospective, multicentre cohort of patients with suspected PCNSL, we validated the high diagnostic value of MYD88-CSF, IL10, and CXCL13. In selected clinical scenarios, combined CSF biomarker testing may be sufficient for a diagnosis, without the need for brain biopsy, although results should be interpreted within the full clinical context. For patients not fulfilling the CSF biomarker threshold diagnostic brain biopsy remains necessary.

092CNSL前瞻性临床试验SCNSL/CNS复发或预防CAR-T/细胞治疗PF983

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤car-t复发后的治疗模式和临床结果，重点是二次car-t治疗

post–car-t relapse in cns-involved lymphoma: treatment patterns and clinical outcomes with a focus on second car-t therapy

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=77

I 干预措施

分组：由于是回顾性研究，未进行前瞻性随机分组，但根据治疗后分为：；组1：第二次CAR-T治疗；组2：非CAR-T治疗（包括化疗、靶向治疗、放疗）；组3：CD3×CD20双特异性抗体治疗；组4：无进一步治疗

C 对照措施

对照/比较：由于是回顾性研究，未进行前瞻性随机分组，但根据治疗后分为： 组1：第二次CAR-T治疗 组2：非CAR-T治疗（包括化疗、靶向治疗、放疗） 组3：CD3×CD20双特异性抗体治疗 组4：无进一步治疗

O 结局指标

总缓解率（ORR）：57.1%（16/28） 完全缓解率（CR）：46.4%（13/28） 第二次CAR-T组中位无进展生存期（PFS）：6.28个月 第二次CAR-T组中位总生存期（OS）：15.81个月 非CAR-T组中位OS：8.55个月（p≈0.068） 细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）：发生23例（82.1%），均为1-2级 免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）：发生9例（32.1%），仅1例≥3级

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Patients with central nervous system (CNS)-involved lymphoma are often excluded from CAR-T clinical trials. Treatment strategies and outcomes after CAR-T failure in this population remain unclear. Aims: This study aimed to characterize relapse patterns and post-relapse treatment outcomes in CNS-involved lymphoma patients, with a focus on the efficacy and safety of second CAR-T therapy. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed CNS-involved lymphoma patients who relapsed after first CAR-T therapy. Patients were grouped according to post-relapse treatment: second CAR-T, non-CAR-T therapy, or no further treatment. Overall survival (OS) and progression-free survival (PFS) were evaluated, and efficacy and safety of second CAR-T therapy were assessed.

结论（EHA原文）

CNS-involved lymphoma patients have poor prognosis after CAR-T failure, and post-relapse treatment patterns are highly heterogeneous. Second CAR-T therapy can achieve high initial response rates and shows a trend toward improved survival in selected patients, though mortality remains substantial. Further studies with larger cohorts and prospective design are warranted to clarify its true benefit.

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：大剂量甲氨蝶呤（HD-MTX）为基础化疗后，有效者接受自体干细胞移植（ASCT）和/或全脑放疗（WBRT）；无效者接受脑部放疗或鞘内化疗（ITC）作为桥接，继以CAR-T细胞治疗或ASCT

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CNS involvement in PMLBCL is rare and associated with poor outcomes. The clinical features, prognosis and efficacy of modern CNS-directed therapies, including autologous transplantation (ASCT), and anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy (CAR-T), remain poorly defined. Aims: To provide management recommendations for CNS involvement in PMLBCL in routine practice. Methods: Data on pts with PMLBCL and CNS involvement at diagnosis or relapse treated between 2001 and 2024 in 27 centers across 7 countries were analyzed (NCT06024694).

结论（EHA原文）

In the largest series reported to date, durable remissions were achieved in PMLBCL pts with early CNS relapse treated with HD-MTX–based chemo followed by ASCT and/or brain irradiation. CAR-T, preceded by brain irradiation or ITC as bridging, provides long-term disease control even in HD-MTX-refractory pts. In contrast, late CNS involvement in multiply relapsed PMLBCL has a dismal prognosis.

genomic determinants of response and resistance to zanubrutinib in relapsed/refractory primary cns lymphoma: baseline biomarker analysis from the prizm+ trial

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=19

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：泽布替尼；靶点：BTK；类别：化药；分组：试验组1：泽布替尼
