客观缓解率（ORR，2周期后）：11/19例（57.9%）达到完全或部分缓解|||持久缓解（定义为>12个月无进展）：6/19例（31.6%）|||早期进展（12个月内）：其余患者|||CD79B突变在持久缓解者中富集（80% vs 38%）|||MHC I类基因缺失与较短PFS显著相关（HR 4.31, 95% CI 1.12-16.64, P=0.03）|||全基因组倍增（WGD）仅出现在早期进展患者中（31%）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is a rare, aggressive B-cell lymphoma confined to the CNS with frequent relapse after initial therapy and poor outcomes in the relapsed/refractory ( rr ) setting, particularly among older or transplant-ineligible patients. PRiZM + is a phase II platform trial in rrPCNSL ; cohort 1 evaluat es Zanubrutinib monotherapy, targeting constitutive B-cell receptor (BCR) signa l ling that characterizes this disease. R esponse assessment relies primarily on conventional MRI, w ith recognised limitations in distinguishing viable tumo u r from treatment-related effects, and no other prognostic or predictive biomarkers currently guide therapy. Repeat brain biopsies at relapse are rarely feasible due to procedural risk , making archival diagnostic tissue the only feasible source for tissue-based biomarker evaluation . Aims: To determine whether genomic features of diagnostic PCNSL biopsies predict response and durability to Zanubrutinib in rrPCNSL patients enrolled in PRiZM + cohort 1 . Methods: G enomic DNA from formalin-fixed diagnostic brain biopsies from 19 of 20 enrolled patients (pts) in PRiZM + cohort 1 underwent w hole-exome sequencing for mutation profiling, copy number analysis and molecular subt yping using LymphGen and DLBclass classifiers . P rimary endpoint was overall response rate after two Zanubrutinib cycles. Associations with progression-free survival (PFS) were evaluated using univaria ble and multivariable analyses.

结论（EHA原文）

D isruption of MHC class I - associated genes in diagnostic tumour tissue predicts e POD on BTK i therapy and appears more prognostic than early MRI response. These findings implicate immune evasion as a potential mechanism of resistance to BTK inhibition in rrPCNSL and support the value of genomic profiling of diagnostic tissue to aid response prediction .

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Baseline genomic landscape was consistent with prior PCNSL studies, with recurrent mutations in MYD88 (53%), CD79B (47%) and CARD11 (47%). Recurrent copy-number alterations included gains at 3p22.3, 3q29, and 7q21.3 and deletions at 1p13.1, 6p21.32, and 6q21, affecting genes such as BTG2 , CD58 , PRDM1 , and HLA class I/II loci. Whole-genome duplication (WGD) occurred in four tumours and was associated with markedly increased genomic instability. Molecular subtyping assigned 52.6% (10/19) of cases to the DLBclass MYD88/CD79B-driven C5 subtype and 10.5% (2/19) being C2 tumours enriched for TP53 alterations, genomic instability and disruption of MHC class I genes. Concordance between DLBclass and LymphGen classifiers was high. Conclusion: D isruption of MHC class I - associated genes in diagnostic tumour tissue predicts e POD on BTK i therapy and appears more prognostic than early MRI response. These findings implicate immune evasion as a potential mechanism of resistance to BTK inhibition in rrPCNSL and support the value of genomic profiling of diagnostic tissue to aid response prediction .

real-world durable clinical benefits of tirabrutinib and its safety profile in relapsed or refractory primary central nervous system lymphoma: interim analysis from the reveal study

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=19；疾病阶段：复发/难治，原发性

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：替拉鲁替尼；靶点：BTK；类别：化药；分组：试验组：tirabrutinib

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

客观缓解率(ORR)：63.2% (12/19) 完全缓解(CR)：3例 未确认完全缓解(unconfirmed CR)：1例 部分缓解(PR)：8例 中位至缓解时间(TTR)：2.2个月 累积持续缓解率：83.3% (95% CI: 51.6–97.9) 中位缓解持续时间(DOR)：未达到 (95%CI下限: 10.1个月) 治疗相关不良事件(TRAEs)：57.9% 常见不良事件：尿路感染21.1%，白细胞减少15.8%，皮疹15.8% 治疗相关严重不良事件：2例（尿路感染1例，脑出血1例）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Tirabrutinib is a potent, second-generation, highly selective Bruton’s tyrosine kinase inhibitor approved in Taiwan for relapsed or refractory (r/r) primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) based on ONO-4059-02. While clinical trials are promising, real-world evidence regarding the durability of clinical benefit and safety management patterns in routine practice is essential to consolidate its therapeutic role. Aims: We conducted the first nationwide study (the REVEAL study; NCT06714370) in Taiwan to evaluate the real-world effectiveness of tirabrutinib, focusing on response characteristics, and its safety profile. Methods: This REVEAL study enrolled patients aged ≥18 years with r/r PCNSL receiving NHI (National Health Insurance)-reimbursed tirabrutinib monotherapy across 6 medical centers. Efficacy endpoints included objective response rate (ORR), time-to-response (TTR), and duration of response (DOR). Safety endpoints included incidence of adverse events (AEs).

结论（EHA原文）

Tirabrutinib provides rapid and durable treatment responses over a 10.9-month follow-up period in r/r PCNSL patients. These results, along with high cumulative durability and a consistent safety profile, support its role as a key targeted therapy in real-world clinical practice in Taiwan.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: At the data cutoff (September 2025) for the first interim analysis, 19 patients were enrolled. With median follow-up of 10.9 months, tirabrutinib provided promising effectiveness with an ORR of 63.2% (12/19 [complete response in 3, unconfirmed CR in 1, partial response in 8 patients]). The response was characterized by a rapid onset, with a median TTR of 2.2 months. Notably, treatment responses were resilient: among 12 responders, 10 maintained their response during the follow-up period, resulting in a cumulative durable response rate of 83.3% (95% CI: 51.6–97.9). The median DOR has not yet been reached (lower bound 95%CI: 10.1 months). Swimmer plot revealed unique real-world patterns where 9 patients (47.4%) derived continued clinical benefit from ongoing treatment despite initial radiographic assessments of stable disease or initial progression, highlighting that symptomatic stability often guides treatment continuation beyond imaging results. The safety profile was manageable (treatment-emergent AEs 73.7%); common events were urinary tract infection (21.1%), white blood cell count decrease (15.8%), and rash (15.8%). No new safety signals or significant cardiovascular toxicities were observed. Treatment-related AEs (TRAEs) occurred in 57.9% of patients with the majority of onsets occurring within the first 3 months. Treatment-related serious AEs occurred in 2 patients (urinary tract infection in 1 and cerebral haemorrhage in 1 patient). TRAEs were mostly transient; specifically, skin rashes resolved with a median time of 11.5 days. Two Grade 5 events were reported but assessed as unrelated to the treatment. Conclusion: Tirabrutinib provides rapid and durable treatment responses over a 10.9-month follow-up period in r/r PCNSL patients. These results, along with high cumulative durability and a consistent safety profile, support its role as a key targeted therapy in real-world clinical practice in Taiwan.

efficacy and safety of orelabrutinib combined with sintilimab in patients with relapsed/refractory primary central nervous system lymphoma (r/r pcnsl): a prospective multicenter phase ii study

总体缓解率（ORR）：60.7% (17/28) 完全缓解（CR）：28.6% 未确认CR（CRu）：7.1% 部分缓解（PR）：25.0% 疾病控制率（DCR）：78.6% (22/28) 中位无进展生存期（PFS）：8.4个月 1年PFS率：49.7% (95% CI: 34.2-72.3%) 2年PFS率：40.7% (95% CI: 25.5-64.9%) 中位总生存期（OS）：未达到 1年OS率：77.4% (95% CI: 63.0-95.1%) 2年OS率：73.3% (95% CI: 58.2-92.5%) 中位缓解持续时间（DOR）：49.7个月 治疗相关不良事件（TEAEs）：72.4% (21/29) 3-4级TEAEs：13.8% (4/29) 5级事件：无 常见不良事件：疲乏39.3%、出血35.7%、白细胞减少32.1%、感染35.7%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: PCNSL is an aggressive non-Hodgkin lymphoma. While high-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX)-based regimens are first-line standards for newly diagnosed patients, disease relapse remains a major clinical challenge. R/R PCNSL has poor outcomes with high recurrence and limited therapies, and no standard treatment exists, representing an unmet need. Preclinical studies have shown synergistic efficacy of BTK inhibitors (BTKi) plus anti-PD-1 antibodies in B-cell lymphoma (Vincent-Fabert et al. Cell Commun Signal. 2019). Orelabrutinib, a novel BTKi with high CNS penetrance, exhibits efficacy in PCNSL with minimal off-target effects and acceptable safety; sintilimab is a next-generation anti-PD-1 monoclonal antibody. Aims: To evaluate the safety and efficacy of orelabrutinib combined with sintilimab in patients with R/R PCNSL. Methods: This prospective, multicenter, single-arm phase II study (NCT04899427) enrolled immunocompetent adults with R/R PCNSL and eligible organ function. Patients received orelabrutinib (150 mg once daily) plus sintilimab (200 mg on day 1 of each cycle) every 3 weeks for up to 2 years, until progression, unacceptable toxicity, or death. The primary endpoint was the overall response rate (ORR), defined as achievement of partial response (PR) or better, following four cycles of treatment. Secondary endpoints included the 1-year progression-free survival (PFS) rate and safety.

结论（EHA原文）

This prospective phase II study demonstrates that combining orelabrutinib with sintilimab provided significant clinical benefits for patients with R/R PCNSL, including strong response rates and notably durable responses. The manageable safety profile further supports this combination as a valuable treatment option for this challenging population.

orelabrutinib in patients with relapsed or refractory primary or secondary central nervous system lymphoma: a multicenter, open-label, phase ii study

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=61

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Patients with relapsed or refractory primary or secondary central nervous system lymphoma (r/r PCNSL/SCNSL) have a poor prognosis and limited treatment options. Orelabrutinib is a highly selective, irreversible Bruton's tyrosine kinase (BTK) inhibitor with promising preclinical blood-brain barrier penetration. Aims: Evaluate the antitumor efficacy, safety and pharmacokinetics of orelabrutinib in r/r PCNSL/SCNSL patients. Methods: This was a single-arm, multicenter, open-label, phase II trial (Clinical Trial Registration No.: CTR20190854) conducted at 8 sites in China. Employing a Simon's two-stage design, 16 patients were initially enrolled to receive orelabrutinib 150 mg once daily (QD), with ≥4 responders required to proceed to stage two. After meeting the pre-specified efficacy threshold, the study proceeded to stage two, expanding to a total of 39 patients at 150 mg QD and adding 22 patients at an exploratory dose of 200 mg QD. The primary endpoint was objective response rate (ORR) assessed by investigators per International Primary CNS Lymphoma Collaborative Group (IPCG) criteria. Secondary endpoints included disease control rate (DCR), duration of response (DOR), progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS), safety, and pharmacokinetics (PK).

结论（EHA原文）

Orelabrutinib monotherapy demonstrated preliminary antitumor activity and a manageable safety profile in patients with r/r PCNSL/SCNSL, a population with high unmet medical need. Its favorable blood-brain barrier penetration supports further investigation in CNS lymphomas.

客观缓解率(ORR)：总人群83.8%(31/37)，ORT组72.7%(8/11)，ORT+HD-MTX组88.5%(23/26) 完全缓解率(CR)：总人群78.4%(29/37)，ORT组63.6%(7/11)，ORT+HD-MTX组84.6%(22/26) MCD亚组完全缓解率：83.3%(15/18) 中位无进展生存期(PFS)：总人群未达到，ORT组18.3个月，ORT+HD-MTX组未达到 1年无进展生存率：总人群85.8%，ORT组81.8%，ORT+HD-MTX组87.4% 2年无进展生存率：总人群73.1%，ORT组43.8%，ORT+HD-MTX组87.4% 中位总生存期(OS)：总人群未达到 1年总生存率：总人群96.4% 2年总生存率：总人群92.7% 3-4级不良事件发生率：28.2%(11/39)，最常见为白细胞减少和中性粒细胞减少 PFS组间差异：p=0.016

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is a rare form of non-Hodgkin's lymphoma, predominantly diffuse large B-cell lymphomas. High-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX) is the cornerstone of chemotherapy for newly diagnosed PCNSL. Orelabrutinib is a novel BTKi with high blood-brain barrier permeability and has demonstrated efficacy on PCNSL with minimal off-target effects and higher safety. Aims: This study aimed to evaluate the efficacy and safety of a combination regimen consisting of ORT, with or without HD-MTX, in untreated PCNSL patients (pts). Methods: This prospective, multicenter, single-arm, study enrolled untreated PCNSL pts (≥18 years) who received ORT therapy: orelabrutinib 150 mg/day orally, rituximab 375 mg/m² intravenously on day 0, and thiotepa 40mg/m² intravenously on day 1, in a 21-day cycle. HD-MTX (3.5g/m² IV) was administered every 3 weeks to pts ≤60 years with normal renal function. After 4 cycles, pts with a response continued the same dose for up to 4 more cycles, with autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) recommended for those ≤60 years. Maintenance therapy with orelabrutinib continued until 2 years of treatment. Adverse events (AEs) were graded according to Standard 5.0 Common Terminology for Adverse Events. The primary endpoint was the objective response rate (ORR) with secondary endpoints including progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS).

结论（EHA原文）

This study demonstrates that ORT plus HD-MTX can serve as the preferred regimen for patients ≤60 years of age, whereas ORT monotherapy represents a viable alternative for patients >60 years or with renal insufficiency; nevertheless, the rational use of MTX remains a critical determinant for achieving long-term cure in PCNSL.

099CNSL前瞻性临床试验SCNSL/CNS复发或预防BTKiPS2084

替拉鲁替尼治疗复发或难治性继发性中枢神经系统淋巴瘤的疗效和安全性：ii期crystal/ncch2201研究结果

efficacy and safety of tirabrutinib for relapsed or refractory secondary central nervous system lymphoma: results of the phase ii crystal/ncch2201 study

P 患者群体

B细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤，中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=20；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：替拉鲁替尼；靶点：BTK；类别：化药；分组：试验组1：tirabrutinib

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

客观缓解率（ORR）: 66.7%（95% CI 41.0-86.7） 完全缓解率（CR）: 38.9% 部分缓解率（PR）: 27.8% 中位无进展生存期（PFS）: 10.6个月（95% CI 2.8-未达到） 中位总生存期（OS）: 未达到 最常见的治疗相关不良事件（TRAE）: 中性粒细胞减少（80%），淋巴细胞减少（70%），皮疹（55%），发热性中性粒细胞减少（10%）等。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Secondary central nervous system lymphoma (SCNSL) is a devastating complication of systemic lymphoma with limited treatment options. Recent real-world data suggest a median overall survival (OS) of 3.2 months after SCNSL, highlighting a substantial unmet need (Blood Adv. 2025;9:893–905). Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) represents the most common histology of SCNSL and is frequently enriched for activating mutations in MYD88 and CD79B , providing a molecular rationale for Bruton’s tyrosine kinase (BTK) inhibition. Tirabrutinib, a selective second-generation BTK inhibitor, has demonstrated clinical activity in primary CNS lymphoma and is approved in Japan for the relapsed or refractory (R/R) setting. Aims: To evaluate the efficacy and safety of tirabrutinib in patients with R/R SCNSL. Methods: This trial was an investigator-initiated phase II CRYSTAL/NCCH2201 study (jRCT2031220529). Eligible patients had histologically confirmed B-cell non-Hodgkin lymphoma with R/R secondary CNS involvement. Patients with active systemic disease outside the CNS were excluded. Patients were required to have received high-dose methotrexate–based therapy or be intolerant to it. Tirabrutinib was administered orally at 480 mg once daily until disease progression or unacceptable toxicity. The primary endpoint was objective response rate (ORR) as determined by the IPCG criteria, assessed by independent central review (ICR). Blood and tumor samples were collected for exploratory biomarker analyses. The expected ORR was set at 40% and the threshold ORR at 10%. Accounting for up to four ineligible or untreated patients, the planned sample size was set at 20 to achieve 80% power under a binomial test with a one-sided alpha of 2.5%.

结论（EHA原文）

Tirabrutinib demonstrated clinically meaningful activity with a manageable safety profile in heavily pretreated patients with R/R SCNSL. The phase II CRYSTAL/NCCH2201 study supports tirabrutinib as a promising therapeutic option for this disease with extremely poor prognosis.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Twenty patients were enrolled between February 2023 and December 2024. The median age was 75 years (range, 48–81), and all patients had DLBCL, not otherwise specified (DLBCL-NOS) with secondary CNS involvement. Central pathological review classified 9 patients as the germinal center B-cell–like (GCB) subtype, 10 as the non-GCB subtype, and 1 patient as unclassifiable. Three patients had cerebrospinal fluid disease, including one without parenchymal lesions. The median number of prior therapies was 3.5 (range, 1–8). Eighteen patients were evaluable for efficacy by ICR. The ORR was 66.7% (95% CI, 41.0–86.7; p Conclusion: Tirabrutinib demonstrated clinically meaningful activity with a manageable safety profile in heavily pretreated patients with R/R SCNSL. The phase II CRYSTAL/NCCH2201 study supports tirabrutinib as a promising therapeutic option for this disease with extremely poor prognosis.

phase i/ii study of zanubrutinib in combination with rituximab, ifosfamide, carboplatin, and etoposide in relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: interim results of the phase ii part

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=52；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

总人群：ORR 90.9%，CR率72.7%|||队列A：ORR 90.3%，CR率74.2%|||队列B：ORR 92.3%，CR率69.2%|||中位随访5.8个月，6个月PFS率76.3%，6个月OS率90.0%|||队列A：6个月PFS率83.2%，6个月OS率100.0%|||队列B：6个月PFS率62.3%，6个月OS率71.6%|||11例患者（均来自队列A）接受了前期ASCT，截至数据截止无事件|||最常见≥3级不良事件：中性粒细胞减少46.0%，血小板减少46.0%，贫血29.0%|||发热性中性粒细胞减少5例(10.0%)|||1例死于治疗相关脓毒症，无患者因AE停止治疗

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The prognosis of relapsed or refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (R/R DLBCL) is poor, and outcomes are particularly dismal for R/R CNS lymphomas (primary [PCNSL] or secondary [SCNSL]). R-ICE (rituximab, ifosfamide, carboplatin, and etoposide) chemotherapy has shown efficacy in these patients (pts) but the durability of response is limited. Recently, BTK inhibitors have demonstrated encouraging efficacy outcomes in systemic R/R non-GCB DLBCL and R/R CNS lymphomas. Aims: This phase I/II study aims to evaluate the efficacy, safety, and feasibility of combining zanubrutinib, a second-generation BTK inhibitor, with R-ICE (ZR-ICE) in pts with R/R systemic non-GCB DLBCL or R/R CNS lymphomas. Here we report the interim efficacy and safety results from the phase II part. Methods: In the phase I part, zanubrutinib 160 mg daily was established as the recommended phase 2 dose based on a standard 3+3 dose escalation design. In the phase II part, pts with R/R systemic non-GCB DLBCL (cohort A) or R/R CNS lymphomas (PCNSL or SCNSL) (cohort B) received zanubrutinib 160 mg daily in combination with R-ICE. The R-ICE regimen consisted of rituximab 375 mg/m² IV (D1), ifosfamide 1670 mg/m² IV (D1–3), etoposide 100 mg/m²/day IV (D1–3), and carboplatin AUC 5 IV (D2). Pts who were candidates for upfront autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) and achieved CR or PR after 3 cycles proceeded to ASCT. Pts who were not candidates for upfront ASCT received up to 6 cycles of ZR-ICE. Cohort B pts achieving CR or PR after 6 cycles of ZR-ICE or 3 cycles of ZR-ICE followed by ASCT received zanubrutinib 320 mg daily as maintenance for up to 24 months.

结论（EHA原文）

ZR-ICE demonstrated promising efficacy with a manageable safety profile in R/R systemic non-GCB DLBCL and R/R CNS lymphomas. These interim results support continued enrollment of this ongoing phase II study.

medz-r方案作为新诊断的原发性中枢神经系统淋巴瘤诱导治疗的真实疗效和安全性

real-world efficacy and safety of the medz-r regimen as induction therapy in newly diagnosed primary central nervous system lymphoma

P 患者群体

I 干预措施

客观缓解率(ORR): 93.0% 完全缓解率(CR): 91.2% 中位随访22.0个月 1年无进展生存率(PFS): 84.7% 1年总生存率(OS): 87.5% 接受巩固/维持治疗者1年PFS: 100%; 未接受者: 80.0% (p=0.0033) 治疗相关不良事件(TRAEs): 77.9% (多为1-2级) 3-4级血液学毒性: 白细胞减少 23.7%, 血小板减少 15.3% 肝毒性: 23.7% (1-2级) 肾毒性: 23.7% (1-2级) 3-4级感染: 5.1% 出血事件: 3.4% (轻度)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is a rare and aggressive non-Hodgkin lymphoma with a poorer prognosis compared to systemic diffuse large B-cell lymphoma. High-dose methotrexate-based combinations remain the cornerstone of induction therapy, but outcomes are still suboptimal. Our previous phase II trial reported a complete response (CR) rate exceeding 90% with the MEDZ-R regimen in newly diagnosed PCNSL patients under 70. Aims: To evaluate the real-world efficacy and safety of the MEDZ-R regimen as induction therapy in newly diagnosed PCNSL. Methods: This multicenter, retrospective real-world study enrolled newly diagnosed PCNSL patients from five institutions. Patients received 5-6 cycles of the MEDZ-R regimen: rituximab (375 mg/m2, day 0), methotrexate (3.5 g/m2, day 1), etoposide (50 mg/m2, days 3–5), liposomal doxorubicin (30 mg/m2, day 3), and zanubrutinib (160mg BID, days 3–21) every 3 weeks. Consolidation (reduced-dose radiotherapy or autologous stem cell transplantation) or maintenance was recommended for patients achieving CR. Radiological assessment was performed every two cycles during induction. Primary endpoint was CR rate. Secondary endpoints included objective response rate (ORR), PFS, OS, and safety (CTCAE v5.0).

结论（EHA原文）

In this real-world study, the MEDZ-R regimen demonstrated high efficacy (CR >90%) and a manageable safety profile as induction for newly diagnosed PCNSL. These findings support its potential as a promising treatment option.

12 years update on overall survival in patients with primary central nervous system lymphoma (pcnsl) treated with high-dose chemotherapy and temozolomide

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=40；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Treatment of primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is associated with low response rates and poor survival using conventional radio and chemotherapy. Due to its favorable toxicity profile, temozolomide has emerged as a new option for treatment of PCNSL in young patients. In this study, we report a series of PCNSL patients treated with an innovative regimen combining high dose of both cytarabine and methotrexate with temozolomide without radiotherapy or intrathecal chemotherapy. Aims: It is to evaluate the combination of Temozolomide, high dose of both Cytarabine and Methotrexate without radiotherapy. This study evaluates the overall survival after 12 years of publication of our first report. Methods: The study was performed at that time at Almwassat charity hospital and al Bairouni university cancer center. Forty patients with histologically confirmed PCNSL median age 52 years (range 20-65) years were included. Biopsies were cultured, and a karyotyping was made in 32 patients. An induction chemotherapy was started, and methotrexate 3 gr/m² over 12 h on day 1, cytarabine 3 gr/m² every 12 h on day 1 and temozolomide 150 mg/m² from day 2 through day 6 with a total of 6 cycles were given monthly. Patients were evaluated every 3 months by magnetic resonance (MRI) with contrast.

结论（EHA原文）

After the publication of our first report in 2013, treatment of PCNSL with high dose chemotherapy and Temozolomide seems to give a prolonged overall survival rate compared with other studies with minimal long-term toxicity.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Elderly patients with primary CNS lymphoma (PCNSL) are frequently unsuitable for consolidative whole-brain radiotherapy (WBRT) or autologous stem-cell transplantation (ASCT) because of neurotoxicity and treatment-related risks. Lenalidomide is active in relapsed PCNSL, but prospective data on its use as maintenance are limited. Aims: This study aimed to assess the efficacy and tolerability of lenalidomide maintenance in elderly, consolidation-ineligible patients with primary CNS lymphoma following methotrexate-based chemoimmunotherapy. Methods: We conducted a multicenter phase II trial of lenalidomide maintenance in adults with PCNSL who achieved partial response after 2–6 cycles of methotrexate- and rituximab-based chemoimmunotherapy and were not candidates for WBRT/ASCT. Lenalidomide 15 mg was given orally on days 1–21 of 28-day cycles for up to 12 cycles or until progression or toxicity. The primary endpoint was 2-year progression-free survival (PFS) from maintenance initiation.

结论（EHA原文）

Lenalidomide maintenance after chemoimmunotherapy is feasible in elderly, consolidation-unsuitable PCNSL patients and warrants further evaluation in comparative trials.

the optimate-trial: an investigator-initiated randomized phase iii study to optimize matrix induction in newly diagnosed primary cns lymphoma (trial in progress)

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=298；疾病阶段：初治，原发性

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：Arm A（4周期MATRix）；试验组2：Arm B（R-MTX预处理后接2周期MATRix）

C 对照措施

O 结局指标

安全性分析人群共298例（Arm A：147例，Arm B：151例）|||至少发生1次3-5级不良事件：Arm A 90.5%，Arm B 86.8%|||诱导期间3-5级不良事件：Arm A 89.8%（132/147），Arm B 83.4%（126/151）|||巩固期间/后3-5级不良事件：Arm A 72.6%（61/84），Arm B 73.0%（84/115）|||致死性不良事件（5级）：诱导期共9例（Arm A 7例，Arm B 2例），巩固期/后共7例（均为Arm B）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary CNS lymphoma (PCNSL) is an aggressive extranodal diffuse large B-cell lymphoma with a dismal prognosis. Curative-intend treatments are associated with substantial toxicity. Induction with MATRix followed by high-dose chemotherapy and autologous stem cell transplantation (HDT-ASCT) is widely used in fit patients ≤70 years. The OptiMATe trial (NCT04931368) evaluates whether a de-escalation of induction can reduce treatment associated morbidity while maintaining efficacy and increasing the proportion of patients who proceed to consolidation HDT-ASCT. Aims: To compare event-free survival (EFS) between standard induction therapy and a de-escalated induction strategy in patients with newly diagnosed PCNSL. Methods: OptiMATe is a multicentre, open-label, randomized phase III trial across 68 European centres enrolling immunocompetent patients ≤70 years with newly diagnosed PCNSL. Patients are randomized 1:1 to Arm A (four MATRix cycles) or Arm B (R-MTX pre-treatment followed by two MATRix cycles). Patients achieving at least partial remission proceed to thiotepa-conditioned high-dose chemotherapy and HDT-ASCT. The primary endpoint is EFS; key secondary endpoints include overall and progression-free survival, safety, neurocognition, and quality of life, with a minimum follow-up of 24 months.

结论（EHA原文）

This is the largest randomized phase III de-escalation trial in newly diagnosed primary CNS lymphoma. The study has shown excellent feasibility, outstanding recruitment, and no unexpected toxicity signals. The most recent follow-up and safety data will be presented. \n The study is supported by the German Federal Ministry for Research, Technology, and Space (BMFTR) and Cancer Research UK. The sponsor of the trial is Klinikum Stuttgart, UK sites are coordinated by Cancer Research UK Southampton Clinical Trials Unit and Italian sites by the International Extranodal Lymphoma Study Group.

high doses of methotrexate and cytarabine with or without intravitreal methotrexate injections in a cohort of 31 hiv-negative patients with primary vitreoretinal lymphoma

P 患者群体

原发性玻璃体视网膜淋巴瘤；N=31；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

最佳客观缓解率(ORR): 97% (30/31, 95% CI 78-99) 完全缓解(CR): 90% (28/31) 中位随访时间: 30个月（范围5-112） 2年无进展生存率(PFS): 49% (95% CI 28.2-66.6) 2年总生存率(OS): 85% (95% CI 64.4-94.0) 复发率: 48% (15/31)，其中仅眼部复发13%，仅脑部复发40%，两者均有47% 死亡: 9例(28%)，其中6例死于淋巴瘤

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary vitreoretinal lymphoma (PVRL) is a rare large B‑cell lymphoma involving the vitreous and/or retina, with a high risk of CNS dissemination. Optimal management remains undefined: most reported series have been managed with local treatments (intravitreal methotrexate [IVT‑MTX] and ocular radiotherapy [ORT]), which offer limited CNS protection, while the benefit of intensified systemic regimens adapted from PCNSL is still uncertain. Aims: To evaluate efficacy and tolerability of high‑dose methotrexate–cytarabine (MA)–based chemotherapy ± IVT‑MTX in PVRL patients (pts) treated in two referral Italian centres. Methods: HIV‑negative pts with ocular symptom‑driven referral treated between 2015 and 2025 were included based on: 1) diagnosis of PVRL via ophthalmologic assessment, with confirmation by conventional cytology and/or biomarkers (e.g., MYD88 L265P , elevated IL‑10, clonal IGH) in ocular fluids; 2) MA‑based first‑line treatment ± IVT‑MTX; pts with extra‑ocular disease (inside or outside the CNS) were excluded. Responses per IPCG criteria. Biomarker groups were defined as single positive (MYD88 L265P or high IL‑10) or double‑positive.

结论（EHA原文）

MA–based chemotherapy ±IVT‑MTX achieved high response rates with acceptable toxicity in PVRL. Relapse occurred in 48% of patients, predominantly involving the brain—alone or combined with ocular disease—whereas isolated ocular relapse was uncommon. The potential benefit of consolidative approaches (ORT or ASCT) and the high detectability of CSF molecular biomarkers warrant prospective evaluation. \n \n

106DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S283

综合多组分分析确定了与大b细胞淋巴瘤car-t治疗后不同结果相关的基因组亚型

integrated multi-omic profiling identifies genomic subtypes associated with differential outcomes after car-t therapy in large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=112

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Lisocabtagene maraleucel；Tisagenlecleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

1. BN2亚型 vs 其他亚型：PFS 16% (95% CI 6-46, p=0.017)，PFS6显著更低(p=0.009)，CR率显著更低(p=0.041) 2. 多变量Cox回归：BN2与较差的PFS和PFS6独立相关(均p<0.05) 3. 炎症TME亚型：1年PFS 19% (95% CI 7-52) 4. DHIT阳性 vs DHIT阴性：1年PFS 46% vs 31%（数值上有利） 5. GCB亚组中，DZsig阳性与阴性PFS相似（因样本量小未正式检验）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Outcomes after CD19-directed CAR-T cell therapy in large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) remain heterogeneous and are not fully explained by established clinical prognostic models. Tumor genomic architecture and microenvironmental states may influence CAR-T efficacy, but their integrated impact in real-world cohorts remains incompletely defined. We performed a multi-omic analysis to identify biological determinants of clinical variability after CAR-T therapy. Aims: To define tumor-intrinsic genomic and transcriptomic features associated with resistance to CAR-T cell therapy in LBCL. Methods: We conducted a retrospective cohort study of patients with LBCL treated with commercial CAR-T therapy between 2016 and 2022. Pre-CAR-T tumor specimens underwent whole-exome sequencing (WES) and RNA sequencing (RNA-seq), followed by integrated genomic and transcriptomic analyses using a standardized multi-omic computational pipeline (BostonGene, Waltham, MA). Genomic subtypes were assigned using the established LymphGen framework ( Wright et al . , Cancer cell, 2020 ) and Lymphly, a hierarchical genomic classification algorithm developed to improve molecular stratification of LBCL. The tumor microenvironment (TME), and double hit signature (DHIT) were classified according to Kotlov et al . ( Cancer Discovery, 2021 ), dark zone (DZsig) signature in accordance with Harris et al. ( Leukemia Lymphoma , 2025). Associations between molecular features and progression-free survival (PFS), 6-month PFS (PFS6), and complete response (CR) were evaluated. Subgroups with fewer than 10 cases were excluded from statistical comparisons but retained for visualization.

结论（EHA原文）

Multi-omic profiling identifies biologically defined high-risk subgroups after CAR-T therapy, highlighting BN2 as a genomically driven resistance phenotype. Genomic classification may refine patient selection and enable mechanism-based therapeutic strategies in LBCL.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Among 112 patients with available molecular data, median follow-up was 66 months (IQR 46-73). CAR-T products included axicabtagene ciloleucel (49%), tisagenlecleucel (38%), and lisocabtagene maraleucel (13%). Fifty-four percent of tumors were germinal center B-cell type, 46% activated B-cell type, and 17% were DHIT-positive. \n WES data were available in 99 patients. BostonGene’s Lymphly classifier assigned genomic subtypes to a larger proportion of evaluable cases compared with LymphGen and demonstrated improved outcome discrimination ( Fig. 1A ). Inferior outcomes were primarily driven by the BN2 subtype, which was associated with worse PFS (16%, 95% CI 6-46, p=0.017), lower PFS6 (p=0.009), and reduced CR rates (p=0.041) compared with other evaluable subgroups ( Fig. 1B ). In multivariable Cox models adjusting for relevant clinical covariates, BN2 remained independently associated with inferior PFS and PFS6 (both p \n RNA-seq data were available for 55 patients. RNA-defined TME subtypes and DHIT status were not significantly associated with PFS in univariable analyses. The inflammatory TME subtype demonstrated numerically inferior outcomes, with a 1-year PFS of 19% (95% CI 7-52) compared with 36% and 41% in the mesenchymal and depleted subtypes, respectively, whereas DHIT-positive cases showed numerically favorable 1-year PFS (46% vs 31%) ( Fig. 1C ). Within the GCB subgroup, the Dzsig showed similar PFS between DZsig-positive and DZsig-negative cases ( Fig 1D ); formal statistical testing was not performed due to limited sample size. Conclusion: Multi-omic profiling identifies biologically defined high-risk subgroups after CAR-T therapy, highlighting BN2 as a genomically driven resistance phenotype. Genomic classification may refine patient selection and enable mechanism-based therapeutic strategies in LBCL.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: High-grade B cell lymphoma (HGBL) not otherwise specified (NOS) and HGBL with MYC and BCL2 rearrangements (HGBL-MYC/BCL2) are considered distinct entities in the WHO 5th edition classification. Both represent difficult-to-treat subtypes, particularly in the relapsed/refractory (R/R) setting. As the standardized diagnostic category “HGBL with MYC and BCL2 rearrangements” is relatively new, precise outcome data remain limited, as many reports rely on broader definitions. As these entities can also be underrepresented in pivotal trials, defining real-world, entity-specific outcomes after CD19 CAR T cell treatment is essential. Aims: Describe real-world (RW), entity-specific outcomes after CD19 CAR T-cell therapy in HGBL-NOS and HGBL-MYC/BCL2 and compare them with the outcomes of a comprehensive diffuse large B cell lymphoma (DLBCL)-NOS EBMT registry cohort. Methods: Adult patients (pts) diagnosed with HGBL-NOS or HGBL-MYC/BCL2, or DLBCL-NOS who received CD19 CAR T therapy between 2018 and 2023 and were reported to the EBMT registry were included.

结论（EHA原文）

In this large EBMT RW cohort, pts with HGBL-NOS and HGBL-MYC/BCL2 achieved promising PFS, despite a high-risk clinical profile at infusion. The results indicate that CD19 CAR T cell therapy may mitigate the adverse biology of HGBL in the R/R setting. Despite its limitations, including the retrospective design, absence of central pathology review, and potential under-reporting of MYC/BCL2-rearranged cases, these findings provide contemporary, entity-specific benchmarks and support CD19 CAR T as a very relevant therapeutic option for R/R HGBL, informing treatment sequencing and future study design.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: In total 5298 pts were included: 5066 DLBCL-NOS, 177 HGBL-MYC/BCL2, and 55 HGBL-NOS. Median age was 62.6 years (y) and did not differ between groups (p=0.51). Median time from diagnosis to CAR T was shorter in both HGBL cohorts (10.4 months (mo) for MYC/BCL2; 10.9 mo for NOS) compared with DLBCL-NOS (15.3 mo; p Conclusion: In this large EBMT RW cohort, pts with HGBL-NOS and HGBL-MYC/BCL2 achieved promising PFS, despite a high-risk clinical profile at infusion. The results indicate that CD19 CAR T cell therapy may mitigate the adverse biology of HGBL in the R/R setting. Despite its limitations, including the retrospective design, absence of central pathology review, and potential under-reporting of MYC/BCL2-rearranged cases, these findings provide contemporary, entity-specific benchmarks and support CD19 CAR T as a very relevant therapeutic option for R/R HGBL, informing treatment sequencing and future study design.

108DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S241

大b细胞淋巴瘤常规治疗与cd3xcd20双特异性抗体桥接t细胞治疗的综合分析

comprehensive analysis of bridging to car t-cell therapy in large b-cell lymphoma with conventional treatment or cd3xcd20 bispecific antibodies

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=112

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：格菲妥单抗；艾可瑞妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：双特异性抗体桥接（Epcoritamab或Glofitamab），后续CAR-T细胞治疗；试验组2：常规化疗/无桥接，后续CAR-T细胞治疗

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：双特异性抗体桥接（Epcoritamab或Glofitamab），后续CAR-T细胞治疗；试验组2：常规化疗/无桥接，后续CAR-T细胞治疗

O 结局指标

严重血细胞减少症（III-IV级）发生率：BisCAR组3.0%，ConCAR组17.8%（p=0.0082） 细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：BisCAR组71.5%，ConCAR组73%（p=1.0） 免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）发生率：BisCAR组26.9%，ConCAR组28.9%（p=0.832） 治疗相关死亡率：BisCAR组3.0%，ConCAR组8.9% 桥接后总缓解率（ORR）：BisCAR组70.1%，ConCAR组61.1% CAR-T输注后1个月总缓解率：BisCAR组80.6%，ConCAR组72.1% CD25 CAR-T细胞平均荧光强度（MFI）：BisCAR组高于ConCAR组（p=0.023）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Bispecific antibodies (bABs) are used as holding or bridging prior to CAR T-cell treatment. However, the impact of this strategy on CAR T-cell safety and efficacy remains unclear. While T-cell redirecting therapies may adversely affect T-cell fitness, other preclinical data suggest synergistic effects. Aims: This study aimed to evaluate safety and efficacy of bAB-based holding/bridging with epcoritamab or glofitamab compared to conventional chemotherapy/no bridging prior CAR T-cell therapy in relapsed/refractory large B-cell lymphoma (r/r LBCL), including an analysis of immune- and CAR T-cell subsets. Methods: We assessed patient characteristics, prior lines of treatment, progression-free (PFS) and overall survival (OS), and safety outcomes of bAb-based and conventional holding/bridging and subsequent CAR T-cell therapy, including but not limited to cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS). In a subset of patients, detailed flow-cytometric analysis of peripheral blood mononuclear cells (PBMCs) before and after bridging and after CAR T-cell infusion was performed. CAR-copies were assessed via PCR.

结论（EHA原文）

Our data shows that bAB-based bridging prior to CAR T-cell therapy is feasible, safe and effective in r/r LBCL. Furthermore, bAb-based bridging demonstrated superior efficacy with a favorable toxicity profile compared with conventional approaches. Interestingly, our analyses show glofitamab-induced transient immune-cell activation without evidence of negative or detrimental effects on CAR T-cell function and expansion. In summary, our findings support bAb bridging as a promising strategy.

glofitamab和epcoritamab治疗英国大b细胞淋巴瘤的真实经验：324名患者队列中缓解持续时间和影响反应因素的扩展分析

real world experience of glofitamab and epcoritamab for large b cell lymphoma in the uk: extended analysis of duration of remission and factors affecting response in a cohort of 324 patients

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=324；疾病阶段：广泛期

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：艾可瑞妥单抗；格菲妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：glofitamab；试验组2：epcoritamab

O 结局指标

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Glofitamab (glofit) and epcoritamab (epcor) are CD3-20 bispecific antibodies (BsAb) licensed for relapsed/refractory large B cell lymphoma (RR LBCL), real-world data can help understand safety, responses and optimal patient selection. Aims: The aim of this extended analysis is to better understand risk factors impacting response to BsAb and to determine long term outcomes for responding patients. Methods: A retrospective analysis of anonymised consecutive patient data from 34 UK centres. Patients commenced glofit or epcor November 2023 to May 2025. Extended follow-up for responding patients was collected until February 2026. \n Response assessments were locally reported. Toxicities were retrospectively graded according to CTCAE v5.0, CRS and ICANS were graded against ASTCT. \n All patients commencing BsAb are included in safety and efficacy evaluable populations. Baseline data, safety and response rates were compared using chi-squared and Wilcoxon rank-sum tests. Duration of response (DoR) and duration of complete response (DoCR) were measured from date of best response. Progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) were measured from date of first dose. DoR, DoCR, PFS and OS were assessed using Kaplan-Meier survival analysis. Multivariable analyses were performed to evaluate predictors of PFS and CR rate using Cox regression and logistic regression.

结论（EHA原文）

This analysis is the largest real world data series on BsAbs to date. Our data demonstrates that both glofitamab and epcoritamab are effective treatment options in RR LBCL with updated data confirming durable complete remissions comparable to trial data in this high risk population. Some patients are unable to commence the 2 nd cycle of treatment and have very poor outcomes. Identified risk factors for poor response should be used to improve patient selection and guide prognosis.

110DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2349

b细胞恶性肿瘤从car-t评估到白细胞分离的时间：与输注速率和结果的关系

time from car-t evaluation to leukapheresis in b-cell malignancies: association with infusion rates and outcomes

P 患者群体

B细胞肿瘤，大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=409

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Lisocabtagene maraleucel；Tisagenlecleucel；布瑞基奥仑赛；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

白细胞分离率：axi-cel 90.1%（256/284），brexu-cel 92%（46/50），liso-cel 90.2%（55/61），tisa-cel 100%（14/14）；总体约10%未进入白细胞分离 白细胞分离中位时间：10天（IQR 8） 输注率：2周内白细胞分离者91.5%（p=0.02），3周内白细胞分离者90.7%（p=0.01） 大B细胞淋巴瘤患者中，接受输注者的完全缓解率（2周截止）：66.7% vs 68.8%（p=0.53）；中位无进展生存期：13.0 vs 13.6个月（p=0.94）；中位总生存期：29.4 vs 25.5个月（p=0.69） 大B细胞淋巴瘤患者中，接受输注者的完全缓解率（3周截止）：68.5% vs 63.6%（p=0.31）；中位无进展生存期：15.1 vs 13.6个月（p=0.78）；中位总生存期：29.0 vs 16.0个月（p=0.47）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy has improved outcomes in relapsed/refractory B-cell malignancies. The pathway from referral to infusion is complex and resource-intensive, encompassing evaluation, leukapheresis, manufacturing, and infusion. With expanding CAR-T use, many payers now require formal review of evaluation data prior to approval, a process that can take up to two weeks and delay leukapheresis. The effect of time from evaluation to leukapheresis on infusion rates and outcomes remains unclear. Aims: To evaluate: (1) the proportion of patients proceeding from evaluation to leukapheresis across commercial CAR-T products; (2) the likelihood of infusion based on time from evaluation to leukapheresis ( 2 weeks; 3 weeks); and (3) complete response (CR), progression-free survival (PFS), and overall survival (OS) in large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) patients according to leukapheresis timing. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed all patients with B-cell lymphoma evaluated for commercial CAR-T at Mayo Clinic Rochester since 2018. We calculated rates of leukapheresis and infusion. Patients were stratified by time from evaluation to leukapheresis using 2- and 3-week cutoffs. Among patients with LBCL, CR rates, median PFS, and median OS were compared by leukapheresis timing.

结论（EHA原文）

In this large single-center cohort, nearly 90% of evaluated patients proceeded to leukapheresis, with a median time to leukapheresis of 10 days. Earlier leukapheresis was associated with a higher likelihood of infusion, and delayed leukapheresis was significantly associated with attrition to treatment. Although patients with delayed leukapheresis who ultimately received CAR-T had comparable CR, PFS, and OS, prognosis was extremely poor among patients with LBCL who did not proceed to infusion, underscoring the importance of minimizing leukapheresis delays.

111DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2338

起始材料和car t产物的配对单细胞分析确定了与dlbcl临床反应相关的cd8+temra衰老程序

paired single-cell analysis of starting material and car t product identifies cd8+ temra senescence programs linked to clinical response in dlbcl

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=47

I 干预措施

分组：GEP组(良好扩增和预后)：CD19/22 CAR T；PEP组(不良扩增和预后)：CD19/22 CAR T

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：GEP组(良好扩增和预后)：CD19/22 CAR T；PEP组(不良扩增和预后)：CD19/22 CAR T

O 结局指标

6个月时完全缓解(CR)患者数：23例 6个月时部分缓解(PR)患者数：8例 6个月时疾病进展(PD)患者数：16例 CD8+ TEMRA衰老程序与反应相关：PEP组CD8+ TEMRA富集衰老程序，GEP组CD8+ T细胞富集增殖程序

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Responses to CAR T therapy in relapsed/refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) remain heterogeneous. T-cell states in leukapheresis starting material (SMAT) may imprint the manufactured drug product (DP), yet programs propagated from SMAT to DP that govern in vivo expansion and outcome are undefined. We therefore profiled paired SMAT and DP by single-cell RNA sequencing (scRNA-seq) to delineate programs linked to clinical response and nominate actionable targets. Aims: Define SMAT T-cell features predicting expansion/response after CD19/22 CAR T in DLBCL, and trace them in DP to guide optimization. Methods: We retrospectively reviewed r/r DLBCL patients treated with CD19/22 CAR T at Tongji Hospital (01/2024–06/2025). Response was assessed by PET/CT at month 6 (Lugano 2014). For extreme-phenotype sampling, CR and PD cases were ranked by in vivo expansion AUC0–28 (serial peripheral-blood qPCR of CAR transgene copies): top five CR were GEP (Good Expansion & Prognosis) and bottom five PD were PEP (Poor Expansion & Prognosis). Paired SMAT and DP samples (20 total) underwent 10x Genomics 3′ scRNA-seq. After QC, we obtained 39,927 SMAT T cells and 78,694 DP T cells. UMAP-based clustering, differential abundance and expression, pseudotime trajectory, pathway enrichment, and TCellSI functional state scoring were used to compare T-cell programs between GEP and PEP and across SMAT-to-DP transition, including CD4:CD8 ratio dynamics.\n

结论（EHA原文）

Paired SMAT/DP scRNA-seq in r/r DLBCL extremes showed CD8 TEMRA drives outcome. PEP had senescent c0-TEMRA (MAPK/p38, AKT–mTOR) and DP CD8 exhaustion (LAG3/TOX/TIGIT) with CD8 loss and CD4:CD8 ratio imbalance. GEP retained proliferative SMAT and naïve/cytotoxic DP CD8 with balanced CD4:CD8 ratio. These features inform biomarkers and targets.

longitudinal ctdna dynamics around car-t cell therapy and their impact on treatment efficacy in large b-cell lymphoma.

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=127

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：longitudinal ctdna dynamics around car-t cell therapy and their impact on treatment efficacy in large b-cell lymphoma.

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

中位无进展生存期（PFS）：10.1个月（95% CI 8.5–NR）|||早期复发（3个月内）发生率：41.7%（53/127）|||早期复发相关因素：LDH、铁蛋白、CRP升高，BTG1、IGLL5、HIST1H1C/HIST1H1E、FOXO1、CD58变异，≥2个TP53变异|||ctDNA VAF：PA组>8%、PI组>2%与早期复发相关|||PI新变异和PA-to-PI克隆VAF变化与PFS缩短相关

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Clonal dynamics and the emergence of resistant subclones are key drivers of relapse after CD19-directed CAR-T therapy. Circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) enables longitudinal tracking of these molecular changes; however, the relationship between variants detected before CAR-T apheresis, infusion and those present at relapse remains incompletely defined Aims: Our aim was to characterize ctDNA variant dynamics across CAR-T treatment timepoints and to assess clonal overlap between pre-treatment and relapse samples in large B cell lymphoma (LBCL) Methods: We analysed 127 LBCL patients treated with CAR-T. cfDNA was profiled from 224 plasma samples collected at pre-apheresis (PA) (n=103), pre-infusion (PI) (n=94), and relapse (n=24); 70 patients had paired PA–PI samples. Targeted cfDNA sequencing used the CAPP-Seq Lymph panel (135 genes). Somatic variants required PASS, ≥100×, VAF ≥1%, and >10 supporting reads, filtering for artifacts, germline/benign variants, and population frequency ≥1%; analyses were restricted to non-synonymous and splice-site variants. Statistics were performed in RStudio

结论（EHA原文）

Longitudinal ctDNA profiling reveals marked clonal dynamics across CAR-T treatment in LBCL, with both clonal expansion and the emergence of previously undetectable variants contributing to treatment failure. Molecular changes occurring between PA and PI, as well as patterns of clonal overlap and evolution at relapse, are strongly associated with CAR-T efficacy. Importantly, these findings demonstrate that PA and PI samples are not interchangeable, underscoring that variant selection for ctDNA monitoring is more complex than commonly assumed and critical for anticipating relapse

effects of antibiotic-exposure and levofloxacin-prophylaxis on outcomes after cart in large b-cell lymphomas

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=124

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Antibiotics (AB) are major drivers of dysbiosis, which has been shown to affect outcomes after immunotherapies, including chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CART) therapy. The role of prophylactic treatment with levofloxacin (levo) in hematologic patients remains controversial, being effective and well-tolerated strategy to prevent febrile episodes but also associated with detrimental effects after allogeneic transplantation. Moreover, the emergence of multi-resistant pathogens has risen concerns on its widespread use. Aims: We investigated the impact of AB-treatment and levo-prophylaxis on outcomes after CART in large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL). Methods: We retrospectively analyzed 124 LBCL patients treated with anti-CD19 CART at the Hematology Institute of Bologna. Considering the effect on dysbiosis, we evaluated the AB-exposure within 30 days before CART, whereas levo-prophylaxis (500 mg/day) within 30 days after CART. Analyses were performed using R.

结论（EHA原文）

Our study confirms the detrimental effects of AB-exposure on survival and NT occurrence after CART, as reported in the literature. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study to evaluate levofloxacin prophylaxis after CART, showing no significant effect on outcomes nor advantages on infection occurrence after CART. Further investigation is needed to understand the long-term effects of prophylaxis and the interactions with the microbiome.

CRS等级：司妥昔单抗组1级84.6%，2级15.4%，3级0%，4级0%；对照组1级59.0%，2级31.1%，3级8.2%，4级1.6%；≥2级CRS发生率：司妥昔单抗组15.4%，对照组41.0%（p=0.026）||ICANS发生率：司妥昔单抗组26.9%，对照组45.9%（p=0.151）||严重ICANS（≥2级）：司妥昔单抗组3.8%，对照组27.9%（OR=9.66，p=0.010）||住院时间中位数：司妥昔单抗组14天（IQR 13-15），对照组18天（IQR 15-25）（p=0.0002）||ICU入住率：司妥昔单抗组3.8%，对照组27.9%（p=0.010）||CMV再激活：司妥昔单抗组32.0%，对照组45.9%（p=0.336）||细胞减少症：司妥昔单抗组57.7%，对照组45.9%（p=0.355）||3级感染：司妥昔单抗组7.7%，对照组18.0%（p=0.328）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Chimeric Antigen Receptor (CAR) T-cell therapy is associated with significant and potentially life-threatening toxicities, such as CRS and ICANS. 5-17% of patients treated with Axi-cel will experience grade ≥3 CRS and 9%-20% grade ≥3 ICANS, ICU admission rates can reach up to 21%. Studies have explored strategies to mitigate this toxicity, with contradictory outcomes. Aims: The primary objective of this study was to evaluate the impact of early siltuximab rescue for persistent CRS in patients with R/R DLBCL undergoing CAR T-cell therapy with Axi-cel. Methods: Retrospective, single-center analysis of 87 adult patients with R/R B-cell lymphomas treated with Axi-cel between November 2022 and December 2025 comparing two clinical protocols implemented according to institutional policy. Patients were divided into two cohorts. In both, patients received two doses of tocilizumab (if CRS persisted administered 8 hours apart starting at the onset of grade 1 CRS). In the first cohort (Siltuximab group), patients with persistent CRS received up to two 11mg/kg doses of siltuximab combined with dexamethasone. In the second historical cohort (Control group) patients with persistent CRS continued with up to two subsequent doses of tocilizumab, also in combination with dexamethasone.

结论（EHA原文）

Early switch to siltuximab seems to ameliorate Axi-cel cytokine-related toxicity without increasing adverse events in comparison to continue with tocilizumab. These findings support the development of clinical trials with this promising strategy to mitigate CAR T-cell-related toxicities.

复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤的发病率和预后以及基于人群的新型t细胞封端疗法的实施

incidence and outcome of relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma and implementation of novel t-cell-engaging therapies in a population-based setting

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=2259；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：incidence and outcome of relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma and implementation of novel t-cell-engaging therapies in a population-based setting

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

2年总生存率：78%（95% CI 76-80） 2年无进展生存率：69%（95% CI 67-71） 复发/难治疾病5年累积发病率：23%（95% CI 21-25） 复发/难治患者2年总生存率：38%（95% CI 34-43） 复发/难治患者2年无进展生存率：26%（95% CI 22-30） 复发/难治患者中接受T细胞衔接疗法比例：15%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: T-cell-engaging therapies have substantially changed the treatment landscape for patients with large B cell lymphoma (LBCL) in recent years. The logistical challenges and financial burden of these therapies underscore the importance of evaluating their implementation in clinical routine. In Sweden, chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) T-cell therapy was approved for third-line treatment in 2019 and for early second-line in 2024. During the study period, access to bispecific antibodies was limited to clinical trial settings and compassionate use programs. Aims: Using Swedish population-based registers, we aimed to report contemporary outcomes for patients with LBCL from primary diagnosis through first and subsequent relapses, and evaluate uptake of novel therapies. Methods: We identified all patients with a primary diagnosis of LBCL in 2019-2024 in the Swedish Lymphoma Register (SLR). Patients were followed until death or end of study (16 Dec 2025). Through a development project, the SLR is being updated with complete information regarding R/R disease and treatment from medical records, and here we present data for two thirds of the population. The cumulative incidence of R/R disease was estimated in the presence of the competing risk of death. Overall survival (OS) and progression-free survival (PFS) were estimated from the date of diagnosis using the Kaplan-Meier method. Separate analyses were performed for patients with R/R disease by age group.

结论（EHA原文）

In this population-based study of LBCL patients treated in 2019-2025 we confirm a 5-year incidence of R/R disease of 23%. This is similar to previous population-based assessments from our group, but lower than what is generally stated in the literature. Two-thirds of R/R patients were older than 70 years and outcomes differed markedly between age groups. Only a minority (15%) of all R/R patients received T-cell-engaging therapies, which may reflect that CAR T was limited to third or later lines during most of the study period, as well as the advanced age distribution in this real-world population.

outcomes of second-line axicabtagene ciloleucel and comparison to autologous stem cell transplantation in early relapsed/primary refractory large b-cell lymphoma patients

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=194；疾病阶段：早期，复发，难治，原发性；治疗线数/场景：二线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；分组：试验组1：axicabtagene ciloleucel；对照组1：大剂量化疗联合自体干细胞移植（HDCT/ASCT）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：axicabtagene ciloleucel 对照组1：大剂量化疗联合自体干细胞移植（HDCT/ASCT）

O 结局指标

客观缓解率（ORR）：81% 完全缓解率（CR）：52% 2年无进展生存率（PFS）：51% 2年总生存率（OS）：60% ≥3级神经毒性发生率：19% ≥3级细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：16% 匹配后1年总生存率（OS）：Axi-Cel组76% vs HDCT/ASCT组72%（p=0.94） 匹配后1年无进展生存率（PFS）：Axi-Cel组57% vs HDCT/ASCT组43%（p=0.093）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD19-directed chimeric antigen receptor T (CAR-T) cells represent the standard of care (SOC) approach in the second-line treatment (2L) for patients with primary refractory/early relapsed large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL). However, real‐world data on the safety and efficacy of CAR-T in 2L are limited, particularly in comparison to high-dose chemotherapy and autologous stem cell transplantation (HDCT/ASCT) administered for patients with a chemosensitive disease in 2L. Aims: Here we provide real-world data on R/R LBCL patients treated with CAR-T cells in 2L and compare them to the former SOC HDCT/ASCT. CAR-T patients in this analysis were treated with axicabtagene ciloleucel (Axi-Cel) due to its initially better availability in Europe. Methods: We conducted a retrospective analysis of 194 R/R LBCL patients of whom 112 were treated with Axi-Cel, and 82 with HDCT/ASCT. The HDCT/ASCT group presented with a chemosensitive disease after bridging therapy in their last staging prior to HDCT/ASCT, while the Axi-Cel group included both, patients with chemosensitive and -refractory disease. Patients with a late relapse (> 12 months) and/or more than one line of prior therapy were excluded. To enable a comparison between the treatment groups, propensity score matching (PSM) was performed via logistic regression with parameters significantly associated with OS in univariate analysis (bulky disease and secondary International Prognostic Index (sIPI)) as covariates.

结论（EHA原文）

Our real-world data on the safety and efficacy of Axi-Cel align with findings from the ZUMA-7 approval study, demonstrating the efficacy and safety of Axi-Cel in 2L R/R LBCL treatment. Despite the selection of only chemosensitive patients in the HDCT/ASCT group, treatment with Axi-Cel demonstrated comparable OS, with a trend towards superior PFS compared to patients treated with HDCT/ASCT.

impact of tp53 mutation on cd19-chimeric antigen receptor t-cell therapy in large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

I 干预措施

O 结局指标

TP53突变发生率：55/139（39.6%），包含48个独特突变位点，错义突变占92.7%。 在4-1BB CAR-T产品中，TP53突变患者vs野生型患者的中位PFS为6.3个月 vs 未达到（p=0.024）。 在CD28 CAR-T产品中，TP53突变与野生型患者的PFS无显著差异。 TP53野生型患者的CAR-T细胞最大扩增（Cmax）显著高于突变型患者。 TP53突变患者的γδT细胞在白细胞分离前显著减少。 单细胞RNA测序显示TP53突变患者肿瘤组织中T细胞功能受损（激活、效应、迁移、黏附能力降低）。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: TP53 mutation is a well-established adverse prognostic factor in large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL). However, its role in predicting response to CD19-chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy remains controversial. While several studies have suggested that TP53 mutation confers inferior outcomes after CAR-T treatment, others have reported no significant association. The underlying mechanisms and potential modulating factors, such as CAR costimulatory domains, are poorly understood. Aims: This study aimed to: (1) comprehensively characterize the TP53 mutation spectrum in relapsed/refractory LBCL (R/R LBCL) patients receiving CD19-CAR-T;(2) evaluate the independent prognostic value of TP53 mutation for progression-free survival (PFS); (3) investigate the impact of TP53 mutation on CAR-T cell expansion, toxicity, peripheral blood T-cell subsets, and tumor microenvironment T-cell functionality using flow cytometry, CyTOF, and single-cell RNA sequencing. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed 139 R/R LBCL patients treated with CD19-CAR-T at Ruijin Hospital (2018–2024). TP53 mutations were identified via next-generation sequencing (152-gene panel) from tumor tissues. Mutation types and loci were annotated. CAR-T cell expansion (Cmax) was assessed by flow cytometry. Peripheral blood T-cell subsets were analyzed by CyTOF prior to leukapheresis. Single-cell RNA sequencing was performed on tumor tissues to evaluate T-cell functional status. Univariate and multivariate Cox regression were performed to identify predictors of PFS.

结论（EHA原文）

Our data demonstrate that TP53 mutation is frequent in R/R LBCL and is associated with reduced CAR-T expansion, altered peripheral T-cell subsets (notably γδ T-cell depletion), and impaired T-cell functionality in the tumor microenvironment. Despite these effects, TP53 mutation does not independently predict toxicity. Importantly, the negative prognostic impact of TP53 mutation on PFS was observed only in patients receiving 41BB-costimulated CAR-T, whereas CD28-based products appeared to overcome this effect.

弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤的真实总体生存率比较：car t细胞疗法与双特异性抗体

comparative real‑world overall survival in diffuse large b‑cell lymphoma: car t‑cell therapies versus bispecific antibodies

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=561

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；格菲妥单抗；艾可瑞妥单抗；靶点：CD19；CD20，CD3；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；双特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：双特异性抗体组（epcoritamab，glofitamab）；试验组2：CAR T细胞治疗组（tisacel，axicel，lisocel）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：双特异性抗体组（epcoritamab，glofitamab）；试验组2：CAR T细胞治疗组（tisacel，axicel，lisocel）

O 结局指标

2年总生存率：双特异性抗体组47.5% vs CAR T细胞治疗组67.3%|||死亡风险比（RR）：1.468（95%CI 1.116-1.932）|||风险比（HR）和95%CI：文中未给出具体数值，但描述显著差异|||log-rank检验：χ2=20.034, p<0.0001

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Treatment options for diffuse large B‑cell lymphoma (DLBCL) have expanded, especially in relapsed/refractory (R/R) cases, with CAR T‑cell therapies and CD20×CD3 bispecific antibodies (BsAbs) being notable advances. While trials suggest CAR T‑cells may be more effective and improve survival, these findings come from controlled populations that may not mirror clinical practice. Aims: This study aims to evaluate overall survival (OS) in DLBCL patients treated with CAR T‑cells or BsAbs using real‑world data (RWD). Methods: A retrospective analysis of RWD was conducted using TriNetX Dataworks Global database on February 21, 2026. Two cohorts were analyzed: (1) DLBCL patients ≤60 years old treated solely with BsAbs (epcoritamab/glofitamab), and (2) DLBCL patients ≤60 years old treated solely with CAR T-therapies (tisacel/axicel/lisocel). Patients treated with both therapeutic options were excluded from analysis to control for “crossover” between cohorts and impact on OS. Standardized mean differences were used to ascertain the distribution balance among baseline variables. Kaplan-Meier analysis, log-rank test, hazard ratios (HR), risk ratios (RR), and 95% confidence intervals (CI) were used to assess the primary outcomes, which were risk of death and OS. Propensity score matching (PSM) was utilized to account for the effects of specific known confounders.

结论（EHA原文）

In this real-world analysis of DLBCL patients ≤60 years old, treatment with BsAbs was linked to worse OS and higher death risk compared to CAR T-cell therapies. These findings remained consistent before and after PSM, highlighting the robustness of the results. While CAR T-cell therapies showed better survival over 2 years, the data's aggregate nature limits detailed clinical interpretation, including disease and treatment factors affecting outcomes. Still, the results support using CAR T-cell therapies over BsAbs for eligible younger patients with R/R DLBCL and emphasize the need for more research with patient-level data to improve comparative assessments.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 561 patients with DLBCL were enrolled, including 123 treated with BsAbs and 438 treated with CAR T-cell therapies. The mean age at the index event (initiation of BsAbs for Cohort 1; initiation of CAR T-cell therapy for Cohort 2) was 47.2±9.2 for Cohort 1 and 44.5±11.3 for Cohort 2 (p=0.015). There were 63% and 66% male patients, respectively (p=0.664). Over a 2-year follow-up period from the index event, Cohort 1 had a significantly higher risk of death compared to Cohort 2 (RR 1.468, 95%CI 1.116-1.932). 121DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF994

波兰淋巴瘤研究组（plrg）的倾向评分匹配分析：复发/难治性dlbcl中polatuzumab br与tafasitamab来那度胺的比较

polatuzumab-br vs tafasitamab-lenalidomide in relapsed/refractory dlbcl: a propensity score–matched analysis from the polish lymphoma research group (plrg)

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=206；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；苯达莫司汀；利妥昔单抗；来那度胺；坦昔妥单抗；靶点：CD79B；DNA；CD20；IKZF3，IKZF1，CSNK1A1，CRBN；CD19；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；化药；单特异性抗体；分子胶降解剂；分组：试验组1：polatuzumab vedotin，bendamustine，rituximab（Pola-BR）；试验组2：tafasitamab，lenalidomide（Tafa-Len）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：polatuzumab vedotin，bendamustine，rituximab（Pola-BR）；试验组2：tafasitamab，lenalidomide（Tafa-Len）

O 结局指标

总缓解率（ORR）：Pola-BR组显著高于Tafa-Len组|||完全缓解率（CR）：Pola-BR组更高|||部分缓解率（PR）：Pola-BR组更高|||中位无进展生存期（PFS）：Pola-BR组优于Tafa-Len组|||1年总生存率（OS）：Pola-BR组50% vs Tafa-Len组44%（p=0.20）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: This multicenter study conducted by the Polish Lymphoma Research Group (PLRG) compared real-world outcomes of two salvage regimens—polatuzumab vedotin with bendamustine and rituximab (Pola-BR) and tafasitamab plus lenalidomide (Tafa-Len)—in patients with relapsed/refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (R/R DLBCL). Direct comparative data remain limited. Aims: To verify and compare real-world outcomes for Pola-BR and Tafa-Len regimens in R/R DLBCL patients in a routine clinical setting. Methods: In this retrospective analysis, 206 patients with R/R DLBCL treated with Pola-BR (n=152) or Tafa-Len (n=54) in the second or subsequent lines were identified. Propensity score matching (PSM) was performed based on 14 baseline clinical and disease-related variables, including age, sex, ECOG performance status, DLBCL cell-of-origin subtype, clinical stage, IPI at diagnosis and at salvage, type of first-line failure (primary refractory disease vs early relapse vs late relapse), number of prior treatment lines, refractoriness to the last therapy, disease status, bulky disease, and B symptoms at salvage. After PSM, 36 matched patients in each group were included in the comparative analysis.

结论（EHA原文）

In this PSM analysis of real-world PLRG data, Pola-BR achieved higher response rates and longer PFS than Tafa-Len in high-risk R/R DLBCL, while OS was comparable. Tafa-Len was developed for transplant-ineligible patients, and primary refractory disease was excluded from L-MIND. However, our cohort was largely composed of primary refractory cases, which may not represent the optimal setting for this regimen. At that time, novel T-cell–engaging (TCE) therapies were not available in the second line. With expanding access to CAR T-cell therapy and bispecific antibodies, TCE approaches should be incorporated early for primary refractory disease and early relapse, consistent with benefits shown in second-line CAR-T trials and the STARGLO study. The optimal positioning of Pola-BR and Tafa-Len in R/R DLBCL requires further clarification given their meaningful efficacy and manageable safety profiles.

real-world comparative study of the effectiveness, safety, and health care resource utilization (hcru) of lisocabtagene maraleucel and bispecifics in third-line or later large b-cell lymphoma (lbcl)

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=273；治疗线数/场景：三线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：Lisocabtagene maraleucel；格菲妥单抗；艾可瑞妥单抗；靶点：CD19；CD20，CD3；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰；双特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：lisocabtagene maraleucel；试验组2：双特异性抗体（epcoritamab, glofitamab）

O 结局指标

总生存期（OS）：调整后HR 0.62（P=0.023）；liso-cel组中位OS未达到，BsAb组11个月 无进展生存期（PFS）：调整后HR 0.53（P=0.004）；liso-cel组中位PFS 12个月，BsAb组5个月 客观缓解率（ORR）：调整后liso-cel组81%，BsAb组64%（P=0.004） 完全缓解率（CRR）：调整后liso-cel组61%，BsAb组28% 细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）：liso-cel组40%（1-2级39%，≥3级0），BsAb组26%（1-2级19%，≥3级3%） 免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）：liso-cel组20%（1-2级14%，≥3级5%），BsAb组7%（1-2级3%，≥3级3%） 住院率和ICU入住率：liso-cel组低于BsAb组

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Lisocabtagene maraleucel (liso-cel) and CD3×CD20 T-cell engaging bispecific antibodies (BsAb) are approved LBCL therapies; liso-cel in second line or later and BsAb in third-line (3L) or later (3L+) in the United States (US). Understanding their comparative effectiveness, safety, and HCRU in the real-world (RW) setting can inform optimal treatment selection. Aims: To compare RW effectiveness, safety, and HCRU among patients with R/R LBCL treated with liso-cel or BsAb in the 3L+ setting. Methods: Patients with LBCL who were newly treated with liso-cel or BsAb (epcoritamab, glofitamab) in the 3L+ setting (April 2022–May 2025) were identified from the US Flatiron Health Research Database, which collects longitudinal electronic health records from the routine clinical setting. Baseline differences were adjusted using inverse probability of treatment weighting (IPTW) for efficacy, safety, and HCRU. Sensitivity analysis was conducted in 3L-only patients.

结论（EHA原文）

In this retrospective, RW analysis, liso-cel demonstrated significantly better efficacy and similar HCRU and safety vs BsAb as a 3L+ therapy for LBCL; further data are needed to compare these treatments in earlier lines of therapy. EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 273 patients were included, with 161 receiving liso-cel and 112 receiving BsAb (median [IQR] age at index, 72 y [62–77] vs 75 y [65–81]; DLBCL, not otherwise specified, 87% vs 76%; high-grade B-cell lymphoma, 2% vs 8%; elevated LDH, 28% vs 54%; bulky disease, 66% vs 66%; 3L, 70% vs 54%; and median follow-up time of 12.4 mo vs 9.1 mo). In both unadjusted and adjusted analyses, liso-cel was associated with a statistically significant improvement in OS (adjusted HR, 0.62; P =0.023) and PFS (adjusted HR, 0.53; P P =0.004) and CRR (61% vs 28%; P Table 1 ). \n In a sensitivity analysis of 3L-only patients (liso-cel, n=113; BsAb, n=60), liso-cel had a statistically significant benefit for OS (HR, 0.35; P P with higher ORR (83% vs 64%) and CRR (65% vs 27%) vs BsAb. \n Any-grade cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) incidence was higher with liso-cel, mostly due to grade 1–2 events ( Table 2 ). There was no grade ≥3 CRS with liso-cel and low rates of grade ≥3 ICANS overall. Rates of prolonged cytopenia (liso-cel, 32%; BsAb, 29%) and infections (liso-cel, 8%; BsAb, 14%) were comparable between cohorts. There were lower hospitalization and ICU admission rates with liso-cel vs BsAb across most time periods ( Figure 1 ). Conclusion: In this retrospective, RW analysis, liso-cel demonstrated significantly better efficacy and similar HCRU and safety vs BsAb as a 3L+ therapy for LBCL; further data are needed to compare these treatments in earlier lines of therapy. 12个月OS率：66.3% (95% CI 59.0-74.4) || 中位PFS：12.7个月 (95% CI 10.4-NR) || 12个月PFS率：53.8% (95% CI 47.0-61.7) || 总体缓解率：81.3% || 完全缓解率：71.1% || 细胞因子释放综合征发生率：95%（2-4级：37%；3-4级：4%） || 免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征发生率：47%（2-4级：26%；3-4级：12.5%） || 移植适合患者中位PFS：axi-cel组未达到 vs CIT组4.60个月 (HR 2.06) || 移植不适合患者中位PFS：axi-cel组未达到 vs CIT组2.50个月 (HR 2.84)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Clinical trials have demonstrated the superiority of anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy over standard chemoimmunotherapy (CIT) as second-line (2L) treatment for patients with refractory or early-relapsed large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL). However, real-world (RW) comparative data remain limited, particularly according to transplant eligibility. Aims: We aimed to describe RW outcomes of axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel) as 2L treatment for LBCL in Spain and to compare progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) between these patients and a RW cohort (non-CAR-T) treated with 2L CIT, stratified by transplant eligibility. Methods: We conducted a retrospective, multicenter, RW study including patients with LBCL receiving 2L treatment in Spain. The CAR-T cohort comprised patients treated with axi-cel (03/2024 to 12/2025), while the non-CAR-T cohort included patients treated with CIT from a large retrospective GELTAMO dataset (01/2013 to 12/2023), encompassing both transplant-eligible (T-E) and transplant-ineligible (T-I) patients. Propensity score matching was applied to balance baseline clinical characteristics between cohorts (gender, age, refractoriness, histology, IPI and stage).

结论（EHA原文）

In this large RW Spanish cohort, axi-cel as 2L showed high response rates, favourable survival, and manageable safety. After adjustment, axi-cel provided a clinically meaningful PFS advantage over CIT in both T-E and T-I patients. An OS benefit was seen in T-I, while in T-E it may have been mitigated by subsequent CAR-T use in ≥3L. These findings support CAR-T as an effective 2L strategy for LBCL in routine practice.

I 干预措施

研究设计描述：same ai, different doctors: expertise determines response to treatment recommendations in lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

LLM可接受性：83% (95% CI: 74.5-89.1%) LS拒绝而GH接受的建议：8个（16%），GH拒绝而LS接受的建议：1个（2%）（McNemar p=0.039） GH修改建议比例：32%，LS修改建议比例：6%（p=0.002） 被拒绝的案例中，77%涉及潜在危害（次优治疗或毒性问题） 时间信息处理错误：2例（4%）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Relapsed/refractory DLBCL management involves rapidly evolving therapies (CAR-T, bispecific antibodies, ADCs) often lacking comparative evidence. LLMs are explored as decision-support tools, yet their clinical acceptability and influence on physicians with varying expertise remain poorly characterized. While LLMs achieve high scores on medical benchmarks, their readiness for clinical deployment remains uncertain. Aims: To evaluate clinical acceptability of LLM-generated R/R DLBCL treatment recommendations, assess their influence on hematologist decision-making, and characterize patterns of unacceptable recommendations. Methods: We developed \"Ariadne\", a RAG-augmented LLM with curated R/R DLBCL treatment database and guidelines. Fifty validated cases were evaluated by paired Lymphoma Subspecialists (LS) and General Hematologists (GH) (100 evaluations). Experts provided treatment recommendations, reviewed LLM outputs, and rated acceptability. Rejection reasons were collected. Analysis used GEE with cluster-robust standard errors.

结论（EHA原文）

RAG-enhanced LLMs achieved 83% acceptability in R/R DLBCL recommendations, comparable to their performance on health benchmarks. However, important limitations challenge clinical deployment readiness.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The LLM achieved 83% acceptability (95% CI: 74.5-89.1%). Concordance analysis revealed asymmetry: LS rejected 8 recommendations (16%) that GH accepted versus 1 (2%) reverse (McNemar p=0.039). Behavioral influence differed markedly: GH modified recommendations significantly more than LS (32% vs 6%, p=0.002), a 5-fold difference. Conclusion: RAG-enhanced LLMs achieved 83% acceptability in R/R DLBCL recommendations, comparable to their performance on health benchmarks. However, important limitations challenge clinical deployment readiness.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: We previously showed that for large B cell lymphoma (LBCL) patients treated with 3 rd line (3L) CD19 CAR-T at three UK National Health Service (NHS) CAR-T centres in 2019-2022, 25% of patients travelled >100km; and that the most deprived patients experienced poorer survival, driven by higher rates of pre-infusion drop-out and COVID-19 death (Dragoi et al, BJHaem, 2025). Aims: We aimed to evaluate the impact of distance to CAR-T centre, socio-economic deprivation, and ethnicity on LBCL outcomes following 2L CAR-T in the UK. \n \n Methods: We analysed these factors in a cohort of 204 patients approved for 2L axicabtagene ciloleucel at eight CAR-T centres in England between May 2023 and November 2024, with median follow-up of 16.4 months (IQR 12.0-20.1). Postcode-level data on deprivation were derived using the English “Index of Multiple Deprivation” (IMD) 2019, with patients grouped by high (IMD 1-3), intermediate (IMD 4-7) and low (IMD 8-10) deprivation. \n

结论（EHA原文）

Our data suggest similar outcomes for patients receiving 2L axi-cel irrespective of socio-economic deprivation, ethnicity or distance to centre in a diverse UK cohort, contrasting with findings at 3L. Moving CAR-T to earlier treatment line, more pro-active bridging strategies, and the decline in the COVID-19 pandemic, may have helped mitigate competing risks felt by more deprived patients; although deprivation, ethnicity and distance may impact on patient experience and outcomes in ways not captured here. Furthermore, the effect of these factors on rate of referral for CAR-T was not examined and warrants separate analysis. We saw fewer patients travelling >100km - attributable to an increase in the number of UK CAR-T centres - but for those still facing this barrier, outcomes were equivalent, underlining that they should still be offered CAR-T and the necessary support to travel.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The distribution by deprivation was: 58 Low (28.9%), 102 Medium (50.7%), and 41 High (20.4%). The distribution by ethnicity was: 166 White (89.2%), 15 Asian (8.1%), 5 Black (2.7%) (18 Unknown). There was a trend to greater proportion of ethnic minority patients from more deprived areas (Low 7.3%, Medium 10.6%, High 17.5%, p=0.14). Patients from the most deprived areas travelled less for CAR-T (median distance by IMD: Low 42.6km, Medium 43.1km, High 29.6km, p=0.026), likely reflecting the inner-city location of most centres. 8% of patients travelled >100km. \n There were no significant differences in baseline characteristics (including age, stage, LDH, bulk, IPI) according to deprivation. 94.7% of patients received bridging therapy, with no significant differences by deprivation. Importantly, there were no differences in vein-to-vein time, or drop-out rate by deprivation (92.0% infused for whole cohort). \n In the low deprivation group, there was a trend to superior response to bridging (overall response rate by IMD: Low 68.0%, Medium 43.1%, High 44.1%, p=0.099), and more grade 3+ CRS events (% by IMD: Low 9.4%, Medium 3.2%, High 0%, p=0.024); but no significant difference in grade 3+ ICANS, tocilizumab/steroid use or ICU admission. There were no significant differences in complete metabolic response rate, PFS/OS, or non-relapse mortality by deprivation. There were no significant differences in toxicity / efficacy outcomes in ethnic minority patients, or for patients travelling >100km. There were no reported COVID-19 deaths in this cohort, highlighting the evolution in COVID-19 risk. \n \n Conclusion: Our data suggest similar outcomes for patients receiving 2L axi-cel irrespective of socio-economic deprivation, ethnicity or distance to centre in a diverse UK cohort, contrasting with findings at 3L. Moving CAR-T to earlier treatment line, more pro-active bridging strategies, and the decline in the COVID-19 pandemic, may have helped mitigate competing risks felt by more deprived patients; although deprivation, ethnicity and distance may impact on patient experience and outcomes in ways not captured here. Furthermore, the effect of these factors on rate of referral for CAR-T was not examined and warrants separate analysis. We saw fewer patients travelling >100km - attributable to an increase in the number of UK CAR-T centres - but for those still facing this barrier, outcomes were equivalent, underlining that they should still be offered CAR-T and the necessary support to travel.
