hbv-dna–guided monitoring for hepatitis b virus reactivation enables safe management without routine antiviral prophylaxis after car t-cell therapy in r/r lbcl

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=25；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：hbv-dna–guided monitoring for hepatitis b virus reactivation enables safe management without routine antiviral prophylaxis after car t-cell therapy in r/r lbcl

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

HBV-DNA再激活发生率：2/25（8%）；2例再激活患者均成功使用核苷类似物治疗，HBV-DNA水平迅速下降；无乙肝相关性肝炎发生；23例患者随访期间HBV-DNA持续阴性；中位随访时间16.9个月（范围1.3-62.4），其中17例随访超过1年。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Data regarding hepatitis B virus (HBV) reactivation after chimeric antigen receptor (CAR) T-cell therapy are limited, and optimal strategies for monitoring and prophylaxis remain unclear. In the US and Europe, prophylactic antiviral therapy has been recommended for patients (pts) with B-cell lymphoma who are positive for hepatitis B core antibody (HBcAb). In contrast, Japanese guidelines recommend HBV-DNA–guided monitoring for patients receiving anti-CD20 antibody-containing chemotherapy; however, specific recommendations for CAR-T therapy remain unestablished. Aims: This study aimed to clarify the incidence and clinical features of HBV reactivation after CAR T-cell therapy and to assess the feasibility of HBV-DNA–guided monitoring without routine antiviral prophylaxis. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed pts with large B-cell lymphoma who received anti-CD19 CAR T-cell therapy at National Cancer Center Hospital, Tokyo, Japan between December 2020 and January 2026. HBV serological status was confirmed in all pts prior to CAR T-cell infusion. According to the Japanese hepatitis B treatment guidelines, pts positive for either HBcAb or hepatitis B surface antibody (HBsAb) underwent serial HBV-DNA monitoring, except for those with isolated HBsAb positivity associated with prior HBV vaccination. We excluded pts with 1) isolated HBsAb positivity due to vaccination, 2) hepatitis B surface antigen (HBsAg) positivity requiring nucleotide analog therapy, 3) a history of HBV reactivation requiring nucleotide analog therapy prior to CAR T-cell therapy, or 4) early disease progression preventing HBV-DNA testing after CAR T-cell therapy.

结论（EHA原文）

Although HBV reactivation can occur following CAR T-cell therapy, the incidence was low (2/25, 8%) in our cohort. Reactivation was successfully controlled through HBV-DNA–guided monitoring and timely nucleotide analog therapy, and no cases of hepatitis. Among pts with resolved HBV infection managed with HBV-DNA monitoring alone, 23 pts maintained persistently negative HBV-DNA levels and did not require prophylactic nucleotide analog. These findings highlight the clinical benefit of avoiding unnecessary long-term nucleotide analog exposure and suggest that an HBV-DNA–based monitoring strategy without routine prophylaxis represents a feasible management option after CAR T-cell therapy, particularly in regions where HBV-DNA testing is readily accessible.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Selecting patients for chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy is essential to minimise preventable adverse outcomes and support appropriate use of healthcare resources, yet it remains largely subjective in current clinical settings. Existing tools to evaluate co-morbidities include the cumulative illness rating scale (CIRS), “Severe4” and Cellular Therapy Comorbidity Index (CTCI). However, individual scores may not reflect the complex interplay between disease burden and kinetics, frailty and pre-existing co-morbidities. We propose a stepwise framework that systematically integrates frailty and comorbidity assessments to enable objective stratification of patients along a fitness continuum. This approach aims to guide optimization of the “borderline fit” patients to access CAR-T therapy safely whilst minimizing undue risk in patients on the far end of the fitness spectrum. Aims: We aim to correlate comorbidity assessments with clinical outcomes and develop a framework that integrates comorbidity and frailty assessments to optimally balance safety and equity of CAR-T access in clinical practice. Methods: Data from 80 patients with relapsed refractory diffuse large B cell lymphoma treated with CAR-T therapy between 2020-2025 in two treating institutions in Singapore were retrospectively analysed. Outcomes included overall survival (OS), progression-free survival (PFS), and severe treatment-related complications, defined as Grade ≥3 cytokine release syndrome, immune-effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome, or immune effector cell-associated haematotoxicity. Patients’ fitness and comorbidities were assessed using ECOG, Karnofsky, CIRS, Severe4 and CTCI.

结论（EHA原文）

Combining CIRS, Severe4, and CTCI improves outcome stratification compared with any individual score alone. When integrated with frailty assessment, this approach can refine patient selection to allow safer access to potentially eligible candidates.

128DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF1249

治疗前脑磁共振白质变化提示小血管疾病预测嵌合抗原受体t细胞治疗后免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性

pre-treatment white matter changes on brain mri suggesting small vessel disease predict immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity after chimeric antigen receptor t-cell therapy

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=93

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CAR-T(达博生物)；类别：CAR-T，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

ICANS累积发生率：低Fazekas组11%，中Fazekas组20%，高Fazekas组44%（p=0.03）||多因素分析：Fazekas评分与ICANS独立相关（HR 1.51, 95% CI 1.09-2.10）||延长神经症状（≥28天）发生率：低组1.6%（1/64），中组0%（0/20），高组22%（2/9）（p=0.046）||细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：各组无差异（p=0.32；≥2级CRS p=0.87）||无进展生存期和总生存期：各组无差异（p=0.82和p=0.70）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) is an important adverse effect following chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy, and some patients experience prolonged neurologic symptoms. Therefore, prevention and early risk stratification are crucial; however, pre-treatment predictors of ICANS are limited. Because disruption of the blood–brain barrier with leakage of cytokines or inflammatory cells into the central nervous system (CNS) has been implicated in ICANS pathogenesis, we focused on small-vessel disease–related white matter changes as markers of vascular fragility and reduced resilience to neurotoxicity. Aims: We aimed to determine whether the pre-treatment Fazekas score (AJR Am J Roentgenol. 1987; 149:351), reflecting brain white matter changes, is associated with ICANS and prolonged neurologic symptoms after CAR-T therapy. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed 93 patients who underwent commercial CAR-T therapy for large B-cell lymphoma at Okayama University Hospital between December 2019 and June 2025 with brain magnetic resonance imaging (MRI). The Fazekas score (0–6, sum of periventricular and deep white matter ratings) was assessed on pre-infusion MRI, excluding lesions attributable to prior CNS events or lymphoma involvement, and categorized into three groups: low (0–2), intermediate (int; 3–4), and high (5–6). Prolonged neurologic symptoms were defined as lasting for ≥28 days.

结论（EHA原文）

Our data suggest that pre-existing brain white matter changes are associated with both the development of ICANS and the risk of prolonged neurologic symptoms. Incorporating brain MRI and Fazekas scoring before CAR-T therapy may help refine neurotoxicity risk stratification and could be particularly informative regarding CAR-T product selection and identification of patients who need closer ICANS surveillance.

中文结果摘录（原表）

efficacy of car-t cell therapy in double-expressor tp53-positive relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: a multicenter real-world study

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=53；疾病阶段：复发/难治

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Double-expressor TP53-positive diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) represents a highly aggressive subtype associated with poor prognosis. Outcomes are particularly dismal in relapsed/refractory (r/r) patients. Chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy has emerged as an effective treatment option for r/r DLBCL; however, its efficacy in this high-risk biological subgroup remains unclear. Aims: To evaluate the clinical efficacy, overall survival (OS), and progression-free survival (PFS) of CAR-T therapy in patients with double-expressor TP53-positive r/r DLBCL. Methods: This multicenter retrospective study included patients with double-expressor TP53-positive r/r DLBCL who received CAR-T therapy between February 1, 2017, and December 31, 2025, at three tertiary centers. Clinical data were collected and analyzed using SPSS software. Overall response rate (ORR) at 1 and 3 months, median OS, and median PFS were assessed.

结论（EHA原文）

In patients with double-expressor TP53-positive r/r DLBCL, CAR-T therapy induces initial responses; however, durability remains limited, with short median PFS and OS observed in this high-risk population. These findings suggest that additional therapeutic strategies, including combination or consolidation approaches, may be required to improve long-term outcomes.

130DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗PF1026

阿昔布他烯-西洛卢塞一线治疗dlbcl的早期毒性：2l与≥3l治疗的现实比较

early toxicity of axicabtagene ciloleucel by line of therapy in dlbcl: a real-world comparison of 2l vs ≥3l treatment

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=413；疾病阶段：早期

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；分组：2L组：axicabtagene ciloleucel；≥3L组：axicabtagene ciloleucel

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：2L组：axicabtagene ciloleucel；≥3L组：axicabtagene ciloleucel

O 结局指标

CRS任何级别发生率：2L组95%，≥3L组92%|||CRS≥3级发生率：2L组4%，≥3L组8%（p=0.002）|||CRS中位发病时间：两组均为2天|||CRS中位持续时间：2L组4天，≥3L组5天（p=0.02）|||托珠单抗使用率：2L组61%，≥3L组62%|||托珠单抗中位剂量：2L组1.5剂，≥3L组2剂（p=0.03）|||皮质类固醇使用率：2L组48%，≥3L组32%（p<0.001）|||ICANS任何级别发生率：2L组51%，≥3L组55%|||ICANS≥3级发生率：2L组14%，≥3L组20%（p=0.05）|||ICANS中位发病时间：2L组5天，≥3L组6天|||ICANS中位持续时间：2L组3天，≥3L组4天（p<0.001）|||ICU入住率：2L组21%，≥3L组24%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel) is approved for relapsed/refractory large B-cell lymphoma, with early toxicities driven by cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS). Pivotal studies reported typical early onset within the first week and a considerable burden of grade ≥3 events, prompting interest in whether toxicity differs when axi-cel is administered in second line (2L) versus later lines (≥3L). Aims: To compare early toxicity patterns (CRS and ICANS) of axi-cel in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) treated in 2L versus ≥3L, including timing, severity, duration, and toxicity-directed interventions. Methods: This retrospective, multicenter study on behalf of the GETH-TC (Spanish Group of Stem Transplantation and Cell Therapy) group compared consecutive DLBCL patients receiving axi-cel in second line from April 2024 (following regulatory approval in Spain) with a previously published historical cohort from our group treated between 2018 and 2021 in third or later line (Bailén et al. Transpl Cell Ther 2022). Patients were grouped by line of therapy at infusion: 2L vs ≥3L. CRS and ICANS were graded per ASTCT consensus criteria. Endpoints included incidence (any grade; grade ≥3), time-to-onset (days from infusion), duration (days), ICU admission, and treatment (tocilizumab, corticosteroids, anakinra if applicable). Comparative analyses used χ²/Fisher for categorical and Mann-Withney/t-test for continuous variables.

结论（EHA原文）

In this real-world DLBCL axi-cel cohort, second line of therapy was associated with lower rates of grade ≥3 early toxicities (CRS and ICANS) as compared to ≥3L. Despite this reduced incidence of high-grade toxicity, corticosteroid use for CRS was more frequent in the 2L cohort, likely reflecting a temporal shift toward earlier and more proactive toxicity management in the more recent treatment period. Further analysis are needed to discard an impact of disease characteristics on these findings.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of N=413 patients were included (2L n=184, ≥3L n=229). Baseline characteristics are summarized in Table 1. Briefly, the 2L cohort showed a better ECOG performance status at infusion, lower R-IPI, lower prior ASCT exposure, lower rates of bulky disease and elevated LDH, and more frequent use of bridging therapy. No differences were observed in the median time from apheresis to infusion between groups. Comparing 2L vs ≥3L, any-grade CRS occurred in 95% vs 92%, with grade ≥3 CRS in 4% vs 8% (p=0.002). Median time-to-onset was 2 days in both groups and median duration 4 vs 5 days (p=0.02). Tocilizumab was administered in 61% vs 62% patients (median doses 1.5 vs 2, p=0.03), and corticosteroids were administered in 48% vs 32% (p ICU admission related to toxicity occurred in 21% vs 24%. No differences were observed in non-relapse mortality (NRM). Conclusion: In this real-world DLBCL axi-cel cohort, second line of therapy was associated with lower rates of grade ≥3 early toxicities (CRS and ICANS) as compared to ≥3L. Despite this reduced incidence of high-grade toxicity, corticosteroid use for CRS was more frequent in the 2L cohort, likely reflecting a temporal shift toward earlier and more proactive toxicity management in the more recent treatment period. Further analysis are needed to discard an impact of disease characteristics on these findings.

international expert consensus on real-world car t-cell eligibility in large b-cell lymphomas: an e-delphi study

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=23

I 干预措施

专家共识：international expert consensus on real-world car t-cell eligibility in large b-cell lymphomas: an e-delphi study

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

对一线治疗后2-4周期内进行中期PET评估应答，共识率82.6% 疾病稳定患者应转诊，共识率87.0% 疾病进展患者应转诊，共识率100% 年龄不能作为绝对禁忌证，共识率100% ECOG PS 0-2自动转诊，共识率91.3% 肌酐清除率>30 mL/min自动转诊，共识率82.6% 心功能为核心标准，共识率78.2%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Despite robust clinical evidence, regulatory approval and guideline recommendations in second- and third-line settings, disparities persist for referring patients with relapsed or refractory diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (r/r DLBCL) for chimeric antigen receptor T-cell therapy (CAR T). Recent studies estimate only one-third of CAR T-eligible patients are ultimately treated, partly due to uncertainty regarding referral eligibility criteria. Consensus-driven guidance is needed to support equitable, timely referral practices. Aims: To identify and characterize consensus on core clinical eligibility criteria to guide referral of patients with r/r DLBCL by community-based physicians to specialized centers for evaluation for CAR T. Methods: An e-Delphi study was conducted in accordance with established consensus reporting standards. All study materials, designed in alignment with ACCORD (ACcurate COnsensus Reporting Document) guidelines, received approval from an independent steering committee of clinical experts, and independent institutional review boards. A panel of 23 expert hematology and/or oncology clinicians in USA, Canada, UK, France, Germany, and Italy, anonymously responded to statements via a web-based questionnaire (≥75% consensus threshold).

结论（EHA原文）

Round 1 analysis demonstrates robust international expert consensus on referral eligibility for CAR T in patients with r/r DLBCL. The panel strongly endorsed broad eligibility for referral independent of ASCT eligibility, and provided clarity regarding disease status, age, performance, and organ function as core referral criteria. These consensus recommendations have the potential to reduce unwarranted variation in referral practices and support more equitable access to CAR T. Final recommendations will be presented at congress.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Anti-CD19 CAR T-cell is approved in second line (L2) for patients with refractory or early relapsed large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL). In L3+, prolonged immune defects associated with infections and non-relapse mortality. However, immune reconstitution (IR) and infectious risk after L2 CAR T-cell therapy remain insufficiently characterized. Aims: To describe immune deficiency after L2 anti-CD19 CAR T-cell in R/R LBCL, including: (1) lymphocyte B and T subsets recovery and immunoglobulin levels, (2) incidence, timing and type of infections after month 3 (M3), and (3) association with survival outcomes. Secondary aims were to explore factors associated with immune deficiency and infectious complications, and the impact of immunoglobulin (Ig) supplementation. Methods: We performed a retrospective analysis including consecutive patients with R/R LBCL treated in L2 with commercial anti-CD19 CAR T cells between 01/04/2022 and 31/12/2024. Immune monitoring included serum Ig and lymphocyte subsets (including CD4+ T cells and B cells) at M1, M3, M6, M9, M12, and beyond when available. Hypogammaglobulinemia (HypoGG) was defined as hypoGG 200/mL, 2/detectable B cells, and 3/IgG >4 g/L) as: no IR, 1, or 2 criteria. Landmark comparison of occurrence of infection post-M3 was performed, and factors associated with reconstitution were explored.

结论（EHA原文）

In this real-world L2 R/R LBCL population treated with anti-CD19 CAR T cells, immune deficiency remained frequent, with persistent hypoGG, B-cell aplasia and delayed CD4+ T-cell recovery in a substantial proportion of patients. Infectious complications were common and extended beyond the early post-infusion period. These findings support systematic immune monitoring after L2 CAR T-cell and may help refine prophylactic and Ig replacement strategies.

receipt of holding therapy is associated with inferior outcomes across the car t treatment pathway in relapsed/refractory large b cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=219；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：receipt of holding therapy is associated with inferior outcomes across the car t treatment pathway in relapsed/refractory large b cell lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

意向治疗人群总生存期：HT组中位OS 5.7个月 vs 无HT组26.6个月，调整后HR=2.03（95%CI 1.29-3.17，p=0.002） 输注后总生存期：HT组中位OS 12.3个月 vs 无HT组未达到，调整后HR=2.12（95%CI 1.11-4.04，p=0.023） 接受BT与未接受BT的输注后OS：中位OS 47.9个月 vs 37个月，调整后HR=1.05（95%CI 0.54-2.05，p=0.88）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Although CD19-directed chimeric antigen receptor T cell (CAR T) therapy has improved outcomes for relapsed/refractory large B cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL), up to a third of referred pts don’t reach infusion. While outcomes associated with bridging therapy (BT) have been described, there is a lack of data reporting on the association of holding therapy (HT) administered between referral and apheresis across the full intention-to-treat (ITT) pathway. Aims: To evaluate the association of receipt of HT across the complete CAR T treatment journey from referral through infusion. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed 219 patients (pts) with R/R LBCL referred for axicel or tisacel at Princess Margaret Cancer Centre (2017-2024), with follow-up through August 2025. Outcomes were assessed across sequential treatment phases: referral to apheresis (HT), apheresis to infusion (BT), and post-CAR T infusion. HT and BT were selected at the discretion of the treating physician. Cox models evaluated overall survival (OS) in the ITT, apheresed, and infused cohorts. Kaplan-Meier curves estimated OS, with multivariable Cox models assessing the association of HT and BT with outcomes.

结论（EHA原文）

In this cohort of pts referred for CAR T evaluation, receipt of HT but not BT was independently associated with inferior OS across the CAR T treatment journey through to infusion. This distinction is clinically important as it identifies the pre-apheresis interval as a critical prognostic window, suggesting that pts requiring disease control prior to apheresis represent a high-risk population whose inferior outcomes persist despite eventual CAR T infusion. \n

总人群（2011-2025年，666例）： - 中位OS（从一线治疗开始）：35个月（95% CI 29-47） - 2年OS率：57% - 中位rwTTNT：11个月 - 接受二线治疗比例：38% - 未接受二线治疗仍存活：27% - 死亡前未接受二线治疗：35% 近期队列（2019-2025年，337例）： - 中位OS：39个月（95% CI 26-56） - 2年OS率：58% - 中位rwTTNT：11个月 - 接受二线治疗比例：32% - 未接受二线治疗仍存活：36% - 死亡前未接受二线治疗：32%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: LBCL is curable in ~60% of pts treated with first-line (1L) chemoimmunotherapy (CIT); however, outcomes remain poor for pts with HR disease, defined as International Prognostic Index (IPI) 4-5. RW data on contemporary outcomes and subsequent therapy pathways in this population are limited. Aims: To evaluate RW treatment patterns, time to next treatment (rwTTNT), overall survival (rwOS), and utilization of second-line (2L) therapies in pts with HR LBCL treated with 1L CIT. Methods: This retrospective study used electronic health records from the US-based Flatiron Health database. Pts had HR LBCL, initiated 1L therapy Jan 1, 2011-Feb 28, 2025 (all pts), or Jan 1, 2019-Feb 28, 2025 (recent cohort, a subset of all pts), and had ≥6 mo follow-up opportunity through Aug 31, 2025. Outcomes were rwTTNT, rwOS, 1L therapy utilization, and pathway to 2L therapy and were analyzed descriptively.

结论（EHA原文）

Outcomes remain poor among pts with HR LBCL despite newer 1L CIT regimens. A significant proportion of pts (73%) progressed to 2L or died even before receiving 2L, highlighting a critical unmet need for improved 1L therapies. Differences in rwOS, but not rwTTNT, between all pts and the recent cohort suggest evolution of 2L+ therapies over time. Study limitations include unknown rationales for and possible misclassification of specific therapy/drug combinations as well as different duration of follow-up and censoring between the recent cohort and all pts. \n RR and JM contributed equally.

I 干预措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

1. 多重免疫荧光显示T细胞浸润在不同患者间存在巨大变异 2. 无监督聚类识别出六种TIME亚型，各自与不同的总生存期相关 3. B细胞丰富、免疫贫乏的肿瘤预后较差；B细胞贫乏、CD8+T细胞丰富的肿瘤预后更优 4. 差异基因表达分析发现B细胞丰富、免疫贫乏的TIME中BRCA1、NASP、MYBL2、HELLS、BIRC5、HMGA1上调 5. 空间分析显示，预后较差的TIME中PD1+T细胞与肿瘤细胞之间的吸引显著更多 6. 邻域分析识别出五种反复出现的细胞邻域结构

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is a heterogeneous disease with variable clinical outcomes. Success of standard treatment with immunochemotherapy (R-CHOP) is still limited, with a 5-year overall survival of 75%. Current clinical risk stratification relies primarily on the International Prognostic Index (IPI), based on clinical parameters. \n The tumor immune microenvironment (TIME) is increasingly recognized as a critical determinant of tumor progression, yet its heterogeneity and spatial organization remain largely uncharacterized. While the PD1/PD-L1 axis is central to immune regulation, immune checkpoint blockade has demonstrated limited efficacy in DLBCL, underscoring the need for deeper insight into tumor-immune interactions. Incorporating spatial immune metrics with genetic information and clinical parameters may refine biological understanding and prognostic modeling. Aims: This study aimed to (i) in depth investigate the role of infiltrating T-lymphocyte subsets in relation to clinical outcomes and to (ii) identify novel biomarkers for better patient stratification by linking T cell infiltration and spatial organization of the tumor immune microenvironment to genetic factors and outcome. Methods: The study included 650 patients diagnosed with DLBCL between 2000-2014 in southern Sweden. 365 patients diagnosed with DLBCL-NOS were selected for analysis. To investigate T cell infiltration, a 6-plex panel targeting DAPI, CD20, CD3, CD8, FoxP3 and PD1 was applied to TMA slides. Transcriptional analysis was performed using GeoMx DSP. DNA samples from 74 of 365 patients were sequenced with a targeted panel (GMS lymphoid panel, TWIST Bioscience).

结论（EHA原文）

Across patients we identified substantial heterogeneity in the tumor immune microenvironment, revealing six distinct TIME subtypes with different clinical outcomes. Spatial, transcriptional, and neighborhood‑level analyses demonstrated that poor‑prognosis TIMEs were characterized by dysfunctional T cell organization, altered T cell-tumor interactions, and unique gene expression patterns, highlighting spatial immune architecture as a promising biomarker to improve patient stratification beyond current models. \n

real-world efficacy and genomic landscape of polatuzuma vedotin-based first-line therapy in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma: a focus on tp53 mutations and treatment response

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=236；治疗线数/场景：一线

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：Pola-R-CHP（polatuzuma vedotin，利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松）；对照组：R-CHOP（利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，长春新碱，泼尼松）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：Pola-R-CHP（polatuzuma vedotin，利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松） 对照组：R-CHOP（利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，长春新碱，泼尼松）

O 结局指标

完全缓解率：Pola-R-CHP组81.6% vs R-CHOP组66.3%，加权OR=2.26，95%CI 1.16-4.39，P=0.017 无进展生存期：加权HR=0.41，95%CI 0.21-0.80，P=0.009；估计1年PFS：91.4% vs 74.2%；2年PFS：84.6% vs 63.6%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The POLARIX trial established the Pola-R-CHP regimen as the standard first-line treatment for newly diagnosed diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). However, its efficacy in real-world populations, especially in patients with TP53 mutations, remains to be fully elucidated. Aims: To compare the efficacy and survival outcomes of Pola-R-CHP and R-CHOP in newly diagnosed DLBCL patients in a real-world cohort using inverse probability treatment weighting (IPTW). The study also explores the molecular characteristics and prognostic impact of TP53 mutations using next-generation sequencing (NGS). Methods: We retrospectively included 236 newly diagnosed DLBCL patients who received Pola-R-CHP or R-CHOP as first-line treatment at Renji Hospital from February 2023 to June 2025. IPTW were used to balance baseline confounders. Extreme weights were trimmed at the 99th percentile to ensure model stability. NGS analysis was performed on available tissue samples to assess molecular features.

结论（EHA原文）

This real-world study confirms that the Pola-R-CHP regimen induces deeper remission and significantly improves PFS compared to R-CHOP in newly diagnosed DLBCL patients, especially those with TP53 mutations.

integrated molecular and metabolic profiling identifies determinants of outcome with loncastuximab tesirine in relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=41；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：泰朗妥昔单抗；靶点：CD19；类别：缬氨酸-丙氨酸 VA，PBD二聚体：SG3199，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；分组：所有患者：loncastuximab tesirine

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

总缓解率(ORR)：53.7%（完全缓解17.1%，部分缓解36.6%）|||中位无进展生存期(mPFS)：3.6个月|||基线ctDNA≥245 hGE/mL与较低PFS相关（中位PFS 2.7 vs 7.8个月）|||基线TMTV>135 mL与较短PFS相关（中位PFS 2.6 vs 7.8个月）|||第3周期ctDNA阴性患者PFS更优（8.6 vs 3.7个月）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Relapsed or refractory large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) remains associated with poor prognosis. Loncastuximab Tesirine is a CD19 directed antibody drug conjugate with demonstrated clinical activity in heavily pretreated disease. However, treatment benefit is heterogeneous and no validated biomarkers currently enable biological stratification or prediction of outcome, underscoring the need to define determinants of response. Aims: To evaluate the prognostic and predictive role of circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) and total metabolic tumor volume (TMTV), alone and in combination, in patients with relapsed or refractory LBCL treated with Loncastuximab Tesirine. Methods: This single-center retrospective analysis included 41 patients with relapsed or refractory LBCL treated at Humanitas Research Hospital within the LOTIS 1 and LOTIS 2 trials. ctDNA and TMTV were analyzed prior to therapy initiation (Baseline, BL), at cycle 3 (C3) and at end of treatment (EoT). ctDNA was assessed using Cancer Personalized Profiling by Deep Sequencing (CAPP-Seq) and the tumor burden was expressed as haploid genome equivalents per mL (hGE/mL) of plasma. Copy number variation (CNV) analysis from ctDNA was performed using CNVkit to detect focal and broad chromosomal alterations. 3 patients with undetectable BL ctDNA were excluded from subsequent analyses. TMTV was calculated using an SUV threshold of 4.0. Optimal biomarker cutoffs were defined by ROC analysis. Progression-free survival (PFS) was estimated using the Kaplan-Meier method, censoring patients at the time of stem cell transplantation when applicable.

结论（EHA原文）

In this cohort treated with Loncastuximab Tesirine, baseline tumor burden captured by ctDNA and TMTV appears to be the main determinant of outcome in this polyrefractory setting. Baseline biomarkers do not predict depth of response but influence durability of benefit, and early ctDNA clearance identifies patients with improved disease control. Lack of prognostic impact of TP53 alterations and CD19 loss suggests alternative resistance mechanisms. Integrated molecular and metabolic profiling enables meaningful risk stratification in relapsed or refractory LBCL.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The newly diagnosed diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) patients with extra nodal organ involvement (ENI) occur in approximately 30-40% and have limited efficacy and poor survival in the era of rituximab. Therefore, the R-EPOCH regimen was generally adopted for such patients in our center. Pola-R-CHP has been proven to improve the progression-free survival (PFS) of some patients in first-line treatment. However, there is still insufficient data available for ENI-DLBCL. This study conducted a retrospective analysis of the clinical data of 83 newly diagnosed patients with ENI-DLBCL. The efficacy and safety of the Pola-R-CHP and R-EPOCH regimens were compared, aiming to provide reasonable treatment for such patients. Methods: This is a real-world, single-center, retrospective, observational study. 83 patients who adopted the two regimens were enrolled. 结论（EHA原文）

139DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLADCPF1012

结外代谢肿瘤体积确定受益于pola-r-chp的大型b细胞淋巴瘤亚群

extranodal metabolic tumor volume identifies large b‑cell lymphoma subgroups that benefit from pola‑r‑chp

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=625

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：维泊妥珠单抗；靶点：CD79B；类别：缬氨酸-瓜氨酸 VC，MMAE，抗体，抗体偶联物ADC；分组：试验组：Pola-R-CHP（polatuzumab vedotin，利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松）；对照组：R-CHOP（利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组：Pola-R-CHP（polatuzumab vedotin，利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松） 对照组：R-CHOP（利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，泼尼松）

O 结局指标

1. 3年无进展生存率（PFS）：两组整体相似，未报告具体数值。 2. 在低TMTV（<350 mL）且高EN/TMTV亚组中，Pola-R-CHP组3年PFS为96.3%，R-CHOP组为74.0%。 3. 在低TMTV且高EN/TMTV亚组中，Pola-R-CHP组3年总生存率（OS）为100%，R-CHOP组为80.2%。 4. 高TMTV（≥350 mL）与较差生存相关（HR 2.72 [95% CI 2.02–3.67]）。 5. 治疗交互作用：Pola-R-CHP仅在低TMTV且高EN/TMTV亚组中显著改善PFS（HR 0.11 [95% CI 0.02–0.81]）。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: R‑CHOP has been the standard first‑line regimen for large B‑cell lymphoma (LBCL) for over two decades, until the POLARIX trial demonstrated improved progression‑free survival (PFS) with polatuzumab vedotin (PV) in Pola‑R‑CHP. However, overall survival (OS) did not differ, and there remains no validated strategy to identify patients who benefit most from PV‑based therapy. Aims: \n To determine whether the composition of total metabolic tumor volume (TMTV), particularly extranodal burden, improves frontline treatment stratification between Pola‑R‑CHP and R‑CHOP in LBCL. \n Methods: We retrospectively analyzed patients with newly diagnosed LBCL treated with R‑CHOP or Pola‑R‑CHP from 2007 to 2025. Baseline positron emission tomography-computed tomography was used to quantify TMTV and extranodal metabolic tumor volume. The proportion of extranodal disease (EN/TMTV) was derived. Associations with 3-year PFS and treatment interactions were evaluated using multivariable Cox models with interaction terms. Survival was assessed using Kaplan Meier analysis.

结论（EHA原文）

High EN/TMTV identifies a subgroup with low tumor burden who appear to derive particular benefit from Pola‑R‑CHP. Imaging‑derived extranodal burden may provide a rapid, non‑invasive biomarker to guide frontline regimen selection and could complement emerging molecular classifiers. External validation integrating molecular and imaging data is warranted.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma with hemophagocytic lymphohistiocytosis as the initial presentation (HLH-onset DLBCL) is a highly aggressive clinical subtype characterized by a \"tumor-inflammation self-driving loop\". This population exhibits unique clinical features and an extremely poor prognosis; however, robust risk-stratification models and systematic evaluations of treatment strategies remain scarce. Aims: This study aimed to: 1) identify independent risk factors for early death (ED, ≤30 days) and develop a bedside scoring model (ED-SSM); 2) establish a novel long-term prognostic system (OS-PSS); 3) evaluate the impact of treatment intensity using inverse probability of treatment weighting (IPTW); and 4) characterize the genomic landscape using targeted next-generation sequencing (NGS). Methods: A total of 130 treatment-naïve patients with HLH-onset DLBCL admitted between January 1, 2019, and January 1, 2025, were retrospectively analyzed. Multivariable logistic and Cox proportional hazards models identified prognostic determinants. IPTW was implemented to balance six core baseline parameters (age, platelets, APTT, LDH, albumin, and ferritin) to minimize selection bias. Targeted NGS (475-gene panel) was performed on 38 patients to identify mutational clusters and molecular subtypes.

结论（EHA原文）

HLH-onset DLBCL is characterized by high early mortality and unique molecular features. Our ED-SSM and OS-PSS models enable precise bedside risk stratification. Crucially, concurrent standard-intensity lymphoma-directed therapy is essential for improving survival, even in fragile patients. The enrichment of the MCD subtype suggests that integrating targeted agents, such as BTK inhibitors, warrants further investigation.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The tumor microenvironment (TME) is increasingly recognized as an important contributor to therapeutic response across malignancies. While cellular composition has been studied in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), the spatial organization of tumor and immune cells and its link to clinical outcome remain insufficiently characterized . Aims: This study aimed to characterize the cellular composition and spatial architecture of the DLBCL microenvironment and correlate these features with clinical outcomes following frontline chemotherapy. Methods: We analyzed diagnostic tumor samples from patients with aggressive B-cell non-Hodgkin lymphoma (B-NHL) treated with standard chemo- or chemoimmunotherapy. Multiplexed immunofluorescence based on CO-Detection by indEXing (CODEX, n=156) and Xenium spatial transcriptomics (n=68) were used to characterize the spatial proteome and transcriptome respectively. Cellular composition and spatial relationships were assessed using radius-based cellular neighborhoods, pairwise cell–cell proximities, and ligand-receptor analysis.

结论（EHA原文）

The study demonstrates that microenvironmental features, including immune cell composition and spatial organization, have prognostic relevance in aggressive B-NHL. Beyond overall cell frequencies, spatial proximities provide additional stratification of outcomes, highlighting the importance of spatially resolved phenotypes for predicting therapy response and guiding biomarker development.

impact of vincristine dose modifications or substitution on clinical outcomes in r-chop treated patients with dlbcl

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=294

I 干预措施

C 对照措施

O 结局指标

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Standard 1 st line treatment for diffuse large B‑cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is the R‑CHOP regimen (rituximab, cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, vincristine, and prednisone). Vincristine is for many patients associated with treatment‑limiting neurotoxicity. In clinical practice, management options include dose reduction or omission of vincristine or substitution with vinblastine in case neurotoxicity occurs. Several registry studies have shown that omission of vincristine from R‑CHOP does not compromise survival. Aims: This study compares clinical outcomes in patients with DLBCL treated with R-CHOP with or without vincristine dose modifications or substitution with vinblastine. Methods: Patients aged ≥18 years diagnosed with de novo DLBCL between January 2006 and December 2020 and treated with R‑CHOP–based 1 st line therapy in the North Denmark Region were identified through the Danish National Lymphoma Registry. Treatment cohorts were defined according to continuation of standard R‑CHOP, reduction or omission of vincristine, or substitution with vinblastine. \n A complete-case landmark analysis was performed with a landmark set at 105 days after diagnosis, corresponding to the time where all eventual treatment modifications to vincristine were observed completed. Overall survival (OS) and disease-free survival (DFS) were assessed using the Kaplan-Meier estimator in patients who continued standard R-CHOP versus those who received modified treatment with vincristine. Both crude and adjusted (age, sex, and stage) OS and DFS estimates were presented and compared using the log-rank tests.

结论（EHA原文）

In this population‑based cohort of patients with de novo DLBCL, modification of vincristine during R‑CHOP therapy either through dose reduction, omission, or substitution with vinblastine, no significant differences in overall survival or disease‑free survival compared with continued standard full-dose vincristine throughout the R‑CHOP-therapy were found. These findings suggest that adjustments of vincristine doses can be implemented without compromising long‑term clinical outcomes.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 294 patients were included. Among these, 210 patients (71%) with a median age of 68 years (range 19-84) continued full-dose vincristine throughout the R-CHOP-therapy, while 84 patients (29%) with a median age of 67 years (range 19-84) transitioned to modified treatment. Baseline demographics and disease characteristics were largely comparable between groups. In both groups, the majority were male (58%) and had performance status 0-1 (88%). Extra nodal disease was present in 60% and 62% of cases, respectively, and low-intermediate risk disease (IPI 0-2) in 56% and 54%. In the modified cohort, 14 (17%) underwent vincristine dose reduction, 10 (12%) had vincristine omitted, 38 (45%) received vinblastine substitution, and 22 (26%) experienced both reduction and substitution. \n The landmark analysis showed no statistically significant difference in adjusted OS (p=0.90) or DFS (p=0.79). The two years OS estimates were 80% (75%, 86%) and 83% (76%, 92%) between patients remaining on R‑CHOP and those who received modified vincristine treatment, respectively (Figure 1). The corresponding two years DFS estimates were 77% (72%, 83%) and 78% (69, 88%). The five years OS estimates were 72% (65%,79%) and 72% (62%,84%) and the five years DFS estimates were 68% (61%,75%) and 67% (56%,79%). Both curves demonstrated a gradual decline over 10 years without clear separation between treatment strategies. Conclusion: In this population‑based cohort of patients with de novo DLBCL, modification of vincristine during R‑CHOP therapy either through dose reduction, omission, or substitution with vinblastine, no significant differences in overall survival or disease‑free survival compared with continued standard full-dose vincristine throughout the R‑CHOP-therapy were found. These findings suggest that adjustments of vincristine doses can be implemented without compromising long‑term clinical outcomes.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The majority of US DLBCL patients are diagnosed and receive cancer care in community settings (Sineshaw et al., 2023), where patient characteristics, care services, and resources can vary; these factors can influence treatment management and outcomes. R-CHOP has been the preferred 1L therapy recommended by clinical guidelines. As of 2023, the introduction of Pola-R-CHP has expanded treatment options. However, there has been limited real-world data published on 1L utilization in the community oncology settings. Aims: The goal of this analysis was to characterize treatment patterns and outcomes by 1L treatment in this setting. Methods: This study included patients with DLBCL (not otherwise specified) who initiated a 1L regimen within the US Oncology Network from January 1, 2020, to January 31, 2025. Structured electronic health record data was analyzed until death or the last contact by September 2025. Time-to-next-treatment or death (TTNTD) was estimated using Kaplan-Meier methods with corresponding 95% confidence intervals (CIs). Refractory disease was defined as initiation of second-line (2L) therapy ≤ 6 months of the end of 1L. Relapsed disease was defined as initiation of 2L > 6 months after the end of 1L. Line of therapy was based on regimen start and stop dates. Treatment patterns and outcomes were presented overall and by 1L regimen (R-CHOP, Pola-R-CHP, or Other).

结论（EHA原文）

In the US community setting, Pola-R-CHP utilization is increasing over time, but R-CHOP remains the most common 1L treatment. 2‑year TTNTD was similar for R‑CHOP and Pola‑R‑CHP, although additional follow‑up is needed to assess the effectiveness of newer regimens, such as Pola‑R‑CHP. This data highlights an unmet need for optimizing frontline therapy selection and supportive pathways, as well as continued novel therapy development, to improve real-world effectiveness.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: ZFP36L1 is an AU-rich element (ARE)–binding RNA-binding protein of the TTP family that promotes ARE-dependent mRNA decay and post-transcriptional gene regulation. Although ZFP36L1 has been implicated in multiple malignancies, its clinical and biological relevance to the progression of diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) remains to be fully elucidated. Aims: To define the prognostic significance of ZFP36L1 in DLBCL and to characterize associated transcriptional programs, immune contexture, and mitochondrial translation–related features with functional validation. Methods: RNA-seq and clinical data from 600 de novo DLBCL patients treated with R-CHOP were analyzed. An optimal cutoff for ZFP36L1 expression was determined using time-dependent ROC analysis, which stratified patients into ZFP36L1-high (n = 280) and ZFP36L1-low (n = 320) groups. Overall survival (OS), progression-free survival (PFS), and baseline clinicopathologic variables were compared between groups. Differential expression and pathway enrichment analyses were conducted using RNA-seq data.

结论（EHA原文）

ZFP36L1 downregulation identifies a high-risk DLBCL subset and is linked to enhanced mitochondrial translation programs and an immunosuppressive microenvironment. ZFP36L1 may serve as a prognostic biomarker and inform risk stratification, providing a rationale for therapeutic targeting in DLBCL patients.

基于治疗组学数据预测弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤患者的早期预后

early outcome prediction of diffuse large b-cell lymphoma patients using on-treatment omics data

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=115；疾病阶段：早期

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：early outcome prediction of diffuse large b-cell lymphoma patients using on-treatment omics data

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

Combined information on both dying and living cells might reflect tumor and immune response on treatment and is independent of baseline patient and tumor characteristics, holding promise for clinical implementation in the future. For further validation…

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Currently, standard-of-care treatment for patients with Diffuse Large B-Cell Lymphoma (DLBCL) consists of 6 cycles of R-CHOP facing two significant issues:\n \n Ineffective treatment: 30-40% of patients either relapse or do not respond. An early switch to alternative treatments could improve outcome of these patients. \n Overtreatment: fewer cycles of therapy might be sufficient for some patients with low-risk disease, allowing de-escalation to 4 cycles reducing unnecessary toxicities. \n \nEarly outcome prediction could tackle both issues. Currently available tools (International Prognostic Index (IPI), interim PET-scans and other biomarkers) have prognostic significance but their low predictive power does not allow use in clinical practice yet. Aims: We aimed to combine pre-treatment data with on-treatment liquid-biopsy derived data to predict patient outcomes. Specifically, we used both circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) and extracellular vesicle (EV) derived omics. EVs are small lipid nanoparticles that are secreted by both healthy and tumor cells. As such, data from EVs are informative of tumor cells, the microenvironment and the immune response. We hypothesized that better predictions are possible earlier on by combining all the above mentioned data. Our main goal was to stratify patients into three groups with pre-determined clinically relevant 2yr progression-free survival (PFS) rates (Low-risk > 90%, Intermediate-risk 20-90%, High-risk Methods: We used data from 2 clinical studies (HOVON-152 and HOVON-902), involving a unique dataset from 115 DLBCL patients treated with R-CHOP and R-CHOP-like regimens, containing four different data modalities:\n Pre-treatment baseline characteristics \n \n Age, IPI score, sex, BCL2 and BCL6 translocation status \n \n On-treatment (after 1 cycle of R-CHOP) liquid biopsy characteristics: \n \n CtDNA-derived copy numbers \n EV-derived whole transcriptomics mRNA sequencing \n EV-derived miRNA sequencing \n \nAll sequencing was performed on the Novaseq 6000 using paired-end sequencing. We explored all possible combinations of modalities to predict 2yr PFS using a logistic-ridge regression model. Models were trained by using 10x nested cross validation and performance was compared by the AUC on all test sets. Patient stratification was compared to the current gold standard method, interim PET-CT scan (iPET).

结论（EHA原文）

The combination of ctDNA copy numbers and EV-derived mRNA expression after 1 cycle of therapy was able to identify high-risk patients with a predictive value of 100%. Combined information on both dying and living cells might reflect tumor and immune response on treatment and is independent of baseline patient and tumor characteristics, holding promise for clinical implementation in the future. For further validation, we will expand our dataset data with 95 more patients.

Combined information on both dying and living cells might reflect tumor and immune response on treatment and is independent of baseline patient and tumor characteristics, holding promise for clinical implementation in the future. outcomes of consolidative radiotherapy and survival in limited-stage primary gastric diffuse large b-cell lymphoma achieving complete response: a multicenter study from china

5年总生存率（OS）：CT+RT组98.5%，CT-alone组86.4%（P=0.06）|||5年无进展生存率（PFS）：CT+RT组92.2%，CT-alone组83.5%（P=0.04）|||5年局部控制率（LRC）：CT+RT组97.6%，CT-alone组95.8%（P=0.5）|||标准化死亡比（SMR）：CT+RT组0.64（95%CI 0.17-1.64, P=0.54），CT-alone组1.41（95%CI 0.68-2.60, P=0.25）|||淋巴瘤特异性死亡累积发生率：CT-alone组2.3%，CT+RT组1.6%（P=0.53）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary gastric diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (PG-DLBCL) accounts for approximately 30% of all gastric lymphomas.While R-CHOP has been the standard first-line treatment for over two decades,achieving long-term disease control in a majority of PG-DLBCL patients,the necessity of consolidative radiotherapy (RT) for those reaching complete remission (CR) remains controversial in the rituximab era. Aims: This study aims to evaluate the role of consolidative radiotherapy and survival outcomes in patients with limited-stage PG-DLBCL who achieved CR after first-line chemotherapy(CT). Methods: Adult patients with limited-stage PG-DLBCL who achieved CR after first-line chemotherapy were retrospectively reviewed from May 2008 to September 2024 across two Chinese institutions. Survival outcomes were estimated using the Kaplan-Meier method and compared with the log-rank test. Standardized mortality ratios (SMRs) were calculated to assess curability by comparing observed deaths with expected deaths in the age- and sex-matched general Chinese population (UN World Population Prospects 2024). A competing risk framework differentiated lymphoma-specific mortality (LSM) from non-lymphoma mortality (NLM), with cumulative incidence functions (CIFs) compared using Gray’s test.

结论（EHA原文）

For limited-stage PG-DLBCL achieving CR after first-line chemotherapy, consolidative RT provides limited survival benefit due to exceptional local control and survival normalization. Competing risk analysis identifies NLM as the primary late mortality driver. While RT may not be mandatory for all, it may serve as a strategic enabler for chemotherapy de-escalation. The next step is to further investigate whether RT can serve as a key enabler for chemotherapy de-escalation.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 202 patients were included, with a median age of 55 years (range from 18 to 81). 96 (47.5%) patients received consolidative RT after chemotherapy , while 106 (52.5%) received CT alone. R-CHOP-like regimens were used in 83.2% of cases, with 48% and 48% completing baseline and post-treatment PET/CT assessments, respectively. With a median follow-up of 80.8 months, the 5-year OS, PFS, and LRC rates were 98.5% , 92.2% and 97.6% in the CT+RT group , compared to 86.4% (P=0.06), 83.5(P=0.04)and 95.8% (P=0.5) for the CT-alone group, respectively. Although a statistical difference in PFS was observed, consolidative RT did not significantly improve OS or LRC, consistent with the exceptionally low local recurrence rate (only 6 cases) across the entire cohort. A total of 14 deaths were recorded during follow-up. Notably, only 3 patients (21.4%) died of lymphoma-specific causes, 11 patients (78.6%) died of non-lymphoma-related causes, including second primary malignancies (n=3), hepatic disease (n=1), and other unknown causes (n=7). Survival outcomes were favorable and equivalent to the age- and sex-matched general population in both groups, with SMR of 0.64 (95% CI: 0.17–1.64; P = 0.54) for the CT+RT group and 1.41 (95% CI: 0.68–2.60; P = 0.25) for the CT-alone group, indicating that patients achieved life expectancy comparable to the general population. Competing risk analysis revealed that NLM was a prominent contributor to late mortality events, whereas the cumulative incidence of LSM remained low and comparable between the CT-alone and CT+RT groups (2.3% vs 1.6%, p = 0.53). Conclusion: For limited-stage PG-DLBCL achieving CR after first-line chemotherapy, consolidative RT provides limited survival benefit due to exceptional local control and survival normalization. Competing risk analysis identifies NLM as the primary late mortality driver. While RT may not be mandatory for all, it may serve as a strategic enabler for chemotherapy de-escalation. The next step is to further investigate whether RT can serve as a key enabler for chemotherapy de-escalation.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: High-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX) remains widely used as CNS prophylaxis in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), despite a lack of confirmatory randomized clinical trials. Nephrotoxicity, an important HD-MTX-related adverse event, can delay the delivery of curative immunochemotherapy but its occurrence has not been extensively studied in this setting. Aims: To explore the association between HD-MTX in first-line treatment of DLBCL and nephrotoxicity. Methods: Adults aged 18-79 years with first diagnosis of DLBCL between 01/07-2015 and 31/12-2023 were identified from the Danish Lymphoma Registry. Patients without CNS involvement and with no prior history of kidney disease, according to national laboratory registries and/or diagnosis registries, were included if they were treated with R-CHOP(-like) immunochemotherapy. \n Eligible patients were grouped by use of HD-MTX in first line (HD-MTX group vs no-HD-MTX group). The primary endpoint was the 5-year cumulative incidence of stage ≥G3a chronic kidney disease (CKD). Secondary endpoints were 5-year cumulative incidence of stage G5 CKD and 1-year cumulative incidences of any-stage acute kidney injury (AKI) and stage ≥2 AKI. CKD (stage ≥G3a) was defined as renal replacement therapy or two measurements of eGFR \n Death and re-treatment/relapse were treated as competing risks. Inverse probability of treatment weighting (IPTW) was used to adjust for differences in age, sex, hypertension, diabetes, bulk, Ann Arbor stage, number of extranodal sites, LDH, kidney involvement, B-symptoms, and Charlson Comorbidity Index.

结论（EHA原文）

The use of HD-MTX as CNS prophylaxis was not associated with CKD in patients with DLBCL. However, HD-MTX did lead to a substantially higher cumulative incidence of AKI, which could lead to untoward delays in immunochemotherapy or dose reductions. Without firmly documented efficacy of early intercalated HD-MTX, its use should be deferred till after completion of standard immunochemotherapy.

treatment access eliminates racial disparities but cannot overcome structural poverty: a national analysis of survival equity in curable lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=91246

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：R-CHOP（利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，长春新碱，泼尼松）；对照组：未接受R-CHOP（其他治疗）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：R-CHOP（利妥昔单抗，环磷酰胺，多柔比星，长春新碱，泼尼松）||对照组：未接受R-CHOP（其他治疗）

O 结局指标

接受R-CHOP的患者与未接受者相比，生存期减少4.5个月，每1000人生命年损失373年；未保险患者比私人保险患者损失3.6个月（303 LYL/1000），Medicaid患者损失3.7个月（307 LYL/1000）；高剥夺患者比无剥夺患者损失7.2个月（532 LYL/1000）；种族生存差异可通过平等R-CHOP交付完全消除。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B cell lymphoma is one of the few aggressive cancers we can cure, yet who receives that chance depends heavily on zip code, insurance status, and where a patient seeks care. Guideline discordance and socioeconomic disadvantage are known to worsen survival in DLBCL, yet prior studies rely on relative risk estimates and do not separate treatment-attributable from structural contributions to survival inequity. Aims: We aimed to quantify absolute survival penalties across insurance, deprivation, geography, race, and facility type, and to decompose each penalty into its preventable and structural components using a national cohort of 91,246 patients. Methods: Using the National Cancer Database, we identified patients with DLBCL diagnosed between 2014 and 2020. Guideline-concordant therapy was defined as multiagent chemotherapy plus rituximab. Inverse probability of treatment weighting balanced all 40 covariates before analysis. Survival penalties were quantified as restricted mean survival time differences at 36 months, expressed as life years lost per 1,000 patients. Socioeconomic deprivation was quantified using a composite score derived from five NCDB provided variables: zip code level income quartile, educational attainment quartile, insurance status, urban-rural classification, and distance to the treating facility. Each variable was dichotomized and summed to generate a score ranging from 0 to 5, then categorized as none (0), low (1), Moderate (2), High (3-5). Analyses were repeated within the 55,618 R-CHOP recipients to separate preventable from structural penalties.

结论（EHA原文）

Racial survival disparities in DLBCL are entirely preventable through equitable R-CHOP delivery. Socioeconomic penalties are harder to close. Poverty follows patients through the clinic door, and the majority of the survival gap driven by insurance inadequacy and deprivation persists regardless of treatment received. Eliminating survival inequity in curable lymphoma demands both equitable care delivery and the structural interventions that extend well beyond it.

It has a high negative predictive value after first-line treatment. DS score from 1 to 3 are widely considered as PET-negative, and scores of 4 and 5 as PET-positive indicating residual disease, however, false-positive results are relatively common. Aims: To assess the prognostic value of DS after first-line treatment in real-world DLBCL patients. Methods: This retrospective registry study included DLBCL patients with data collected from the medical records of three university hospitals in Finland. Adult patients who had been diagnosed with DLBCL between years 2000 and 2020, and had PET-CT results at the end of first-line treatment, were included in the study. Patients were excluded if they had primary DLBCL of the central nervous system, received radiotherapy to brain, or had immunosuppressive condition, or their PET-CT was positive, but DS could not be obtained. The survival endpoints were overall survival (OS), disease-specific survival (DSS) and progression-free survival (PFS), and they were calculated using the Kaplan-Meier method, and compared using the log-rank test. The Cox regression model was used for the multivariate analysis.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The dark zone signature (DZsig) stems from transcriptional differences between high‑grade B‑cell lymphomas with MYC and BCL2 rearrangements and other germinal centre B‑cell‑like (GCB) diffuse large B‑cell lymphomas (DLBCL). Around 20% of GCB‑DLBCLs are DZsig pos (Ennishi et al., J Clin Oncol, 2019; Alduaij et al., Blood, 2023). DZsig pos cases with TP53 abnormalities show poor survival, whereas those without exhibit favourable outcomes, reflecting prognostic heterogeneity. DZsig is considered a refinement of cell‑of‑origin (COO) classification; however, the drivers of its heterogeneous prognosis remain unclear. Aims: To develop and validate a prognostic scoring system for risk-stratifying DZsig pos -DLBCL. Methods: By calculating the 104 gene DZsig score for RNAseq data, DZsig pos cases were identified from an integrated public cohort (n=238) (Chapuy B et al., REMoDL-B, Lacy S et al., NCI, BCC cohorts) and our centre's cohort (n=21). Excluding BCC, the remaining public cohorts served as the training set (n=114). Immune infiltration gene sets were sourced from Tumuluru et al., Blood, 2025.

结论（EHA原文）

By integrating clinical and genetic factors, the DZPI stratifies DZsig pos -DLBCL into prognostic categories validated in a public cohort and our centre, with the high-risk category associated with a cold immune cluster and inferior survival to inform personalised therapy.

循环肿瘤dna在临床诊断之前很久就揭示了淋巴瘤相关突变

circulating tumor dna reveals lymphoma-associated mutations long before clinical diagnosis

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，经典型霍奇金淋巴瘤；N=46

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：circulating tumor dna reveals lymphoma-associated mutations long before clinical diagnosis

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

ctDNA检出率：31/46 (67%) 的病例在诊断前血浆中检出ctDNA； DLBCL: 13/33 (39%) 通过肿瘤信息指导的SNV检出ctDNA；20/33 (61%) 通过MNV检出ctDNA； cHL: 9/13 (69%) 通过MNV检出ctDNA； 最早检出时间：DLBCL诊断前106个月，cHL诊断前55个月； cHL中ctDNA水平与sTARC强相关（r=0.86）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The interval between early lymphoma-driving events and clinical presentation is poorly defined. Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) and classic Hodgkin lymphoma (cHL) arise from germinal-center (GC) B cells and carry recurrent genetic alterations. Incidental findings from noninvasive prenatal testing and population biobanks have identified tumor-specific somatic variants in plasma prior to cHL diagnosis. In cHL, serum thymus and activation-regulated chemokine (sTARC), a validated biomarker, is elevated long before symptom onset. Aberrant somatic hypermutation produces clustered in-cis substitutions, known as multi-nucleotide variants (MNVs), which frequently affect super-enhancers (SE) and other key B-cell regulating loci early in lymphomagenesis. MNVs provide a distinct mutational footprint that may enable highly sensitive tumor detection in cfDNA in pre-diagnostic plasma. We hypothesize that cfDNA analysis can capture these oncogenic events and map the temporal trajectory of lymphomagenesis. Aims: By integrating single nucleotide variant (SNV) and MNV calling, we aim to identify early molecular aberrations preceding clinical diagnosis of DLBCL and cHL. Methods: We analyzed pre-diagnostic plasma from the Dutch Lifelines biobank in a retrospective case-cohort of 33 DLBCL and 13 cHL patients, including matched diagnostic tumor tissue samples and white blood cells for 41 cases. Targeted sequencing of 115 genes (~391 kbp), including SEs of 14 genes was performed. SNV analysis was restricted to DLBCL, as tumor cell content in cHL tissue is too low to reliably call SNVs. MNVs were called using our in-house developed MNVista tool.

结论（EHA原文）

Summary/Conclusion: ctDNA can be detected years prior to B-cell lymphoma diagnosis. In total, 31/46 cases had detectable ctDNA in pre-diagnostic plasma samples. Our data show that MNV-approaches are sensitive and can be used for pre-diagnostic ctDNA detection in a tumor-informed setting. They provide novel insight in the rise of early molecular aberrations in DLBCL and cHL and support the use of ctDNA as liquid biopsy to aid in early diagnosis of patients suspected of lymphoma.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Patients with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) and primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) experiencing relapse after autologous hematopoietic cell transplantation (AHCT) have poor outcomes. Methods: The study population consisted of 119 patients with systemic DLBCL and 40 patients with PCNSL who underwent AHCT between 2000 and 2019 in three University Hospitals in Finland (Kuopio, Tampere, Oulu). 结论（EHA原文）

Our new risk classification for post-transplant relapse divides systemic DLBCL patients into three groups with significantly different RFS rates. Larger studies are needed to validate this classification.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The gut microbiota plays a pivotal role in immune regulation and cancer biology. Emerging evidence indicates that gut dysbiosis may contribute to the development of diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), the most prevalent and aggressive subtype of non-Hodgkin lymphoma. However, the specific microbial alterations associated with DLBCL have not been comprehensively synthesized. Aims: To systematically evaluate and synthesize evidence on gut microbiota (GMB) alterations associated with DLBCL, with a focus on species-level microbial signatures. Methods: A systematic review and meta-analysis of thirteen studies involving 4,087 cases was conducted. Both observational and Mendelian randomization (MR) studies were included. Random-effects models were used to calculate pooled odds ratios (ORs) for MR studies, while observational studies contributed to qualitative assessment. Microbial changes were analyzed at the species level to enhance biological interpretation.

结论（EHA原文）

This first comprehensive synthesis identifies a reproducible species-level microbial signature in DLBCL characterized by loss of beneficial taxa and enrichment of pro-tumorigenic microbes. These alterations may promote lymphomagenesis through inflammatory, metabolic, and immune-modulatory mechanisms. Our findings highlight the gut microbiota as a latent biomarker source and therapeutic target, supporting microbiota-modulating strategies in precision lymphoma care. \n Mendelian randomization studies detected a borderline overall association of gut microbiota and DLBCL. However, stratified analyses per taxa showed significant pooled OR shifting towards depletion for; Alistipes, Ruminococcaceae UCG011, Eubacterium coprostanoligenes group. Also, shifting towards abundance for; Bilophila Desulfovibrionaceae, Coprobacter \n Our qualitative analysis revealed abundance of pathogenic and pro-inflammatory taxa in treatment-naïve DLBCL patients, comprising Bacteroidetes_p, Bacteroides spp., Clostridium difficile, Enterobacteriaceae_f, Enterococcaceae_f, Fusobacteriia_c, Escherichia coli spp., Proteobacteria_p , and others. Concurrently, there was a marked depletion of beneficial commensals, including Bifidobacterium_g., Faecalibacterium_g, Roseburia_g., Eubacterium_g, Lachnospira_g and Lactobacillus_g., which are critical for maintaining gut barrier integrity and regulating immune homeostasis. The shift toward a microbiota dominated by inflammatory and opportunistic taxa, alongside the loss of beneficial species, may contribute to systemic immune dysregulation and disease progression in DLBCL.

overlaying tp53 loss and aneuploidy with distinct diffuse large b-cell lymphoma subtypes refines tumor classification and enhances risk stratification

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=1123

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：overlaying tp53 loss and aneuploidy with distinct diffuse large b-cell lymphoma subtypes refines tumor classification and enhances risk stratification

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

TP53+肿瘤的非整倍体评分显著高于TP53-肿瘤（p<0.001）|||TP53+/A+状态覆盖了大多数A53/C2亚型病例|||A+肿瘤富集生发中心B细胞样亚型，B细胞含量减少，DNA复制和修复程序改变|||TP53+与原发性难治和较差生存相关|||A+与较好预后相关，尤其在TP53+肿瘤中

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Genetic subtypes are widely used to stratify diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). Yet, patients within the same subtype often exhibit heterogeneous outcomes. While chromosome number alteration (CNA)-driven subtypes such as A53 and C2 capture genomic instability, they encompass tumors with variable degrees of aneuploidy. Loss-of-function (LOF) TP53 alterations and aneuploidy have each been associated with adverse prognosis, but their independent and combined effects in DLBCL remain insufficiently defined. Aims: To refine genomic stratification of DLBCL by disentangling the effects of TP53 loss and quantitative aneuploidy, we introduced two novel genomic instability statuses into Lymphly, our previously developed DLBCL genetic subtype classification framework. These statuses are TP53+/−, denoting TP53 LOF alterations, and A+/−, an aneuploidy-based status. This approach explicitly distinguishes TP53 loss from aneuploidy within Lymphly subtypes. Methods: We analyzed 1,123 DLBCL samples with genome-wide CNA profiling. Survival data were available for 579 samples. The aneuploidy score was defined as the number of chromosome arms deviating from average ploidy (excluding acentric arms). The distribution was bimodal (range 0–39), with a nadir at ~15. K-means clustering defined A+ tumors as those with >14 arm-level CNAs. TP53+ status was defined as TP53 LOF mutation or deletion. We also analyzed previously assigned A53/C2 cases to assess the concordance of these existing CNA-based subtypes with the Lymphly statuses. To evaluate the utility of the Lymphly statuses, we characterized their expression profiles and assessed their ability to stratify patients based on survival outcomes.

结论（EHA原文）

TP53 loss and high aneuploidy represent independent and clinically meaningful genomic dimensions in DLBCL, in addition to Lymphly subtypes. Their integration into Lymphly refines the existing A53/C2 classification and improves risk stratification based on biologically grounded, actionable insights. Our findings provide a robust framework for patient stratification based on genomic features, offering potential benefits for trial design, patient selection, and treatment decision-making.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: TP53+ tumors had significantly higher aneuploidy scores than TP53− tumors (p /− and A+ /− statuses captured most of the A53/C2 cases analyzed, demonstrating the ability of these two Lymphly statuses to delineate the sample composition and underlying biology of the A53 and C2 subtypes. \n Biologically, A+ tumors were enriched for the germinal center B-cell–like cell-of-origin (GCB COO), exhibited reduced B-cell content, and showed altered DNA replication and repair programs. Clinically, TP53+ was associated with primary refractoriness and inferior survival, whereas A+ was associated with improved prognosis, particularly among TP53+ tumors. Conclusion: TP53 loss and high aneuploidy represent independent and clinically meaningful genomic dimensions in DLBCL, in addition to Lymphly subtypes. Their integration into Lymphly refines the existing A53/C2 classification and improves risk stratification based on biologically grounded, actionable insights. Our findings provide a robust framework for patient stratification based on genomic features, offering potential benefits for trial design, patient selection, and treatment decision-making.

Optimal treatment management in the geriatric population is challenging due to the high-risk disease biology and their age-specific vulnerabilities. Combination chemotherapy is effective, however, due to frailty often a dose-reduced regimen is administered. This large population real-world study compares demographic, clinical and survival characteristics of patients older than 75 years and compares Academic Cancer Programs (ACP) vs Community Cancer Programs (CCP). Aims: To determine whether the treatment approach (adjusting for: age, race/ethnicity, insurance status, Charlson-Deyo comorbidity score, and distance from the treating facility) among elderly patients (equal or over 75 years old) with DLBCL in academic versus community hospitals influences overall survival in this lymphoma population. Methods: A retrospective analysis using the National Cancer Database was conducted on 103,671 patients (ACP: 51,848; CCP: 51,823) diagnosed with DLBCL between 2004 and 2022 was carried out. ACP included academic and National Cancer Institute-designated research centers; CCP included community, comprehensive community, and integrated network cancer programs. Kaplan-Meier and Cox regression models were used to compare overall survival (OS), adjusting for: age, race/ethnicity, insurance status, Charlson-Deyo comorbidity score, and distance from treating facility.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Understanding prognostic differences within heterogenous diseases can potentially change the way we approach individual patients. In early-stage Diffuse Large B-cell Lymphoma (DLBCL), extranodal sites such as testis, kidney and lung have been linked to poorer survival, but evidence supporting this association remains unclear. Aims: This study aimed to compare survival between primary extranodal and nodal-only disease and evaluate survival by extranodal site in early-stage (Ann Arbor stage I-II) DLBCL. Methods: We conducted a population-based cohort study, using data from the Swedish Lymphoma Register. The cohort consisted of adult patients diagnosed with stage I and II DLBCL in Sweden between 2007 and 2023, with follow-up through May 16 th 2024. Patients with involvement in the bone marrow, liver, pleura, ocular or central nervous system (CNS), as well as those with multiple extranodal sites, were excluded, as these features are consistent with stage IV DLBCL. Overall survival (OS) was estimated using the Kaplan-Meier method and compared using the log-rank test. Hazard ratios (HRs) with 95% confidence intervals, adjusted for potential confounding factors, were estimated using Cox proportional hazards models.

结论（EHA原文）

In this nationwide cohort of patients with early-stage DLBCL, the results suggest that extranodal involvement is not associated with poorer survival compared to nodal-limited disease. However, substantial site-specific heterogeneity exists, indicating that early-stage DLBCL is a clinical diverse group rather than a uniform entity. 弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤的完全客观3变量预后评分：两个独立队列共776名患者的开发和外部验证

a fully objective 3‑variable prognostic score for diffuse large b‑cell lymphoma: development and external validation in two independent cohorts totaling 776 patients

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=776

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：a fully objective 3‑variable prognostic score for diffuse large b‑cell lymphoma: development and external validation in two independent cohorts totaling 776 patients

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

开发并外部验证了一个基于年龄>75岁、白蛋白<3.5g/dL和LDH>正常上限的三变量预后评分。该评分将患者分为低危、中危、高危组，在两个独立队列（训练集402例，验证集374例）中均展现出稳健的风险分层能力。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The International Prognostic Index (IPI) and NCCN‑IPI remain widely used in diffuse large B‑cell lymphoma (DLBCL), but they include evaluator‑dependent variables such as performance status, extranodal involvement, and Ann Arbor stage, all of which are subject to interobserver variability. Serum albumin has repeatedly been reported as a strong prognostic factor but is not incorporated into existing indices. A simplified and fully objective prognostic score based solely on routine laboratory and demographic variables could improve reproducibility and clinical applicability. Aims: To identify robust prognostic factors using data‑driven methods and to construct an objective prognostic score that minimizes subjectivity while preserving discrimination. \n Methods: Patients were drawn from two independent Japanese institutions: 402 patients formed the derivation cohort and 374 the external validation cohort. Candidate predictors included age, albumin, LDH, performance status, extranodal involvement, and Ann Arbor stage. Albumin was dichotomized at 3.5 g/dL and LDH at the upper limit of normal based on widely accepted clinical thresholds, ensuring consistency with routine practice. For age, multiple dichotomization schemes (55–85 years) were evaluated using LASSO Cox regression with 1,000 bootstrap resamples, and restricted cubic spline modeling was used to assess the continuous effect of age and identify structural changes in risk. Models incorporating different predictor combinations were compared using C‑index and interpretability, and the final model was externally validated.

结论（EHA原文）

We developed and externally validated a simplified and fully objective 3‑variable prognostic score for DLBCL based on age, albumin, and LDH. The score demonstrated robust risk stratification across two independent cohorts totaling 776 patients and offers a reproducible and clinically practical alternative to existing prognostic indices. Because it relies solely on universally available variables, this score can be readily implemented in routine clinical practice.

中文结果摘录（原表）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is an aggressive, heterogeneous malignancy arising in nodal or extranodal sites. Among these, primary breast DLBCL (PB-DLBCL) represents a distinct entity characterized by unique clinicopathological features and an increased risk of central nervous system recurrence. However, systematic studies are currently lacking due to its rarity. Aims: This study conducted an integrated analysis to elucidate the distinct biological characteristics of PB-DLBCL and delineate its similarities and differences compared to nodal and IP-DLBCL. Methods: This single-center study enrolled 703 DLBCL patients (134 PB, 363 nodal, and 206 IP), excluding those with secondary extranodal involvement. Baseline clinical characteristics and survival data were retrospectively collected. Inverse probability of treatment weighting (IPTW) was applied to mitigate potential confounders. We performed DNA (n=223; 63 PB, 127 nodal, 33 IP) and RNA sequencing (n=121; 58 PB, 48 nodal, 15 IP) on the DLBCL cohort. The LymphGen algorithm was applied to subcategorize patients based on their genetic alteration profiles. Microenvironmental signatures were identified using the Lymphoma Microenvironment (LME) classification. A novel immortalized PB-DLBCL cell line was established and is intended for subsequent mechanistic research and evaluation of therapeutic strategies.

结论（EHA原文）

Overall, our comprehensive analysis defines PB-DLBCL as a distinct biological entity, distinguishable from nodal and IP-DLBCL. The prevalence of specific molecular subtypes and recurrent epigenetic dysregulation highlight the potential for novel precision therapeutic strategies.

clonal complexity defines distinct tumor-intrinsic biology and prognosis in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=74；疾病阶段：复杂性

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：clonal complexity defines distinct tumor-intrinsic biology and prognosis in diffuse large b-cell lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

5年无事件生存率：Poly-CC肿瘤患者41.5%，Mono-CC肿瘤患者71.1%（Log-rank p=0.079）|||ABC亚型中5年无事件生存率：Poly-CC肿瘤31.5%，Mono-CC肿瘤83.3%（p=0.0450）|||GCB亚型中5年无事件生存率：Poly-CC肿瘤50.0%，Mono-CC肿瘤55.5%（p=0.66）|||Poly-CC肿瘤Ki-67阳性率显著高于Mono-CC肿瘤（p=0.00227）|||Poly-ABC肿瘤中致病性突变数量显著高于Mono-ABC肿瘤（p=0.0147）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Intratumor heterogeneity (ITH) is increasingly recognized as a determinant of clinical outcome across cancers, yet its practical assessment remains challenging, particularly in routine biopsy specimens. We developed a simple method to quantify ITH from copy number variation (CNVs) data derived from formalin-fixed, paraffin-embedded (FFPE) samples, generating a Clonal Composition (CC) number that estimates the number of coexisting subclones. This approach was previously validated in ovarian cancer and hepatocellular carcinoma, where higher CC numbers were associated with inferior outcomes. Here, we apply this framework to diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), a disease with established inter-patient genetic heterogeneity but unresolved intratumor evolutionary complexity. Aims: We aimed to determine whether ITH can be quantitatively assessed in DLBCL, and to evaluate its association with the gene expression profiles, mutational landscape, tumor micro environment, and clinical outcomes, and to elucidate its impact on disease biology. Methods: Gene expression, copy number analyses and gene mutation analysis were performed in patients with newly diagnosed advanced-stage DLBCL using FFPE tumor specimens. CC number was calculated using a clustering approach that clusters all segments with same the B-allele frequency (BAF) and log2 ratio (log2R) values obtained from whole-genome copy number assay and then combines clusters corresponding the same percentage of aberrant cells (%AC). The correlations between CC number and biological, clinical characteristics, and prognosis were analyzed (Kindai University Faculty of Medicine Ethics Committee: Approval number R03-283).

结论（EHA原文）

These results suggest that clonal complexity captures tumor-intrinsic features and biological diversity in DLBCL, especially in ABC subtype, offering novel insights into the disease pathogenesis.

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=42

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：genomic architecture of irf4 rearrangements in children and adult large b-cell lymphomas

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

IRF4重排检测率：FISH检出38/42例；SV-NGS检出85%的病例；IRF4::IGH易位在CAYA LBCL-IRF4中占81%；成人DLBCL中IRF4断裂点位置不同；新发现IRF4::MIR142和IRF4::BATF易位；突变谱：BCR/NF-κB通路基因突变频繁，成人组有KMT2D、DTX1、MYD88-L265P突变；儿童组无LymphGen分类，成人组有EZB或MCD亚型；预后：年龄>40岁患者EFS显著较差。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Large B‑cell lymphoma with IRF4 rearrangement (LBCL‑ IRF4 ) predominantly affects children and young adults (CAYA) and typically presents as localized disease with an excellent outcome. Although IRF4 :: IGH translocations are detected in most cases, cryptic rearrangements have been proposed, and it remains unclear whether all IRF4 rearrangement ( IRF4 -R) share a common genomic architecture, involve non‑IG partners, or evade detection by FISH. NGS has revealed a distinct mutational profile including IRF4 and NF‑κB pathway mutations. Whether diffuse large B-cell lymphomas (DLBCL) with IRF4 -R in adults represents the same biological entity is uncertain. Aims: To define IRF4 ‑R architecture, characterize the mutational profile, and determine whether CAYA and adult IRF4 -R tumors share similar genomic features, supporting more precise diagnosis. Methods: We assembled a retrospective cohort of 42 patients including 28 pediatric (median age: 11y) and 7 young adult (median age: 29.5y) LBCL- IRF4 as well as 7 adult DLBCL with IRF4 -R (median age: 67.5y). All cases were classified according to current classification of Lymphoid Neoplasms. FISH analyses for BCL2 , BCL6 , MYC , IGH, and IRF4 were performed using commercial and custom break-apart probes, with additional custom probes to validate novel IRF4 partners. Copy‑number alterations were assessed by Oncoscan/Cytoscan arrays (n=42), and cell‑of‑origin was determined using the Lymph2Cx assay. Structural variants (SV) and mutations were profiled in 37 tumors using a custom targeted NGS panel (SV-NGS) covering 168 lymphoma‑related genes and key SV loci. Whole‑exome sequencing (WES) was performed on 38 cases. Genetic DLBCL subtypes were assigned using the LymphGen algorithm.

结论（EHA原文）

In conclusion, IRF4 -R architecture and mutational profile diverge according to age, supporting that not all adult cases should be classified as LBCL- IRF4 .

I 干预措施
