摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL) comprises biologically heterogeneous entities with variable clinical outcome. Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma/high-grade B-cell lymphoma with concurrent MYC and BCL2 rearrangements (DLBCL/HGBL- MYC/BCL2, hereafter HGBL-DH (double-hit)) represents a distinct entity characterized by frequent early refractory or relapsed disease. These patients are treated with more intensified treatment regimens than patients with DLBLC without MYC and BCL2 rearrangements (DLBCL-NOS (not otherwise specified)), however outcomes for HGBL-DH patients remain substantially inferior to those of DLBCL-NOS patients. Additional biomarkers to identify high-risk patients within the HGBL-DH subgroup are lacking. While MYC rearrangements ( MYC -R) in relation to its partner gene (Ig or non-Ig) and copy numbers at the MYC chromosome 8q locus have been studied in great detail, the relation of the various architectures with outcome has remained underexplored. Aims: We aimed to stratify HGBL-DH patients based on their complete genomic architecture, and study the association with patient outcome in a large set of LBCL patients enriched for MYC translocations. Methods: We obtained comprehensive next-generation sequencing of 76 HGBL-DH and 660 DLBCL-NOS samples derived from four clinical trials and one multicenter cohort. From this sequencing, we derived genomic mutations, translocations, and genome-wide copy number alterations. MYC-R and large-scale chromosome 8 gains were integrated to resolve their complete genomic architecture.

结论（EHA原文）

In conclusion, HGBL-DH patients with chromosome 8q copy number gain defines a subgroup of HGBL-DH patients with high risk of refractory/relapsed disease, while HGBL-DH patients without chromosome 8q gain have comparable outcomes to DLBCL-NOS patients. This allows upfront risk stratification and guiding of tailored treatment strategies based on chromosome 8q status.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: A small proportion of large B cell lymphoma carry MYC and BCL6 rearrangements, the so called MYC/BCL6 double hit lymphoma (DHL), of which there are conflicting reports regarding the prognosis. Occasional studies suggested this is likely due to the presence of pseudo MYC/BCL6 DHL, that is, those carried a single t(3;8) or MYC::BCL6 fusion, which likely had a better prognosis. However, the number of such studies is limited, and more studies are needed to confirm it. Aims: To explore the prognostic significance of MYC::BCL6 fusion in MYC/BCL6 DHL patients. Methods: FISH analysis was performed on unstained formalin-fixed, paraffin-embedded 4µm tissue sections or bone marrow aspirate smears using IGH::BCL2 dual-color dual-fusion probes; MYC dual-color break-apart probe, BCL6 dual-color break-apart probe, and MYC::BCL6 dual-color dual-fusion probes. Patient OS was analyzed using the Kaplan-Meier method and compared using the log-rank test (GraphPad Prism).

结论（EHA原文）

The clinicopathologic features were largely similar betwen MYC/BCL6 DHL patients with or without MYC::BCL6 fusion. MYC::BCL6 fusion is not a prognostic factor in MYC/BCL6 DHL patients.

丹麦人群淋巴瘤感染相关死亡率的时间趋势研究

temporal trends in infection-related proportional mortality in lymphoma: a danish population-based study

P 患者群体

外周T细胞淋巴瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，淋巴瘤，滤泡性淋巴瘤，霍奇金淋巴瘤；N=15849

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：temporal trends in infection-related proportional mortality in lymphoma: a danish population-based study

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

总体感染相关比例死亡率（2001-2005）：25.6% (95% CI: 22.9-28.6) 总体感染相关比例死亡率（2006-2010）：33.8% (95% CI: 30.8-37) 总体感染相关比例死亡率（2011-2015）：33.6% (95% CI: 30.8-36.6) 总体感染相关比例死亡率（2016-2020）：26.7% (95% CI: 24-29.6) PTCL患者感染相关比例死亡率：36.9% (95% CI: 32.5-41.4) HL患者感染相关比例死亡率：33.4% (95% CI: 28.3-39.0) FL患者感染相关比例死亡率：29.3% (95% CI: 25.2-33.8) DLBCL患者感染相关比例死亡率：28.5% (95% CI: 26.8-30.3)

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Lymphomas are heterogeneous cancers characterized by substantial variations in outcomes across histological subtypes. Over the past two decades, both treatment strategies and supportive care have undergone notable changes, which may have influenced the extent to which infections contribute to cause of death among lymphomas over time. Aims: To examine temporal trends in proportional mortality from infections in patients with lymphoma, both overall and stratified by histological subtype and treatment. Methods: This proportional mortality study included adult Danish patients (≥ 18 years) with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), follicular lymphoma (FL), peripheral T-cell lymphoma (PTCL), and Hodgkin’s lymphoma (HL) diagnosed in the period 2001-2020 and registered in the Danish National Lymphoma Registry (LYFO). The primary endpoint was proportional mortality from infections evaluated in restricted 5-year intervals. Mortality fully or partially attributed to infections was identified based on the presence of infections listed on death certificates. Secondary analyses included trends over time by age, first-line treatment, performance status, and lymphoma subtype.

结论（EHA原文）

A rising trend of infection-related deaths was observed among patients with DLBCL, HL, PTCL, and FL from 2001-2005 to 2006-2010. This pattern was also observed among those receiving standard first-line treatment for DLBCL, HL, and FL . In the most recent calendar period (2016-2020), infection-related mortality declined, which may reflect improved supportive care measures such as wider use of granulocyte-colony stimulating factor and antimicrobial prophylaxis. The observed stability in proportional mortality related to infections over time, despite a substantial increase in the median age of patients and more frequent use of curative chemotherapy in older patient groups, is consistent with improvements in supportive care.

164DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究PMBCL/特殊亚型CAR-T/细胞治疗PF986

O 结局指标

1年无进展生存率（1y-PFS）：总体57%（95%CI: 43-72%）|||1年总生存率（1y-OS）：总体62%（95%CI: 48-76%）|||1年非复发死亡率（1y-NRM）：17%（95%CI: 6-27%）|||1年累积复发率：26%（95%CI: 13-39%）|||按HSCT时缓解状态分层：CR组1y-PFS 78%（95%CI: 62-95），1y-OS 78%（95%CI: 61-95）；PR组1y-PFS 35%（95%CI: 15-55），1y-OS 47%（95%CI: 27-67）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Relapsed or refractory large B-cell lymphoma (rrLBCL) is associated with poor outcomes. Chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy cures 30-50% of rrLBCLs, but many still relapse or progress. CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies (BsAb) show 50-60% overall response rates, with complete responses (CR) in 23-40%, in both CAR-T-naïve and -exposed pts. Nevertheless, over half of responders relapse with 1-year progression-free survival (1y-PFS) of ~80% and ~30% after CR or partial response (PR), respectively. Allogeneic hematopoietic stem cell transplant (HSCT) may be curative in selected cases, possibly enhanced by graft-versus-lymphoma effects in BsAb-sensitive pts. Consolidation with HSCT in BsAb responders is an important mater of investigation, but non-relapse mortality (NRM) and uncertain survival benefit remain major concerns. Aims: This is a retrospective EBMT study aimed to address the efficacy and toxicity of consolidative HSCT in rrLBCL patients responding to BsAbs. Methods: Adults with rrLBCL who achieved CR or PR after BsAb therapy and received consolidation HSCT between January 2018 and February 2025 were included. Primary end-points were PFS and NRM. PFS was analyzed according to Kaplan-Meier method and estimated from the date of HSCT until PD, relapse, death, or last visit of follow-up, whichever occur first. NRM was analyzed using cumulative incidence function with relapse as competing event.

结论（EHA原文）

With the limitations inherent to the absence of a suitable comparator and to its retrospective nature, this study suggests that the NRM of consolidative HSCT following BsAb is not higher than that reported with the same approach in pts with rrLBCL. The 1y-PFS observed is similar to those reported with BsAb alone in both CR and PR cohorts. A longer follow-up and further investigation in larger cohorts may clarify the potential benefits of this strategy.

165DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究PMBCL/特殊亚型CAR-T/细胞治疗PF1414

axicabtagene ciloleucel在台湾复发/难治性弥漫性大b细胞淋巴瘤和原发性纵隔b细胞淋巴瘤患者接受两种系统治疗后的成本效益

cost-effectiveness of axicabtagene ciloleucel in taiwanese patients with relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma and primary mediastinal b-cell lymphoma after two lines of systemic therapy

P 患者群体

原发纵隔大B细胞淋巴瘤，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；疾病阶段：复发/难治，原发性

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Tisagenlecleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰；分组：试验组1：axicabtagene ciloleucel；对照组1：tisagenlecleucel

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：axicabtagene ciloleucel|||对照组1：tisagenlecleucel

O 结局指标

无折扣生存年：axi-cel 11.63年 vs tisa-cel 7.86年，增量3.77年|||质量调整生存年(QALY)：axi-cel 6.84 QALYs vs tisa-cel 4.33 QALYs，增量2.51 QALYs|||总折扣成本：axi-cel NTD 9.24M (USD 307,991) vs tisa-cel NTD 9.26M (USD 308,557)|||增量成本效果比(ICER)：axi-cel占优（成本更低，效果更好）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is the most common aggressive B-cell lymphoma in Taiwan and continues to contribute substantially to the national lymphoma disease burden. Although a proportion of patients can achieve long-term remission with frontline therapy, a clinically important subgroup progresses through multiple lines of treatment. In the third-line and beyond (3L+) setting, effective therapeutic options remain limited, resulting in poor long-term survival. The management of 3L+ DLBCL therefore represents a significant clinical and policy challenge, particularly in the context of emerging one-time cellular therapies and the need to prioritize healthcare resources. \n In Taiwan, chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR T-cell) therapies have been introduced into clinical practice, yet access differs by product. Currently, the National Health Insurance (NHI) reimburses tisagenlecleucel (tisa-cel) for 3L+ treatment, while axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel) remains unreimbursed, underscoring the need for robust local economic evidence to inform reimbursement decisions. Aims: This study aims to assess the cost-effectiveness of axi-cel compared to tisa-cel as a 3L+ treatment for DLBCL and primary mediastinal B-cell lymphoma (PMBCL) in Taiwan from the perspective of National Health Insurance. Methods: To account for potential long-term survival and cure effects associated with CAR T-cell therapy, a partitioned survival mixture cure model (PS-MCM) adapted with Taiwan-specific parameters was used to evaluate the clinical and economic outcomes of axi-cel and tisa-cel. The model included three health states: pre-progression survival, post-progression survival, and death. Clinical efficacy inputs were derived from trial data adjusted using a matching-adjusted indirect comparison (MAIC) to enable comparative analysis in the absence of head-to-head trials. Costs and resource use were informed by the Taiwan NHI database, local clinical expert opinion, and published literature. Background mortality was based on the 2023 Taiwan life tables. A lifetime horizon (40 years), monthly cycles, and a 3% annual discount rate were applied. Measured outcomes included total costs, quality-adjusted life years (QALYs), and incremental cost-effectiveness ratios (ICERs).

结论（EHA原文）

This analysis shows that axi-cel delivers greater health benefits at lower overall costs than tisa-cel in patients with 3L+ R/R DLBCL and PMBCL, representing a dominant treatment option. These findings further support axi-cel’s value for reimbursement consideration in Taiwan.

risk for cytokine release syndrome in patients with large b-cell lymphoma treated with cd3xcd20 bispecific antibodies: an international multicenter retrospective study

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies (BsAbs) have emerged as a highly effective \"off-the-shelf\" immunotherapy for relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL). However, cytokine release syndrome (CRS) remains the primary toxicity limiting their clinical use. While a predictive model for CRS risk was recently developed for glofitamab (Gritti et al., Blood Adv. 2024), its utility is limited by the need for specific parameters and a lack of validation across the broader class of CD3xCD20 BsAbs. There is a critical need for an easily applicable, universal clinical tool to identify patients at low risk for clinically significant (grade 2+) CRS to optimize management strategies and potentially facilitate outpatient administration. Aims: The primary objective of this multicenter retrospective study is to develop and validate a clinical score to identify patients with R/R LBCL at low risk of developing grade 2+ CRS following the first or full therapeutic dose of a CD3xCD20 BsAb. In this abstract preliminary analysis and characterization of the incidence of CRS will be presented. Methods: This is a retrospective, international, multicenter study. Data were collected from adult patients with R/R LBCL, including diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL), LBCL transformed from indolent lymphoma (t-LBCL), high-grade B-cell lymphoma (HGBCL), and primary mediastinal B-cell lymphoma (PMBCL) treated with CD3xCD20 BsAbs, including glofitamab and epcoritamab. CRS was graded according to the 2019 ASTCT criteria. Pre-treatment clinical factors, laboratory parameters, and radiologic data were analyzed. Missing data were handled using multiple imputation by chained equations. Candidate predictors were selected using penalized regression (LASSO). Variables identified as stable predictors were subsequently entered into a multivariable logistic regression model to identify independent factors associated with CRS.

结论（EHA原文）

In LBCL, CRS risk factors largely converge on disease burden and kinetics. Analysis of this multi-national large cohort of patients is ongoing, full results and the predictive score will be presented at the meeting.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary Mediastinal Large B-cell Lymphoma (PMBCL) is an aggressive B-cell lymphoma predominantly affecting young adults. While frontline chemoimmunotherapy achieves favorable outcomes, patients with relapsed/refractory (R/R) disease face poor prognosis. Immunotherapy, such as PD-1 inhibitors, has demonstrated clinical activity, but response rates remain heterogeneous. Recent studies have identified TCF1+ progenitor exhausted T-cells within the tumor microenvironment (TME) as a critical determinant of immunotherapy efficacy in various malignancies. These TCF1+ T-cells possess stem-like properties and self-renewal capacity, enabling sustained anti-tumor responses upon immune checkpoint blockade. However, their predictive value in R/R PMBCL remains poorly characterized. Aims: This study aimed to investigate the association between the proportion of intratumoral TCF1+ T-lymphocytes and clinical outcomes in patients with R/R PMBCL receiving immunotherapy. Methods: We analyzed 27 patients with R/R PMBCL who received immunotherapy as second-line therapy (anti-PD-1 monotherapy or PD1 plus chemotherapy). Patients were stratified based on the proportion of TCF1+ cells among CD8+ tumor-infiltrating lymphocytes (TILs) assessed by immunohistochemistry: high TCF1+ group (n=12, TCF1+ ≥25%) and normal/low TCF1+ group (n=15, TCF1+

结论（EHA原文）

A high proportion of intratumoral TCF1+ T-lymphocytes is strongly associated with superior response rates and significantly prolonged survival in patients with R/R PMBCL treated with immunotherapy. These findings support the integration of TCF1+ T-cell assessment into clinical decision-making and may facilitate the development of personalized treatment strategies in R/R PMBCL.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Adolescents and young adults (AYA) (ages 16–39) with lymphoma require tailored treatment strategies that address unique molecular pathologies, long-term complications, and psychosocial factors. However, due to the low incidence in this age group, comprehensive data regarding the clinical and biological characteristics of AYA aggressive B-cell lymphomas (BCLs) remain limited. Aims: To elucidate the clinical, pathological, and molecular landscape of mature aggressive BCLs in the AYA population. Methods: We studied 119 cases diagnosed with mature aggressive BCL between 2012 and 2020. Clinical and pathological data were collected from the Japan National Hospital Organization (NHO) registry for AYA patients. Centralized pathological review was performed. Formalin-fixed paraffin-embedded (FFPE) specimens were analyzed using immunohistochemistry (IHC), FISH, targeted sequencing (TS), and RNA sequencing (RNA-seq). This study was approved by the NHO Central Research Ethics Committee and conducted in accordance with the Ethical Guidelines for Life Science and Medical Research in Japan (UMIN000046477).

结论（EHA原文）

AYA mature aggressive BCLs exhibit significant molecular and histological heterogeneity that may be unique to this age group. Although the overall prognosis for aggressive BCL in the AYA population is relatively favorable, the identification of high-risk or biologically distinct subsets through integrated TS, RNA-seq, and histological analysis underscores the potential for more precise treatment stratification in this population.

169DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PF1257

going for seconds: clinical outcomes and response predictors following second cd19 car t-cell infusion

P 患者群体

B细胞急性淋巴细胞白血病，弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，滤泡性淋巴瘤；N=12

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Lisocabtagene maraleucel；Tisagenlecleucel；zorpocabtagene autoleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰；分组：单组：接受第二次CD19 CAR T细胞输注的患者，使用药物包括axi-cel、tisa-cel、liso-cel、MB-CART19.1

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

最佳总体缓解率（ORR）：91%（完全缓解58%，部分缓解33%）|||中位无进展生存期（PFS）：9.2个月（范围0.9–58.7）|||中位随访时间：11.9个月（范围0.9–58.7）|||死亡人数：7例，其中5例因复发/进展

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: CD19-directed CAR T-cell therapy has transformed outcomes in relapsed or refractory B-cell malignancies. Nevertheless, a substantial proportion of patients relapse after an initial response to CAR T cell therapy (CAR1) and prognosis after progression remains poor. In selected patients with late relapse, reinfusion of a cryopreserved second bag of the identical CAR-T product (CAR2) has been employed as a salvage strategy. This approach allows interrogation of disease- and host-intrinsic determinants of restored sensitivity to the same CART product. However, clinical experience remains limited, and the biological factors underlying differential outcomes after CAR2 are poorly understood. Aims: We sought to identify determinants of restored therapeutic sensitivity to CAR2 by contrasting durable responders with patients experiencing repeat relapse. Methods: We performed a multicenter retrospective observational cohort study of adults with B-cell malignancies relapsing after CAR1 who received CAR2 infusion. 12 patients were included (DLBCL n=7, FL n=1, B-ALL n=4) treated with axi-cel (n=6), tisa-cel (n=2), liso-cel (n=1) or MB-CART19.1 (n=3). 10 of 12 patients received a back-up bag (2nd bag) of the leukapheresis product collected prior to CAR1. The remaining two patients underwent another round of leukapheresis after CAR1. Variables captured for both infusions included toxicity profiles, best response according to Lugano criteria as well as PFS and OS.

结论（EHA原文）

In this real-world cohort, CAR2 appears to be a feasible salvage strategy in selected patients. Late CAR1 relapse and better response to CAR1 emerge as predictors of response to CAR2. In addition, differences in LDH levels at CAR2 reinfusion are observed between responders vs non-responders while toxicity severity diminished between CAR1 and CAR2 within the same patient. Further analyses investigating biological mechanisms underlying these associations are ongoing and will be presented.

170DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2098

基线中性粒细胞与淋巴细胞比值（nlr）对双特异性抗体治疗后淋巴瘤患者生存结果的影响

impact of baseline neutrophil-to-lymphocyte ratio (nlr) on survival outcomes in patients with lymphoma following bispecific antibody treatment

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤，滤泡性淋巴瘤；N=494

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：艾可瑞妥单抗；格菲妥单抗；莫妥珠单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

1. 中位无进展生存期（PFS）：总体6.2个月；高NLR组（>5.0）3.8个月 vs 低NLR组12.1个月，HR=1.45（95%CI 1.1-1.8，p<0.01） 2. 中位总生存期（OS）：总体21.5个月；高NLR组（>5.3）8.8个月 vs 低NLR组21.5个月，HR=1.4（95%CI 1.06-2.05，p=0.02） 3. 总体缓解率（ORR）和完全缓解率（CRR）文中未给出具体数值。

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Bispecific antibodies (BsAbs) approved for relapsed/refractory (R/R) follicular lymphoma (FL) and diffuse large B-cell lymphomas (DLBCL) harness T-cells to mediate anti-tumor activity. T-cell fitness and the immunosuppressive tumor microenvironment may influence treatment response and outcomes. The NLR is a readily available biomarker that correlates with inflammation and immune suppression by myeloid cells. While elevated NLR at diagnosis is associated with inferior outcomes in DLBCL, its prognostic relevance in patients (pts) treated with BsAbs remains unknown. Aims: We sought to evaluate whether the baseline NLR may be prognostic of BsAb efficacy and aimed to identify NLR thresholds associated with response and survival outcomes. Methods: We conducted a multicenter retrospective study of adult pts with R/R LBCL who received BsAbs (glofitamab (glofit), epcoritamab (epco) or mosunetuzumab (mosu)) outside of a clinical trial between 2023 and 2026 at 10 centers in the Collaborative US Bispecifics Consortium (CUBIC). Efficacy outcomes included overall response rate (ORR), complete response rate (CRR), progression free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS). Optimal NLR cutoffs were identified using receiver operating characteristic (ROC) curve analysis for ORR/CRR, and using maximally selected rank statistics for PFS/OS, with performance assessed by 5-fold cross-validation. Logistic regression was used to evaluate NLR (modeled continuously and dichotomized) in relation to ORR /CRR, and Cox proportional hazards models were used to assess its association with PFS/OS. All models were adjusted for baseline clinical and pathological covariates, with statistical significance defined as α = 0.05.

结论（EHA原文）

A high pre-tx NLR (>5.0) is associated with inferior PFS and OS in pts treated with BsAbs, independent of disease subtype or specific agent. NLR is a readily available prognostic marker of response and survival, unlike more complex assays of T-cell phenotype and function. Further investigation into the immunobiological mechanisms driving BsAb resistance in non-responders is warranted.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: 494 pts were included; 68% (n=338) with LBCL/HGBCL (25% transformed), 19% FL (n=94), 13% other histologies (n=62). Pts received glofit (41%), epco (35%), or mosu (24%). Prior to BsAb, median age was 69 yrs (range 22-93) and 64% had stage 4 disease. The median pre-treatment (tx) WBC was 5.4 (range 0.1-205), ANC was 3.5 (range 0-82), ALC was 0.70 (range 0-197), and NLR was 10 (range 0-274). There was no difference among age, sex, stage, elevated LDH, or prior therapies (CAR-T, auto-SCT, number of prior lines of therapy) among pts with pre-tx high NLR vs low NLR. Use of BsAb was similar other than lower use of mosu among pts with high NLR vs low NLR (13% vs 31%). At a median follow up of 13 months, the median PFS and OS among all pts were 6.2 months and 21.5 months, respectively. The optimal cutoff for a high NLR was determined to be 5.0 for PFS and 5.3 for OS. For high vs low NLR, the median PFS and OS were 3.8 vs 12.1 months and 8.8 vs 21.5 months, respectively. After adjusting for baseline clinico-pathological variables, high NLR was independently associated with an inferior PFS (NLR>5.0, HR 1.45, 95% CI 1.1-1.8, p 5.3, HR 1.4, 95% CI 1.06-2.05, p=0.02) compared to low NLR (Figure 1). NLR as a continuous variable was also significantly associated with PFS (p=0.02) and OS (p Conclusion: A high pre-tx NLR (>5.0) is associated with inferior PFS and OS in pts treated with BsAbs, independent of disease subtype or specific agent. NLR is a readily available prognostic marker of response and survival, unlike more complex assays of T-cell phenotype and function. Further investigation into the immunobiological mechanisms driving BsAb resistance in non-responders is warranted.

171DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2085

瑞典一项基于人群的研究：复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤患者接受car-t治疗与自体干细胞移植的感染率以及普通人群的感染率

infection rates in patients treated with car-t versus autologous stem cell transplant for relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma and in the general population: a swedish population-based study

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=3264；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

分组：试验组1：CAR-T治疗；对照组1：自体干细胞移植（ASCT）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组1：CAR-T治疗|||对照组1：自体干细胞移植（ASCT）

O 结局指标

总体感染发生率（每人年）：CAR-T组2.96 (2.63-3.32)，ASCT组1.05 (0.96-1.15)，一般人群0.28 (0.26-0.29)|||CAR-T与ASCT的感染发生率比（IRR）：2.52 (95% CI 2.15-2.96)|||CAR-T与一般人群的IRR：9.26 (95% CI 7.96-10.76)|||最常见感染类型均为细菌感染，病毒和真菌感染在CAR-T和ASCT组更常见|||淋巴瘤复发是CAR-T（96%）和ASCT（76%）患者的主要死因；感染是ASCT患者非复发死亡的主要原因（14%），CAR-T患者无感染相关死亡

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Infectious diseases are the leading cause of non-relapse mortality (NRM) in patients with relapsed/refractory large B-cell lymphoma (R/R LBCL) treated with chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR-T) therapy or autologous stem cell transplant (ASCT). Direct population-based comparisons of infection rates among patients treated in clinical routine and the general population are limited. Aims: To compare incidence rates of infection in R/R LBCL patients treated with CAR-T versus ASCT, and versus matched comparators from the general population. Methods: LBCL patients treated with CAR-T or ASCT for between September 2019 – February 2024 were identified through the Swedish Lymphoma register and the National Patient Register (NPR). Patients were matched 1:10 according to birth year, sex and year of CAR-T/ASCT to comparators from the general population. Infectious disease according to ICD-10 codes from hospital in- and outpatient visits in the NPR or dispensing of an anti-infective medication (excluding standard prophylaxis medications) in the National Prescribed Drug Register was counted as an infectious episode. Follow-up started at CAR-T/ASCT (or matched index date) and ended at death, allogeneic transplantation, treatment switch between CAR-T/ASCT, or administrative censoring (March 1, 2024). Infection incidence rates (IR) and incidence rate ratios (IRR) were estimated using Poisson regression with log person-time offset and robust standard errors. Time since treatment was modelled using restricted cubic splines.

结论（EHA原文）

R/R LBCL patients treated with CAR-T had several-fold higher infection rates compared with ASCT and the general population. The higher incidence of infections appeared to persist for at least four years after CAR-T. A hypothesized mechanism for this prolonged risk of infections in CAR-T patients may be the persistence of functional CAR-T cells and off-target B-cell aplasia in relapse-free patients. As expected, the leading cause of NRM in ASCT patients was infections. Contrary to previous studies, there was no mortality from infections after CAR-T. This may be attributable to an increased use of immunoglobulin treatment or improved management of infectious complications.

172DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PS2074

real-world outcomes of glofitamab plus gemcitabine and oxaliplatin in relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma: a european multicenter cohort

P 患者群体

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: *Contributed equally Gemcitabine and oxaliplatin with glofitamab (Glo-Gem-Ox, STARGLO regimen) is now approved in relapsed/refractory (r/r) diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) in Europe. Nevertheless real-world evidence regarding this regimen is sparse and important sub-groups such as transformed indolent or double hit (DH) - lymphoma were not included in the privotal trial. Aims: To evaluate response, progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS), safety/toxicity and bridging intent in a multicenter real-world cohort treated with Glo-Gem-Ox, including transformed low grade and DH - lymphoma. Methods: We retrospectively analyzed 149 consecutive patients with r/r LBCL treated with Glo-Gem-Ox across multiple European centers. Transformed low-grade and DH cases were included according to the recorded histopathologic diagnosis. Baseline characteristics included age, Ann Arbor stage, LDH, IPI, number of prior therapy lines, and prior CAR-T therapy. Best overall response (BOR) was categorized as CR (including metabolic CR) and PR. PFS was calculated from treatment initiation to documented PD or death from any cause. Overall survival (OS) was defined as the time from treatment initiation to death from any cause and was estimated using the Kaplan–Meier method. Median follow-up was estimated using the reverse Kaplan–Meier method.

结论（EHA原文）

Glo-Gem-Ox demonstrated high response rates and promising outcomes despite short follow-up in this high-risk real-world r/r LBCL cohort including transformed and DH - cases that were excluded from the pivotal trial. The treatment was frequently used as a bridging therapy to CART-T or alloPBSCT. These findings support its relevance in routine practice and warrant further evaluation.

173DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PF978

car-ipi的开发和验证，这是一种基于机器学习的复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤预后评分，用抗cd19-cart细胞治疗

development and validation of car-ipi, a machine learning–derived prognostic score for relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma treated with anti-cd19 car t cells

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=2259；疾病阶段：复发/难治

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CD19靶向CAR-T(爱康得生物)；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

CAR-IPI模型在测试集的表现： C-index中位数：67.9%（范围67.1-68.2） 6个月AUC中位数：74.3%（73.4-75.4） 12个月AUC中位数：74.5%（73.7-75.2）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Anti-CD19 chimeric antigen receptor (19CAR) T-cell therapy has transformed the prognosis of large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), yet nearly half of treated patients relapse. Response to and survival after 19CAR T cells is influenced by patient-, tumor- and treatment-related factors. However, no validated prognostic score currently identifies patients at high risk of progression or relapse. Aims: To develop a robust international prognostic score, named CAR-IPI, predicting progression-free survival (PFS) after 19CAR T cell therapy for LBCL, independently of CAR product or line of therapy, using machine-learning (ML) approaches and routinely available clinical and biological variables. Methods: Patients from the French DESCAR-T registry receiving 19CAR T cells for LBCL in 2 nd line or more were selected (n=2259). The cohort was randomly split into training (80%, n=1807) and testing (20%, n=452) sets. Eighteen clinically relevant variables were screened. The treatment line (2 nd vs 3 rd or more) and CAR product were combined into a single variable and added to the models as an additional variable or as strata. Missing data were imputed 10 times independently in training and testing sets. Three ML approaches were applied: elastic net (EN) penalized Cox model, random survival forests (RSF), and support vector machine (SVM). Predictive performances were assessed in each imputed test set using the C-index and time-dependent AUC at 6 and 12 months. A simplified version of the score including four variables (sCAR-IPI) was derived from the 10-variable score CAR-IPI.

结论（EHA原文）

Using ML approaches, we developed CAR-IPI, a robust 10-variable prognostic score based on parameters routinely available at lymphodepletion. Both CAR-IPI and its simplified 4-variable version accurately predicted PFS after 19CAR T-cell therapy in LBCL, independently of CAR product and treatment line. The model outperformed existing scores (IPI, CAR-HEMATOTOX) and may improve risk stratification, patient selection and individualized therapeutic strategies.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

174DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究转化/RichterCAR-T/细胞治疗PF1246

cd19/cd12双特异性car-t细胞治疗后携带癌症易感性基因突变的dlbcl患者继发性外周t细胞淋巴瘤

secondary peripheral t-cell lymphoma in a patient of dlbcl harboring cancer susceptibility gene mutation following cd19/cd22 bispecific car-t cell therapy

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=1；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CD19/CD22靶向CAR-T(同仁医院)；靶点：CD19，CD22；类别：CAR-T，自体细胞，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

确认克隆起源：T细胞受体（TCR）测序显示CAR-T产物和PTCL组织具有相同的克隆重排（TRBD101/TRBJ2701和TRGV801/TRGJ101）|||基因组分析：全基因组测序发现TET2致病性体细胞突变（p.R1261H, p.E1755），在PTCL中变异等位基因频率更高|||胚系突变：患者携带BLM p.L107Ffs*36突变，导致基因组不稳定性|||其他致癌事件：包括KMT2A和ATM的11q23.2q25缺失、X染色体丢失、CAR载体整合至抑癌基因（NF1, CBX5, RNF213）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Chimeric antigen receptor (CAR)-T cell therapy has revolutionized treatment for relapsed/refractory B-cell malignancies, but rare secondary T-cell malignancies have emerged as a serious safety concern. Aims: We report a case of secondary peripheral T-cell lymphoma (PTCL) definitively proven to originate from infused CD19/CD22 bispecific CAR-T cells, with comprehensive molecular characterization of oncogenic mechanisms. Methods: A 66-year-old woman with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) and history of breast and cervical cancers received autologous CD19/CD22 CAR-T cells in November 2024 following CNS relapse. Nine months post-infusion, she developed a lower lip mass diagnosed as PTCL, not otherwise specified (PTCL-NOS). Comparative genomic analysis of the CAR-T product and PTCL tissue was performed. Whole genome sequencing (WGS), T-cell receptor (TCR) clonality assessment, single-cell RNA sequencing (scRNA-seq), and targeted mutation analysis were conducted on pre-infusion CAR-T product, peripheral blood mononuclear cells (PBMCs), and PTCL tissue.

结论（EHA原文）

This case provides unequivocal molecular evidence of CAR-T cell malignant transformation driven by three convergent factors: (1) pre-existing TET2 driver mutations representing clonal hematopoiesis, (2) germline BLM deficiency exacerbating genomic instability, and (3) insertional mutagenesis from CAR vector integration. These findings underscore the critical importance of pre-infusion genomic screening of CAR-T products for CHIP-related mutations, cancer susceptibility gene testing in patients with prior malignancies, and lifelong surveillance for secondary malignancies in CAR-T recipients.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Pola-R-CHP (polatuzumab vedotin with rituximab, cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, and prednisone) has been approved for first-line treatment of diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL). However, real-world outcomes data compared against R-CHOP (rituximab, cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, and prednisone) remain limited, especially in Asian cohorts where POLARIX subset analysis has suggested overall survival (OS) benefit. Aims: We aim to evaluate the efficacy of Pola-R-CHP in a real-world Asian setting for first-line treatment of DLBCL. Methods: We conducted a retrospective observational study (APOLLO: Asian POLA-R-CHP reaL-world Outcomes) in an international, multi-centre cohort from Singapore and Hong Kong, involving patients with newly diagnosed DLBCL between January 2015 to 2026. Physician assessed best response rates after treatment completion were documented. Analyses were conducted using Kaplan-Meier models and Cox proportional-hazards analysis. Given differences in follow-up duration between cohorts, analyses were restricted to the first 24 months, during which adequate follow-up was observed in both groups. Restricted mean survival time (RMST) at 24 months was also calculated to compare survival within the fixed time horizon.

结论（EHA原文）

Our early real-world data suggest that Pola-R-CHP may provide significant OS and PFS benefit over R-CHOP, including in patients with IPI scores 3-5 and in non-GCB DLBCL, highlighting its potential role in higher-risk disease.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: \n Clonal hematopoiesis (CH) in diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) has been insufficiently characterized across compartments and over time, limiting understanding of its biological and clinical relevance. Aims: i ) Characterize CH from the myeloid compartment and plasma cfDNA; ii ) evaluate the clinical impact of CH in newly diagnosed DLBCL and its association with disease molecular subtypes; iii ) assess the clonal dynamics of CH at baseline and at end of treatment (EOT); iv ) determine the prevalence and clinical significance of tumor infiltrating (TI)-CH in DLBCL. Methods: \n \n We analyzed 453 samples from 157 newly diagnosed DLBCL patients treated with R-CHOP–like regimens using CAPP-Seq–based NGS targeting 28 CH-related genes. Samples included peripheral blood (PB) Ficoll isolated granulocytes (n=151), serial plasma cfDNA [n=107 baseline, n=47 at cycle (C) 3, and n=92 at EOT], and lymph node biopsies (n=56). Clonal fitness was estimated from weighted regression on logit-transformed VAF (Fig. 1E). DLBclass clustering was available for 102 patients. \n

结论（EHA原文）

\n Multi-compartment profiling shows that CH in DLBCL is frequent and detectable in multiple compartments, enriched in specific molecular subtypes, and associated with an increased risk of second primary malignancies. R-CHOP–based therapy promotes expansion of CH clones, including early emergence of PPM1D mutations. While CH in PB did not significantly affect survival, TI-CH DNMT3A mutations emerged as an independent predictor of inferior PFS and OS in DLBCL treated with CIT.

Results: \n Median age of the cohort was 67 years. Both DNMT3A and TET2 mutations significantly associated with an increased risk of second primary malignancies (5-year CIF: 7.1 vs 16.3, P =0.03; 7.3 vs 19.4, p . 摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Epstein-Barr virus-positive diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (EBV+ DLBCL) is an aggressive subtype accounting for 10%–15% of DLBCL cases worldwide. Despite advances in chemoimmunotherapy, patients with EBV+ DLBCL continue to experience inferior outcomes compared to EBV-negative counterparts. The International Prognostic Index (IPI) is widely used for DLBCL risk stratification, but no dedicated prognostic model exists for EBV+ DLBCL. Emerging evidence suggests that pretreatment plasma EBV-DNA level may serve as a prognostic biomarker. However, models incorporating this parameter are lacking. We therefore conducted a retrospective study to develop a prognostic model integrating plasma EBV-DNA level for EBV+ DLBCL. Aims: To evaluate the prognostic impact of plasma EBV-DNA level on overall survival (OS) and progression-free survival (PFS), and to develop a predictive model for OS in patients with EBV+ DLBCL. Methods: This single-center retrospective study enrolled 58 patients diagnosed with EBV+ DLBCL at West China Hospital, Sichuan University between January 2010 and January 2025. OS and PFS were analyzed using the Kaplan-Meier method and multivariable Cox proportional hazards regression, and plasma EBV-DNA level was log10-transformed for the regression model. A nomogram was constructed based on the Cox model to visualize probability estimates for OS. The model's discriminatory performance was quantified by Harrell's C-index, after verifying the proportional hazards assumption with the Schoenfeld residuals test.

结论（EHA原文）

The prognostic model incorporating plasma EBV-DNA level, presence of HLH, and ECOG-PS ≥2 demonstrated robust predictive performance for outcomes in patients with EBV+ DLBCL, and may facilitate risk stratification and individualized treatment decisions.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Ki67 index was ≥20% in all 53 patients assessed, and CD30 positivity was 76.6% (36/47). After a median follow-up of 39 months (range 0.7–137.4), the 1-year, 3-year, and 5-year OS rates were 62.1%, 48.3%, and 36.2%, respectively, and the corresponding PFS rates were 60.3%, 44.8%, and 34.5%. \n Univariate analysis revealed that plasma EBV-DNA level, presence of HLH, ECOG-PS ≥2, and age ≥60 years are independent prognostic factors for both OS and PFS. Multivariate Cox proportional hazards model identified plasma EBV-DNA level (log10-transformed) (HR 1.75; 95% CI, 1.28-2.38; P Conclusion: The prognostic model incorporating plasma EBV-DNA level, presence of HLH, and ECOG-PS ≥2 demonstrated robust predictive performance for outcomes in patients with EBV+ DLBCL, and may facilitate risk stratification and individualized treatment decisions.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is a rare, aggressive malignant tumor with poor prognosis, and the optimal standard treatment remains undefined. High-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX) based regimens continue to be the first-line treatment for newly diagnosed PCNSL. In PCNSL, alterations in B-cell receptor (BCR) signaling pathway-related genes, such as MYD88 and CD79B , have been shown to mediate responses to Bruton’s tyrosine kinase inhibitors (BTKi). Aims: This single-center retrospective analysis aims to evaluate the efficacy of BTKi plus HD-MTX based chemotherapy regimen as indution treatment for newly diagnosed PCNSL patients in a real-world cohort. Methods: We enrolled adult patients with histologically confirmed primary CNS large B cell lymphoma who had received induction treatment with the HD-MTX based chemotherapy regimen, and the combination of BTKi (included ibrutinib, zanubrutinib and orelabrutinib) between January 2020 and June 2025. HD-MTX is defined as ≥3.0 g/m2. When patients achieved complete response (CR) or partial response (PR), autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) or whole brain radiation treatment (WBRT) was recommended as consolidation treatment. Treatment responses were assessed by MRI/PET. Categorical variables were analyzed using chi-square or Fisher's exact tests. Survival was estimated with the Kaplan-Meier method. R software, version 4.3.2 were used for data analysis. A two-sided P

结论（EHA原文）

This single-center retrospective analysis confirms the efficacy of adding BTKi especially orelabrutinib as indution treatment in a real-world Chinese patient population. These results support the use of BTKi-containing treatment regimens as a first-line therapy for PCNSL in clinical practice.

a disease specific prognostic score for immunodeficiency-associated primary cns lymphoma: an international primary cns lymphoma collaborative group (ipcg) study

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：a disease specific prognostic score for immunodeficiency-associated primary cns lymphoma: an international primary cns lymphoma collaborative group (ipcg) study

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

最佳总体缓解率（ORR）为77%（完全缓解50%；部分缓解27%）|||RM-based化疗ORR达85%，利妥昔单抗组68%，甲氨蝶呤组52%（p<0.01）|||中位总生存期（OS）为54个月|||多变量分析：年龄（HR 1.05/年）、KPS<70（HR 2.08）、EBV阳性（HR 3.26）为独立不良预后因素|||预后评分（年龄>60岁、KPS<70、EBV阳性）将患者分为三组：≤1个危险因素中位OS 135个月，2个危险因素中位OS 29个月，3个危险因素中位OS 3个月

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Immunodeficiency-associated primary central nervous system lymphoma (ID-PCNSL) constitutes a clinicopathologically distinct PCNSL variant. Large clinical studies are lacking and existing prognostic models, developed using immunocompetent cohorts, may not be applicable to this patient population. Aims: To characterize clinical and radiological features, treatment outcomes, and prognostic factors in ID-PCNSL and to develop a disease-specific prognostic score. Methods: The International Primary CNS Lymphoma Collaborative Group (IPCG) conducted a retrospective multicenter study of ID-PCNSL, diagnosed between 2003-2024, at 23 centers across 7 countries. Clinical, radiological, and pathological data were collected. Survival outcomes were assessed using Kaplan–Meier estimates and multivariable Cox regression. Independent predictors of survival were combined to derive a prognostic score and compared with established MSKCC and IELSG models.

结论（EHA原文）

This large international cohort defines the clinical spectrum of ID-PCNSL and demonstrates substantial heterogeneity in outcomes. Immune reconstitution combined with RM-based therapy is associated with high response rates across immunodeficiency subtypes. A simple prognostic score based on age, performance status, and EBV status provides robust risk stratification, remains informative in RM-treated patients, and outperforms established models developed for immunocompetent PCNSL.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 308 patients with ID-PCNSL were identified. Underlying immunodeficiency resulted from immunosuppressive therapy for organ transplantation (41.2%) or autoimmune disease (36.7%), and from HIV infection (21.7%). All tumors were classified as diffuse large B-cell lymphomas, with Epstein–Barr virus (EBV) detected in 79.2%. \n Most patients (91.4%) received curative-intent induction therapy, predominantly systemic chemotherapy (97.5%), while radiation alone was uncommon (2.1%). Rituximab–methotrexate (RM)–based regimens were most frequently used (69.8%), followed by rituximab-based (15.6%) and methotrexate-based therapy alone (12.7%). Best overall response rate (ORR) to first-line therapy was 77% (complete response 50%; partial response 27%). RM-based chemotherapy achieved higher ORR (85%) compared with rituximab-based (68%, p=0.01) or methotrexate-based regimens alone (52%, p \n Outcomes were heterogeneous, with a median overall survival (OS) of 54 months ( Fig. 1A) . Multivariable analysis identified increasing age (HR 1.05 per year, 95% CI 1.02–1.07; p Fig. 1B ), Karnofsky Performance Status (KPS) Fig. 1C ), and EBV positivity (HR 3.26, 95% CI 1.47–7.33; p=0.004; Fig. 1D ) as independent predictors of inferior OS. A prognostic score incorporating these factors (age >60 years, KPS Fig. 1E ) stratified patients into three risk groups with median OS of 135, 29, and 3 months for patients with ≤1, 2, and 3 risk factors, respectively (p Fig. 1F ). The score retained prognostic significance in patients treated with RM-based regimens. Compared with MSKCC and IELSG scores, the new model demonstrated improved performance with lower AIC and higher concordance index and time-dependent AUC. Conclusion: This large international cohort defines the clinical spectrum of ID-PCNSL and demonstrates substantial heterogeneity in outcomes. Immune reconstitution combined with RM-based therapy is associated with high response rates across immunodeficiency subtypes. A simple prognostic score based on age, performance status, and EBV status provides robust risk stratification, remains informative in RM-treated patients, and outperforms established models developed for immunocompetent PCNSL.

分组：学术癌症项目组（ACP）：学术/研究项目（包括NCI指定中心）；社区癌症项目组（CCP）：社区、综合社区和综合网络癌症项目

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：学术癌症项目组（ACP）：学术/研究项目（包括NCI指定中心）；社区癌症项目组（CCP）：社区、综合社区和综合网络癌症项目

O 结局指标

总生存期（OS）：ACP组中位生存期0.48年，CCP组0.32年；2年生存率：ACP 30.8% vs CCP 23.2%；5年生存率：ACP 18.9% vs CCP 12.8%；10年生存率：ACP 8.8% vs CCP 5.2%|||早期死亡率：30天死亡率ACP 3.1% vs CCP 3.9%；90天死亡率ACP 10.3% vs CCP 13.0%|||未接受治疗比例：ACP 6.2% vs CCP 11.6%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary Central Nervous System Lymphoma (PCNSL) is a rare, aggressive subtype of non-Hodgkin lymphoma with increasing incidence in the U.S (ACSPMID:19273630). Outcomes in older adults remain poor; prior cohorts of patients aged >70 years reported a 2-year overall survival of 50% (NCBIPMID:32241841). Facility-level differences in care have been reported, but their impact on older adults is unclear. We compared academic vs community cancer programs in elderly PCNSL to evaluate demographic, socioeconomic, and survival differences. Aims: Primary Aim: To evaluate whether treatment facility type (Academic Cancer Programs vs Community Cancer Programs) is associated with differences in overall survival (OS) among patients aged ≥75 years with primary CNS lymphoma (PCNSL) using a national database. Methods: A retrospective cohort study of patients diagnosed with PCNSL between 2004-2022 using the National Cancer Database (NCDB) for patients ≥75 years old. Patients were classified by treatment facility: ACP (academic/research programs including NCI-designated centers) vs. CCP (community, comprehensive community, and integrated network cancer programs). Demographic, clinical, and treatment characteristics were compared using chi-square and Wilcoxon tests. Kaplan-Meier and Cox proportional hazards models were used to compare overall survival (OS), adjusting for age, race/ethnicity, insurance status, Charlson-Deyo comorbidity index, and distance traveled for care.

结论（EHA原文）

Among patients aged ≥75 years with PCNS, OS differed significantly by treatment facility type, with a statistically and clinically meaningful survival advantage observed among patients treated at ACP compared with CCP. OS difference was consistent across short- and long-term follow-up with lower early mortality, higher rates of treatment delivery, and shorter time to initiation of therapy at ACP. These results point to system-level gaps in care for older adults with PCNSL and underscore the need to strengthen referral pathways to ACP and build structured academic–community partnerships. Doing so could expand timely access to specialized multidisciplinary care and clinical trials for vulnerable patients more often treated in lower-resource settings. \n

brain-lym: defining immune-molecular phenotypes in primary cns lymphoma

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) is a distinct, immune-privileged diffuse large B-cell lymphoma with high relapse rates despite high-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX)–based polychemotherapy. While immune-directed treatments, like CAR T-cells and bispecific antibodies are increasingly explored, the immune-molecular architecture of PCNSL and its relation to therapy response remain poorly defined (PMID: 33664848, 36402300) . Defining clinically relevant immune-molecular subgroups is essential to enable rational implementation of immunotherapy. Aims: To perform a nationwide integrated in-depth DNA and RNA analysis of PCNSL tumors, linking immune-molecular profiles to treatment response to identify subgroups with potential therapeutic implications. Methods: Patients with histologically confirmed PCNSL (2000–2022) treated with ≥1 cycle HD-MTX-based chemotherapy were included. DNA and RNA were extracted from FFPE. Gene-expression profiling using the BLYM-777 panel (biology-driven 777-gene lymphoma panel, PMID: 35454765) assessed tumor-intrinsic and microenvironment signatures. Targeted next-generation sequencing was performed for mutational profiling.

结论（EHA原文）

To our knowledge, this is one of the largest nationwide integrated DNA/RNA analyses of HD-MTX treated PCNSL linking immune-molecular profiles to standardized clinical response categories. According to Kotlov et al., GEP data identified three subgroups with distinct immune characteristics: immune-low, immune-evasive and immune-rich. These findings provide a biological framework for immune-based patient stratification in future PCNSL trials.

182CNSL回顾性/真实世界研究SCNSL/CNS复发或预防CAR-T/细胞治疗PS2235

autologous hematopoietic stem cell transplantation combined with cd19 car-t cell therapy for central nervous system lymphoma: a clinical efficacy and safety analysis

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Central nervous system lymphoma (CNSL) has an extremely poor prognosis with limited efficacy from conventional therapies. Although CD19-targeted chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CD19 CAR-T) therapy has achieved breakthroughs in systemic B-cell lymphomas, its application in CNSL faces challenges including the blood-brain barrier, the unique CNS immune microenvironment, and potential neurotoxicity. Autologous hematopoietic stem cell transplantation (ASCT) can reduce tumor burden through myeloablative conditioning and create a favorable environment for CAR-T cell expansion, suggesting synergistic potential with sequential combination. Currently, clinical evidence for ASCT combined with CD19 CAR-T therapy in CNSL remains extremely limited. Aims: To evaluate the clinical efficacy and safety of ASCT combined with CD19 CAR-T cell therapy in patients with CNSL. Methods: Clinical data were retrospectively collected from CNSL patients who received ASCT combined with CAR-T therapy at the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University between July 2023 and August 2025. All patients received myeloablative conditioning chemotherapy followed by autologous stem cell infusion and subsequent sequential infusion of CD19 CAR-T cells. The primary endpoints were objective response rate (ORR) and complete response rate (CRR). Secondary endpoints included overall survival (OS), progression-free survival (PFS), CAR-T cell peak expansion, hematopoietic reconstitution time, and treatment-related adverse events.

结论（EHA原文）

ASCT combined with CD19 CAR-T therapy demonstrates excellent efficacy and a favorable safety profile with newly diagnosed and relapsed/refractory CNSL, warranting further validation in larger cohorts with extended follow-up.

183CNSL回顾性/真实世界研究SCNSL/CNS复发或预防CAR-T/细胞治疗PS2092

glofitamab单药或联合治疗复发/难治性原发性或继发性中枢神经系统淋巴瘤：一项多中心回顾性研究

glofitamab monotherapy or combination therapy in patients with relapsed/refractory primary or secondary central nervous system lymphoma: a multicenter retrospective study

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=96；疾病阶段：复发/难治，继发性，原发性

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：格菲妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：试验组1：glofitamab单药治疗；试验组2：glofitamab联合其他治疗（联合药物由医生决定）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：glofitamab单药治疗；试验组2：glofitamab联合其他治疗（联合药物由医生决定）

O 结局指标

客观缓解率（ORR）：91.8%（95% CI 84.0%-96.8%） 完全缓解率（CRR）：66.6%（95% CI 55.8%-75.8%） 中位无进展生存期（PFS）：15.8个月（95% CI 12.8-未达到） 6个月PFS率：78.8%（95% CI 71.0%-88.7%） 12个月PFS率：62.0%（95% CI 50.2%-77.0%） 细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率：40.6%（均为1-2级） 免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）发生率：8%

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Patients with relapsed or refractory primary or secondary central nervous system lymphoma (R/R PCNSL/SCNSL) have a dismal prognosis with limited subsequent treatment options. The efficacy and safety profiles of bispecific antibody therapy in this population remain ambiguous. Aims: To evaluate the efficacy and safety of glofitamab-based therapy in patients with relapsed/refractory central nervous system lymphoma (R/R CNSL). Methods: R/R CNSL patients who received at least one dose of glofitamab across 24 Chinese medical facilities were investigated. All patients had histologically confirmed diffuse large B-cell lymphoma with documented CNS involvement and were heavily pretreated by chemotherapy, whole brain radiotherapy, or CAR-T therapy. After providing informed consent, patients received obinutuzumab (1000 mg on cycle 1 day 1) as premedication, followed by glofitamab step-up dosing: 2.5 mg on cycle 1 day 8, 10 mg on cycle 1 day 15, and 30 mg on cycle 2 day 1, then 30 mg every 3 weeks thereafter for up to 12 cycles, with or without combination agents at the physician’s discretion. CNS response was assessed by IPCG criteria using contrast-enhanced brain/spine MRI and CSF analysis. For SCNSL, systemic disease was evaluated by whole-body PET-CT scan per Lugano 2014. The primary endpoint was the objective response rate (ORR), defined as the proportion of patients who achieved a confirmed best overall response (BOR) of complete response (CR) or partial response (PR). Secondary endpoints included complete response rate (CRR), progression-free survival (PFS), overall survival (OS), and safety profiles (incidences of CRS and ICANS).

结论（EHA原文）

These findings demonstrate that glofitamab-based therapy yields substantial antitumor activity with a manageable safety profile in heavily treatment-experienced R/R CNSL patients, indicating a potentially promising treatment paradigm.

development and validation of a clinicopathological prognostic model for primary central nervous system lymphoma

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=180；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：development and validation of a clinicopathological prognostic model for primary central nervous system lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

中位年龄60岁（18-82岁）；男性占56.67%；DLBCL病理亚型占95%；多变量Cox回归显示年龄≥60岁（HR:2.58），ECOG-PS≥2（HR:4.28），MYC表达（HR:2.76）为独立预后因素；模型在训练集和验证集的AUC分别为0.74和0.89

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: The IELSG and MSKCC prognostic scoring systems, while commonly used for primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL), present certain limitations in clinical practice. The IELSG model is constrained by the inconsistent availability of LDH and CSF protein measurements, whereas the MSKCC system relies solely on age and Karnofsky performance status, potentially limiting its prognostic scope. Aims: This study seeks to establish and validate a novel prognostic model leveraging real-world clinical data to enhance predictive accuracy and practical applicability. Methods: A retrospective analysis was conducted on 180 newly diagnosed PCNSL patients (≥ 18 years) treated at our center between January 2012 and January 2025. Overall survival (OS) served as the primary endpoint, with progression-free survival (PFS) as the secondary endpoint. Patients were randomly divided into training (70%) and validation (30%) cohorts. Univariable and multivariable Cox regression analyses were performed to identify factors associated with OS. A novel prognostic model was constructed based on multivariable findings and subsequently assessed for calibration, discriminative ability, and clinical utility in both cohorts.

结论（EHA原文）

This study presents a novel prognostic model integrating age, ECOG-PS, and MYC expression to predict OS in newly diagnosed PCNSL patients. By incorporating high-risk clinicopathological features associated with tumor aggressiveness, this model may facilitate more individualized treatment planning.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The median age at diagnosis of the enrolled 180 patients was 60 years (range: 18–82 years), with 56.67% (102/180) being male. Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) constituted the predominant pathological subtype (95%, 171/180). Treatment modalities included subtotal/total tumor resection in 135 cases (75%), biopsy alone in 45 cases (25%), high-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX)-based chemotherapy in 67 cases (37.22%), and combination therapies (including radiotherapy or hematopoietic cell transplantation) in 30 cases (16.7%). Multivariable Cox regression identified age ≥ 60 years (HR: 2.58, p 2 (HR: 4.28, p p (Figure 1A) . The model exhibited good discrimination, with area under the curve values of 0.74 and 0.89 in the training and validation cohorts, respectively (Figure 1B-C) . Calibration curves demonstrated high consistency between the predicted probabilities and actual observations. Furthermore, risk stratification based on this model revealed significant differences in survival status among patients in different risk groups, indicating that this risk stratification strategy can effectively differentiate patient prognosis (Figure 1D-E) . Conclusion: This study presents a novel prognostic model integrating age, ECOG-PS, and MYC expression to predict OS in newly diagnosed PCNSL patients. By incorporating high-risk clinicopathological features associated with tumor aggressiveness, this model may facilitate more individualized treatment planning.

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Patients with diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) and primary central nervous system lymphoma (PCNSL) experiencing relapse after autologous hematopoietic cell transplantation (AHCT) have poor outcomes. Factors predicting the risk of post-transplant relapse risk are unknown. Aims: The aim of this multicenter real-world study was to identify factors impacting post-transplant outcomes in systemic DLBCL or PCNSL. Methods: The study population consisted of 119 patients with systemic DLBCL and 40 patients with PCNSL who underwent AHCT between 2000 and 2019 in three University Hospitals in Finland (Kuopio, Tampere, Oulu). Data were retrospectively collected from patients’ medical records including e.g. patient and disease characteristics and outcome. Early relapse was defined as occurring

结论（EHA原文）

PCNSL patients receiving AHCT after their first relapse were significantly more likely to experience post-transplant relapse if their pre-mobilization response was worse than CR. Our new risk classification for post-transplant relapse divides systemic DLBCL patients into three groups with significantly different RFS rates. Larger studies are needed to validate this classification.

对于预测CNS淋巴瘤：敏感性100%（95%CI: 77.1-100%），特异性94.4%（95%CI: 77.3-99.1%），阳性预测值（PPV）未提供，阴性预测值100%（95%CI: 83.9-100%）

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Primary Vitreoretinal Lymphoma (PVRL) is a rare subtype of predominantly aggressive B-cell lymphoma that manifests in the vitreus and/or retina and is associated with poor clinical outcomes mostly due to frequent involvement of the central nervous system (CNS). PVRL remains a diagnostic challenge for ophthalmologists, pathologists and hematologists, as standardized diagnostic guidelines are lacking. Aims: In this retrospective single-center analysis, we aimed to evaluate the utility of multiparametric flow cytometry analysis (MPFC) for the diagnosis of PVRL in vitrectomy samples. Furthermore, we wanted to assess the sensitivity, specificity and predictive values of MPFC in identifying patients at risk for CNS lesions after identification of monoclonal B-cells in the vitreus. Methods: A total of 49 pars plana vitrectomy (PPV) samples were analyzed for monoclonal B-cells (CD45, CD19, CD5, CD10 and immunoglobulin light chains κ/λ) using MPFC. Statistical comparisons between positive and negative samples were conducted using the Mann–Whitney U test. \nTo determine the diagnostic accuracy of MPFC for predicting CNS involvement following identification of a monoclonal B-cell population in the vitrectomy sample, 34 patients were followed for a median of 31 months, and MPFC findings were validated against subsequent definitive evidence of lymphoma, including CSF analysis, imaging by MRI or CT and clinical evolution. Sensitivity, specificity, positive predictive value (PPV), and negative predictive value (NPV) of MPFC were calculated.

结论（EHA原文）

MPFC analysis of vitrectomy samples represents a valuable diagnostic tool in suspected PVRL. Detection of intravitreal monoclonal B-cells was associated with increased risk of concomitant or subsequent CNS involvement, supporting the need for systematic CNS staging upon initial diagnosis as well as close surveillance during the first year after diagnosis.

cost-effectiveness of axicabtagene ciloleucel for treating taiwanese patients with relapsed/refractory diffuse large b-cell lymphoma and high-grade b-cell lymphoma after first-line treatment

摘要（EHA原文）

Background: Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) is the predominant and aggressive non-Hodgkin lymphoma subtype in Taiwan, accounting for 60% of B-cell lymphomas and 2.19% of all cancer cases in 2023. Despite chemoimmunotherapy such as R-CHOP being the standard first-line (1L) treatment, outcomes remain poor for patients with relapsed or refractory (R/R) DLBCL and high-grade B-cell lymphoma (HGBL), particularly those who are refractory to 1L therapy or relapse within 12 months, highlighting an unmet need in second-line (2L) treatment. Recently, chimeric antigen receptor T-cell (CAR T-cell) therapy, including axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel), has demonstrated promising clinical benefits and has been approved as a 2L option in the United States, Europe, and Taiwan. Aims: This study aims to evaluate the cost-effectiveness of axi-cel versus standard of care (SoC) as a 2L treatment for Taiwanese patients with DLBCL and HGBL. Methods: A three-state partitioned survival model (event-free, post-event, and death) was used to estimate the cost-effectiveness of axi-cel versus SoC (i.e., chemoimmunotherapy ± high-dose therapy and autologous stem cell transplantation) as 2L treatment from the Taiwan National Health Insurance (NHI) perspective. Clinical outcomes were informed by the ZUMA-7 randomized controlled trial, enrolling patients with R/R DLBCL and HGBL within 12 months after 1L therapy. Healthcare resource use and costs were informed by NHI data and literature. The model applied a lifetime horizon with monthly cycles, a starting age of 61.1 years based on NHI data, and a 3% annual discounting. Quality-adjusted life years (QALYs), total costs, and incremental cost-effectiveness ratios (ICERs) were estimated in US dollars (exchange rate: 1 USD = 30 NTD). Treatment crossover in the ZUMA-7 standard-of-care arm was adjusted using rank preserving structural failure time models, and adverse event costs were based on local expert inputs and NHI data.

结论（EHA原文）

Axi-cel yields substantial clinical benefits and represents a cost-effective use of NHI resources for the 2L treatment of DLBCL and HGBL in Taiwan. These findings support the clinical and economic value of early CAR T-cell adoption for eligible patients.
